-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2223962c5d5c4f598df1ac488edeee8b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2223962c5d5c4f598df1ac488edeee8b");'><span id='2223962c5d5c4f598df1ac488edeee8b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=974')">972-974年</a>，33-35岁</div><div id='2223962c5d5c4f598df1ac488edeee8b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　春，游学长安，有诗。作品：花雨比下秦中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_81781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>花雨比下秦中</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81781")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_81781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81781'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81781'>雨里飞花片片红，雨微花乱转溟濛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81781'>川原何处连天草，帘幕无人半日风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81781'>寂寞刘桢新病后，凄迷庄舄苦吟中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81781'>可堪更是黄昏景，燕冷莺寒恨想同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81781'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_81781_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　秋，游学长安，有诗。作品：离怀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_81796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>离怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81796")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_81796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81796'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81796'>离怀如醉复如痴，脉脉无言不展眉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81796'>秋草空牵幽意在，征轩疑有断魂随。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81796'>残星更漏门开处，斜月<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作日）</span>帘栊酒醒时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81796'>此恨谁能解消遣，因题红叶偶成诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81796'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_81796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　本年，游学长安，结识韩丕，居骊山白鹿观读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=973&endYear=973')">973年</a>　本年，与韩丕居骊山白鹿观读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=974')">974年</a>　春，游学长安，有诗寄宋白。作品：寄蒲城宋白小著。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一五。孙谱系此诗于开宝五年，此据马伟《田锡入仕前游学活动考述》（载杨渭生主编《徐规教授从事教学科研工作五十周年纪念文集》，杭州大学出版社1995年版）改。）</span><div id='poem_81801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄蒲城宋白小著</a><span class='authorDate'>（974年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81801")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_81801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81801'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81801'>春日闲销一局棋，春愁还得数篇诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81801'>高吟大醉何人问，英略雄图久<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作欠）</span>已知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81801'>破产虽无容足所，丈夫岂合以家为。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81801'>时来富贵终须有，懒学梁鸿赋五噫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81801'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_81801_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
蒲城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='59f5c94481594999bf72dfaff2421813_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("59f5c94481594999bf72dfaff2421813");'><span id='59f5c94481594999bf72dfaff2421813_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=975')">974-975年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='59f5c94481594999bf72dfaff2421813' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=974')">974年</a>　本年，由长安迁至蒲城宋白处寄居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=974')">974年</a>　本年，寄居蒲城，上书梁周翰，求汲引。作品：贻梁补阙周翰书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1147445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贻梁补阙周翰书</a><span class='authorDate'>（974年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147445")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147445'>十一月日，进士田锡谨斋沐拜手，献书于补阙执事：锡每见仕进之心，皆欲人特达之遇，而觊遭逢之幸，不揣道何如也，才何如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147445_comment'></div>迨为明哲之鉴，揣摩其术，高下其才，特达之遇果不为丛脞所役，则怅然觖望，以为鉴失于己，而啧有烦谤之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147445_comment'></div>君子则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147445_comment'></div>不患无通明之知，患艺之未精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147445_comment'></div>不患无特达之遇，患才之未备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147445_comment'></div>不以得失荣辱，汩其趣向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147445_comment'></div>昔牛僧孺欲干有司之试，先以文章卜进退于韩愈，愈高其才，遽命改馆，俟其亡而访焉，乃大署其门而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147445_comment'></div>翌日辇毂之下，僧孺之名无翼而飞，藉藉众口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147445_comment'></div>此所谓级名阶第，不在于彼，而在于此，束缊知妇，势使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147445_comment'></div>凡有司以至公之明，当抡材之任，岂欲自擅于公器哉，亦候同列推择，慰荐茂异，以济己之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147445_comment'></div>陆贽在唐，为海内之闻人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147445_comment'></div>当其掌文之柄，录贤拔善，得贾棱、王涯、李观、韩愈、崔群辈二十三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147445_comment'></div>于时梁肃在谏垣，为之援引，肃之所言者八人，韩愈在其选中，至今称陆忠州、韩吏部，果何如人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147445_comment'></div>岂唯春官氏为国家求贤，而赖同列之推善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147445_comment'></div>抑士君子为先达，常汲汲于外，导后进以为己任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147445_comment'></div>仕进亦岂专务求于人，固当先求诸己；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147445_comment'></div>岂在求诸名，当先求诸实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147445_comment'></div>实茂而名自至，己修而人后知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147445_comment'></div>故特达之遇，不可邀而得也，才与贤相遇，道与义相际，言未发于外，而意已熟于中矣，何暇訾诹慄斯，以徼福哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147445_comment'></div>锡不逮古人远矣，自十有五志于学，逮今二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147445_comment'></div>所吐之文非超绝横厉，骇人耳目，但屑屑在模范轨辗间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147445_comment'></div>又未能鹰扬虹伸，与群俊角逐，而尚在贫贱中，未尝不惕然愧耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147445_comment'></div>虽迂疏钝讷之若是，然志有所自守，迹有所自明，必也跻一第，拜一命，庶几无忝于时，无愧于心，不使识者指目而窃笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147445_comment'></div>斯愿斯恳，非英信明达之大贤，固不敢妄发斯言以取谴怒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147445_comment'></div>今明公鉴如止水，公如平衡，言如钩绳，动为律度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147445_comment'></div>刚决之气，断于奖激；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147445_comment'></div>融和之色，形于接纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147445_comment'></div>锡是用曲俗之态，短绠之智，愿为门下之士，期明公以通达之识，照其邪直，烛其妍媸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147445_comment'></div>茍若万分之一可偕士林之末，则明公英特之遇不施于仆，仆遭逢之幸不自于明公，则直在锡也，曲在公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147445_comment'></div>亦犹南医善蠲人之疾，疾者亦自善导养，能消息其气，以合于医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147445_comment'></div>但俟锱铢善良之药，则㸌然洞散其湫底羸露之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147445_comment'></div>而南医持其疾以邀丰腆之酬，一旦为北医急于仁义，投以灵饵，起于瞑眩，南医虽悔，其可复追！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147445_comment'></div>故君子临仁义，速不旋踵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147445_comment'></div>锡今所谓消息其气，以合于善良之药者也，善医者幸早图之，无为他人搀惠而悔追弗及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147445_comment'></div>抑近世仕进之子，不敢历公卿士大夫之门，虑殖嫌疑于栽培之地，而耦俱生谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147445_comment'></div>设使负非常之才，有非常之名，彼世疑俗嫌，又何畏忌违去之有哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147445_comment'></div>必若伏奏于丹墀之下，导扬其名于天子，使赫然超拔，虽谗慝之口欲疵疠讆訾，于正人哉，岂徒涉猜履谤而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147445_comment'></div>使其人为囚奴，为俘虏，为负贩，为仇雠，而道有可贵，尚当哀穷悼屈，洗磨振擢，趣其亟也若濡救焚灼、提引沦溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147445_comment'></div>况冠儒之冠，服儒之服，与群俊俯仰，耀广场之风彩，而不敢挺然与之为迒蹊，则岂唯负于才良，其实负于邦国也，其次负于己心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147445_comment'></div>锡愧无超迈之才，以成明公特达之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147445_comment'></div>然观前辈以一言一辞瑰壮峻爽，为当世有名之士飞腾吹嘘，如杜牧《阿房宫赋》，李华《吊墀战场文》，李翱《高悯女碑》，高迈《长明灯颂》，如观灵凤一毛，则五彩九苞从而可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147445_comment'></div>锡自省介言只辞，不足买声彩于拟议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147445_comment'></div>然录长掩短，亦可彰君子奖善之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147445_comment'></div>谨以所编鄙陋之文五十轴，贽于几阁，卜进退于明公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147445_comment'></div>济命谓之进，方敢进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147445_comment'></div>若犹未也，则有圣人六经在，当复厉精于其间，而决取舍于至公而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147445_comment'></div>不量狂瞽，干冒明哲，恭俟报复，惶惧惶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147445_comment'></div>锡拜手上<span class='inlineComment2'>（《咸平集》卷三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147445_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1147445'>役：</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1147445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=975&endYear=975')">975年</a>　夏，寄居蒲城，有诗咏时事。作品：夏日即事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_81795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏日即事</a><span class='authorDate'>（975年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53793'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53793'>紫皇御天方视事，将择灵官补仙吏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53793'>宝盘初赐红霞馔，斗魁挹酒空淋漓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_53793'>又有骊龙长万尺，波涛为屋渊为室。<div id='poem_sentence_6_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_53793'>能探骊珠折得桂，方许骖鸾驾凤皇，方令碧落为星郎<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_53793'>君曾再对珠旒试，君才堪作仙宫吏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_53793'>骊珠粲粲蟾枝香，紫烟华绶黄霓裳。<div id='poem_sentence_11_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_53793'>风装云驭惯升陟，太霄瀚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>海尝翱翔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_53793'>愿以横天之鹏为逸驾，垂天之虹作飞梁。<div id='poem_sentence_13_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_53793'>驰雷走电以惊策，叱风挥雨前启行。<div id='poem_sentence_14_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_53793'>结水精佩云锦章，随君一至于仙乡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_53793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_53793'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_53793_0'>⑴ 所以房星之精姓东方，字曼倩，受天命，佐炎汉；昴星之灵其姓萧，其名何，贵为相，封于酂。复有中台称茂先，读书三十车，乃为晋朝辅相之大臣。又有长庚字太白，下笔一万字，是为唐朝之俊人。予知下则诞而为俊杰，上则列之为星辰。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_53793_0'>⑵ 原作瀚，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_53793_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81789")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_81789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81789'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81789'>寂寂闲居客至稀，静中滋味意何归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81789'>因探易象知深旨，自喜吟高得化机。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81789'>桑露乍寒蚕欲老，草烟才暖蝶交飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81789'>樊川物景终南翠，遂性空思杜紫微。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81789'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_81789_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　春，寄居蒲城，有诗。作品：惜春词。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_81851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惜春词</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81851")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81851'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81851'>春色初从江国来，湖边杨柳岭头梅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81851'>梅花飞雪柳垂带，递次相将时节催。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81851'>春力欺寒过江北，深谷黄鹂生羽翼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81851'>晓月轻烟禁苑啼，南园桃李已成蹊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81851'>就中何处芳菲好，春波飞絮魏王堤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81851'>我忆去年暮春月，京洛新妆丹凤阙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81851'>天津水绿烟树深，万井笙歌牡丹发。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81851'>天子銮舆驾幸时，嵩峰瑞霭笼郊圻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81851'>扈从千官与万骑，翊卫羽休兼佽飞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81851'>六宫随驾罗珠翠，诸王从行陪七贵。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81851'>香气成霞金犊车，呜珂中节虹龙驷。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81851'>朱桥细柳端门前，画舫横塘会节园。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81851'>朝花贵侠珊瑚席，夜烛娇娥玳惠筵。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81851'>西楼残月深宫漏，明河半沈垂北斗。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81851'>纵饮贪欢意未阑，紫陌喧喧人已繁。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81851'>玉钩挂帘开雉尾，晓日赭袍朝至尊。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81851'>方今寓止临清渭，杜门无与天涯异。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81851'>殊忘诗酒狂荡心，但悦琴书高古意。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81851'>可惜春芳渐欲归，五陵烟草方离离。<div id='poem_sentence_18_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_81851'>回忆当时洛阳道，歌魂空与残花飞。<div id='poem_sentence_19_81851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_81851'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_81851_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6d53bb600aa94718a36b2a7d984b42d9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6d53bb600aa94718a36b2a7d984b42d9");'><span id='6d53bb600aa94718a36b2a7d984b42d9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年</a>，39岁</div><div id='6d53bb600aa94718a36b2a7d984b42d9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>二月，寄居蒲城，有书寄胡旦。作品：答胡旦书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1147443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答胡旦书</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147443")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147443'>秀才即先辈：人来得书，窃知宁适，慰悦之外，感荷良深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147443_comment'></div>兼蒙见招，俾与文会，良期美信，莫尚于兹，甚善甚善！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147443_comment'></div>余念自出蜀至咸、镐间，今已六稔，再迁家，两遇权停贡举，羁旅中支离契阔，幽忧愁辛，大丈夫壮节殆亦销烁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147443_comment'></div>今吾子书中怜余家贫援寡，久住关辅，乃知我者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147443_comment'></div>古人所重者交结，翼道佑德，激切奋发，何莫由斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147443_comment'></div>故吕布、袁遂为奔走之交，晋文、介推为急难之友，垂在信史，有志者慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147443_comment'></div>余每自惟，无英才大略以为慷慨事，又无嘉辞优学以为君子儒，而吾子过听虚名，相厚之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147443_comment'></div>往年得澶渊之书，前岁偶渭北之会，今春得夷门之信，适足见惠然相顾之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147443_comment'></div>《易》不云乎：君子定其交而后求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147443_comment'></div>《语》不云乎：君子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1147443", 1147443, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>以文会友</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147443_comment'></div>古乐府有《结客少年场》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147443_comment'></div>今三者君皆兼之，恭佩徽音，敢不勉信与学，以为奉交之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147443_comment'></div>古人云：易失者时，难得者知音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147443_comment'></div>余尝读《西汉书》，见高祖以英武取天下，而文帝以道德化海内，措刑不用几四十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147443_comment'></div>于时最称俊才而年少者有贾谊，观其所上书，真卿相才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147443_comment'></div>然当宣室受釐之际，思鬼神事，诏谊问之，不觉膝之前席，然终不能大用，惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147443_comment'></div>迨至有唐贞元、长庆间，儒雅大备，洋洋乎可以兼周、汉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147443_comment'></div>帝王好文，士君子以名节文藻相乐于升平之世，斯实天地会通之运也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147443_comment'></div>自数百载罕遇盛事，今锡与君偶斯时焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147443_comment'></div>自吕状元蒙正得第之后，有御制诗以赐之，闻两制中得与上倡和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147443_comment'></div>昔汉世祖以《外戚传》赐窦融，以《河渠书》赐王景，唐太宗、玄宗与侍从臣以文赋相酬酢，今复睹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147443_comment'></div>况吾子负倜傥之气，怀磊落之才，将来振海内之名，鼓天下之动，广视阔步于场屋，飞声走响于公卿，高掇荣名，若坐会稽，临沧海，投犗十二而钓取巨鳌也，孰不伟之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147443_comment'></div>然锡自得君书，三复窥绎，其中有云：「将来举公，有宋、李、赵三才子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147443_comment'></div>君欲以文彩声称与之相较胜，亦犹洞庭震泽，幅员千里，吞纳江汉，虽飞涛骇湍，浮天沃日，得不委之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147443_comment'></div>壮哉，真场籍中燕魏豪侠也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147443_comment'></div>君既不以余鄙陋浅近，许与为交游，若使各言其志，则余尝闻孟轲称仲尼曰「德之流行，速于置邮而传命」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147443_comment'></div>又曰：「至仁无敌」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147443_comment'></div>《礼》称颜子「得一善必拳拳服膺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147443_comment'></div>《语》曰：「德不孤，必有邻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147443_comment'></div>设使至艺如至仁，自然无敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147443_comment'></div>德茍修，而众善必为己邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147443_comment'></div>名载德而行，故君子金玉其名，砥砺其行，行茂而名荣，人莫得而胜之也，又何必肝胆楚越，而使人莫己胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147443_comment'></div>昔郭代公在国学，家寄三百万钱适至，为急难者告之，倾装以赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147443_comment'></div>代公器局之名，从而得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147443_comment'></div>又王起知举，命白敏中疏贺报，甚而欲以状元待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147443_comment'></div>白敏中曰：「一第何门不致，奈何轻我至交」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147443_comment'></div>斯则交友之情，从而见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147443_comment'></div>器局之名，当师范代公而求之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147443_comment'></div>交友之情，当企慕白敏中而修之，则何适而不为君子也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147443_comment'></div>吾子勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147443_comment'></div>暮春之月，必获命驾，会挹非晚，欣惬豫深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147443_comment'></div>谨奉书感谢，幸赐详察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147443_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147443_comment'></div>京兆田锡再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1147443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>二月，寄居蒲城，有书寄何士宗。作品：答何士宗书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷三。何士宗，诸书无传，曾官荆州转运使、河东转运使等，参马伟《田锡入仕前游学活动考述》，载杨渭生主编《徐规教授从事教学科研工作五十周年纪念文集》，杭州大学出版社1995年版。）</span><div id='poem_1147444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答何士宗书</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147444")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147444'>二月日，京兆田锡谨致书伸感谢之意于秀才即先辈足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147444_comment'></div>锡自为羁旅之人，久居关辅之地，每思朋英友贤之会，为唱予和汝之文，安知道不远人，天弗违愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147444_comment'></div>当渭北杜门之暇日，有流阳寄信之来人，款关称云：两书偕至，一则安定见寄之札翰，一则长者相投之简笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147444_comment'></div>骇闻斯言，欣然而出，屦及于寝门之外，带及乎宾阶之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147444_comment'></div>得二贤之书，对使乎朗读，喜与抃会，形相翼飞，胜获连城之珍，若听在悬之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147444_comment'></div>因自退省，何从而来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147444_comment'></div>且予秉笔非俊豪之才，待问无优深之学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147444_comment'></div>智不足以详论大事，名不足以推伏众人，岂谓骤承君子之交，便以国士遇我？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147444_comment'></div>诚为误听，安敢克当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147444_comment'></div>然英气吐虹蜺，嘉辞敌珠玉，激余以善道，来我以良期，不觉增慷慨之壮图，生抑扬之锐志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147444_comment'></div>亦犹观白起长平之胜，入亚夫细柳之营，鼓噪而屋瓦皆飞，令严而天子按辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147444_comment'></div>懦夫为之增气，势使之然，敢不悦投分之见知，重一言之然诺？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147444_comment'></div>虽未窥卫玠之容貌，未交夷甫之谈谐，在君子以道为心，以信为体，文彩为貌，声称为言，又何必敷衽相亲，晤言以接，方云识面，始谓知心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147444_comment'></div>故千里之喻，比肩倾盖，若同曩日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147444_comment'></div>《略例》云：「隆墀永叹，远壑必盈」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147444_comment'></div>《管子》曰：「无翼而飞者声也，不根而固者情也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147444_comment'></div>哲人交结之旨，尺书邀激之辞，吻合予心，适令得志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147444_comment'></div>况今主上以文明之道化四海，良相以清静之理育万方，卿大夫以名节相高，士君子以儒雅取进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147444_comment'></div>钟是鼎新之运，乐乎升平之时，茍不左交英豪，右结俊造，与振藻名场之会，陪鸣珂帝里之游，则亦是包羞，安能免诮？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147444_comment'></div>方俟夙仆夫之驾，赴同人之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147444_comment'></div>岂唯一咏一觞，为文章之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147444_comment'></div>一名一第，阶云霄之高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147444_comment'></div>余欲以六经为寰区，以史籍为藩翰，聚诸子为职方之贡，疏众集为云梦之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147444_comment'></div>然后左属忠信之櫜鞬，右执文章之鞭弭，以与韩、柳、元、白相周旋于中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147444_comment'></div>未喻此旨于君何如尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147444_comment'></div>愿言之志，尚难罄输，幸稍留意，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147444_comment'></div>锡拜上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1147444_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=975&endYear=975')">975年</a>　本年，至东京，与宋白游汴水。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4959ea07e3e74effb5a94cb8be21f173_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4959ea07e3e74effb5a94cb8be21f173");'><span id='4959ea07e3e74effb5a94cb8be21f173_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>，38岁</div><div id='4959ea07e3e74effb5a94cb8be21f173' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　秋，于开封府参加发解试，作赋。作品：开封府试人文化成天下赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《咸平集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1147163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开封府试人文化成天下赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以「焕乎人文，化成天下」为韵。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147163")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147163'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147163'>大哉至明之君，膺景运，集洪勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147163_comment'></div>跻域中于皇极，化天下以人文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147163_comment'></div>时属升平，焕声明于礼乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147163_comment'></div>道尊儒雅，发谟猷于典坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147163_comment'></div>岂不以丕光大之远图，阐雍熙之至化？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147163_comment'></div>金革斯偃，朝堂多暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147163_comment'></div>遒人述职，方下采于诗声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147163_comment'></div>真宰经邦，亦耻言于强霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147163_comment'></div>美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147163_comment'></div>文之为用也，至化攸先，明乎焕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147163_comment'></div>比万汇流形于厚地，三辰垂象于穹天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147163_comment'></div>藻火衮裳，礼之文也，始饰容而有烂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147163_comment'></div>羽旄缀兆，乐之文也，将达节以相宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147163_comment'></div>故尧舜化民以仁，禹汤跻俗以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147163_comment'></div>致玄德以招著，见皇风之光被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147163_comment'></div>是以鲁史述汤之德也，则曰「齐圣广渊」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147163_comment'></div>《虞书》美尧之仁也，则曰「聪明文思」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147163_comment'></div>宜乎笾豆品数，车服采章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147163_comment'></div>成均掌庠序之齿列，瞽宗司金石之铿锵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147163_comment'></div>绘宗庙之彝器，炳日月于太常：皆文之于外者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147163_comment'></div>黎民阅之以恭肃，靡不昭彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147163_comment'></div>迨乎《易》之教也，厥旨精微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147163_comment'></div>《书》之训也，俾人贞干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147163_comment'></div>《诗》之教也，致流俗之惇厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147163_comment'></div>《春秋》之教也，惩贼臣之叛乱：斯乃文之于内者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147163_comment'></div>万国化之中正，炳然明焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147163_comment'></div>是知抚育中区，恭临宝图，纳生灵于富寿，致品汇于昭苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147163_comment'></div>亦犹挹水于器，而方圆自适；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147163_comment'></div>以木从绳，而规模罔踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147163_comment'></div>是以洋洋邹鲁之风，宜乎盛矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147163_comment'></div>穆穆唐虞之化，猗欤焕乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147163_comment'></div>今我后功格昊穹，泽流区夏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147163_comment'></div>复风俗于淳古，播咏歌于大雅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147163_comment'></div>悦灵台之偃伯，庆华阳之归马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147163_comment'></div>小臣幸与试于王庭，抃蹈于双阙之下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1147163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　秋，于开封府参加发解试，作论。作品：府试守在四夷论。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_1147472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开封府试守在四夷论<span class='inlineComment2'>（限五百字已上成）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147472")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147472'>《春秋》以天下有道，守在四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147472_comment'></div>详丘明之书，观古人垂训，以为明君在上，以道德化育；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147472_comment'></div>良相作弼，以谟猷经纬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147472_comment'></div>故地天交泰，品物咸亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147472_comment'></div>和气感于天，故四时六气无差节候矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147472_comment'></div>至化孚于地，故群动万汇悉遂于生成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147472_comment'></div>当是时，诸侯之国秉璋执圭，奉朝廷之政令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147472_comment'></div>四夷之长率贡纳贽，服帝王之威德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147472_comment'></div>然圣人以道为城池，以仁为网罟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147472_comment'></div>牢笼御备，使悉备于术内；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147472_comment'></div>范围包纳，俾咸入于彀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147472_comment'></div>故《春秋》曰「天生五材，民并用之」，又曰「谁能去兵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147472_comment'></div>《孟子》曰「至仁无敌于天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147472_comment'></div>是则干戈之用，以顺时教战也，用以威戎心也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147472_comment'></div>仁义之用，以观俗设教也，俾以遂物性也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147472_comment'></div>以时教战者，春蒐冬狩，因农之隙，阅兵之实，俾民知御寇之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147472_comment'></div>所谓安不忘危，理不忘乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147472_comment'></div>故仲尼曰：「不教民战，是谓弃之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147472_comment'></div>斯乃御侮之大端，而防患之先备者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147472_comment'></div>守在四夷之义，其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147472_comment'></div>虽以道德羁縻以服其心，然以威武震耀以制其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147472_comment'></div>守之至理，请试别白而论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147472_comment'></div>鲁史曰：「圣达节，次守节」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147472_comment'></div>是则君子理一身，则守五常之教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147472_comment'></div>圣人理天下，则守万机之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147472_comment'></div>守而得其道，则百职具举，而庶政允釐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147472_comment'></div>百职既具举，而庶政既允釐，则四夷不得不畏服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147472_comment'></div>守之一说，亦取蒐狩之狩，谓天下有道，海内无事，威制之柄，唯在四夷，故曰守在四夷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147472_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147472_comment'></div>戎人之心不可以仁信责之，不可以礼教束之，怙强则骚边，畏威则款塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147472_comment'></div>故贾谊有安边之策，晁错有御戎之辞，载在前书，确为嘉论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147472_comment'></div>以为尧舜之圣，禹汤之明，文武之德，其覆之也如昊穹，煦之也若春景，万物靡不浃，群品靡不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147472_comment'></div>当时比屋可封，而外户不闭，犹未能销释兵革，亦未能彻去备御，务在化中国以道，而制外夷以术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147472_comment'></div>今国家承百王之后，应五运之兴，阴阳和，风雨时，日月贞明，黎元胥悦，封疆万里，琛贡交至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147472_comment'></div>虽汉武伸荡定之志，唐时置羁縻之郡，未侔于今日，未偕于圣朝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147472_comment'></div>方今乃守在四夷之秋也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1147472_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　秋，于开封府参加发解试，对策三道。作品：对开封府试策三道。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1147462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开封府试策第三道</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147462")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147462'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147462'>问：周均井赋，汉重力田，皆敦本之良规，为后代之成式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147462_comment'></div>税关市者始防游惰，论盐铁者亦救弊俗，何淳古之渐醨，遂末作而忘返？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147462_comment'></div>不耕而食者塞路，不织而衣者实繁，浮泛之户渐多，兼并之家日富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147462_comment'></div>恃豪强者或势侵于州县，逼饥寒者亦难守于丘园，以至赋籍不增，版图亦耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147462_comment'></div>近世谈论之士，亦有沿革之书，皆非永远之谋，唯取一时之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147462_comment'></div>我国家政同三代，道迈百王，博访群谋，思臻至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147462_comment'></div>秀才道穷秘奥，识洞古今，来副虚求，必怀良策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147462_comment'></div>且井田之利，可以复于古否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147462_comment'></div>力啬之科，可以行于今否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147462_comment'></div>游惰者何以使之返本，兼并者何以使之均齐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147462_comment'></div>禁豪强者何法，拯饥冻者何术？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147462_comment'></div>试为缕陈，无甚高论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147462_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1147462'>对：昔黄帝设井田之法，周文用土著之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147462_comment'></div>故生民之众寡，由是而详焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147462_comment'></div>王者之征赋，由兹而均也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147462_comment'></div>洎秦君图霸，商鞅适变，废哲王经久之术，济强国纵横之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147462_comment'></div>井田遽废，阡陌骤兴，兼并之弊遂生，赋舆之法不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147462_comment'></div>洎汉家垂统，武帝事边，以盐铁六筦之财，佐疆埸连年之用，末作益甚，而黎元愈困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147462_comment'></div>后代救时之弊者，或以土断禁流亡之俗，或以常平均丰歉之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147462_comment'></div>牢笼万邦，平准百货，信史备载，斯言可徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147462_comment'></div>夫井田之赋，千古绝迹，不可复也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147462_comment'></div>力田之科，前王所行，未足尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147462_comment'></div>使游惰者返本，莫若利其衣食之源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147462_comment'></div>使饥冻者相济，莫若抑兼并之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147462_comment'></div>兼并既抑，则贫富自均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147462_comment'></div>贫富既均，则豪强自禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147462_comment'></div>其术安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147462_comment'></div>在乎王者提利权而均国用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147462_comment'></div>重轻万货，歛散百谷，乃其术焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147462_comment'></div>锡愧无待问之才，幸与观光之试，智策无取，方略靡详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147462_comment'></div>忧畏徬徨，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147462_comment'></div>谨对。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1147462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　秋，于开封府参加发解试，得解。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年10月</a>　十月，在东京，有诗寄宋白、韩丕。作品：府解后有诏旨权停贡举因成长句寄太素兼简韩丕茂才。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_81787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81787?labeling=true' target='_blank'>府解后有诏旨权停贡举因成长句寄太素兼简韩丕茂才</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81787")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_81787_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81787'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81787'>一名倜傥动皇州，寄应王门作解头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81787'>将领风骚推李杜，较量英勇让曹刘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81787'>春闱有诏俄中辍，秋赋随时亦暂休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81787'>金殿制科思取应，远飞章句问嘉谋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81787'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_81787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_81787'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_81787_0'>⑴ 自注：曹公谓刘备曰：天下英雄唯我与君尔。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_81787_0'>⑵ 自注：寻有敕开贡举，太素时为左拾遗知兖州。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_81787_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年11月</a>　十一月，在东京，有书上吕端，求汲引。作品：上开封府判书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1147447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上开封府判书</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147447")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147447'>十一月日，进士田锡谨斋沐奉书，献于郎中执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147447_comment'></div>锡辄叙狂愚之恳，上祈英察之明，幸不罪于僭干，望稍垂于怜恕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147447_comment'></div>惶惧惶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147447_comment'></div>《礼》称强学以待问，《易》曰藏器而俟时，诗人垂采菲之辞，君子贵怜才之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147447_comment'></div>锡虽鄙陋，常佩斯言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147447_comment'></div>加以遭逢今幸于升平，激发蝼怀于忠节，思欲一历科场之试，一登卿相之门，观光彩于鸿都，与周旋于造士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147447_comment'></div>然才非挺特，无经邦纬俗之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147447_comment'></div>学未该通，无备问专对之卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147447_comment'></div>但营营谋进，屑屑求知，岂无识者以见嗤，谅亦小人之自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147447_comment'></div>必若择取纤微之善，爱忘瑕谪之非，则蝼蛄亦有五能，而铅锷亦堪一割也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147447_comment'></div>愿敷斯志，罔避枝辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147447_comment'></div>锡闻于《易》曰：「舆尔灵龟，观我朵颐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147447_comment'></div>是戒人之躁进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147447_comment'></div>又曰：「君子见几而作，不俟终日」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147447_comment'></div>是戒人不知变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147447_comment'></div>是则动不可涉观颐之躁，静不可失见几之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147447_comment'></div>今皇上嗣守丕图，殆将周岁，孚大信，霈洪恩，用贤才，黜不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147447_comment'></div>英威果断，有类太宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147447_comment'></div>豁达大度，无异汉祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147447_comment'></div>所以亿兆仰之如日月，裔夷畏之若雷霆，四方肃然，天下大定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147447_comment'></div>乃品物咸亨之际，地天交泰之秋，会议朝堂，公卿则耻言霸道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147447_comment'></div>献能宗伯，士人方歌咏皇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147447_comment'></div>宜乎儒雅道光，贤豪时至，遂令朝在布衣之伍，暮升华绶之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147447_comment'></div>自古汲善拔才，进人之速，未有若斯之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147447_comment'></div>矧复亲王尹正于京府，朝臣司掌于卿书，考艺观能，称廉举秀，当为国荐贤之柄，实求仁弗让之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147447_comment'></div>至有薄才如稊米之微，介善比涓流之细，亦思赴沧溟而委润，与公廪之均输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147447_comment'></div>众才幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147447_comment'></div>鄙人幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147447_comment'></div>锡本颇剑南，徙家关右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147447_comment'></div>淮阴寄食，常慷慨于壮图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147447_comment'></div>方皆上书，愿纵横于见用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147447_comment'></div>固不暇复归故里，求荐他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147447_comment'></div>于是斋庄洁诚，僶俛从事，因拜章于北阙，求就试于南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147447_comment'></div>至精果动于天心，拔解许依于王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147447_comment'></div>幸遇明公以邹、枚之才辩，赞尧、舜之亲贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147447_comment'></div>嘉谋日新，诗礼益哲王之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147447_comment'></div>善计泉涌，钩距成大尹之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147447_comment'></div>衡平而轻重无欺，水定而融明洞鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147447_comment'></div>故群彦尽繄于激发，小人亦翼于矜怜，所谓良工度木之秋，先达援才之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147447_comment'></div>然则言无利害，不足激识者之知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147447_comment'></div>事不崛奇，不足动通人之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147447_comment'></div>是以王璘以缬襦霸誉，奉春以短褐趋朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147447_comment'></div>郦生长揖于时君，王猛踞见于国相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147447_comment'></div>岂不知谦能基德，礼可藩身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147447_comment'></div>然以贱干尊，邈若阶天之险；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147447_comment'></div>以卑谒贵，慄如履虎之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147447_comment'></div>茍不设机变以先声，冀当涂之动念，则夕锦讵知于文彩，哑钟谁辩于舂容？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147447_comment'></div>故有君卿具以自彰，怀长绳而请试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147447_comment'></div>郭代公以轻财见异，裴中令以阴德受知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147447_comment'></div>外黄小儿，一言当而霸王息怒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147447_comment'></div>杞梁女子，一哭恸而长城为摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147447_comment'></div>所以感人以言，不得不切；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147447_comment'></div>从权济志，不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147447_comment'></div>愿形捭阖之书，以卜见知之念，岂徒然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147447_comment'></div>盖欲以尘露至微之益，为刍荛见采之言，幸望怜恕之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147447_comment'></div>锡惶惧惶惧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147447_comment'></div>锡闻忠莫大于进贤，仁莫先于奖善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147447_comment'></div>见义而勇谓之卑，临事无惑谓之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147447_comment'></div>然人不易知，深心有山川之险；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147447_comment'></div>物难求备，良材有大小之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147447_comment'></div>今亲王以荐贤之柄委明公，明公以无实之心举多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147447_comment'></div>然明试之下，与贡之人，染翰飞文，藻鉴必详乎工府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147447_comment'></div>英材大略，盈庭岂识乎是非？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147447_comment'></div>设使有辅相之才，秀帅之器，君子履行，哲人询谋，未喻执事以何理而得之，以何术而知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147447_comment'></div>若知而荐之，则明公有大忠于国家也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147447_comment'></div>荐而用之，则明公有大赖于贤俊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147447_comment'></div>且复卑能或似于狂愚，诈佞或侔于纯信，又未喻执事以何术而察之，以何理而详之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147447_comment'></div>矧投之盈几之文，加以在公之务，虽卑能周物，庖丁之刃有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147447_comment'></div>若千虑一失，君子之明亦损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147447_comment'></div>莫若采择群舆之议，精详与夺之机，询当朝文学之人，观就试文章之士，则自然不役聪明而尽得其善，不劳智力而皆得其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147447_comment'></div>能于诗者观其所试之诗，能于赋者阅其所试之赋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147447_comment'></div>善于论则以论取，精于策则以策求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147447_comment'></div>随其所长，观其所试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147447_comment'></div>勿舆其所有而责其所无，勿遗其所长而陋其所短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147447_comment'></div>无求工于力分之外，无求备于赴应之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147447_comment'></div>所谓鉴周而妍陋靡遗，理当而贤愚自辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147447_comment'></div>若有宏才大略之士，倜傥不羁之才，封章为达于冕旒，文解迥高其等第，冀贤王得而荐之，明主得而用之，岂非明公发解之善异于古人乎，进人之名光于今日乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147447_comment'></div>是谓导滥觞于骇渎之源，封沃土于干霄之木也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147447_comment'></div>唯锡傥于众人之末，或有一艺之长，亦俟明公济勺水于涸鳞，假顺风于弱羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147447_comment'></div>岂唯鄙夫获遭逢之幸，固亦大贤有特达之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147447_comment'></div>狂瞽之言，采听是望，不任惶龟祷愿之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147447_comment'></div>锡再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_81_1147447_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='40c2f19106824de9a2ee3f0e9aa52238_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("40c2f19106824de9a2ee3f0e9aa52238");'><span id='40c2f19106824de9a2ee3f0e9aa52238_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年</a>，39岁</div><div id='40c2f19106824de9a2ee3f0e9aa52238' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年3月</a>　三月，在东京，与胡旦、何士宗举行文会。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年4月23日</a>　四月二十三日，在东京，上书卢多逊，干谒求引。作品：上中书相公书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1147442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上中书相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年4月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147442")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147442'>四月二十三日，乡贡进士田锡谨以长书一通，献于相公黄閤之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147442_comment'></div>惶恐震骇，不知所裁，幸相公容而察之，使获尽其愚衷，则可以免僭踰之诛，而蒙容恕之惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147442_comment'></div>夫以贱干贵，遭逢实难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147442_comment'></div>以言感人，听信亦寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147442_comment'></div>盖贵贱之际，若天壤之相悬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147442_comment'></div>言感之间，非聪明而弗悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147442_comment'></div>今相公以英贵之重，居廊庙之尊，功业辉光，仁义流布，事无微而不烛，理无深而不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147442_comment'></div>故在位庶寮，与仕进之辈，孰不受陶铸之大惠，靡不希颜嘱之馀辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147442_comment'></div>锡是以载徵敷叙之辞，上觊钧台之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147442_comment'></div>昔文王称睿圣，犹询及刍荛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147442_comment'></div>周公曰圣人，亦下礼贫贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147442_comment'></div>邴吉问服辕之喘，齐相念涉淄之寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147442_comment'></div>路左长谣，而晏子动容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147442_comment'></div>门下献书，而姚崇弗罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147442_comment'></div>斯皆相公熟闻之事，儒生常叙之谭，固不假形于书简而后知，亦不劳伸于比喻而方见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147442_comment'></div>然相公以房、杜之策略，佐尧、舜之事机，入造膝于一人，出劳神于百揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147442_comment'></div>所务者国家大事，所思者社稷宏谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147442_comment'></div>动唯万务之繁，静悦寸阴之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147442_comment'></div>而白屋之士，片艺自沽，求谒见于黄扉，进干祈于重顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147442_comment'></div>求名者不过为希科第，在位者不越为冀迁升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147442_comment'></div>若是者累累然接踵于门栏，藉藉焉取容于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147442_comment'></div>无宏才大略，以裨于采听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147442_comment'></div>无英气异行，以动于礼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147442_comment'></div>所以相君之门非深严也，由所谒之人非英特也，宜其情弗上通，而言弗下应焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147442_comment'></div>相君之听非忽略也，由所吐之言无利害也，宜其进未速见，而退未能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147442_comment'></div>是以古人知崇重之难接，非奇伟之莫伸，故有危冠长剑以饰容，长揖抗礼以自异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147442_comment'></div>锡常研几于此，而取类于彼，悦怿自得，始终可图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147442_comment'></div>以为凡欲一谒公卿之门，一达生平之志，胡不观往古所行之事，酌于今未兆之机，焉敢曲徵异辞，聊欲直叙往事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147442_comment'></div>昔齐宣志在驰骋，而淳于之荐客非贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147442_comment'></div>阖庐志在仇雠，而伍员之所言未当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147442_comment'></div>非言未当也，其言非阖庐之志也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147442_comment'></div>非客不肖也，其人非齐宣之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147442_comment'></div>故徼福者先意而为事，事无不合；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147442_comment'></div>希宠者见几以设谋，谋无不谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147442_comment'></div>观大《易》之言，则曰「几者事之微」也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147442_comment'></div>详《春秋》之旨，则曰「需者事之贼」焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147442_comment'></div>进与退必以时，而谋与断交相养也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147442_comment'></div>今相公知小人在此一书也，罪小人亦此一书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147442_comment'></div>虽知言出而罪入，固宜偷合茍容，与众人碌碌焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147442_comment'></div>茍万一志意相投，宠遇下及，则安可违利趣害，而贻识者之讥也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147442_comment'></div>幸相公英明而察焉，望相公仁恕而容焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147442_comment'></div>锡以羁旅之人，怀丛脞之艺，去国三千里，宦游二十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147442_comment'></div>贫贱琐屑，迂懦闇钝，不言而晓，言之且惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147442_comment'></div>年龄在躬，三十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147442_comment'></div>昔在于蜀，同与科场者，今皆列丹陛，升清贯，出奉帝皇之命，入居台省之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147442_comment'></div>而小人犹食人之食，衣人之衣，困为旅人，辱在徒步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147442_comment'></div>当明天子在上，贤宰相当国，仁犹及于草木，信尚孚于豚鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147442_comment'></div>安可负六尺之躯，怀丈夫之志，而终日屑屑，不能自奋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147442_comment'></div>非知己之罪，实自贻之戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147442_comment'></div>寒贱幽忧之苦，不足为相公言之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147442_comment'></div>希求遭逢之幸，不敢于相公伸之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147442_comment'></div>言之则亵黩聪明，申之则干犯英贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147442_comment'></div>然又何以回特达英果之遇，济进趋变化之机？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147442_comment'></div>孟子云：「位卑而言高者，罪也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147442_comment'></div>今无寸禄之位，而吐僭高之言，郦生五鼎之烹，田光伏剑之节，岂独古人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147442_comment'></div>今幸而为相公言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147442_comment'></div>锡生平所著文约百轴，择其自善者得二十编，虽缮写献投，为举人事业，固不乞用为卖名之货，亦不足为希赏之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147442_comment'></div>其实邀相公之知，回相公之鉴者，在此一书尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147442_comment'></div>昔相公奉使于吴，而知吴可取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147442_comment'></div>相公在西掖为侍从之臣，旦夕论思，而谓蜀可灭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147442_comment'></div>相公在翰林，吁谟宥密，益亲帝衮，而致吴越王来归阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147442_comment'></div>以是知擒吴灭蜀，平百越而来四夷，岂非相公赞成帝谟，而密用良画哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147442_comment'></div>所以先帝取天下，平海内，二十年间，强不敢掩弱，大不敢加小，信泰来之运钟于圣朝，升平之时归于今上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147442_comment'></div>今主明而相贤，本丰而基固，天下安危之柄，总之于主上，而持之于相公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147442_comment'></div>夫盛事难兼，而良时不再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147442_comment'></div>且老农有三载之储，犹悦然而自裕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147442_comment'></div>良贾获千金之利，尚怡然而自多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147442_comment'></div>矧相公遇太平天子而佐之，获太平之民而理之，岂不以功名辉赫而自裕乎，岂不以志意纵横而自多乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147442_comment'></div>且自古乱世多而理世少，君子寡而小人众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147442_comment'></div>以姚崇之贤而值玄宗晚年，稍溺情于逸乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147442_comment'></div>以裴度之量而遇宪、穆之际，未致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147442_comment'></div>今天子春秋鼎盛，好文而稽古；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147442_comment'></div>天下底定，内宁而外安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147442_comment'></div>此相公可意之秋也，生民受赐之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147442_comment'></div>夫制理于未乱，禁邪于未形，则君子明智先见之常道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147442_comment'></div>兵书曰「善战者无赫赫之名」，盖制胜于未形未兆之前也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147442_comment'></div>古人云：「天下有道，则守在四夷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147442_comment'></div>方今边鄙无虞，戎夷畏服，契丹遣其爱子，入朝贡奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147442_comment'></div>是相公慎择边吏，俾务大体，无使邀功而搆怨之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147442_comment'></div>邀功则事生，事生则怨生，是邀功之人，不能布天子之大信于外夷也，相公能不介意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147442_comment'></div>小人狂愚，一至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147442_comment'></div>《春秋》不云乎：「嫠不恤其纬，而周宗是忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147442_comment'></div>然狂夫之言，圣人择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147442_comment'></div>昔魏武恶杨脩之智而杀之，千载之后，人皆非之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147442_comment'></div>韩信纳左车之说，百战之胜，人皆美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147442_comment'></div>汤曰天下愚夫，「一能胜余」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147442_comment'></div>舜闻一善，沛然而悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147442_comment'></div>茍言利国家，则言之者无罪，而闻之者足以自戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147442_comment'></div>相公怜而察之，则以为小人方谋仕进，茍非设奇，则无以警骇听闻也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147442_comment'></div>若相公鄙而浅之，则适足邀抚掌大噱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147442_comment'></div>相公若以片文知于小人，则锡有二十编之文，愿受知于门下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147442_comment'></div>若以一言知于下走，则锡有鄙闻陋见，愿见采于舆人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147442_comment'></div>若以怜亡国之馀，恤宦游之困，而锡钧镕于匹夫，则羁旅之人自兹而振矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147442_comment'></div>昔唐时名辈在科场间，亦以设奇取誉，如尹枢自放状元、王璘衣缬之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147442_comment'></div>又若刘禹锡、柳宗元之为人，皆以大儒之业，当壮年获志于科第，自谓跬步万里，坐邀大位，而言无畏忌，志务倜傥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147442_comment'></div>迨升郎署，席未遑暖，而众毁已炽，或出刺遐徼，而流离不复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147442_comment'></div>或终老散地，而诗酒自宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147442_comment'></div>壮图弗伸，晚年方悟，非当时弗用也，由锐气误物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147442_comment'></div>仕进之仵，茍能鉴往失而慎将来，则安可不为良相之用乎，安可不受良相之知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147442_comment'></div>揣小人艺能，固与往贤悬邈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147442_comment'></div>然遽以刍荛之见，骤希庙堂之知，死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147442_comment'></div>相公若以为适时之机，自伸之术，慕王泠然求知宰相，尹枢自放状元，斯亦觊相公稍霁威怒而深察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147442_comment'></div>锡惶恐顿首再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1147442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年5月</a>　五月，在东京，上书杜舍人，求汲引。作品：贻杜舍人书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷三。杜舍人，名不详，疑为杜镐。）</span><div id='poem_1147441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贻杜舍人书</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147441")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147441'>五月日，进士田锡谨拜手奉书舍人座右：锡尝以言而当，智也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147441_comment'></div>默而当，智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147441_comment'></div>进而受知于识者，才也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147441_comment'></div>退而无咎于躬，知进退也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147441_comment'></div>《易》谓「动静不失其宜，其道有光」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147441_comment'></div>粤若志在济民，名未为人知，必反经合道，用奇矫时，名乃一日千里，诸葛坚卧，太公钓国，郦生长揖，王猛扪虱之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147441_comment'></div>夫才略为根干，知己为羽翼，不俟终日，可与论几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147441_comment'></div>锡天付直性，非茍图名利者也，窃尝以儒术为己任，以古道为事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147441_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147441_comment'></div>图名不以道，虽使名动朝右，不取也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147441_comment'></div>得位不以道，虽贵为王公，不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147441_comment'></div>锡谓进贤为道也，诛谗邪为道也，济天下使一物不失所为道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147441_comment'></div>昔伊尹五就桀，欲理之速也，不得已归于汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147441_comment'></div>伊尹固不以名，不以位，但济天下之志汲汲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147441_comment'></div>夫有君子之行，不有君子之文者，汉申屠嘉、周勃也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147441_comment'></div>有君子之文，不有君子之行者，唐元稹、陆贽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147441_comment'></div>其中人也，发若彍弩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147441_comment'></div>其稔毒也，隐如敌国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147441_comment'></div>所谓以名以位，务乎仇覆人，与伊尹相反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147441_comment'></div>与其有文也，宁有行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147441_comment'></div>孔子曰：「惟名与器，不可以假人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147441_comment'></div>士有大功于国，天子则彰其名，赐其器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147441_comment'></div>赐之既不滥，受之亦不喜，盖公共也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147441_comment'></div>小人则饰诈勉道，便僻希旨，盗我名器，以为身荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147441_comment'></div>明公谓之何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147441_comment'></div>锡幸不佞，从士君子之后，安敢去彼取此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147441_comment'></div>明公有君子之行，称于识者，自迩及远，如兰蕙当风，苾芬袭人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147441_comment'></div>如冬阳夏阴，人来归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147441_comment'></div>锡于是冒炎暑，涉远道，一拜高义，求他日之羽翼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147441_comment'></div>《周易·泰》：拔茅汇，征吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147441_comment'></div>茅之连茹，以其汇类，征往乃亨吉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147441_comment'></div>天地交，万稹通，君子道长之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147441_comment'></div>天在地下，以贵下贱之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147441_comment'></div>小人狂瞽，奋笔伸志，若默于明公，失则多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147441_comment'></div>是用喋喋谔谔，黩于聪明，取《春秋》「言以足志，志以足言，不言谁知其志」之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147441_comment'></div>幸赐留意，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147441_comment'></div>锡再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1147441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年8月</a>　八月，在东京参加礼部试，作赋。作品：南省试圣人并用三代礼乐赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《咸平集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1147164' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147164' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147164?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南省试圣人并用三代礼乐赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以「皇猷昭宣，礼乐备举」为韵。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（978年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147164")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147164'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147164'>吾皇帝膺运承乾，唯师古以为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147164_comment'></div>化邦家而辑睦，因礼乐以昭宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147164_comment'></div>虽三代令王，稽沿革而殊矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147164_comment'></div>而千龄圣运，能损益而焕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147164_comment'></div>岂不以乐也者本乎天，礼也者本乎地，将化民以成俗，信有教而无类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147164_comment'></div>礼能加肃，先俎豆之有仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147164_comment'></div>乐以导和，宜笙镛之大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147164_comment'></div>昔夏后之御历也，宪章于舜，祖述于尧，推历稽人统之正，用寅为岁首之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147164_comment'></div>牲用乎骊，能降神于肸蚃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147164_comment'></div>声均《大夏》，又何取于《箫韶》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147164_comment'></div>所以致皇猷穆穆，而王道昭昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147164_comment'></div>又若有商之统天也，以应天顺人，惟干戈兮是举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147164_comment'></div>以逆取顺守，致彝伦兮攸叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147164_comment'></div>恭为礼本，嘉尚白于衣冠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147164_comment'></div>《濩》为乐称，表均和于律吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147164_comment'></div>其以宗周之致理也，以道合乎地者称帝，仁合乎天者为皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147164_comment'></div>能兼帝皇之盛德，是为圣哲之令王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147164_comment'></div>骍犊贵诚，加以用宗彝之郁鬯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147164_comment'></div>黄钟本律，其始导天统于阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147164_comment'></div>是知三王之救衰弊而拯黎元也，不相袭乎至音，靡相沿乎大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147164_comment'></div>亦犹五材迭用，运元化以成功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147164_comment'></div>四序交新，致岁功而有体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147164_comment'></div>今皇上嗣位而致升平也，前古之遗文必复，百王之阙政皆修，是以文章明备，声教同流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147164_comment'></div>明堂辟雍，表尊崇于儒术；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147164_comment'></div>宫悬乐府，方远播于鸿猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147164_comment'></div>矧今卜代继于周姬，登歌美乎象箾，方期驾玉辂于鲁道，封金泥于泰岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147164_comment'></div>遐方咸走于梯航，太史远颁于正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147164_comment'></div>小臣稽首而称之曰：穆穆皇皇，有以见我宋之礼乐也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1147164_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年9月1日</a>　九月一日，在东京参加进士科殿试，作赋。作品：御试不阵而成功赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《咸平集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1147165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147165?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御试不阵而成功赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以「功德双美，威震寰海」为韵。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（978年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147165")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147165'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147165'>圣人以德御天下，威加域中，谅至仁以无敌，故不阵以成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147165_comment'></div>徵《道德》之格言，谓乎善战；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147165_comment'></div>取《春秋》之经武，自服皇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147165_comment'></div>是知恩始孚于万灵，武实加乎七德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147165_comment'></div>安民和众以为本，禁暴戢兵而是式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147165_comment'></div>所以堂堂之阵弗施，而唯取柔怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147165_comment'></div>整整之旗何用，而陋乎刚克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147165_comment'></div>昔者成汤革夏，泽及万邦，勍敌靡由乎力制，匪人自悦而心降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147165_comment'></div>岂比夫祖龙霸秦，恃山河之百二；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147165_comment'></div>淮阴事汉，称智勇以无双。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147165_comment'></div>又若武王克商，灵旗前指，岂鹅鹳之是列，匪鱼丽之称美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147165_comment'></div>自然威宣，有亳民率服以来归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147165_comment'></div>师济盟津，众悦随而戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147165_comment'></div>是知王者之取天下也，泽普群动，恩流九围，道德为城池之固，忠信为甲胄之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147165_comment'></div>所以箪食壶浆，迓王师而自速；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147165_comment'></div>靡旗乱辙，望圣德以如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147165_comment'></div>宜乎师克在和，动先观衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147165_comment'></div>仁义之施也，若风雨之速；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147165_comment'></div>威武之加也，若雷霆之震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147165_comment'></div>《传》称因垒，美崇伯之归周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147165_comment'></div>《书》曰舞干，纪有苗之服舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147165_comment'></div>今圣朝以民济寿域，道洽人寰，将铸剑于农器，方虚候于玉关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147165_comment'></div>弭祸乱于未形，恩能服众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147165_comment'></div>布英威于有截，礼以防闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147165_comment'></div>下臣赓歌之曰：化洽无私兮，功符不宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147165_comment'></div>取仁义为胜兮，岂干戈砺乃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147165_comment'></div>德上冠于唐虞，政下任乎元凯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147165_comment'></div>孙、吴之阵法奚取，韩、白之兵机弗采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147165_comment'></div>宜乎车同轨而书同文，至化方流于寰海。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1147165_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年9月1日</a>　九月一日，在东京参加进士科殿试，作诗。作品：二仪合德诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_81812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御试二仪合德诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（七言六韵，用心字为韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（978年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81812")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_81812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81812'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81812'>圣主承祧兑泽深，乾坤玄化合尧心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81812'>黄舆比厚旋生植，白日齐明远照临。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81812'>周普至仁符积载，霶流睿渥若春霖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81812'>游鳞在藻方谐性，犷俗乘桴自献琛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81812'>和悦感人生瑞霭，穆清流咏在薰琴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81812'>小臣幸与观光试，敢效祈招颂德音。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81812'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_81812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年9月1日</a>　九月一日，在东京参加进士科殿试，作论。作品：御试登讲武台观兵习战论。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_1147473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御试登讲武台观兵习战论<span class='inlineComment2'>（限五百字已上成）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（978年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147473")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147473'>《春秋》曰：「天生五材，民并用之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147473_comment'></div>又曰：「谁能去兵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147473_comment'></div>是知尧舜禹汤而下，迨于宗周之至圣，鲜不以仁义道德牢笼天下，而以甲兵武备以制海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147473_comment'></div>故仲尼曰：「不教民战，是谓弃之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147473_comment'></div>故周有井田之法，春蒐夏苗，秋猕冬狩，乘三农之隙，以教民战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147473_comment'></div>夫武有七德，禁暴戢兵，安民和众之为用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147473_comment'></div>故古先帝王临御天下，持威制之柄于上，以制四夷而齐万国，得不以兵为本焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147473_comment'></div>昔晁错上汉文之书曰：「兵不坚利，与空手同」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147473_comment'></div>是知兵不得不坚，而战不得不习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147473_comment'></div>唐开元之际，海内无事，明皇幸于骊山，讲兵而阅焉，于时称为威盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147473_comment'></div>今国家自先帝临御以来，弭祸乱而安黎元，胜兵数百万，所谓霸王之器在手，故远戎服畏，诸侯恭肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147473_comment'></div>岂非甲兵之用善，弛张卷舒由圣人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147473_comment'></div>今陛下乘乾坤交泰之时，而当寰海宴清之际，虽以诗书礼乐以化天下，而致民于富寿之域；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147473_comment'></div>然能遵尧、舜、禹、汤之用心，而弗忘战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147473_comment'></div>以是知卜年之祚方远，而卜世之基弥固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147473_comment'></div>登崇高之台以讲武焉，讲武之大体，实观兵之威武焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147473_comment'></div>既威且武，而有习战之术，以是众战，则何敌弗克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147473_comment'></div>夫是三令五申，虽古之习战之法，而《易》贵师贞之吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147473_comment'></div>今睿谋神武，以兵战之机以时习焉，天下畏天威而服圣德，岂非前书者云「善师者不阵」者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147473_comment'></div>四夷之心，咸走梯航，玉帛而来朝者，由陛下德先胜，而兵有威也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147473_comment'></div>今论兵甲之利，府库之备，士卒之勇，土田之广，疆埸之安，虽汉武承文、景之羡财而利甲兵者，弗能加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147473_comment'></div>区域之安，蒸黎之泰，风雨时顺，天地气和，虽太宗革隋之馀而善整武备者，亦弗能至焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1147473_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年9月1日</a>　九月一日，在东京参加进士科殿试，以第二名及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年9月2日</a>　九月二日，在东京，与新登科人赐宴于迎春苑，受赐绿袍、靴、笏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年11月20日</a>　十一月二十日，在东京，释褐将作监丞，通判宣州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年</a>　本年，登进士第前，在东京，作书与人，求汲引。作品：贻青城小著书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷四。青城小著，名不详。）</span><div id='poem_1147446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贻青城小著书</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147446")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147446'>月日，进士田锡谨奉书致明公足下：锡尝读大《易》书，得君子「定其交而后求」之义，乃知君子之交以道义，小人之交以势利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147446_comment'></div>势利为交，有时而改矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147446_comment'></div>道义之交，不可得而变矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147446_comment'></div>有时而改者，张释之宾客、廉颇故吏是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147446_comment'></div>不可得而变者，仲尼、颜氏子，子皮、公孙侨是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147446_comment'></div>锡每读圣人之书，慕君子之行，正直自守，耿介独立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147446_comment'></div>非有好古博雅之道，纯信英特之气，锡则视之蔑如，非吾侪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147446_comment'></div>窃尝闻足下有明允之行，怀高奇之文，蓄不羁之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147446_comment'></div>有是三者，修于躬而播于人，锡所以希慕德风，欲定交于足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147446_comment'></div>然锡名迹未著，不为人知，一旦遽捧尺书，欲定交于足下，足下必按剑瞋目，不知其所由来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147446_comment'></div>请以锡之行止，为足下委曲而言之，冀足下详信而稍意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147446_comment'></div>锡，蜀人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147446_comment'></div>当小国时，尝以艺文干于时，时不我知，委颓废弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147446_comment'></div>锡自谓鹏跃北溟，固为枪榆者所非，谁复能效儿女子戚戚愤闷，思茍于身计耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147446_comment'></div>洎吾皇平定中区，蜀为内地，锡滞若匏系，介在一隅，约《国风》以伸辞，玩大《易》以知命，栖息环堵，服膺大道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147446_comment'></div>虽然，长者之辙交于陈平之门，天将屈我一时，而伸我以道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147446_comment'></div>厚我以文，而遇我以知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147446_comment'></div>不然，安得弘农杨公徽之、安定梁公周翰、广平宋公白，皆博我以雅道，勉我以大来矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147446_comment'></div>今窃聆高义，欲伸于足下，未喻足下能洞豁襟怀，俾锡以生平之志，一达于聪明乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147446_comment'></div>且士大夫所贵者，树德如亲仁，博学以师古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147446_comment'></div>师得古道，以为己任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147446_comment'></div>亲乎仁人，以结至交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147446_comment'></div>至交立，则君子之道胜，胜则可以倡道和德，同心为谋，上翼圣君，下振逸民，使天下穆穆然，复归于古道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147446_comment'></div>其若德树而未有邻，学博而不求知，则君子之道孤弱，孤弱则未能斥小人而行古道，安得圣君而翼之，安得逸民而振之，安得天下而理之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147446_comment'></div>足下登进士第，升拔萃科，出为青城佐，将来为达官，享大位，岂不从今日树君子之党，济他日之志乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147446_comment'></div>若使小人得志，摈吾侪于下位，虽有国士慷慨之志不得伸，虽有忠臣謇谔之心不得用，道孤党削，则足下为何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147446_comment'></div>锡已定交于向者三君子矣，今又伸志于足下，庶使我忠壮朋党久大，器业得全矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147446_comment'></div>昔魏徵得房玄龄、杜如晦为党，所以成贞观之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147446_comment'></div>姚元崇得宋璟为党，所以致开元之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147446_comment'></div>裴度无党，初为中人魏简、词臣元稹排之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147446_comment'></div>韦贯之无党、为张宿诬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147446_comment'></div>锡每读唐史至此，未尝不慨然兴愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147446_comment'></div>今布露真恳，足下以为狂瞽乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147446_comment'></div>以为倜傥乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147446_comment'></div>惟明公察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147446_comment'></div>锡拜上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1147446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年</a>　本年，登进士第前，在东京，上书宋太宗，请复乡饮酒礼。作品：请复乡饮礼书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1147284' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请复乡饮礼书</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147284")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147284'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147284'>月日，乡贡进士臣田锡惶恐顿首，献书皇帝陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147284_comment'></div>臣闻圣人建大业，得大位，制礼以经邦国，作乐以和神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147284_comment'></div>五礼行于朝廷，远方之民有终身不得观之者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147284_comment'></div>六乐奏于宗庙，远方之俗有终身不得闻之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147284_comment'></div>于是制乡饮之礼，行乡校之间，俾人遍知，冀人易识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147284_comment'></div>盖其礼甚辨，其仪甚详，有祭献之仪，有俎爵之数，命乡人之贤者为主，延乡人之老者为宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147284_comment'></div>揖让拜起皆有仪，升降进退必有位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147284_comment'></div>以金石之乐和其节，以《雅》《颂》之诗道其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147284_comment'></div>自秦承周衰，汉迩秦乱，不能行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147284_comment'></div>至后汉世祖行之，世祖之后复废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147284_comment'></div>至西晋复之，西晋之后又废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147284_comment'></div>至皇唐用之，明著礼文，散颁郡国，咸俾长吏，以化黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147284_comment'></div>至开元中，宣州刺史裴耀卿以为乡饮之仪，唯于贡士之日略得举用，其馀寝停，岂圣王化俗之心，岂良吏知礼之大？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147284_comment'></div>于是拜章奏以上言，自恭勤而行礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147284_comment'></div>月而习之，岁而行之，于是宣州耆老，宣庭寮吏，每闻歌《白华》之什，《华黍》之诗，《南陔》之篇，《由庚》之颂，言孝子养亲之道，述万物遂性之旨，观者皆踊跃，听者有感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147284_comment'></div>盖礼乐之感于外，而精诚之发于中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147284_comment'></div>在唐之世，为唐之牧守，唐之世祚垂三百载，唐之牧守凡几千人，唯耀卿能于一郡之间，独奉先王之礼，犹化其俗，尚移其风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147284_comment'></div>以是知先王之礼不徒行，先王之乐不徒用，但后人行之不得其道，用之不知其微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147284_comment'></div>国家大礼与天地同节，大乐以天地同和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147284_comment'></div>与天地，祭宗庙，祠山川，正齿胄，迨封册冠婚之礼，军旅宾客之容，陛下皆举百王之礼而行之，以六代之乐而明之，所谓礼乐征伐自天子出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147284_comment'></div>矧国家括地三百州，拓土一万里，年谷屡稔，民风大和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147284_comment'></div>朝廷之礼既崇，而远方之民有未亲见之者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147284_comment'></div>朝廷之乐既备，而远方之俗有未亲闻之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147284_comment'></div>愿陛下申明旧典，举行新命，颁乡饮之礼，修乡饮之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147284_comment'></div>使其观祭献之严，则知不忘报本矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147284_comment'></div>睹蘋藻之祀，则知所贵者诚矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147284_comment'></div>见贤者为主，则知懋德者可尊矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147284_comment'></div>视老者为宾，则知高年者可恭矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147284_comment'></div>阅揖让拜起之式，则知谦恭撙节之可学矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147284_comment'></div>见升降进退之容，则知折旋俯仰之可习矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147284_comment'></div>闻《白华》、《南陔》之诗，则知孝于父母矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147284_comment'></div>听雅音正声之奏，则悦于和乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147284_comment'></div>月而习之，岁而行之，稔于礼而自熟，渍于道而弥深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147284_comment'></div>讦愎化为柔和，狠戾迁为贞顺，革恶归善，流邪复正，其何难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147284_comment'></div>盖性相近也，习相远也，不觉自迁于无过之地，不觉自生于知耻之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147284_comment'></div>既无过，又知耻，国家虽设刑，而无淫慝可刑矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147284_comment'></div>朝廷虽设禁，而无过差可禁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147284_comment'></div>若是，则为父者以慈而为教也，为子者以孝而自守也，为兄者以友爱而自得也，为弟者以恭谨而自悦也，为夫者以和而有其室家也，为妇者以柔而事于舅姑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147284_comment'></div>一家率之，一乡慕之，一邑化之，一郡荣之，一国兴之，天下同之，得非王者厉精于礼乐而致之，诸侯折节于礼乐而奉之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147284_comment'></div>若以为古之礼也不可复行，则世祖承盗莽之后而能行之，晋氏承曹魏之乱而能复之，太宗革隋季之淫而能用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147284_comment'></div>若以为俗之薄也难骤化之，则裴耀卿何以化之，宣州之民何以顺之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147284_comment'></div>是知千古绝迹，三代旷礼，犹可缮完补缉，损益裁酌，沿其俗、适其时而明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147284_comment'></div>况贞观之风，开元之化，左顾不远，右眄可及，彝章不泯，令式斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147284_comment'></div>昔舜庭奏乐，而鸟兽率舞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147284_comment'></div>燕谷吹律，而草木遂萌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147284_comment'></div>文王行礼，而虞芮怀惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147284_comment'></div>范宣让功，而栾黡知变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147284_comment'></div>夫金石至和，非有乐于鸟兽，而鸟兽自舞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147284_comment'></div>草木无情，非必应于律吕，而律吕能通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147284_comment'></div>西伯之仁，不以化虞芮，而争讼自息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147284_comment'></div>晋卿之让，不以矫栾黡，而汰虐自亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147284_comment'></div>盖礼乐之进物也速，而谦让之服人也深。<div class='inline'
