id='poem_sentence_51_1147284_comment'></div>况欲以宾主之礼以明之，以祭献之仪以示之，以金石之乐以歌之，以升降之度以化之，以揖让之容以导之，以尊贤之序以命之，以养老之道以喻之，人之心，物之性，得不优而柔之，而自趣之，感而慕之，而自化之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147284_comment'></div>乡饮之礼，化民导俗，夫如是之速也，愿陛下询公卿而复之，望陛下敕牧守而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147284_comment'></div>行之期年，则民知耻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147284_comment'></div>行之再岁，则民知教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147284_comment'></div>行之三载，则民知礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147284_comment'></div>行之而不辍，用之而能久，则比屋可封之俗，不独帝尧之时也，圣代当复见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147284_comment'></div>闻乐而感之者，不独宣州有之也，天下当尽然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147284_comment'></div>天下幸甚，海内幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147284_comment'></div>惟陛下裁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147284_comment'></div>臣不胜慺慺思理之诚，谨昧死奉书以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147284_comment'></div>臣锡诚惶诚恐，顿首再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1147284_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年</a>　本年，登进士第前，在东京，上书宋太宗，请复藉田礼。作品：请修藉田书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_1147285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请修藉田书</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147285")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147285'>月日，乡贡进士臣田锡惶恐顿首，献书皇帝陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147285_comment'></div>臣闻农者国之大本也，谷者人之司命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147285_comment'></div>古先哲王虑农之不勤也，忧人之弃本也，于是设躬耕之仪，立藉田之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147285_comment'></div>行于国，化于天下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147285_comment'></div>勤于身，勉于海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147285_comment'></div>天子履田，谁敢不力于垄亩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147285_comment'></div>天子执耒，谁敢不务于播种？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147285_comment'></div>所以孟陬之月，择日惟良，一人斋戒以晨兴，百辟肃恭而景从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147285_comment'></div>载耒耜于车右，就阡陌于国东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147285_comment'></div>朱纮以饰礼容，青辂以协时令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147285_comment'></div>春景烛物，和风扇野，千亩之首，三推为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147285_comment'></div>内宰诏于后妃，乃献穜稑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147285_comment'></div>甸人率于黎庶，遂终耕垦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147285_comment'></div>所以供粢盛也，以之备醴酪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147285_comment'></div>天地山川之祭，用兹而给焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147285_comment'></div>宗庙社稷之祀，由此而备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147285_comment'></div>是知藉田之礼，乃有五利：劝民不忘本，一也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147285_comment'></div>农有馀蓄，二也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147285_comment'></div>俗知廉耻，三也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147285_comment'></div>政教可喻，四也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147285_comment'></div>盗寇不起，五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147285_comment'></div>用是五利，播于万民，以之兴役则民不雕弊，以之事战则国有馈运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147285_comment'></div>虽有水旱之灾，不害民也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147285_comment'></div>虽值凶荒之岁，不瘁国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147285_comment'></div>是故上之化下，如玺之在涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147285_comment'></div>下之从上，若水之在器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147285_comment'></div>所以乃稼乃穑，宜自我勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147285_comment'></div>乃耕乃殖，宜自我先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147285_comment'></div>虽有货财，不救饿殍之困；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147285_comment'></div>虽有宝玉，不济灾凶之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147285_comment'></div>故历代奉于周制，百王修于藉礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147285_comment'></div>汉、魏、晋、宋之主，齐、梁、隋、唐之朝，或立坛以祀先农，或置廪以为神仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147285_comment'></div>或过三推之数，或颁万斛之种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147285_comment'></div>或许行之于郡县，或亦因之而赏赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147285_comment'></div>今陛下嗣守洪业，勤恤黔黎，四方之书轨大同，九牧之贡输咸至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147285_comment'></div>坐明堂以布政，居宣室以询贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147285_comment'></div>谓小大之狱未明，则慎择法官，喻以无溢之旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147285_comment'></div>谓朝廷之政未理，则优容直臣，大启上言之路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147285_comment'></div>谓贤良未至，则虚伫以待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147285_comment'></div>前古未行之事，陛下行之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147285_comment'></div>今日所急之政，陛下修之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147285_comment'></div>是故五星融明，八谷无害，风雨时若，黎元乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147285_comment'></div>然于千亩之田，尚旷三推之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147285_comment'></div>虽在南之亩，惟西之畴，时歛有多稼之谣，岁取闻如坻之咏，必若载阳之候，或以启蛰之时，命大司农以饬田，诏太常伯以撰礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147285_comment'></div>惟月之吉，即晨以兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147285_comment'></div>八鸾锵锵，前适东郊之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147285_comment'></div>百寮翼翼，相从北阙之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147285_comment'></div>鸣苍佩于宸衮，建青旗于帝车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147285_comment'></div>阊阖来风，振我发生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147285_comment'></div>勾芒司候，佑我播种之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147285_comment'></div>簠簋豆笾，荐先农之坛墠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147285_comment'></div>耒耜黍稷，列公藉之阡陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147285_comment'></div>旭日新景，朝霞暖辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147285_comment'></div>千乘万骑，列于左右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147285_comment'></div>金根玉辂，俨于威仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147285_comment'></div>有司赞礼以降车，侍臣肃容以进耒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147285_comment'></div>绮畴奋一垡之土，褕衣献五稼之种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147285_comment'></div>然后三公继礼，九卿就列，庶寮迭耕，黎民终亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147285_comment'></div>于是顺阳和之德，以农为先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147285_comment'></div>示稼穑之艰，以己率下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147285_comment'></div>以金石丝竹，感和悦之怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147285_comment'></div>以赏庆锡赉，助礼容之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147285_comment'></div>加以发如纶之诏，降藉田之仪，俾诸侯行之以兴稼政，俾远民观之以知帝心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147285_comment'></div>即民之趣耕，若忧风雨之至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147285_comment'></div>民之务本，不遗天地之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147285_comment'></div>仓廪实而知礼节，衣食丰而识廉耻，则末作自归于农亩，游民必复于田业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147285_comment'></div>岂徒粢盛是供，牺牲是养，实将人心无趋末也，民力无枉用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147285_comment'></div>必父诲其子，兄勉乎弟，不使遗地利，失天时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147285_comment'></div>桑麻之勤，由农而繁矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147285_comment'></div>鸡豚之蓄，由农而孳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147285_comment'></div>民以之祠祭则有备，以之赋役则不困，以之馈饷则成礼，以之拯恤则为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147285_comment'></div>若是皆陛下跻之于富寿也，由陛下致之于安逸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147285_comment'></div>既安且逸，则和乐之气感乎天地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147285_comment'></div>既富而庶，则礼让之风行于邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147285_comment'></div>天地感，礼让行，所以麟凤集于郊薮，图书出于河洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147285_comment'></div>故臣以为千亩之耕，五利斯得，其实在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147285_comment'></div>愿陛下宪章《周官》之礼，沿革唐朝之制，躬亲黛耜，勉励黔首也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147285_comment'></div>昔武后，女主也，犹俾中和之节，咸献农书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147285_comment'></div>昭帝，幼主也，犹弄钩盾之田，垂芳史策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147285_comment'></div>矧陛下功业高于往古，文武冠于前王，虽汤仁禹圣，才可同涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147285_comment'></div>汉祖唐宗，未堪较德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147285_comment'></div>而犹阙于藉礼，何以示于黎元？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147285_comment'></div>惟陛下俯循采菲之言，幸复躬耕之礼，无俾前代之主，独擅务农之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147285_comment'></div>臣不胜罄伸诚请之愿，谨昧死奉书以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147285_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚恐，顿首再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_84_1147285_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e7370c9dd34941dba0c7cdff80ebd863_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e7370c9dd34941dba0c7cdff80ebd863");'><span id='e7370c9dd34941dba0c7cdff80ebd863_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年</a>，41岁</div><div id='e7370c9dd34941dba0c7cdff80ebd863' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年9月</a>　九月，被召还京，迁著作郎、京西北路转运判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年9月22日</a>　九月二十二日，在京为著作郎，拜表乞居谏署，献《乐府新解》十卷、《升平诗》三十篇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年9月23日</a>　九月二十三日，在京为著作郎，改授左拾遗、直史馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年9月</a>　九月，在京为左拾遗，有奏状谢传宣。作品：转谏官后谢传宣。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>转谏官后谢传宣状</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147415")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147415'>右，臣今日中使赵诚信至，传宣「昨日所进实封已收得，朕亦子细披览，但安心著撰文字，必不差出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147415_comment'></div>如要上殿，先奏来」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147415_comment'></div>伏以臣诚上达，必凭奏牍之词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147415_comment'></div>天眷下临，忽降出纶之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147415_comment'></div>俯伏闻命，兢惶失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147415_comment'></div>窃以臣改授官资，尘忝清近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147415_comment'></div>志有所蓄，理合备陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147415_comment'></div>仰黩宸严，方忧罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147415_comment'></div>岂谓皇明烛察，比太阳之照临；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147415_comment'></div>圣造优容，同昊穹之覆焘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147415_comment'></div>忧疑遽释，欢抃交并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147415_comment'></div>柏台既免于重难，竹简得专于撰述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147415_comment'></div>况圣朝无事，皂囊虚献替之词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147415_comment'></div>谏省馀闲，缃帙遂讨论之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147415_comment'></div>比在家修史，虽远愧于古人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147415_comment'></div>以恋阙著书，实仰依于明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147415_comment'></div>馀取上殿进止，必先有状奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1147415_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年9月</a>　九月，在京为左拾遗，有奏状谢直史馆。作品：谢兼史职。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢兼史职状</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147416")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147416'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147416'>右，臣叨列谏垣，又兼史职，圣恩曲被，私愿允谐，荣莫如之，幸实多矣，荣幸交集，感惕弥深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147416_comment'></div>告谢之时，虽依常例；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147416_comment'></div>中谢之礼，莫遂对扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147416_comment'></div>盖閤门以既该敕差，内殿即旧无谢例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147416_comment'></div>臣虽已赴职，岂敢宁心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147416_comment'></div>窃念臣近才改官，又乞兼职，实忧冒黩，自掇悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147416_comment'></div>岂谓人欲天从，遽降出纶之命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147416_comment'></div>才微识浅，惭非载笔之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147416_comment'></div>盖陛下恕以迂疏，恤其衰老，置在优贤之地，不离近侍之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147416_comment'></div>献替箴规，敢忘匪懈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147416_comment'></div>述修编撰，唯守靖共。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147416_comment'></div>时政记得见鸿猷，起居注式资润色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147416_comment'></div>纂成日历，赓续季编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147416_comment'></div>冀铅椠之微劳，展涓埃之薄效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147416_comment'></div>讽从五谏，仰遵将圣之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147416_comment'></div>运偶千龄，幸纪太平之事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1147416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年9月</a>　九月，在京为左拾遗，有诗寄宣城相知。作品：寄江南诸相知。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_53789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄江南诸相知</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53789")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53789'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53789'>诗成奏入冕旒前，小谏官资骤转迁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53789'>带职喜为仙馆吏，立班常近御炉烟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53789'>清华拜命知深忝，謇谔非才愧昔贤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53789'>多谢宣城旧知己，寄来新句满花笺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53789'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53789_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='574f3b952ba04b759db967975f4e5912_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("574f3b952ba04b759db967975f4e5912");'><span id='574f3b952ba04b759db967975f4e5912_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年</a>，42岁</div><div id='574f3b952ba04b759db967975f4e5912' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年2月16日</a>　二月十六日，在京为左拾遗，上《请皇帝东封书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年8月15日</a>　八月十五日，在京为左拾遗，上书宰相卢多逊，乞自今谏官上章勿令閤门署具状。作品：上宰相书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_1147448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宰相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（981年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147448")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147448'>八月十五日，将仕郎、守左拾遗、直史馆、监盐院、赐绯鱼袋田锡，谨斋沐奉书，拜献相公黄閤之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147448_comment'></div>锡伏有鄙见，理合上闻，愿垂听察之仁，不罪僭踰之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147448_comment'></div>矧宰相识量，不可不包容众人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147448_comment'></div>大臣聪明，不可不采择片善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147448_comment'></div>今相公佐太平之主，理无事之朝，四海谧宁，万务整肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147448_comment'></div>房、杜功名之炜晔，良、平智略之宏深，比于是时，不独称美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147448_comment'></div>然至明或有所未照，至聪或有所未闻，未喻相公欲闻谠直之言乎，未喻相公欲求尘露之益乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147448_comment'></div>傥容下僚，辄陈管见，不独众人之幸，谅亦相公之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147448_comment'></div>锡去岁至自宣城，入见旒扆，对扬之后，圣旨宣付中书，旋蒙殊恩，授以大著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147448_comment'></div>不数日，又差充京西北路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147448_comment'></div>锡固非俊迈之才，窃慕清华之职，遂拜表乞在馆殿，冀与编修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147448_comment'></div>果回圣主之恩，命作谏垣之吏，仍兼史职，尽契夙心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147448_comment'></div>此皆相公施代天理物之功，从小人所求之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147448_comment'></div>然拜表之际，尝诣閤门，閤门有司未便收接，须候相公台旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147448_comment'></div>又取閤使指挥，往复审详，然后呈进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147448_comment'></div>盖有司禀奉之职，理合宜然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147448_comment'></div>况臣子慎重之心，礼亦可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147448_comment'></div>迩后扈随圣驾，留驻漳川，洎捷奏之爰来，与追班而入贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147448_comment'></div>数日后，因进《圣主平戎歌》，虽寻达于圣聪，亦先禀于台旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147448_comment'></div>又今春二月十六日，复进《请皇帝东封书》，不敢实封，先闻閤使，备言已奉台旨，有司方敢进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147448_comment'></div>仍依常规，先供一状，称不敢妄陈利便，亦不敢希望恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147448_comment'></div>岂有备位谏垣，上书诣閤，而如此委曲，不便伸陈，无乃损相公之明，无乃失至公之体？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147448_comment'></div>设使言事不合理道，以言而误至尊，自有常刑可以加罪，不足一一烦相公台听，不劳一一禀相公指踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147448_comment'></div>锡才列周行，未谙时事，若是近朝体例，须至如斯，相继因仍，未暇釐革，则乞相公申明旷荡之理，采纳愚直之言，应今后谏官上章，不须閤门取状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147448_comment'></div>乃是三公之府，机扃洞开；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147448_comment'></div>百职之仪，纲纪斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147448_comment'></div>锡受相公钧镕之造，荷相公特达之恩，岂合容易干闻，狂简陈述？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147448_comment'></div>盖闻诸道路，称近日左拾遗胡旦上书，希求差遣，圣人问难詶诘，仍于中书取状，似烦圣听，有黩宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147448_comment'></div>今来诣閤上书，不易轻进，可否须覆相府，去留皆系钧衡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147448_comment'></div>锡既闻斯语，实介鄙怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147448_comment'></div>何以？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147448_comment'></div>示人无私曰至公，裁事酌中为大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147448_comment'></div>岂相公佐先帝取吴越，事今上平并汾，识度勋庸，昭昭如此，何烦寻常之见，取次干廊庙之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147448_comment'></div>然缄默不言，实辜陶铸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147448_comment'></div>若披伸不密，亦掇讥嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147448_comment'></div>《易》不云乎：「君不密则失臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147448_comment'></div>盖谓下言上泄，置言者于危疑之地也，故识者不获已而钳口焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147448_comment'></div>锡今进虽奉书，而退必焚稿，幸相公钧台之鉴，恕小人忠谅之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147448_comment'></div>惶恐徬徨，不知所措，伏乞相公熟虑而留念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147448_comment'></div>锡顿首乎拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1147448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年9月8日</a>　九月八日，在京为左拾遗，授河北南路转运副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年9月13日</a>　九月十三日，因入辞宋太宗，上封事言事，获诏奖。作品：上太宗论军国要机朝廷大体。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太宗论军国要机朝廷大体<span class='inlineComment2'>（太平兴国六年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147288")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147288'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147288'>臣伏念自忝谏垣，今已周岁，无一言可裨时政，无一善上答君恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147288_comment'></div>盖以陛下文明，无事可谏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147288_comment'></div>朝廷公正，无事可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147288_comment'></div>然尸禄旷官，忧惭益切；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147288_comment'></div>尽忠补过，夙夜宁忘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147288_comment'></div>今辄以军国要机，朝廷大体，布在一疏，上达四聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147288_comment'></div>宽鈇钺之诛，容微臣之刍荛之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147288_comment'></div>所谓冒万死而不顾，当可言而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147288_comment'></div>又伏念陛下登位以来，未尝罪一直言，未尝戮一敢谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147288_comment'></div>天慈宽裕，睿鉴昭彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147288_comment'></div>虽前王好谏之心，未如陛下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147288_comment'></div>而谏官敢言之节，不及古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147288_comment'></div>不唯负陛下超擢之恩，抑亦亏臣子公忠之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147288_comment'></div>何以安一膳之饱，何以安一裘之温，胡颜立侍从之班，无艺带清华之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147288_comment'></div>碌碌随众，遑遑惜身，不如马之代劳，不及犬之吠盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147288_comment'></div>臣所以奋发之志，思有所伸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147288_comment'></div>激切之词，不敢自隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147288_comment'></div>伏乞陛下察而恕之，容而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147288_comment'></div>臣所言军国要机者一，朝廷大体者四，今为陛下引谕而言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147288_comment'></div>臣闻古先圣人，牢笼天下，弛张睿略，舒卷人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147288_comment'></div>使万人之心如一心，四海之意如一意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147288_comment'></div>有若驭马，又如铸金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147288_comment'></div>善驭者使之驰则驰，使之止则止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147288_comment'></div>善铸者使之圆则圆，使之方则方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147288_comment'></div>茍失其机，又失其时，则万人不一心，四海不一意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147288_comment'></div>亦犹不善驭马，不善铸金，使之驰而不驰，使之止而不止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147288_comment'></div>使之圆而不圆，使之方而不方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147288_comment'></div>若是则危与乱虽未萌，而不得不忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147288_comment'></div>机与时虽未失，而不得不惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147288_comment'></div>故古人云：居安思危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147288_comment'></div>又曰：理不忘乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147288_comment'></div>臣每念有唐之末，天下分离，中原土疆，不过千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147288_comment'></div>自先帝恢张皇业，开辟天下，平吴取蜀，易如破竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147288_comment'></div>唯河东<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1147288", 1147288, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>遗孽</span>，终不能平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147288_comment'></div>洎陛下一举取之，功名光大，世宗、先帝所不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147288_comment'></div>然自河东破后，圣驾回旋，诸军之心，皆望赏赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147288_comment'></div>四海之内，亦俟霈恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147288_comment'></div>岂谓陛下未覃赏捷之恩，未行策勋之礼，经今二载，所谓踰时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147288_comment'></div>今北方之戎，不来朝贡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147288_comment'></div>幽州孤垒，未复封疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147288_comment'></div>臣以国家兵甲之强，朝廷物力之盛，灭戎人甚易，取幽州不难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147288_comment'></div>然自古制御蕃戎，但在示之以威德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147288_comment'></div>示之以威者，不穷兵黩武，不劳人费财；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147288_comment'></div>示之以德者，比之如犬羊，容之若天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147288_comment'></div>或来朝贡，亦不阻其归怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147288_comment'></div>或背欢盟，亦不怒其侵叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147288_comment'></div>臣伏虑陛下以幽州未取，戎贼未平，一旦又来扰边，万乘复思再驾，欲快圣意，欲展睿谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147288_comment'></div>虽举必成功，动无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1147288", 1147288, "Clauses/128/Comments/0")'>遗算</span>，然臣请陛下或展郊禋之礼，或行封禅之仪，因此赏河东之功，因此示策勋之信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147288_comment'></div>人心懈怠者复悦，军功劳苦者终酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147288_comment'></div>帝泽滂沱，物情通泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147288_comment'></div>所谓陛下驾驭其意，镕铸其心，使之驰则驰，使之止则止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147288_comment'></div>使之圆则圆，使之方则方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147288_comment'></div>茍不以威信铸其心，恩惠驭其意，臣恐使之驰则止，使之圆则方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147288_comment'></div>当是时，陛下必念臣今日之言，陛下必思臣今日之谏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147288_comment'></div>此谓军国之要机一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147288_comment'></div>又念交州未下，战士无功，《春秋》谓「老师费财」，兵书曰「顿兵挫锐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147288_comment'></div>臣闻圣人不务广于边鄙，唯务广于德业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147288_comment'></div>武有七德，陛下何不广之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147288_comment'></div>天生四夷，陛下何须收之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147288_comment'></div>必若圣德日新，皇风日远，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1147288", 1147288, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>远夷</span>自然入贡，外域自然来降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147288_comment'></div>茍不来降，又不入贡，彼国自有灾疠，彼人自罹凶荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147288_comment'></div>《尚书》曰：「惟德动天」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147288_comment'></div>又曰：「四夷来王」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147288_comment'></div>《周易》曰：「圣人先天，而天弗违」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147288_comment'></div>天且弗违，况四夷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147288_comment'></div>臣尝读《韩诗外传》，言成王之时，越裳来贡，九译而至，周公问其所以来，其人曰：「天无迅风疾雨，海不扬波三年矣，意者中国殆有圣人，盍往朝之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147288_comment'></div>昔太宗征辽，魏徵苦谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147288_comment'></div>及贞观太平之后，天下州郡三百有六十，羁縻之州有八百，屯田置戍，悉在外荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147288_comment'></div>岂是一一加兵，然后方来内附？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147288_comment'></div>今陛下取交州何速？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147288_comment'></div>况大国视交州，谓之瘴海，去者不习风土，兵在彼中留滞颇久，愿陛下且罢斯役，暂息南征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147288_comment'></div>交州未平，不足损陛下功业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147288_comment'></div>交州既得，不足光陛下威声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147288_comment'></div>臣但以老师费财为可虑，顿兵挫锐为可惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147288_comment'></div>盖征讨之役，费用非轻，皆生民苦力之物，悉诸国所供之赋，乞陛下惜轻费之用，望陛下念征戍之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147288_comment'></div>此谓朝廷之大体一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147288_comment'></div>臣尝读《六典》，左右拾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1147288", 1147288, "Clauses/218/Comments/1")'>遗、补</span>阙，掌供奉讽谏，凡发令举事有不便于时、不合于道者，小则上封，大则廷谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147288_comment'></div>臣又读《唐书》，见给事中得以封驳诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147288_comment'></div>封谓封还诏书而不行，駮谓駮正诏书之所失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147288_comment'></div>又起居郎、起居舍人，得在天阶之下，备书王者之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147288_comment'></div>今来谏官寂无声影，设使诏书有所失审，制敕有不可行，给事中不敢封还而不行，不敢駮正其所失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147288_comment'></div>给谏既不敢违上旨，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1147288", 1147288, "Clauses/236/Comments/0")'>遗补</span>又不敢贡直言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147288_comment'></div>其次起居郎、起居舍人不得立轩陛之间，不得纪言动之事，使圣朝好事或有所遗而不闻，致陛下德音或有不知而不录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147288_comment'></div>加之御史不敢弹奏，左右丞今尚阙员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147288_comment'></div>又中书舍人是陛下近臣，司陛下诰命，臣每于起居日，但见其随班而进，拜舞而回，未尝见陛下召之与言，未尝闻陛下访之以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147288_comment'></div>臣虑其各有所见，欲待问而方言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147288_comment'></div>各有所陈，欲因便而方奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147288_comment'></div>伏乞陛下或询访以事，或宣召与言，冀各尽其诚心，兼得观其器业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147288_comment'></div>又今三馆之中，虽有集贤院书籍，而无集贤院职官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147288_comment'></div>虽有秘书省职官，而无秘书省图籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147288_comment'></div>臣伏读去年九月十一日所降制敕条贯，百官仍于朝堂习仪，又委宪司申举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147288_comment'></div>此则陛下思复古道，大振朝纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147288_comment'></div>臣唯见所习者仪，未见所举者职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147288_comment'></div>如职业各举，则威仪自严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147288_comment'></div>君有君之威仪，臣有臣之礼法，何患百官不整肃，何患庶政不允釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147288_comment'></div>臣乞今后给事中得以封驳诏书，起居郎、起居舍人得以纪录言动，御史得以弹奏，谏官得以抗言，左右丞得以纠辖台司，中书舍人得以祗应顾问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147288_comment'></div>中书舍人得备问，则皇猷日新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147288_comment'></div>左右丞得辖台司，则风宪益整；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147288_comment'></div>谏官抗言，则陛下闻所未闻，知所未知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147288_comment'></div>御史弹奏，则百僚震悚，一人尊严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147288_comment'></div>起居郎、起居舍人得在左右，则盛事无遗，国史大备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147288_comment'></div>给事中得以封駮，则诏敕无误出，政事无错行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147288_comment'></div>此朝廷之大体二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147288_comment'></div>今天下一家，海内万里，四方所凑，辇下骈阗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147288_comment'></div>万货所归，京师富盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147288_comment'></div>军营马监，无不高严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1147288_comment'></div>佛寺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_106_1147288", 1147288, "Clauses/307/Comments/0")'>道宫</span>，悉皆壮丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1147288_comment'></div>陛下又新西苑，复广御池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1147288_comment'></div>池若汉之昆明，苑若周之灵囿，足以为陛下宴游之所，足以为圣朝宏大之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1147288_comment'></div>唯尚书省是前代所营，公宇低隘，南宫二十四司不在其间，六尚书无本厅，诸郎官无廨宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1147288_comment'></div>至于九寺三监，寄在内前廊下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1147288_comment'></div>加以礼部无贡院，试处非省垣，每年试举人权就武成王庙，非太平职司之制度，非清朝文物之规仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1147288_comment'></div>乞陛下俟西苑毕功，御池罢役，重新省寺，用列职官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1147288_comment'></div>此则朝廷之大体三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1147288_comment'></div>臣又每于行路之次，见有羁锢之囚，荷以铁枷，不觉自骇，不知其人所犯何罪，又不知其囚复是何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1147288_comment'></div>臣谨按《刑统》，准狱官令枷杻各有短长，钳锁各有轻重，制度尺寸，并载刑书，未见以铁为枷者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1147288_comment'></div>凡今州县欲笞一小罪，絷一轻囚，必详格文，尽依典法，奉国家所颁之律，遵法寺所定之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1147288_comment'></div>以铁为枷，事出法外，伏乞陛下釐革此法，免伤皇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1147288_comment'></div>昔太宗因看《明堂图》，见人五脏皆系于背，圣慈恻隐，免人笞刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1147288_comment'></div>况太平之时，将刑措而不用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1147288_comment'></div>至仁之主，宜钦恤以居先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1147288_comment'></div>此则朝廷之大体四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1147288_comment'></div>臣所言者要机，乞陛下审而察之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1147288_comment'></div>所举者大体，乞陛下采而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1147288_comment'></div>臣不任感恩思报、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_124_1147288_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2c1a4743978045129c978f6fdb564e2a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c1a4743978045129c978f6fdb564e2a");'><span id='2c1a4743978045129c978f6fdb564e2a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=989')">987-989年</a>，48-50岁</div><div id='2c1a4743978045129c978f6fdb564e2a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　夏，由睦州还京任起居舍人，兼判登闻鼓院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　夏，在京为起居舍人，上表进文集十卷。作品：进文集表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进文集表</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147311")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147311'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147311'>臣锡言：臣闻美盛德之形容谓之颂，抒深情于讽刺莫若诗，赋则敷布于皇风，歌亦揄扬于王化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147311_comment'></div>下情上达，《周礼》所以建采诗之官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147311_comment'></div>君唱臣酬，《舜典》于是载赓歌之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147311_comment'></div>既逢清世，何让古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147311_comment'></div>木铎求规讽之词，弥光圣德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147311_comment'></div>金门献刍荛之说，式表忠怀<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147311_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下以唐、虞莫大之德，修汤、武无敌之仁，富寿于生民，慈俭曰至宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147311_comment'></div>涂山高会，执玉帛者华戎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147311_comment'></div>瑞牒载书，萃郊薮者麟凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147311_comment'></div>让圆灵以玄德，推臣下以赤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147311_comment'></div>皇勋帝功，可以封泰山而禅梁甫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147311_comment'></div>至德大业，可以作《韶》乐而建辟雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147311_comment'></div>永隆千载之基，高冠百王之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147311_comment'></div>伏念臣艺文素浅，学识非精，逢时误受于圣知，中第早尘于睿鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147311_comment'></div>代耕以禄，历试诸艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147311_comment'></div>初命授将作监丞，再命历左右遗补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147311_comment'></div>遇郊丘之恩泽，转记事之班资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147311_comment'></div>尸素为虞，廉勤益励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147311_comment'></div>仍念策名之岁，亲闻金口之言，常令各守谦和，莫忘笔砚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147311_comment'></div>迩后或漳滨近郡，或江外远官，莅事之馀，修词敢怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147311_comment'></div>况带史臣之职，虑孤英主之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147311_comment'></div>尝因叠嶂危楼，既登高而必赋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147311_comment'></div>钓台浅濑，亦倚棹以成诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147311_comment'></div>岂唯抒子牟恋阙之心，其实歌文王南国之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147311_comment'></div>菁英虽寡，编缀靡遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147311_comment'></div>三度拜章，聊举箴规之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147311_comment'></div>八年外任，复归侍从之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147311_comment'></div>因辄上言，却乞在馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147311_comment'></div>蒙圣恩之俞允，仍旧贯以编修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147311_comment'></div>清閤濡毫，愧乏素臣之作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147311_comment'></div>丹墀珥笔，惭非右史之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147311_comment'></div>陛下既以文学知臣，臣敢不以文字报答陛下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147311_comment'></div>今录得在睦州编集中歌诗赋颂共十轴，谨诣东上閤门进献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147311_comment'></div>播乐章于金石，文彩非工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147311_comment'></div>祈睿鉴于冕旒，罪尤可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147311_comment'></div>干冒宸扆，臣无任惶恐激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1147311_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年9月</a>　九月，在京为起居舍人，献《乾明节祝圣寿诗二十韵》，获宋太宗依韵和赐，有谢表。作品：谢御制和祝圣寿诗表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢御制和祝圣寿诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147309")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147309'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147309'>臣锡言：今月十七日，宰臣琼赴中书，伏蒙圣慈宣赐御和臣所进《乾明节祝圣寿诗二十韵》者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147309_comment'></div>俯拜皇恩，仰窥睿藻，骇凡目而怔忪失次，阅圣文而荣抃交并<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147309_comment'></div>伏以华封庆祝之辰，里社呈祥之节，颂声合贡，忠恳冀伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147309_comment'></div>岂谓皇帝陛下降御制而颁宣，命台阶以锡赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147309_comment'></div>始欢呼而跪受，终惕厉以退思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147309_comment'></div>且《书》曰「赓歌」，《诗》称《大雅》，但美升平之际会，或扬德业之形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147309_comment'></div>未闻臣下献葑菲之词，君上答英华之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147309_comment'></div>斯实皇朝新事，玄贶殊恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147309_comment'></div>用纪瑶编六义，常彰于睿思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147309_comment'></div>永光宝运千龄，永固于昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147309_comment'></div>臣无任感恩荷圣、荣耀兢惶、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147309_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年9月16日</a>　九月十六日，在京为起居舍人，上疏请封禅泰山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年9月17日</a>　九月十七日，在京为起居舍人，以本官知制诰，有致谢笏记。作品：谢知制诰笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147352' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147352' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147352?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知制诰笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年9月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147352")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147352_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147352'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147352'>臣锡言：臣伏蒙圣慈赐臣官诰一通，敕牒一道，特授臣知制诰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147352_comment'></div>祗苛宠荣，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147352_comment'></div>伏念臣声光素浅，文艺非高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147352_comment'></div>东观濡毫，不足与史官之列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147352_comment'></div>西垣掌诰，安能司王者之言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147352_comment'></div>岂谓圣慈，擢升清近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147352_comment'></div>演纶凤阁，惭非润色之才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147352_comment'></div>委佩龙墀，忽在论思之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147352_comment'></div>敢不冰泉励节，缃素研几，上酬英主之恩，聊举词臣之职。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1147352_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作宋镐除监察御史制。作品：太子中允御史台推直宋镐可监察御史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147217' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147217' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147217?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太子中允御史台推直宋镐可监察御史制</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147217")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147217_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147217'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147217'>敕：具官宋镐，宪府为寮，公才称职，既茂强明之绩，仍闻尉荐之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147217_comment'></div>霜简迁升，勉服辉光之命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147217_comment'></div>台纲整肃，更观纠察之能。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147217_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作程文度除监察御史充荆湖转运使制。作品：左赞善大夫程文度可监察御史充荆湖转运使。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147218' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147218' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147218?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左赞善大夫程文度可监察御史充荆湖转运使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147218")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147218_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147218'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147218'>敕：国家转输之任，荆湖冲要之邦，必择周才，付兹重委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147218_comment'></div>厥职既称于繁剧，改官宜陟于清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147218_comment'></div>以尔具官程文度，以文学策名，以贞固干事，尝莅京口，郁有政声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147218_comment'></div>俾升执宪之班，往莅泛舟之役，伸尔嘉画，称予懋恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147218_comment'></div>傥奏课之有闻，固陟明之无吝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147218_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作仇延郎可银青阶兼官制。作品：皇城司勘契官仇延郎可银青阶兼官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇城司勘契官仇延郎可银青阶兼官制<span class='inlineComment2'>（将东郊，先除授。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147171")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147171'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147171'>敕具官仇延郎：有司上言，先事列职，俾靖恭于禁籍，宜时茂于朝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147171_comment'></div>假以宫宾，兼之宪职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147171_comment'></div>冀以阶资之宠，参乎仪卫之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147171_comment'></div>恪奉斯恩，无怠所守。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147171_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作胡旦除知制诰制。作品：户部员外郎充史官修撰胡旦可知制诰。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147226' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147226' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147226?labeling=true' target='_blank'>户部员外郎充史馆修撰胡旦可知制诰制</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147226")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147226_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147226'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147226'>敕：朕以王道致时雍，人文化天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147226_comment'></div>而训诰之职，侍从之臣，必敷求其才，简拔精选，俾朕约束言语，与三代同风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147226_comment'></div>以尔具官胡旦，学识该通，笔力遒健，杰出多士，绰有大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147226_comment'></div>自中台为郎，史阁供职，得《春秋》之微旨，见褒贬之馀才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147226_comment'></div>然未司吾言，宁满尔志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147226_comment'></div>是用升于清切之禁，观其润色之词，无令元、白、常、杨，专美前代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147226_comment'></div>勉修儒行，以答殊恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147226_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作李若拙除盐铁判官制。作品：起居舍人李若拙可盐铁判官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>起居舍人李若拙可盐铁判官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147251")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147251'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147251'>敕：朕以管榷之利，军国是资，必求经济之谋，委以重繁之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147251_comment'></div>以尔具官李若拙，素有文学，蔼然声光，加以通明，善于操剸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147251_comment'></div>珥笔轩墀之下，直史是咨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147251_comment'></div>运筹征赋之能，干时攸属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147251_comment'></div>勉倅铜盐之职，更观盘错之才。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年1月</a>　正月，在京为知制诰，上表进《藉田颂》作品：进藉田颂表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span>藉田颂。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_1147310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进籍田颂表</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147310")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147310'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147310'>臣锡言：伏以东郊之仪，籍田之礼，历代久废，明诏复行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147310_comment'></div>阙典既修，无文咸秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147310_comment'></div>三农知劝，讵忘稼穑之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147310_comment'></div>万乘亲耕，将备粢盛之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147310_comment'></div>凡居率土，孰不欢呼？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147310_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏惟皇帝陛下体天覆育，并日照临，以百姓而为心，虑一夫之失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147310_comment'></div>讲求典礼，咨访阙遗，导其衣食之源，务以农桑之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147310_comment'></div>祥符交荐，上瑞必由于丰年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147310_comment'></div>王道已融，听政尚勤于日旰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147310_comment'></div>以为籍于千亩，礼有三推，耒耜置之于辂车，穜稑献之于宫禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147310_comment'></div>表身先于货殖，果德动于昭回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147310_comment'></div>嘉雪应期，盈尺已丰于渥泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147310_comment'></div>大田将稔，载歌方美于京坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147310_comment'></div>《易》曰先天，既便蕃于景贶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147310_comment'></div>《书》称固本，乃勉励于群情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147310_comment'></div>将以致孝享于宗祧，贻庆赖于黎庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147310_comment'></div>圣朝师古，有以见劝农务穑之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147310_comment'></div>来叶美谈，可以播下管登歌之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147310_comment'></div>臣幸逢昌运，忝列侍臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147310_comment'></div>清禁演纶，殊乏论思之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147310_comment'></div>黄门进牍，难偕体物之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147310_comment'></div>敢不祗率鄙怀，比求音于扣寂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147310_comment'></div>讴谣圣德，因献颂以达诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147310_comment'></div>固惭葑菲之文，上黩冕旒之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147310_comment'></div>然国家盛事，已闻野老之歌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147310_comment'></div>臣子为心，合效华封之祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147310_comment'></div>谨诣东上閤门，进《籍田颂》一首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147310_comment'></div>干冒宸严，臣无任惶恐激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1147310_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1147515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>籍田颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147515")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147515'>国家嗣位之十三载，王道清夷，边防静谧，时和岁稔，远至迩安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147515_comment'></div>藉田可复于躬耕，后稷宜修于祀事，足以劝三农之本，备九年之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147515_comment'></div>贵戚知稼穑之艰难，宗庙享粢盛之丰洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147515_comment'></div>于是坐朝堂以端拱，召公卿以就列，谓三事大夫曰：「邦国之本惟民也，黎元之命惟食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147515_comment'></div>使男有馀粟，女有馀布，老者得衰羸之养，少者知耕稼之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147515_comment'></div>衣食既丰，礼节自晓，然后风俗易化，刑罚不用，无乃为王者之所务乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147515_comment'></div>群心允谐，百辟听命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147515_comment'></div>由是金门晓辟，御札初下，布告自迩以及远，号令云行以雨施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147515_comment'></div>翌日命宰臣昉曰：「藉田大礼，尔为之使，俾礼典详而乐章备，百职举而千亩修」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147515_comment'></div>又命翰林学士宋白、贾黄中曰：「尔等司沿革于礼仪，典导从于卤簿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147515_comment'></div>然后百执事骏奔走，各奉其职，无旷厥官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147515_comment'></div>洎献岁发春，乙亥御辰，农祥晨正，农事将起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147515_comment'></div>六宫献穜稑之种，千官从耕藉之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147515_comment'></div>金舆玉乘，和鸾万骑以翼卫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147515_comment'></div>东郊南亩，华夷亿兆以骈阗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147515_comment'></div>观我后冕而朱纮，躬秉黛耜，坻场染屦，御于三推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147515_comment'></div>公卿大夫，自五至九，庶人终亩，礼容皇皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147515_comment'></div>若烟非烟，和气蓊郁，拂青坛而映翠幕，蔼春野而丽朝阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147515_comment'></div>既而奉常变六乐之悬，太仆进六騑之辔，金辂鞶缨之次列，黄麾羽林以驰驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147515_comment'></div>回御凤楼，揭鸡竿而赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147515_comment'></div>所谓圣人作而万物睹，王泽流而颂声起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147515_comment'></div>臣职居禁掖，才愧司言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147515_comment'></div>顾演诰以非工，宁裨润色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147515_comment'></div>因侍耕而献颂，用庆升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147515_comment'></div>美盛德之形容，纪皇猷之万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147515_comment'></div>颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1147515'>圣主文明，时方太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147515_comment'></div>四鄙无事，万邦咸宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147515_comment'></div>贯索星稀，所以措刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147515_comment'></div>泰阶文符，可以偃兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147515_comment'></div>物俗丕变，礼让兴行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147515_comment'></div>条风块雨，年惟顺成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147515_comment'></div>屋粟里布，岁有常征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147515_comment'></div>济济之众，蚩蚩之氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147515_comment'></div>若登华胥，若造大庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147515_comment'></div>藉田之礼，历代久废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147515_comment'></div>乃下御札，宣示中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147515_comment'></div>乃命有司，询谋经制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147515_comment'></div>祖述三皇，宪章五帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147515_comment'></div>蠲洁之享，割牲奠币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147515_comment'></div>清明之诚，三酒五齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147515_comment'></div>后稷豆笾，先农坛陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147515_comment'></div>钟磬罗列，冠剑繁会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147515_comment'></div>千官侍耕，诸侯助祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147515_comment'></div>居靡都鄙，人无华裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147515_comment'></div>叠迹驾肩，掎裳连袂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147515_comment'></div>观我耕藉，劝民树艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147515_comment'></div>布德覃恩，行庆施惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147515_comment'></div>惠泽霶流，天光下济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147515_comment'></div>礼仪彬彬，文物皆新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147515_comment'></div>圣德动天，至诚感神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147515_comment'></div>嘉雪应候，和气先春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147515_comment'></div>梅飘洒道，絮落清尘，驰道若坻，列幄如鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147515_comment'></div>卤簿云罗，车旆星陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147515_comment'></div>辉辉煌煌，阗阗辚辚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147515_comment'></div>三推礼毕，五辂回轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147515_comment'></div>普天之下，率土之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147515_comment'></div>知我劝农，悦我为民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147515_comment'></div>彫几返朴，风化还淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147515_comment'></div>庙祧之享，烝礿之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147515_comment'></div>萧茅鬯酒，藉田而有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147515_comment'></div>黍稷粢盛，藉田而取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147515_comment'></div>洁其簠簋，丰其俎豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147515_comment'></div>致享艺祖，展礼先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147515_comment'></div>祝史正辞，神降之祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147515_comment'></div>繁祉来宜，戬谷允受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147515_comment'></div>时岁丰穰，生物畅茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147515_comment'></div>帝王之孝，永言在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147515_comment'></div>黎元之本，莫重于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147515_comment'></div>惟仓惟箱，如京如坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147515_comment'></div>有醴有酪，为盛为粢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147515_comment'></div>神既歆之，民实赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147515_comment'></div>臣参词臣，官为右史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147515_comment'></div>因献斯颂，得以言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147515_comment'></div>乡饮之礼，行之甚易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147515_comment'></div>庠序之学，复之可以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147515_comment'></div>古典郁堙，由人振起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147515_comment'></div>千载一时，允谓昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147515_comment'></div>时不再来，臣实惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147515_comment'></div>登封降禅，愿陛下行之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1147515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年1月</a>　正月，在京为知制诰，上表进《河清颂》作品：进河清颂表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span>河清颂。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_1147312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进河清颂表</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147312")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147312'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147312'>臣锡言：伏睹中书门下奉宣示澶濮二州奏，今月五日黄河清者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147312_comment'></div>伏以千年之运，圣祚方兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147312_comment'></div>四渎之中，洪河为长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147312_comment'></div>波澜清泚，表嘉瑞以无疆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147312_comment'></div>图牒昭宣，协皇家之有感<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147312_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下唐、虞至德，汤、武圣功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147312_comment'></div>夕惕劳怀，掩文王之勤俭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147312_comment'></div>夙兴求理，侔大禹之咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147312_comment'></div>是以王道融明，犹日中之临照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147312_comment'></div>鸿猷浃洽，比天覆以恢崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147312_comment'></div>夷狄绥怀，边防久静；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147312_comment'></div>黎元富庶，风俗还淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147312_comment'></div>禋宗类帝以严恭，缵祖承祧以祗慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147312_comment'></div>公田载籍，将以奉清庙之粢盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147312_comment'></div>阙典咸修，将以报先农之功烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147312_comment'></div>万邦玉帛，方会于观耕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147312_comment'></div>九曲河源，遽闻于飞奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147312_comment'></div>勾芒应律，东风已泮于轻冰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147312_comment'></div>川后呈祥，习坎不生于浊浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147312_comment'></div>虚明洞乎鉴物，清洁可以濯缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147312_comment'></div>润下朝宗，示寰区之静谧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147312_comment'></div>储灵效祉，知社稷之感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147312_comment'></div>何让重华，临观授出图之异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147312_comment'></div>堪嗤孝武，中流告沈玉之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147312_comment'></div>宜播登歌，永光信史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147312_comment'></div>岂青云干吕，能昭文物之朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147312_comment'></div>沧海无波，更表声明之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147312_comment'></div>伫候白茅藉用，荐三脊于泰坛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147312_comment'></div>明水洁清，首五齐于玄酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147312_comment'></div>告成功于东岱，示底贡于西鳒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147312_comment'></div>升中秘玉检之封，永久嗣瑶图之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147312_comment'></div>臣才非典诰，职忝演纶，文翰是司，岂称代言之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147312_comment'></div>颂声合贡，用彰盛德之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147312_comment'></div>谨诣东上閤门，进《河清颂》一首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147312_comment'></div>干冒宸严，无任惶恐抃蹈激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1147312_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1147514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河清颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147514")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147514'>臣尝览图谍曰：河千年一清，圣人之大瑞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147514_comment'></div>考郦元之《水经》，稽夏书于《禹贡》，洪河千里一曲，上应云汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147514_comment'></div>发昆山而疏砥柱，贯中域而注沧溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147514_comment'></div>骇浪朝宗，通浊泾而一色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147514_comment'></div>灵长荐祉，带清渭之澄澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147514_comment'></div>所以彰睿圣之乘时，表升平之应运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147514_comment'></div>自陛下临御，十有三载，以尧舜之道行风教，以文武之德化要荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147514_comment'></div>礼让兴而刑罚清，兵革偃而边防静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147514_comment'></div>五星不差于轨道，百谷屡报于丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147514_comment'></div>信及豚鱼，应大《易·中孚》之象；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147514_comment'></div>仁敷草木，协《国风》《行苇》之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147514_comment'></div>谅寿域之可跻，宜华封之来祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147514_comment'></div>是以功成则《韶》、《濩》之音必作，理定则俎豆之事毕修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147514_comment'></div>方洁祀于先农，式告虔于后稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147514_comment'></div>青坛翠幄，列于国门之东；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147514_comment'></div>葱犗缥衡，置彼公田之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147514_comment'></div>五辂南辕之在驭，三推御耦以将亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147514_comment'></div>粤若澶渊之滨，雷泽之浒，献岁发春之五日，东风解冱于增冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147514_comment'></div>初涟漪以成文，旋浩渺以交漾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147514_comment'></div>澄清见底，荣光袭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147514_comment'></div>沈潜可鉴于游鳞，浮动远涵于瑞日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147514_comment'></div>守土之吏，乘轺之臣，会父老以载观，驰笺章而上达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147514_comment'></div>圣恩宣示，瑶图让德于圆灵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147514_comment'></div>臣下欢呼，金门拜表以称贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147514_comment'></div>百执事蹈舞以就列，亿兆众歌咏于逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147514_comment'></div>岂不以玄德升闻，而象纬呈休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147514_comment'></div>王泽旁流，而山川荐瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147514_comment'></div>矧太史钩盘之经渎，桃花竹箭之迅湍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147514_comment'></div>人寿之言，古贤惜其难俟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147514_comment'></div>灵源之异，圣出庆于荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147514_comment'></div>与夫《芝房》、《宝鼎》之歌，瑶瓮、醴泉之咏，岂同日而言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147514_comment'></div>臣忝窃代言，惭非称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147514_comment'></div>歌时乐圣，合陈葑菲之词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147514_comment'></div>载笔侍耕，得纪河源之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147514_comment'></div>颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1147514'>圣主千年运，洪河九曲清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147514_comment'></div>地灵储庆异，天意属升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147514_comment'></div>冰泮赪鲂躣，波摇瑞气生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147514_comment'></div>远通灵沼液，高彻绛河明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147514_comment'></div>汉国惭为带，沧浪愧濯缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147514_comment'></div>鉴人曾爽澈，润物达勾萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147514_comment'></div>明日兼淮映，荣光向海倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147514_comment'></div>王正春尚浅，帝甸雪初晴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147514_comment'></div>万国观农祀，千官侍御耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147514_comment'></div>奏章驰象魏，拜表会公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147514_comment'></div>荐祉臻川渎，言祥自水衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147514_comment'></div>出图同表异，习坎象持盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147514_comment'></div>珠溅龙门溜，雷奔砥柱声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147514_comment'></div>莹宜清渭合，湛可玉壶盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147514_comment'></div>更显皇猷洽，弥彰理化行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147514_comment'></div>百王堪让美，三代岂称英？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147514_comment'></div>深广源流远，涵濡品汇贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147514_comment'></div>土膏承积润，水泽效殊祯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147514_comment'></div>群后思东观，吾皇待告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147514_comment'></div>微臣献诗颂，葵藿比忠诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1147514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年1月</a>　正月，在京为知制诰，作三司大将加恩制。作品：三司大将加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三司大将加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147170")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147170'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147170'>敕：躬耕之礼，用示于劝农；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147170_comment'></div>庆赐之恩，必均于效职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147170_comment'></div>以尔等各伸劳绩，常夙夜以在公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147170_comment'></div>例授恩荣，表云雷之霈泽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147170_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年2月20日</a>　二月二十日，在京为知制诰，迁兵部员外郎、知制诰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年闰5月</a>　闰五月，在京为知制诰，作麻希梦致仕制。作品：大理司直前青州录事参军麻希梦可守工部员外郎致仕。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。此文系年参《宋会要辑稿》职官七七之三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1147176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大理司直前青州录事参军麻希梦可守工部员外郎致仕制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年闰5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147176")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147176'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147176'>敕具官麻希梦：朕嗣位十有三载，天下无事，思劝农务本，躬耕籍田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147176_comment'></div>改元乃与物维新，发号则均人之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147176_comment'></div>可以行古道，礼高年，由是赦书有赐爵一级之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147176_comment'></div>而希梦年过九十，以伏生之经术寿考，践历官途，而为廷尉属寮，兼宪府之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147176_comment'></div>督邮罢秩，颐养于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147176_comment'></div>守臣上言，轩墀引见，嘉其华皓，是用旌升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147176_comment'></div>荣之列宿之班，优以悬车之秩，所以表朕养老尚齿之意也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147176_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年7月</a>　七月，在京为知制诰，受宋太宗之命作镇州龙兴寺大悲像及阁碑铭。作品：大宋重修铸镇州龙兴寺大悲像并阁碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷九九。孙谱系此文于端拱二年，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋重修铸镇州龙兴寺大悲像并阁碑铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序端拱二年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（988年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147522")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147522'>国家改元曰端拱之年，有司下镇阳之奏，以大悲铜像镕范既久，高阁精庐缔搆已就，琢他山之石琰，请好词以铭镂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147522_comment'></div>秋七月，天子视朔于明堂之日，王言如纶，乃命词臣，俾濡染摭实之文，叙修□废兴之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147522_comment'></div>臣再拜稽首，惶恐祗肃，以为刻贞石，垂丕休，扬圣朝崇建之本末，视后人耳目之听信，茍非鸿儒硕生，有大手笔，空门实相，达□心观，则安能抽秘思，答明诏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147522_comment'></div>徒以末学肤浅，昧道荒忽，聊叙万分之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147522_comment'></div>夫随感而通，能救诸苦，谓之大慈大悲乎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147522_comment'></div>应变无方，能现诸相，谓之千手千眼乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147522_comment'></div>然真性本空，不生亦不灭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147522_comment'></div>冥数前定，有废□有兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147522_comment'></div>周显德中，世宗纳近臣之议，以为奄有封略不过千里，所调租庸不丰边备，校贯屡空于军实，算□莫济于时须，于是诏天下毁铜像，鼓铸以为钱货，利用以资帑财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147522_comment'></div>金人其萎，梁木其坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147522_comment'></div>化身从革，通有无于市征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147522_comment'></div>圆府流□，岂执著于我相？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147522_comment'></div>而惟镇之邦，惟镇之民，万人聚，千人计，惜成功，□见毁，冀上意以中辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147522_comment'></div>虽卜式出财以有助，而赞皇执议以不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147522_comment'></div>洎像坏之际，于莲叶之中有字曰「遇显即毁」，无乃前定之数乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147522_comment'></div>物不可以终隳，必授之以兴复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147522_comment'></div>时不可以终否，必授之以隆昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147522_comment'></div>我国家应乎天，顺□人，革有周之正朔，造皇宋之基业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147522_comment'></div>南取越，西平蜀，崇道教，兴佛法，无文咸秩，隳像重兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147522_comment'></div>乾德中，乃命重铸大悲之像于是邦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147522_comment'></div>虞衡伐木，司爟用火，法阴阳以为炭，□天地以成炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147522_comment'></div>岂万物之铜，万灵之庸，凭帝力以神速，因匠哲而功倍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147522_comment'></div>既而镕成，满月之容，如冠轻霞，升于颢□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147522_comment'></div>青莲为目，天花饰躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147522_comment'></div>四十二臂，金色曈昽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147522_comment'></div>七十三口，宝相穹隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147522_comment'></div>仰之弥高，瞻之益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147522_comment'></div>洎搆以摩云之阁，如褐蓬壶，倚于辽廊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147522_comment'></div>□□旋题，风清宝铎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147522_comment'></div>十□三袭，危梁□跃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147522_comment'></div>重阶复道，飞栋电㸌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147522_comment'></div>夕月莹其藻绘，朝霞饰其丹雘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147522_comment'></div>有周之毁也既如彼，我宋之兴也复如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147522_comment'></div>今皇帝嗣鸿业，凝睿图，运应千龄，道超三古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147522_comment'></div>成汤克己，称其德也谓「齐圣广渊」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147522_comment'></div>帝尧为心，称其道也曰「聪明文思」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147522_comment'></div>用七德，讲五□，□□礼义德刑为战器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147522_comment'></div>疆四海，宇万方，而以动植黎元跻寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147522_comment'></div>豆笾有践，配烈祖于上□；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147522_comment'></div>金石成文，谒先师于太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147522_comment'></div>列儒臣以侍讲，祀先农以躬耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147522_comment'></div>礼容彬彬，帝仪穆穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147522_comment'></div>六服群辟，罔不率□；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147522_comment'></div>四夷左衽，罔不□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147522_comment'></div>延虎观以议偃兵，访鹣林以俟检玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147522_comment'></div>包匦述菁茅之职，公车献封禅之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147522_comment'></div>岂不由德动天？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147522_comment'></div>天道顺，星辰轨道，风雨咸若，来浙帅，俘晋主，祥麟出，黄河清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147522_comment'></div>天且弗违，况于人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147522_comment'></div>佛犹其依，况于鬼神乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147522_comment'></div>越太平兴国之七年，秋仲□月，粤有苾刍，其名琼法，祗受宣旨，专主佛阁，焚修勤恪，住持教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147522_comment'></div>以为像之设也，□阁之成也，宜周之以廊宇，严之以闬闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147522_comment'></div>于是经之营之，七年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147522_comment'></div>化舆□，鸠众财，人心□，财用备，土木其萃，班、倕斯至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147522_comment'></div>始揆日以悦使，俄有时而告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147522_comment'></div>长廊翼舒，回映□其千柱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147522_comment'></div>重门洞启，壮丽豁然四达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147522_comment'></div>然琼法有如是勤、如是化也，如是缘、如是功乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147522_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147522_comment'></div>民有馀财，方能施佛财；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147522_comment'></div>众有羡利，方能修福利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147522_comment'></div>引而伸之，夫所宝者慈与俭，所修者礼与乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147522_comment'></div>叙彝伦，建皇极，生民所以获福者，中国圣人之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147522_comment'></div>所去者贪嗔痴，所修者戒定慧，诸天由修福生，诸趣由造罪入，超无生、證无漏者，西方释氏之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147522_comment'></div>然非明圣在上，则像法畴依；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147522_comment'></div>非富庶在下，则塔庙不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147522_comment'></div>今公帑有羡财，国廪有馀积，可以营佛事，创梵宫，不害民，不妨农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147522_comment'></div>农亦有馀□，民亦有经产，可以舍净财，结善缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147522_comment'></div>闻钟磬之音，则随喜之心生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147522_comment'></div>睹慈悲之相，则□□□□起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147522_comment'></div>□花由是献，金币由是臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147522_comment'></div>赞睿泽如东溟之深，祝圣寿若南山之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147522_comment'></div>其应如响，获福无量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147522_comment'></div>臣文非润色，职在司言，祗诏徬徨，命笔数四，以为文不迨意，意不迨理，理不达于真谛，文不称于王命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147522_comment'></div>江淹才尽，宁摛五色之毫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147522_comment'></div>相如思迟，徒奉九重之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147522_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_1147522'>吾皇御宇，运膺下武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147522_comment'></div>金玉王度，为佛法主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147522_comment'></div>《易》不云：「圣人而万物睹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147522_comment'></div>《礼》有中庸，《易》有变通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147522_comment'></div>筌蹄至理，与佛□同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147522_comment'></div>臣所谓王泽流而三宝方崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147522_comment'></div>天生蒸民，树之司□，□□帝力，谓衣食自足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147522_comment'></div>所以归依佛，归依法，而获天人之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147522_comment'></div>佛度众生，摄以慈悲，莫测神化，以感应无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147522_comment'></div>所以不可量，不可思，而为□人之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147522_comment'></div>范金成象之容，瞻仰云中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147522_comment'></div>傍双列于□，□严厥功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147522_comment'></div>上栋下宇之制，岌嶪空际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147522_comment'></div>高特出于楼台，彫锼其丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147522_comment'></div>若士若庶，至菩萨前，稽首法愿，结其因缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147522_comment'></div>无远无近，睹菩萨相，膜拜展礼，除其罪障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147522_comment'></div>其毁也无乃示有周□□，其□也□以彰皇宋其昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147522_comment'></div>诏下创立，圣谟洋洋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147522_comment'></div>功成磊落，福善穰穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147522_comment'></div>□镇之邦，在冀之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147522_comment'></div>全赵封圻以画野，恒山郁盘以连岗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147522_comment'></div>慈为云兮敷荫，慧为日兮扬光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147522_comment'></div>祐我圣皇，宝祚□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147522_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_1147522'>端拱二年，岁次己丑，正月癸未朔，十五日丁酉建立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147522_comment'></div>李思顺、李屿、李继元鑴字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_100_1147522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1147522'><span class='label'>按：</span>《常山贞石志》卷一一，台湾新文丰出版公司石刻史料新编本。又见《金石萃编》卷一二五，《八琼室金石补正》卷八五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1147522_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年11月</a>　十一月，在京为知制诰，作王明迁礼部侍郎制。作品：光州刺史王明可礼部侍郎。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。此文系年参《宋会要辑稿》职官四七之三。）</span><div id='poem_1147188' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147188' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147188?labeling=true' target='_blank'>光州刺史王明可礼部侍郎制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147188")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147188_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147188'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147188'>敕：中台六卿之职，斯为重任，而设以卿亚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147188_comment'></div>苟非智识通敏，机务淹详，公望素高，清议惟允，则何以为时瞻重，称吾简求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147188_comment'></div>以尔具官王明，真方特操，沉毅有谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147188_comment'></div>临事彰适变之才，奉上见尽忠之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147188_comment'></div>剖竹每闻于课第，兼襦必蔼于政声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147188_comment'></div>朕尝便殿与言，观其敷奏，方略才用，良足嘉称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147188_comment'></div>宜副畴咨，以旌茂赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147188_comment'></div>春官峻秩，可以贰之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147188_comment'></div>礼闱崇资，谅无忝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147188_comment'></div>尔识量既如彼，而绵历又如此，岂烦训告，勉荷宠光。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1147188_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作王承衍妹封琅琊县君制。作品：永清军节度使驸马都尉王承衍妹王氏封琅琊县君。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147168' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147168' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147168?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永清军节度使驸马都尉王承衍妹王氏封琅邪县君制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147168")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147168_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147168'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147168'>敕：具官王承衍妹王氏，贤明为德，婉淑其仪，环佩中于礼容，兰蕙蔼其令范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147168_comment'></div>嫔于良族，既咏《柏舟》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147168_comment'></div>茂我皇姻，宜封石窌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147168_comment'></div>载协云雷之泽，俾疏汤沐之封。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147168_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作赵希赞可泰州刺史制。作品：朔州观察使左骁卫大将军赵希赞可泰州刺史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147174' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147174' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147174?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朔州观察使左骁卫大将军赵希赞可泰州刺史制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147174")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147174_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147174'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147174'>敕：分朕忧寄，颁于诏条；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147174_comment'></div>亲吾黎民，行其风教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147174_comment'></div>惟良之命，既难其人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147174_comment'></div>作牧之荣，实重其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147174_comment'></div>以尔具官赵希赞，忠贞抗节，毅勇存诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147174_comment'></div>弓冶袭其庆灵，韬钤著于绩效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147174_comment'></div>以拱卫腹心之任，委察廉风俗之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147174_comment'></div>边鄙用宁，茕嫠受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147174_comment'></div>宜膺茂赏，别降玺书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147174_comment'></div>淮甸之邦，汉符剧郡，命以俾乂，畴其允釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147174_comment'></div>伫腾襦裤之谣，达予闻听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147174_comment'></div>岂吝丝纶之诏，奖尔贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147174_comment'></div>佩兹训词，孚予明命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1147174_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作王仲华等母封太君制。作品：右司谏直馆王仲华监察御史潘太初等母封太君。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div
