id='poem_1147179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147179' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147179?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右司谏直馆王仲华监察御史潘太初等母封太君制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147179")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147179_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147179'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147179'>敕：具官王仲华母信都戴氏，圣善之贤，慈仁之训，克生令子，为吾谏官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147179_comment'></div>朱绂彩衣，足荣具庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147179_comment'></div>粉田石窌，未该邑封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147179_comment'></div>嘉其孝养之心，特乞优隆之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147179_comment'></div>宜从子贵，式显母仪，俾新汤沐之封，以适庭闱之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147179_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作诸吏迁官制。作品：御史台孔目官门下省杂事南曹诸司勒留归司等官可中书省主书门下省主事千牛卫长史及簿尉司马勒留并出外县簿尉。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147237")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147237_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147237'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147237'>敕：国家以耕籍之仪，内外洽涵濡之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147237_comment'></div>具官某等，官曹委质，公干小心，星霜备历于劳能，雨露宜均于恩渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147237_comment'></div>省庭禁卫，郡佐邑僚，各励恭勤，以奉尔职。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147237_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作张守中可许州别驾制。作品：前守霸州大城令张守中可许州别驾。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_1147186_comment'></div>民之高年，尚云赐爵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147186_comment'></div>吏之暮齿，忍弃其人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147186_comment'></div>尔早居铜墨之资，尝莅边防之邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147186_comment'></div>眷言衰迈，爰此对扬，特示朝恩，俾升郡佐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作孙运致仕制。作品：前济州金乡令孙运可左赞善大夫致仕。<span id='poem_sentence_1_1147200_comment'></div>尔早纡命服，今享遐龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147200_comment'></div>当殿披陈，临轩召见，宜霈云天之泽，俾光蒲柳之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147200_comment'></div>晋秩宫坊，谅为嘉宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147200_comment'></div>悬车里第，足遂优闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147200_comment'></div>勉思涣汗之文，以协贞颐之吉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147200_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作刘文裕赠官制。作品：故容州观察使刘文裕可赠宁远军节度使。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147230' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147230_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147230'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147230'>敕：朝廷褒赠之恩，臣子哀荣之典，载稽彝训，式表始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147230_comment'></div>具官刘文裕，韬略英才，公侯令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147230_comment'></div>禀直方之器识，茂勋绩于旂常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147230_comment'></div>自廉问宣风，化条绥远，宾海著兼襦之咏，佐时图镂鼎之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147230_comment'></div>奄忽遽闻，悼伤宁弭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147230_comment'></div>宜举饰终之礼，用彰念往之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147230_comment'></div>旌节之荣，藩宣之秩，俾增辉于窀穸，示追宠于明灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147230_comment'></div>真魂有知，钦兹贲饰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1147230_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作供奉官殿直殿前承旨加恩制。作品：供奉官殿直殿前承旨加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147233?labeling=true' target='_blank'>供奉官殿直殿前承旨加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147233")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147233'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147233'>敕具官某：朝廷耕籍之仪，纶綍阶升之命，用均庆赐，以劝劳能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147233_comment'></div>以尔忠于事君，勤于莅事，列班行而素久，经委任以居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147233_comment'></div>既因作解之辰，宜洽惟新之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147233_comment'></div>勉成茂绩，以称殊私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147233_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作宋渥等加恩制。作品：诸卫上将军宋渥等加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147239' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147239' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147239?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸卫上将军宋渥等加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147239")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147239_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147239'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147239'>敕：朕以躬耕之礼，初毕于东郊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147239_comment'></div>庆赐之恩，方行于北阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147239_comment'></div>矧在拱环之列，早彰宿卫之勋，宜茂宠章，以新赏典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147239_comment'></div>具官宋渥等，为吾心腹，列在爪牙，忠贞之大节无渝，英果之威名自得，功崇社稷，勋镂鼎彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147239_comment'></div>拥旄畴昔之殊庸，出綍惟新之宠数，恩光并及，渥泽斯均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147239_comment'></div>俾增井赋之荣，用洽籍田之庆，勉膺嘉命，益励输忠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147239_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作王承衍、魏咸信子加阶勋制。作品：永清彰德等军节度使驸马都尉王承衍男世隆魏咸信男亮并加阶勋如京副使。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147240' class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147240")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147240_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147240'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147240'>敕：具官某男某，生于戚里，为吾外孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147240_comment'></div>禀明训于义方，昭令名于士范，才能可试，庆赐宜均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147240_comment'></div>是用加珥貂骑省之资，帖执简乌台之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147240_comment'></div>茂之勋赏，进以阶资，莅于使局之名，命以副车之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147240_comment'></div>勉图成效，无怠宠光。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147240_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作内班都知押班以下加恩制。作品：内班都知押班以下加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内班都知押班已下加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147248")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147248'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147248'>敕具官某：朕以既举籍田之礼，方覃率土之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147248_comment'></div>矧列轩墀，常亲左右，宜均嘉庆，俾洽鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147248_comment'></div>以尔等奉上之心，无渝忠恪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147248_comment'></div>适时之智，各韫周通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147248_comment'></div>夙宵匪懈以在公，事务服勤以成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147248_comment'></div>爰新渥泽，用示甄升，或进以阶资，或荣其爵邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147248_comment'></div>勉荷云雷之宠，更增班秩之荣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147248_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作幕职加官制。作品：幕职加官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>幕职加官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147252")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147252'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147252'>敕：王者展籍田之礼，庆赐遂行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147252_comment'></div>宾从列幕府之荣，宠章斯洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147252_comment'></div>具官某等，咸怀器业，素蕴筹谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147252_comment'></div>或樽罍亹亹之谈，能申婉画；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147252_comment'></div>或笺奏翩翩之俊，俱蔼声光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147252_comment'></div>渥泽宜均，华资式叙，粉闱兼秩，勋籍增荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147252_comment'></div>勉扬裨赞之才，用答优隆之命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作刘巨川迁太常寺太祝制。作品：秘书省正字刘巨川可太常寺太祝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_1147253_comment'></div>当庆赐遂行之际，申赏延于世之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147253_comment'></div>勿坠家声，勉扬官业。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作林峤等加官制。作品：勒停追官人林峤等加官。<span id='poem_sentence_1_1147254_comment'></div>勉膺霶霈之恩，以补旷遗之过。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作堂后官十五人转官制。作品：堂后官一十五人转官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>堂后官一十五人转官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147255")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147255'>敕：国家行籍田之礼，覃庆赐之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147255_comment'></div>以尔具官某等，素以才能，早彰劳绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147255_comment'></div>丞相之府，既列职以为荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147255_comment'></div>王者之恩，方出纶以均宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147255_comment'></div>兰台美秩，棘寺华资，勉祗荷于宠光，更靖共于官次。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作守当官等二十人受官制。作品：守当官等二十人受官。<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147256'>敕：具官某等，各以劳能，勤于职次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147256_comment'></div>既偶覃恩之际，可膺进秩之荣，宜锡阶资，或升佐职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147256_comment'></div>题舆初命，勉荷殊迁，无忘夙夜之勤，以答云雷之泽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147256_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作刘保勋赠官制。作品：故谏议大夫刘保勋可赠工部侍郎。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147257' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147257' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147257?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故谏议大夫刘保勋可赠工部侍郎制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147257")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147257_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147257'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147257'>敕：生享显秩，殁有追封，表君亲终始之恩，彰臣子忠贞之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147257_comment'></div>况殁于王事，歼我邦良，宜因覃庆之辰，特茂饰终之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147257_comment'></div>故具官刘保勋，早登华贯，素蔼嘉称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147257_comment'></div>玉琯融和粹之诚，冰壶莹洁清之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147257_comment'></div>践更台阁，茂著风猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147257_comment'></div>正直表于搢绅，简廉允于公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147257_comment'></div>洎边朔平戎之役，见驰驱尽瘁之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147257_comment'></div>哲人其萎，悼百身以何赎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147257_comment'></div>徽章有赠，加三襚以宁忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147257_comment'></div>是用旌尔贞魂，因予大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147257_comment'></div>冬官亚卿之秩，可贲漏泉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147257_comment'></div>勤王陨命之灵，谅歆玄泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147257_comment'></div>申恩念往，式表予怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1147257_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作诸吏加恩制。作品：开封府祗候都孔目官左右军巡使及诸王府内知客等加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开封府祗候都孔目官左右军巡使及诸王府内知客等加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147260")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147260'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147260'>敕：国家因庆覃恩，自迩及远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147260_comment'></div>矧京府左右之职，王门亲近之人，必均宠荣，用甄劳绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147260_comment'></div>具官某，选于班秩，择以公才，俾祗事于磐维，观恪勤于夙夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147260_comment'></div>果能尽瘁匪懈，畏法保躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147260_comment'></div>式当作解之辰，宜洽惟新之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147260_comment'></div>勉膺嘉命，益励忠诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147260_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作李继捧母、祖母加封制。作品：耀州节度李继捧母汉阳郡夫人吴氏可进封南阳郡太夫人祖母河西罔氏可特封西河郡太夫人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147262?labeling=true' target='_blank'>耀州节度李继捧母汉阳郡夫人吴氏可进封南阳郡太夫人祖母河西罔氏可特封西河郡太夫人制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1147262'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147262'>敕：耕籍之仪，则后妃献穜稑之种；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147262_comment'></div>闺闱之庆，则命妇进汤沐之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147262_comment'></div>具官李继捧母，贤和并茂，贞淑允修，榛栗得妇贽之容，蘋藻协母仪之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147262_comment'></div>生育令子，为吾帅臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147262_comment'></div>剖符仗钺之荣，既彰家范；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147262_comment'></div>石窌鱼轩之贵，宜懋国封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147262_comment'></div>勉遵内则之规，伫奉公桑之礼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147262_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作沈伦追封制。作品：故左仆射致仕赠侍中沈伦可追封鲁国公。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147264?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故左仆射致仕赠侍中沈伦可追封鲁国公制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147264")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147264'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147264'>敕：追荣念旧，悼往申思，方当覃庆之辰，宜举饰终之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147264_comment'></div>故具官沈伦，岩廊耆德，社稷纯臣，辅邦国以贞方，遗子孙以清白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147264_comment'></div>儒行昭明于信史，忠规模范于搢绅，既谐止足之诚，遽起歼良之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147264_comment'></div>徽音岂昧，庆泽宜优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147264_comment'></div>龟蒙进大国之封，洙泗协漏泉之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147264_comment'></div>式扬嘉命，以慰英魂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147264_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作宰臣三代追封制。作品：宰臣三代追封。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147266' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147266_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147266'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147266'>敕：国家覃庆赐之时，幽显迨追崇之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147266_comment'></div>实因赏以示劝，旌贻厥以延恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147266_comment'></div>某官某曾祖母，淑善慈仁，既作嫔于祖德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147266_comment'></div>贤明轨范，果垂庆于孙谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147266_comment'></div>宜其光大庭闱，昭宣辅弼，汤沐遗荣于封国，云雷饰宠于漏泉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147266_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作赵惟叙等加官制。作品：皇侄孙惟叙等三人加官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇侄孙惟叙等三人加官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147267")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147267'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147267'>敕：朕以劝勉三农，既举籍田之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147267_comment'></div>敦叙九族，宜均出綍之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147267_comment'></div>所以荣茂本枝，繁昌奕世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147267_comment'></div>皇侄孙某等，岐嶷早彰于令器，温恭自毓于贤才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147267_comment'></div>阅《诗》《礼》以饰躬，讽圭璋之比德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147267_comment'></div>或庆隆朱邸，或粹禀青宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147267_comment'></div>协《雅》《颂》于振振，锡贻谋之翼翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147267_comment'></div>是用荣之阶爵，列在拱环，兼中台端揆之资，加宪府准绳之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147267_comment'></div>增其勋赏，进以户封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147267_comment'></div>尔其砺行以砥名，勿怠推忠而尽节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147267_comment'></div>佩此明训，为吾令孙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147267_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作致仕、分司等官加恩制。作品：致仕分司等官加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147268?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致仕分司等官加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147268")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147268_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147268'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147268'>敕：国家行籍田之礼，内外覃庆泽之恩，比雨露以咸均，协地天之交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147268_comment'></div>以尔具官某等，各以才行，萃列班资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147268_comment'></div>或洛邑分曹，荷朝章于结绶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147268_comment'></div>或燕居优秩，得礼典于悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147268_comment'></div>增其井赋之荣，茂以勋阶之赏，俾膺嘉庆，以洽鸿私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147268_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作押东郊进奉衙内指挥使等加恩制。作品：押东郊进奉衙内指挥使并衙前职员等加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147269' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147269' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147269?labeling=true' target='_blank'>押东郊进奉衙内指挥使并衙前职员等加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147269")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147269_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147269'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147269'>敕：籍田之礼，所以献穜稑，奉粢盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147269_comment'></div>躬耕既毕于三推，覃庆是均于万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147269_comment'></div>某等各以将命，来贡明庭，宜嘉勤恪之诚，俾浃涵濡之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147269_comment'></div>勉膺宠异，更励公忠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147269_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作翰林书画待诏等加恩制。作品：翰林书画琴阮医药等待诏加恩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147270' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147270?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翰林书画琴阮医药等待诏加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147270")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147270_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147270'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147270'>敕：籍田之礼久废，今朕行之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147270_comment'></div>庆泽之恩既普，与众同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147270_comment'></div>某等技艺精通，履行纯谨，各奉禁林之职，夙彰艺圃之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147270_comment'></div>覃恩既洽于涵濡，祗宠勿忘于惕励。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147270_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在京为知制诰，作郭贲除太祝制。作品：摄太祝郭贲可正太祝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>摄太祝郭贲可正太祝制</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147273")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147273'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147273'>敕具官郭贲：朕昨率古礼，耕籍田；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147273_comment'></div>祀先农，遵故典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147273_comment'></div>而太常太祝，或有摄官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147273_comment'></div>以尔贲恭命祗肃，奉职勤劳，必也正名，以示优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147273_comment'></div>尔其砥砺，用答恩荣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147273_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年1月13日</a>　正月十三日，在京为知制诰，上疏论边事。作品：上太宗答诏论边事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太宗答诏论边事</a><span class='authorDate'>（端拱二年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147287")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147287'>臣伏睹今月十一日御札，宣示内外文武臣僚，以北鄙多虞，戎人为患，延伫良策，降谕德音，询御侮之嘉谋，问安边之远略，俾悉陈于异见，将择用其所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147287_comment'></div>臣之颛愚，岂足上副宸衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147287_comment'></div>臣之狂直，敢不罄尽鄙怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147287_comment'></div>傥扬纳可裨于事宜，则明圣不罪于狂瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147287_comment'></div>臣每读史传，详观古来戎狄骚边，乃是常事，朝廷设备自有常规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147287_comment'></div>举其大略而言之，不过训练师徒，选择将帅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147287_comment'></div>广增蓄备，多置屯田；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147287_comment'></div>严其池城，明于斥堠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147287_comment'></div>谨于烽火，利其甲兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147287_comment'></div>行间谍以离狄心，禁侵扰以怠敌意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147287_comment'></div>待彼羸弱，因势取之，候其宾服，以德绥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147287_comment'></div>此皆方策备陈，采择可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147287_comment'></div>舍此则未见御戎之术，用此则在知临事之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147287_comment'></div>兵机则不可定谋，边议则须依古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147287_comment'></div>今具条奏，惟陛下择而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1147287'>一、今之御戎，无先于选将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147287_comment'></div>既得将帅，请委任责成，不必降之以阵图，不须授之以方略，自然因机设变，观衅制宜，以此无不成功，以是无不破敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147287_comment'></div>昔汉之西羌犯塞，攻城邑，杀长吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147287_comment'></div>赵充国年七十矣，上使邴吉问曰：「谁可为将」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147287_comment'></div>充国对曰：「无踰老臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147287_comment'></div>以是言之，则请令宰臣已下，各举堪为将帅者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147287_comment'></div>又令宿旧武臣素有闻望者，亦令自举，然后陛下详择而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147287_comment'></div>又赵充国既为将，宣帝遣问曰：「将军度羌虏如何，当用几人」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147287_comment'></div>充国曰：「百闻不如一见，兵难豫度，臣愿驰至金城，图上方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147287_comment'></div>然羌戎逆天背叛，灭亡不久，愿陛下以属老臣，勿以为忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147287_comment'></div>以是言之，昔充国为老将，尚谓百闻不如一见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147287_comment'></div>况今委任将帅，而每事欲从中降诏，授以方略，或赐与阵图，依从则有未合宜，专断则是违上旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147287_comment'></div>以此制胜，未见其长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147287_comment'></div>伏乞速命宰臣，令举良将，及令素有闻望宿旧武臣，自举其能，及举所知者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1147287'>一、将帅行恩信，恤士卒，必丰财货，方得士心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147287_comment'></div>昔赵奢为将，所得王之赏赐，尽与军吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147287_comment'></div>又李牧为将，军市之租，皆用享士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147287_comment'></div>魏尚守云中，其军市租尽以给士卒，出私养钱享宾客军吏，是以匈奴不近云中之塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147287_comment'></div>今国家所命将帅，虽古今异宜，凡有给赐，今则谁敢效古？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147287_comment'></div>散家财，赏士卒，去吝啬，有几何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147287_comment'></div>若以年年供亿挽运，老师费财，曷若厚给将帅，使之赏用也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147287_comment'></div>又闻近侯伯亦有厅直三五十人习骑射，为心腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147287_comment'></div>每出入阵敌，得以厅直随身，翼卫主帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147287_comment'></div>后来不敢养置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147287_comment'></div>昨来杨业陷阵，访闻亦是无自己腹心从人，护助捍御，以致为狄之所获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147287_comment'></div>今虽时异事殊，然废置利害，亦须询访行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1147287'>一、今之御戎，以沿边诸郡有勇智者命为刺史，委之自用方略，警急利便，事讫方奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147287_comment'></div>使人人各尽其才术，此必为陛下各立殊勋，控制侵侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147287_comment'></div>昔后汉郭伋为渔阳太守，时匈奴数抄郡界，边境苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147287_comment'></div>伋乃整饬士马，设攻守之略，匈奴畏惮，不敢入塞，人得安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147287_comment'></div>在职五岁，户口增倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147287_comment'></div>又张堪为骑都尉，破匈奴于高柳，拜渔阳太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147287_comment'></div>捕系奸猾，赏罚必信，人皆乐为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147287_comment'></div>匈奴以万骑入渔阳，堪乃率数千骑奔击，大破之，郡界以静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147287_comment'></div>乃于狐奴开稻田八千馀顷，劝人耕种，以致丰富，百姓歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147287_comment'></div>视事八年，匈奴不敢犯塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147287_comment'></div>以此言之，则沿边诸郡，请令择有智勇者为刺史，必副陛下之忧寄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1147287'>一、今之御戎，更在悦取军情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147287_comment'></div>凡经拣退，尚堪力役者，却与元本料钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147287_comment'></div>其殁阵及守戍死亡兵士，所有在营老幼，宜矜悯优恤，或给赐，令各存活，勿使寒饥，无所归向，又不可取充洒扫裁缝之隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147287_comment'></div>其次，拣中新招到军，虽稍有身首人才，未宜便令管辖旧人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147287_comment'></div>须是经历行阵，稍知军伍次第，微有劳效者，方令充节员，所贵已下亦各甘心，兼易为驱使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147287_comment'></div>若曾有功劳，未得优赏者，即乞别作名目，优异酬赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147287_comment'></div>臣未知朝廷府库钱帛之大数，亦不知国家支费用度之众寡，若陛下省罢塔庙之费耗，回充军旅之赏给，则孰不革其怨心，孰不致其死力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147287_comment'></div>若是破敌，必副陛下平戎之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1147287'>一、今之御戎，亦宜别设条例，等第立赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147287_comment'></div>若得一保垒，或复一障亭，与某官，与若干赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147287_comment'></div>赏不逾时，必诚必信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147287_comment'></div>条例不烦，令军中晓会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147287_comment'></div>此必有果敢智谋之士，副陛下之立赏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1147287'>一、今之御戎，又宜以重赏，召募敢死之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147287_comment'></div>仍以古来选士之科以取士，卒亦于军中择取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147287_comment'></div>应得选士之条目，今举其六七，更可详酌增损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147287_comment'></div>且据兵书言之：取曾习韬钤者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147287_comment'></div>有谋画者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147287_comment'></div>又取能知敌情伪者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147287_comment'></div>取能知山川险易、径路迂直者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147287_comment'></div>取强力过人，能斩虏搴旗者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147287_comment'></div>又取往复数百里，不及暮至者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147287_comment'></div>又取能破格舒钩，或负数百斤、行五十步者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147287_comment'></div>又取趫捷若飞，能逾堑垒，出入无形，堪窥觇者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147287_comment'></div>各区别技能，置立部分，以副将帅之指使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1147287'>一、今之御戎，外则委任将帅，内则询谋宰臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147287_comment'></div>行一事必使宰臣知之，出一诏必令宰臣议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147287_comment'></div>臣闻前年出师向北，命曹彬以下欲取幽州，是侯利用、贺令图之辈误惑圣聪，陈谋画策，而宰臣昉等不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147287_comment'></div>又去年招置义军，刺配军分，宰相普等亦不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147287_comment'></div>岂有议边陲，发师旅，而宰相不与闻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147287_comment'></div>若宰相非才，何不罢免？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147287_comment'></div>宰相可任，何不询谋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147287_comment'></div>今宰相普三入中书，再出蕃镇，重望硕德，元老大臣，人所具瞻，事无不历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147287_comment'></div>乞陛下以军旅之事，机密之谋，悉与筹量，尽其规画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147287_comment'></div>此乃国体，君父至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147287_comment'></div>臣闻偏信生奸，独任成乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147287_comment'></div>侯利用、贺令图等既误陛下机宜于前，无令似侯利用、贺令图者复误陛下机宜于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147287_comment'></div>伏乞陛下一一与宰臣谋议，事事与宰臣商量，悔自前独断之明，用今后公共之理，则事无不允当，下无不尽忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147287_comment'></div>则大臣之间，足以副陛下忧勤之旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_1147287'>一、今之御戎，凡召发兵士，或储般粮草，亦宜谨静，勿使喧烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147287_comment'></div>臣窃闻去年于户税上折科马草，及官中和买当买纳未足之间，即有使臣催督，贫下户妇女有行科校者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147287_comment'></div>又闻汴河乾浅，遂分南河水添注汴河，以待漕运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147287_comment'></div>国家计度何在，而临时一至于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147287_comment'></div>辇毂之下，岂无外国谍人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147287_comment'></div>臣即不知国家见在军储支得几年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147287_comment'></div>若是无九年之粮，实为无备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147287_comment'></div>若是无三年之粮，实为窘急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147287_comment'></div>若不窘急，则何以科校妇女而纳草、添注河水而待漕运也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_100_1147287'>一、今之御戎，在乎辨边上奏报之虚实，察左右蒙蔽之有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147287_comment'></div>奏失利则未必尽言，报大捷则不足深信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147287_comment'></div>陛下未当信而先信，陛下本欲知而未知，如此何以料安危，如此何以策成败？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147287_comment'></div>安危成败之理，乞陛下详而察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_104_1147287'>一、今之御戎，无先用谍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147287_comment'></div>兵书曰：事莫密于间，赏莫重于间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1147287_comment'></div>狄中自有诸国，未审陛下曾探得凡有几国否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1147287_comment'></div>几国与匈奴为仇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1147287_comment'></div>若悉知之，可以用重赏行间谍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1147287_comment'></div>间谍若行，则夷狄自乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1147287_comment'></div>夷狄自乱，则边鄙自宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1147287_comment'></div>昔李靖用间破突厥，心腹之人自离贰也，书在唐史，其事可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1147287_comment'></div>今募能往绝域，斗乱蕃部，使交相侵害，如汉之陈汤、傅介子之流，则不劳师徒，自然归化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1147287_comment'></div>此可以缓陛下忧边之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1147287_comment'></div>其馀谨烽火，明斥堠，亦可以依古法，为警备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1147287_comment'></div>《赵充国传》曰：「五星出东方，中国大利，蛮夷大败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1147287_comment'></div>太白出高，用兵深入，敢战者吉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1147287_comment'></div>虽天道远而难知，然昭昭垂象纬者，为陛下言兵之利害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_118_1147287'>一、今国家富有天下，精卒利兵，计有百万，然无将帅为陛下治兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1147287_comment'></div>昔吴起为将，为士卒吮痈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1147287_comment'></div>霍去病为将，汉帝欲为治第，去病曰：「匈奴未灭，何以家为」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1147287_comment'></div>窦婴为将，得所赐金千斤，陈于庑下，军吏过者辄量取为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1147287_comment'></div>未喻陛下以今之将帅，如吴起、霍去病否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1147287_comment'></div>若以臣所见，则将帅必无其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1147287_comment'></div>何以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1147287_comment'></div>将帅肯为士卒吮痈乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1147287_comment'></div>若赐第宅，肯不要乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1147287_comment'></div>将帅非材，即无威名，何以使匈奴望风而惧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1147287_comment'></div>今有居显位，食厚禄，为国之谋即不足，奉身之谋即有馀，何以副陛下致太平之心，何以致陛下成清净之理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1147287_comment'></div>然以臣所见，凡小小公事，不劳陛下一一用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1147287_comment'></div>若以社稷之大计，为子孙之远图，则在乎举大略，求将相，帝王之大体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1147287_comment'></div>设如人欲理身，先理心，心无邪则身自正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1147287_comment'></div>欲理外，先理内，内既理则外自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1147287_comment'></div>臣谓边上动，由朝廷动之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1147287_comment'></div>边上静，由朝廷静之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1147287_comment'></div>任贤相于内，则百职举而纪纲振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1147287_comment'></div>委良将于外，则四夷静而边鄙安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1147287_comment'></div>臣之愚衷，备于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1147287_comment'></div>已然之患，既陛下遍访直言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1147287_comment'></div>未然之虞，乞陛下常切留意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_140_1147287'>一、已上条奏，悉是国家已然之事，所以劳陛下谋及卿士，询于刍荛，凡百臣僚，悉陈所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1147287_comment'></div>然臣谓国家复有未然之事，得不为陛下言之，得不为陛下忧之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1147287_comment'></div>今戎主一姥而已，用黠虏为谋主，颇有轻中国之志，今春夏必渐退，秋冬必复来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1147287_comment'></div>制之御之，惟在前所筹数事而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1147287_comment'></div>若将来狄人御之而不去，边境备之而未宁，加以匈奴间谍于西蕃，汉家未断其右臂，即秦、陇千里之外，瓜、沙、玉关之西，恐非国家之所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1147287_comment'></div>万一兵歉相仍，寇盗多起，此时何以谋之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1147287_comment'></div>此时何以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1147287_comment'></div>圣人不能不灾，而能御灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1147287_comment'></div>今陛下圣德合天，三边无虞，万里晏然，居安思危之计，得不由未然之事而预防之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1147287_comment'></div>此亦御戎之远意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1147287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_150_1147287'>右臣备位掖垣，忝司诰命，祗奉睿旨，俾陈方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1147287_comment'></div>昧于时事，思虑不精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1147287_comment'></div>然于狂愚，庶或可采。</div><div id='poem_sentence_152_1147287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年8月</a>　八月，在京为知制诰，上疏谏止造开宝寺塔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年10月</a>　十月，在京为知制诰，奉旨至太一宫祈雨，上疏论旱灾。作品：上太宗论旱灾。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《宋朝诸臣奏议》卷三七。）</span><div id='poem_1147299' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147299' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147299?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论旱灾奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（端拱二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147299")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147299_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147299'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147299'>臣今奉敕差在太一宫，用青词文设醮行祈雨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147299_comment'></div>窃以时雨愆亢，圣虑焦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147299_comment'></div>自秋涉冬，诸寺及庙虽遍祠祷，未彰感通，以至陛下亲降乘舆，躬诣诸庙寺观，有以见仁主忧民之旨，圣人恤物之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147299_comment'></div>虽灾沴流行，何代蔑有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147299_comment'></div>而帑廪储积，可备不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147299_comment'></div>然自今岁以来，天见星祅，秋深雷震，继以旱暵之沴，可虞馑饥之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147299_comment'></div>此实阴阳失和，调燮倒置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147299_comment'></div>上侵下之职，而烛理未尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147299_comment'></div>下知上之失，而规过未能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147299_comment'></div>所以成兹咎徵，彰乎降鉴，或天文示变，或沴气生祅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147299_comment'></div>昨陛下以天垂谪告之文，御楼行赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147299_comment'></div>德音朝发，祅星夕消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147299_comment'></div>天不言而感报昭彰，神幽赞而应答遄速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147299_comment'></div>今以粟麦未种，甘雨未降，人心不宁，农望已失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147299_comment'></div>或闻小小寇盗，聚散靡常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147299_comment'></div>嗷嗷蒸黎，忧畏实甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147299_comment'></div>愆阳既盭于寒冱，厥疾乃生于疠疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147299_comment'></div>民或流亡，谷必翔贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147299_comment'></div>尚赖陛下圣德，宗庙庆灵，蠢尔獯戎，骚边稍息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147299_comment'></div>惠然诸国，底贡交修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147299_comment'></div>不然人心一摇，盗计斯得，何以静潢池弄兵之啸聚，何以御胡马南牧之奔冲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147299_comment'></div>惟是秋冬，久无雪雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147299_comment'></div>此乃天意尚欲垂戒，圣心谅亦深思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147299_comment'></div>岂刑系之间，尚未平允？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147299_comment'></div>法令之设，尚尔烦苛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147299_comment'></div>或力役未悉矜蠲，或奢靡未尽撙节？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147299_comment'></div>言路虽启，蹇谔者未必一一听从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147299_comment'></div>王道虽行，孤苦者未必人人受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147299_comment'></div>或刑赏过于常理，或喜怒失于厥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147299_comment'></div>嘉言纳忠，见破于横议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147299_comment'></div>任贤待下，或难于至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147299_comment'></div>若然，则虽旰食劳怀，宵衣轸念，孜孜万务，适足劳于圣躬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147299_comment'></div>翼翼小心，尚未臻于至化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147299_comment'></div>今举大略，上犯宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147299_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「王言如丝，其出如纶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147299_comment'></div>《书》曰：「慎乃出令，令出惟行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147299_comment'></div>今朝廷所言，或异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147299_comment'></div>谋始稍亏于审谨，令出无愧于改更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147299_comment'></div>以是知急速机务，宁无错行！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147299_comment'></div>臣之愚衷，岂敢逭于诛戮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147299_comment'></div>臣之遭遇，安忍负于圣明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147299_comment'></div>是以因事上言，庶裨万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147299_comment'></div>伏望陛下因此时旱，更降诏书，引咎责躬，以答天戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147299_comment'></div>进德覃庆，以安民心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147299_comment'></div>蠲减征徭，简约科禁，搜察淹滞，登进才良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147299_comment'></div>猛士守方，无使黜贤召怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147299_comment'></div>朝臣典郡，正宜选廉任能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147299_comment'></div>或旌别勤劳，或省阅浮泛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147299_comment'></div>振廪通货，以救饿殍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147299_comment'></div>加估收储，以备阙乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147299_comment'></div>蕃戎蹂践之处，士庶陷殁之家，哀亡恤存，悯其馀苦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147299_comment'></div>掩骼置奠，慰彼沉冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147299_comment'></div>闾里再命于复除，孤寡量优其给赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147299_comment'></div>俭约奉己以合礼，谨静息民以安边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147299_comment'></div>详延忠鲠之臣，询究灾祥之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147299_comment'></div>弭灾求理，正在此时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147299_comment'></div>变沴致祥，属当今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147299_comment'></div>若旱沴不已，岁歉相仍，盗聚苇蒲，伺隙而动，狄乘馑塞，幸灾为虞，是则国家之虑实深，朝廷之忧非浅也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1147299_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年12月27日</a>　十二月二十七日，罢知制诰，以户部郎中出知陈州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作王光图迁官制。作品：卫州卫县簿王光图可卫州司理。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147169' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147169' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147169?labeling=true' target='_blank'>卫州卫县簿王光图可卫州司理制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147169")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147169_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147169'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147169'>敕：具官王光图能以公才，往为邑佐，恭勤足以赞宰字，廉慎可以典狱刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147169_comment'></div>不离汲郡之寮，俾掌理官之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147169_comment'></div>当思尽瘁，无陷非辜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147169_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作李克文落起复制。作品：端州防御使李克文落起复依旧端州刺史充本州防御使。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端州防御使李克文落起复依旧端州刺史充本州防御使制</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_1147172'>敕：具官李克文，明于韬略，真以干能，弓箕克嗣于家声，符竹早隆于邦寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147172_comment'></div>顷因礼制，俾夺哀情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147172_comment'></div>洎丧纪以外除，茂朝章以斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147172_comment'></div>任当御侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147172_comment'></div>宠列颁条，眷惟高要之民，实伫抚临之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147172_comment'></div>勉膺嘉命，无替忠规。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147172_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作赵沂迁官制。作品：道州军事推官知长沙县赵沂可将作监丞。<span id='poem_sentence_1_1147175_comment'></div>涵濡郊祀之恩，翊赞官僚之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147175_comment'></div>宜膺庆赏，仍遂优荣。<div class='inline' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147180'>敕：金革从权，礼典既称于无避；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147180_comment'></div>苴麻易制，国恩宜茂于必行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147180_comment'></div>具官陈文颢器识淹深，才谟明允，著公侯之名节，彰竹素之勋劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147180_comment'></div>寄重圭符，尝布诏条之化；<div class='inline' target='_blank'>翰林图画待诏夏侯延祐可庐州巢县令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147189")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147189_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147189'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147189'>敕：具官夏侯延祐，早以艺能，列于禁署，每闻恭恪，克守官箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147189_comment'></div>可以命之亲民，观其莅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147189_comment'></div>遂尔上章之意，勿辜非次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147189_comment'></div>清廉可以保躬，畏慎所以无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147189_comment'></div>「绘事后素」，是为礼欤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147189_comment'></div>能达斯言，必善为政。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147189_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作高丽使者官员授官制。作品：高丽使副判官等授官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147190' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147190' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147190?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高丽使副判官等授官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147190")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147190_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147190'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147190'>敕：朕以推恩示信，覃声教于殊邻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147190_comment'></div>进秩书勋，赏勤劳于将命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147190_comment'></div>式表绥怀之德，用旌恭恪之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147190_comment'></div>具官某，远自辰韩，来朝象魏，涉沧波之万里，输职贡于九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147190_comment'></div>方物充庭，达帅臣之忠节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147190_comment'></div>华簪就列，有专介之礼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147190_comment'></div>言念使乎，宜加朝奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147190_comment'></div>或纡黻从大夫之后，或握兰参郎吏之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147190_comment'></div>勋级增荣，器名非假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147190_comment'></div>勉荷殊常之宠，无忘来远之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1147190_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作高丽使者职员军将授官制。作品：高丽职员军将等授官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147191' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147191' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147191?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高丽职员军将等授官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147191")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147191_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147191'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147191'>敕：具官某等，列外区之右职，达主帅之明诚，远涉沧溟，厎其方物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147191_comment'></div>载念恭勤之节，宜隆旌赏之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147191_comment'></div>宪府华资，储闱美秩，加以参六勋而示赏，表重险以怀来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147191_comment'></div>无忘训激之词，益励忠贞之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147191_comment'></div>勉膺凤綍，归耀鸡林。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147191_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作禁军将校授官制。作品：禁军将校授官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作钟文拯改官制。作品：前资州内江令钟文拯可黄州黄陂令。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147199' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147199' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147199?labeling=true' target='_blank'>前资州内江令钟文拯可黄州黄陂令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147199")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1147199_comment'></div>俾换阙员之命，式补选调之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147199_comment'></div>牛里黄陂，伫闻善政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147199_comment'></div>单车之任，廉干有声，咸俾吾民，实受尔赐，则将奖迁善职，无所吝焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147199_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作郑德明改官制。作品：吏部流外铨勒留官涿州固安簿郑德明可陈州项城簿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吏部流外铨勒留官涿州固安簿郑德明可陈州项城簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作王继荣、陶化成改官制。作品：耀州司法王继荣可邠州宜禄簿前耀州同官尉陶化成可耀州司法。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147202' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147202' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147202?labeling=true' target='_blank'>耀州司法王继荣可邠州宜禄簿前耀州同官尉陶化成可耀州司法制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147202")'>田锡</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_1147202'>敕具官王继荣、具官陶化成：一邑勾稽之任，六联掌法之能，苟非廉明，宁副奖用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147202_comment'></div>今以继荣佐邑理，命化成列掾曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147202_comment'></div>无忝予恩，勉恭尔职。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147202_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作方宁改官制。作品：前舒州太湖尉方宁可和州历阳令。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147203?labeling=true' target='_blank'>前舒州太湖尉方宁可和州历阳令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147203")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147203'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147203'>敕具官吕文仲举具官方宁：今历阳令阙员，方求廉平之吏，俾之抚绥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147203_comment'></div>而文仲称尔理行，是用命尔，往莅厥邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147203_comment'></div>苟三载考绩，课第颇高，是文仲不谬举人，而尔亦不误知己也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147203_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作吕覃起复制。作品：前大理评事吕覃可旧官。<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147204'>敕具官吕覃：孝为百行之本，礼有三年之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147204_comment'></div>尔居亲忧，既去厥职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147204_comment'></div>今除禫制，宜复旧官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147204_comment'></div>狱谳是思，朝章勉称，无忘聿修之训，更扬匪懈之名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147204_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作王九言改官制。作品：前夏州节度推官王九言可宋州观察支使。<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147205'>敕：具官王九言，早彰佐幕之才，能举鞠刑之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147205_comment'></div>秩满受代，课第可酬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147205_comment'></div>睢阳诏条，方藉参赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147205_comment'></div>勉荷甄升之异渥，用伸廉恪之政声。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147206'>敕：具官马守荣，早列班资，颇闻恭谨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147206_comment'></div>屡膺朝委，亦著劳能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147206_comment'></div>向公罔怠于夙宵，莅事足专于才识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147206_comment'></div>苟无劝赏，宁表旌酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147206_comment'></div>是用进阶秩于明庭，列职司于近务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147206_comment'></div>更观勤恪，式副甄升。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作刘永德等改官制。作品：如京副使刘永德可濠州团练副使崇仪副使刘永恭可颍州团练副使供奉官刘永和可武骑尉唐州长史。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147207?labeling=true' target='_blank'>如京副使刘永德可濠州团练副使崇仪副使刘永恭可颍州团练副使供奉官刘永和可武骑尉唐州长史制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147207")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147207'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147207'>敕：具官刘永德等，各荣使职，或列廷臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147207_comment'></div>事吾轩陛之间，虽经任用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147207_comment'></div>更尔内外之命，式示迁除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147207_comment'></div>贰车之荣，上佐之职，恪谨日守，循省勿忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147207_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作傅珏改官制。作品：大理寺法直官傅珏可庐州录事参军。<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147208'>敕：具官傅珏，精彼刑书，直于法寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147208_comment'></div>三载既周于考绩，六联宜示于陟明，用旌丹笔之劳，特茂紫泥之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147208_comment'></div>尔其表仪诸掾，纠正群司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147208_comment'></div>来效傥伸，叙迁宁吝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作张自明改官制。作品：卫尉寺丞张自明可右赞善大夫赐绯。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147209?labeling=true' target='_blank'>卫尉寺丞张自明可右赞善大夫赐绯制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147209")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147209'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147209'>敕：具官张自明，早以时才，列于通籍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147209_comment'></div>尝因左宦，寘彼京寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147209_comment'></div>闻兢慎之聿修，在奖升之可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147209_comment'></div>青宫命秩，茜绶采章，无忘若厉之诚，勉答惟新之宠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147209_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作李寿迁官制。作品：右赞善大夫知大理少卿李寿可秘书丞依前充职。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右赞善大夫知大理少卿李寿可秘书丞依前充职制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147210")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147210'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147210'>敕：朝廷以法律委廉平之士，以爵秩赏劳效之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147210_comment'></div>茂绩既彰，明恩岂吝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147210_comment'></div>以尔具官李寿，参亚寺卿之职，详明邦宪之微，课最宜旌，封章自达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147210_comment'></div>俾陟图书之府，以奖前劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147210_comment'></div>勉膺纶綍之恩，且仍旧贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147210_comment'></div>更体哀矜之旨，勿渝明慎之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147210_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作韩励己、王崇吉授官制。作品：追官人韩励己可青州临淄簿勒停人王崇吉可建州建阳簿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追官人韩励己可青州临淄簿勒停人王崇吉可建州建阳簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147211")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147211'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147211'>敕：具官韩励己等，早历官途，尝因公过，既闻修省，宜复迁升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147211_comment'></div>各膺佐邑之荣，勉赞字人之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147211_comment'></div>无忝兹授，俾饰自新。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147211_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作宗文式授官制。作品：除名人宗文式可东岳庙主簿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147212?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除名人宗文式可东岳庙主簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147212")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147212'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147212'>敕：除名人宗文式，虽效官常，有亏家检，抵律既从于除免，涤瑕宜示于甄升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147212_comment'></div>祗命严祠，无忝勾稽之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147212_comment'></div>荣名官路，更虔如在之诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147212_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作李处耘赠官制。作品：故淄州刺史累赠太子太师李处耘可赠侍中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故淄州刺史累赠太子太师李处耘可赠侍中制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147213")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147213_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147213'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147213'>敕：国家褒赠之恩，臣子哀荣之典，式昭故实，可举而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147213_comment'></div>故具官李处耘，忠亮事君，韬钤立节，既荷葭莩之宠，宜增漏壤之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147213_comment'></div>矧堂构之上言，冀琰词之饰宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147213_comment'></div>俾列珥貂之贵，追酬露冕之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147213_comment'></div>贞魂有知，可膺贲赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147213_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作郭文集授官制。作品：勒停人郭文集可邢州平乡令。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>勒停人郭文集可邢州平乡令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147214")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1147214_comment'></div>涤瑕宜示于恩荣，出綍俾新于邑理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147214_comment'></div>勉膺嘉命，以补前非。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作吴衡等授官制。作品：追官人吴衡可密州安丘令停官人陈吉甫可陈州商水尉刘鼎可晋州汾西簿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147215?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追官人吴衡可密州安丘令停官人陈吉甫可陈州商水尉刘鼎可晋州汾西簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147215")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147215'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147215'>敕：具官吴衡等，各因遗旷，追削官资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147215_comment'></div>既推含垢之恩，宜复惟新之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147215_comment'></div>或升宰字，或掌勾稽，当补过以省循，副尽公于录用。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147215_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作李昭嘏改官制。作品：相州永定令李昭嘏可濮州鄄城令。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147216?labeling=true' target='_blank'>相州永定令李昭嘏可濮州鄄城令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147216")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147216_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147216'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147216'>敕：具官李昭嘏，临莅邑政，颇著廉能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147216_comment'></div>部送军储，尝闻了办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147216_comment'></div>洎繁难之试可，亦勤干以足称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147216_comment'></div>既召对于轩墀，宜践更于铜墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147216_comment'></div>抚绥劝课，称兹宠荣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147216_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作朱允元授官制。作品：赐中丞知贵州朱允元可国子博士。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐中丞知贵州朱允元可国子博士制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147219")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147219'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147219'>敕具官朱允元：南海列郡，贵为冲要之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147219_comment'></div>尔昔颁诏条，分忧寄，而廉干之外，方略用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147219_comment'></div>尝与转输，掩捕寇贼，溪洞既闻于静谧，裤襦谅蔼于声光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147219_comment'></div>茍无旌酬，宁示奖劝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147219_comment'></div>是用升尔为学官之秩，亦表吾通籍之间，有能副予委任，可以为边吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147219_comment'></div>勉膺宠命，无替始终。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147219_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作源护迁官制。作品：司门郎中知福州源护可兵部郎中依前知州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147220' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147220' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147220?labeling=true' target='_blank'>司门郎中知福州源护可兵部郎中依前知州制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147220")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147220_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147220'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147220'>敕：朝廷命南宫郎分吾忧寄，而荐历繁剧，以课第上闻者，得不特隆异奖，超授名曹，以劝赏焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147220_comment'></div>具官源护，早践周行，素彰公干，所至为理，雅有政声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147220_comment'></div>方兹念劳，懋其成绩，会以章奏，达于听闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147220_comment'></div>予于宠荣，固无所吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147220_comment'></div>是用命尔为司戎大夫，在郎署间实为华显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147220_comment'></div>东冶名郡，勉布诏条，无怠初终，伫聆殊效。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147220_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作石保兴落起复制。作品：起复如京使顺州团练使石保兴可落起复加金紫光禄大夫依旧官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147221' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147221' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147221?labeling=true' target='_blank'>起复如京使顺州团练使石保兴可落起复加金紫光禄大夫依旧官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147221")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147221_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147221'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147221'>敕：内列近司，外分忧寄，委任之恩斯茂，旌酬之命宜隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147221_comment'></div>具官石保兴，忠谅存诚，恭谦得礼，克嗣弓箕之业，颇知钤略之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147221_comment'></div>宠之以剖符，荣之以练武，而能敏于莅事，勤以奉公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147221_comment'></div>于贵介诸子之间，无简傲骄人之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147221_comment'></div>尝因在疚，爰举夺情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147221_comment'></div>既终制以加恩，必进阶以懋宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147221_comment'></div>勉荷惟新之泽，无忘尽瘁之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147221_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作张崇敏、康廷弼授官制。作品：界归明人张崇敏张廷弼可将军。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>界归明人张崇敏康廷弼可将军制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147222")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147222'>敕具官张崇敏：朕以环列之尹，翼卫之班，苟非忠贞，宁称甄奖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147222_comment'></div>以尔名彰毅勇，识蕴变通，尝受职于虏廷，愿输忠于魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147222_comment'></div>驰驱入塞，既倾葵藿之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147222_comment'></div>优异推恩，宜濡云天之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147222_comment'></div>拱宸峻秩，爪牙之寄攸亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147222_comment'></div>事主良规，金石之识益固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147222_comment'></div>勉膺嘉命，弥励匪躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147222_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1147222'>敕：康廷弼，志禀忠良，心明逆顺，耻列酋渠之职，来归礼义之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147222_comment'></div>臣节可嘉，予恩岂吝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147222_comment'></div>是用置于拱环之秩，总诸交戟之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147222_comment'></div>赏尔勤劳，袭朝廷之冠盖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147222_comment'></div>表吾宠异，参宸极之爪牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147222_comment'></div>勉思尽瘁于夙宵，无忝殊常之渥泽<span class='inlineComment2'>（《咸平集》卷二八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147222_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1147222'>「界」上疑有脱字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1147222_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作陈文广、林思问改官制。作品：前果州西充尉陈文广可陈州南顿令前秦州清水尉林思问可耀州华原令。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147223' class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147223")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147223_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147223'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147223'>敕具官某等：民乃朕之赤子，尔为朕之命官，念黎庶之是亲，实惨舒之攸系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147223_comment'></div>以尔尉司罢秩，俱闻捕获之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147223_comment'></div>宰邑阙员，命布清廉之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147223_comment'></div>勉思恭慎，以答恩荣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147223_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作李涉授官制。作品：习进士李涉可宛丘簿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147224' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147224' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147224?labeling=true' target='_blank'>习进士李涉可宛丘簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147224")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147224_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147224'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147224'>敕：李涉文艺饰身，进修为业，虽月桂未题于金榜，而县花宜佐于铜章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147224_comment'></div>仍以尔父居枢近之司，有义方之训，试尔公干，列于官途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147224_comment'></div>勉赞亲民，勿忝殊渥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147224_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作党待问改官制。作品：大名府参军党待问可郓州卢县簿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147225' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147225' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147225?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大名府参军党待问可郓州卢县簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147225")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147225_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147225'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147225'>敕：具官党待问，早居官序，颇历公途，俾伸莅事之才，往佐亲民之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147225_comment'></div>恪勤自励，甄录斯酬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1147225_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作刘泽改官制。作品：陈州参军刘泽可光州司理判官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈州参军刘泽可光州司理判官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147227")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147227'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147227'>敕：具官刘泽，移易更员，佐理刑狱，既资廉干，俾无滞留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147227_comment'></div>尔方自乞于效官，予即命之以莅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147227_comment'></div>勿孤奖擢，更励恪勤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作赵日用授官制。作品：敕赐同学究出身赵日用可徐州彭城主簿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕赐同学究出身赵日用可徐州彭城主簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147228'>敕具官赵日用：以尔兄作掾饶阳，殁于王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147228_comment'></div>存亡之念，良所嗟称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147228_comment'></div>昆仲之间，宜加甄录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147228_comment'></div>佐邑为理，莅事效官，慎守廉勤，以酬奖擢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147228_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作宋可观改官制。作品：许州司法宋可观可许州司理。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147229' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147229' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147229?labeling=true' target='_blank'>许州司法宋可观可许州司理制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147229'>敕具官宋可观：尔事郡为司法掾，而长吏选擢，可典狱刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147229_comment'></div>无以丹笔之重轻，而侮黄沙之鞠效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147229_comment'></div>往践厥职，勿累知人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147229_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作朱泽迁官制。作品：将作监丞朱泽可右赞善大夫。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147231?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将作监丞朱泽可右赞善大夫制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147231")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147231_comment'></div>可茂劳能之赏，用彰旌陟之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147231_comment'></div>勉祗命于储闱，冀增荣于闺籍。</div><div target='_blank'>庐州慎县尉卢显忠可庐州合淝令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147232'>敕：具官卢显忠，格令近条，全火获贼，殊其考课，旌以劳能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147232_comment'></div>尔效官既著于廉勤，举职颇闻于屏肃，宜更黄绶，俾佩铜章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147232_comment'></div>尔其惠恤茕嫠，敦励风俗，使农桑知劝，而舆赋及期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147232_comment'></div>当议奖升，勿忘终始。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1147234_comment'></div>勉守官箴，勿辜朝奖。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作褚德臻改官制。作品：襄州邓城尉权知榖城县事褚德臻可榖城令。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1147235' class='_poem'><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147243_comment'></div>傥能砥砺，别议恩荣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_1147244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追官人高绅等授官制</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1147244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147244'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147244'>敕：追官人高绅等，各因谴累，追削官资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147244_comment'></div>既当覃庆之时，宜霈惟新之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147244_comment'></div>廷评理掾，礼寺京寮，勉励在公，思补前过。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作冯源改官制。作品：洪州观察推官冯源可永清军书记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147245?labeling=true'
