class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147245_comment'></div>傥副知己，宁吝加恩？</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1147245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作路表正改官制。作品：汝州团练推官前知绛州太平县事路表正可河南府推官。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147246' class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147281")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147281'>敕：朝廷设谏诤之臣，举箴规之职，虽云慎选，实在无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147281_comment'></div>何以？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147281_comment'></div>忠谠在乎人，而用舍由乎上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147281_comment'></div>或直言未当，或敢谏不从，徒为备员，适谓虚器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147281_comment'></div>以尔某素有文学，颇历官常，效用以来，声尘有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147281_comment'></div>观其风度之淹雅，赜其理行之贞方，是用升于谏垣，列为近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147281_comment'></div>《六典》谓事之大者庭诤，事之小者上封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147281_comment'></div>尔无越思，靖恭斯职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147281_comment'></div>尔无养望，或忝厥官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147281_comment'></div>伫闻蹇谔之名，称我清华之选。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1147281_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在京为知制诰，作《幕职州县官料钱敕》作品：幕职州县官料钱敕。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147282' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147282' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147282?labeling=true' target='_blank'>幕职州县官料钱敕</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147282")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147282_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147282'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147282'>敕：王者设官分职，求才任能，俾庶绩以允釐，即黎元之受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147282_comment'></div>然责其廉则丰其禄，督其理则足其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147282_comment'></div>朕自临御以来，十有四载，或亲民之吏，或佐幕之寮，观其考课之间，悉乃廉平之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147282_comment'></div>茍不均其资俸，何以绝其顗觎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147282_comment'></div>自来应幕职、州县官料钱，皆一分见钱，二分折色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147282_comment'></div>今有司建议，事贵酌中，宜令今后中停支与见钱，一半支与折色，俾令稍足，更励向公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147282_comment'></div>凡尔庶寮，勉荷优渥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147282_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='533cbd55dd824056b1edda62f595f5ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("533cbd55dd824056b1edda62f595f5ce");'><span id='533cbd55dd824056b1edda62f595f5ce_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=997')">994-997年</a>，55-58岁</div><div id='533cbd55dd824056b1edda62f595f5ce' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　春，在京，除工部员外郎，有谢表。作品：谢特授工部员外郎表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。据《咸平集》卷二四《谢特授工部员外郎表》和卷二七《乞住涟水军寄居》，田锡未赴单州，其授工部员外郎时已在东京。）</span><div id='poem_1147339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢特授工部员外郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（994年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147339")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147339'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147339'>臣锡言：臣今月二十六日，蒙恩特授工部员外郎，为无例于崇政殿告谢，寻于二十七日谢恩讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147339_comment'></div>臣伏睹台司引见左降官凡百馀人，唯臣独授官资，复齿班列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147339_comment'></div>循省荣惧，不知所裁<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147339_comment'></div>臣伏以受恩特深，叙感亦切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147339_comment'></div>苟不披露肝鬲，敷陈始终，则何以表圣人特达之恩，何以见微臣遭逢之幸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147339_comment'></div>伏念臣禀受之性，愚直自知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147339_comment'></div>遐远之人，孤危自奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147339_comment'></div>遇陛下肇登宝位，亲主文衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147339_comment'></div>臣词艺非长，器能无取，轩墀之下，赐以策名，科第之中，复在殊级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147339_comment'></div>扬历官序，便居侍从之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147339_comment'></div>临莅公途，常守廉勤之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147339_comment'></div>此外不忘笔砚，载成咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147339_comment'></div>始因进《升平词》，擢为谏官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147339_comment'></div>后因上《封禅书》，令知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147339_comment'></div>迁授非次，报答无由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147339_comment'></div>是以有所见闻，辄形章疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147339_comment'></div>靡详事理，屡贡刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147339_comment'></div>臣子之心，唯思谠切；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147339_comment'></div>君亲之意，不罪狂愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147339_comment'></div>陛下所以赐臣奖喻敕书，欲广上言之路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147339_comment'></div>陛下因臣特降御劄，旁求敢谏之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147339_comment'></div>德至明而无不照临，道至大而无不包纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147339_comment'></div>臣又尝因圣节，辄贡芜词，蒙陛下怡天眷而优容，降宸章以宣和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147339_comment'></div>臣又尝因时雪辄进歌行，珠旒亦赐于披观，金口曾垂于嗟赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147339_comment'></div>臣至愚至陋，无艺无能，有如此徼荣，有如此遭遇，虽杀身无补于万一，而过分宁免于颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147339_comment'></div>洎阁下改官，淮阳典郡，素无政术，但守诏条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147339_comment'></div>然京辅之间，豪猾难理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147339_comment'></div>州郡之职，智虑不周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147339_comment'></div>负陛下拔擢之恩，孤陛下忧勤之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147339_comment'></div>致有公过，上烦圣聪，每思受恩既异于常伦，受责亦宜于加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147339_comment'></div>陛下尚宽朝典，俾副戎车，不踰年逢赦量移，未周岁抽归引见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147339_comment'></div>臣得生还帝里，获面天颜，庆幸已多，私愿已适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147339_comment'></div>岂期圣造复置周行，自众多罪人之中，授清华外郎之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147339_comment'></div>拜官之后，受命以来，夙夜省循，俯仰惭惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147339_comment'></div>感君恩之特异，倍激私诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147339_comment'></div>虑公道之或亏，实忧官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147339_comment'></div>将何名节，用赎疏遗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147339_comment'></div>敢不遵临深履薄之言，守补过尽忠之训？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147339_comment'></div>冀伸微效，上答鸿私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1147339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　春，在京，除工部员外郎，有致谢笏记。作品：谢除工部员外郎笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147353?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢工部员外郎笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（994年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147353")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147353_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147353'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147353'>臣锡言：伏念圣慈赐臣官告一通，敕牒一道，特授臣工部员外郎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147353_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147353_comment'></div>伏念臣素乏时才，谬分忧寄，爰因公过，出佐方州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147353_comment'></div>未逾年逢赦量移，未周岁蒙恩引见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147353_comment'></div>自循过咎，敢望恩劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147353_comment'></div>岂谓圣造矜容，宸慈光被，俾归郎署，复齿班行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147353_comment'></div>敢不进思尽忠，退思补过，上答乾坤之施，用明砥砺之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147353_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年8月</a>　八月，在京为工部员外郎，上疏论时政。作品：论时政奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八六。）</span><div id='poem_1147300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论时政奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳化五年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147300")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147300'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147300'>臣伏闻去岁或霖潦作沴，或疠疫为灾，陛下忧劳太切，勤俭过中，乃至进菲薄之膳羞，御补浣之服饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147300_comment'></div>又复发廪减储，以饘济众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147300_comment'></div>损民抑理，以粟爵人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147300_comment'></div>今闻自迩及遐，被原带隰，秋稼大稔，流庸复归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147300_comment'></div>茍非英圣之至诚，岂致丰年之上瑞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147300_comment'></div>所虑者，河西尚警，剑外未宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147300_comment'></div>此则天机制御之时，睿圣绥怀之际，固大臣之与议，岂微臣之敢知！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147300_comment'></div>惟闻静以徐清，即时底定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147300_comment'></div>动无遗策，不日乂宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147300_comment'></div>若以民间利病，臣不尽知，时政阙失，臣不备见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147300_comment'></div>所思者唯制科可设，乡饮可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147300_comment'></div>制科设，则贤良方正之人得伸其志，直言敢谏之士得罄其怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147300_comment'></div>乡饮行，则孝悌之行自修，淳厚之风自复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147300_comment'></div>储闱建后，用光主鬯之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147300_comment'></div>王府设官，宜制正名之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147300_comment'></div>馆殿之职，可补吏员；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147300_comment'></div>枢近之司，亦委编录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147300_comment'></div>其次讲求典礼，更访诸儒，优恤蒸黎，可询群彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147300_comment'></div>冬年可以立仗，俾仪卫之式瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147300_comment'></div>雨雪可以放朝，冀礼容之允肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147300_comment'></div>邦国庠序，兴复宜先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147300_comment'></div>州郡城池，增修亦便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147300_comment'></div>常平之廪，因稔加储；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147300_comment'></div>底贡之财，因时立制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147300_comment'></div>或为民祈谷，耕于藉田；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147300_comment'></div>或齿胄尊儒，行之国学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147300_comment'></div>征税宽则与民偕足，法令简则俾人易从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147300_comment'></div>抑臣闻君子恐惧于所未闻，戒谨于所未至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147300_comment'></div>故未萌者所以易虑，未兆者所以易谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147300_comment'></div>谋于外则先靖于中，制于远则当思于近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147300_comment'></div>雈蒲聚啸，既劳我师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147300_comment'></div>沙漠乘秋，复窥王略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147300_comment'></div>师老则民力重困，寇玩则狡心必萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147300_comment'></div>今河、湟委输，方牵国用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147300_comment'></div>井络凋弊，实轸宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147300_comment'></div>安之既在于睿谋，讨之亦劳于神算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147300_comment'></div>夫理丝而棼之则愈乱，烹鲜而扰之则靡全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147300_comment'></div>御众以宽，惟新圣德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147300_comment'></div>临下以简，素在帝心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147300_comment'></div>臣之至愚，但思报国，臣之寡识，安能合时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147300_comment'></div>管窥之辞，庸以塞诏，刍言之拙，仰冀留中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1147300_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　本年，在京为工部员外郎，上奏状乞直馆。作品：乞直馆。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞直馆状</a><span class='authorDate'>（994年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147399")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147399'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147399'>右，臣辄披丹恳，上黩宸严，进退忧虞，难逃罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147399_comment'></div>寠贫困迫，须至敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147399_comment'></div>伏念臣遭逢盛时，际会英主，谬因文学，误受圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147399_comment'></div>尘忝既深，骤列演纶之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147399_comment'></div>劳能莫展，岂伸报国之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147399_comment'></div>迨至授以正郎，委之近郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147399_comment'></div>时才闇懦，有孤委任之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147399_comment'></div>公过谪迁，旋遇庞鸿之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147399_comment'></div>洎归丹阙，复赏通班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147399_comment'></div>尸禄旷官，弥深惕惧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147399_comment'></div>陈力就列，将赎贪叨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147399_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈，俯垂照亮，念臣曾备员于东观，尝寓直于西垣，愿伸撰述之微劳，上纪文明之盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147399_comment'></div>干冒旒扆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1147399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>　本年，在京为工部员外郎，诏直集贤院，有致谢笏记。作品：谢直集贤院笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147354' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147354' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147354?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢直集贤院笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（994年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147354")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147354_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147354'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147354'>臣锡言：伏蒙圣慈赐臣敕牒一道，令直集贤院者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147354_comment'></div>祗膺荣命，感惧交并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147354_comment'></div>伏念臣学识才能，不偕时彦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147354_comment'></div>华资显职，屡忝恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147354_comment'></div>未伸微劳，复沾殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147354_comment'></div>金殿集仙之职，玉陛近侍之荣，内省庸虚，益惭尸素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147354_comment'></div>敢不服勤儒行，砥砺臣诚，上酬覆载之恩，永报照临之德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147354_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=995&endYear=995')">995年</a>　本年，在京为工部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=996&endYear=996')">996年1月</a>　正月，在京为工部员外郎，复户部郎中，有致谢笏记。作品：谢复户部郎中笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢复户部郎中笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（996年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147355")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147355'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147355'>臣锡言：伏蒙圣慈赐臣官告、敕牒，授前件官，依前充职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147355_comment'></div>祗膺宠命，感惧交并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147355_comment'></div>伏以庆赐方行，殊私骤及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147355_comment'></div>郎曹念旧，既承牵复之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147355_comment'></div>帝泽惟新，实系遭逢之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147355_comment'></div>伏念臣器能无取，文学非优，早扬历于清华，每兢惭于尸素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147355_comment'></div>岂期圣造，擢置荣班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147355_comment'></div>复五品之华资，益知忝冒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147355_comment'></div>乐千年之景运，弥觉光荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147355_comment'></div>唯勤忠恪之诚，上报照临之德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1147355_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=996&endYear=996')">996年1月</a>　正月，在京为户部郎中，有谢皇太子笏记。作品：谢皇太子笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢皇太子笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（996年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147356")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147356'>臣蒙恩授户部郎中，仍旧直集贤院充职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147356_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147356_comment'></div>伏念锡素无才识，早玷官常，爰当庆赐之辰，复荷优隆之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147356_comment'></div>此皆伏蒙皇太子鸿私广被，睿德无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147356_comment'></div>致粉署之殊荣，爰升贱品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147356_comment'></div>荷储闱之大造，徒激微诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147356_comment'></div>永励恪勤，上酬覆焘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147356_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年1月</a>　正月，在京为户部郎中，代李惟清作让表。作品：代李给事惟清让密地表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1147340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李给事惟清让密地表</a><span class='authorDate'>（997年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147340")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147340'>臣某言：今月日，伏蒙圣慈赐臣官告、敕牒，以本官同签署枢密院公事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147340_comment'></div>丝纶之命，恩出非常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147340_comment'></div>枢务之荣，任当不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147340_comment'></div>循涯增惕，闻宠若惊<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147340_comment'></div>臣闻天高听卑，陈力就列，古既存诸方策，今得敷为让章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147340_comment'></div>窃以臣本诸生，素非奇士，偶读书史，遂玷科名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147340_comment'></div>遭逢盛时，骤居清列，才能无取，器业无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147340_comment'></div>历官以来，微效蔑有，常忧陨越，每诫满盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147340_comment'></div>而陛下擢于流品之中，置诸华显之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147340_comment'></div>升为大谏，谠言无补于清朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147340_comment'></div>迁拜冬郎，驳奏岂伸于厥职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147340_comment'></div>才微任重，既而罢钱谷之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147340_comment'></div>责浅恩宽，尚命以藩宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147340_comment'></div>番禺重地，交广要冲，上奉诏条，外抚荒服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147340_comment'></div>敷宣朝旨，遵守官箴，饮冰洁于诚心，食檗苦其清节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147340_comment'></div>洎改转输之命，惭非干济之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147340_comment'></div>三年海滨，偶免遗旷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147340_comment'></div>千里阙下，仰恋圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147340_comment'></div>诏书爰来，冕旒入觐，未踰月复其官秩，不浃旬授此恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147340_comment'></div>兢惶失图，宠用过分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147340_comment'></div>盖深严之地，近密之谋，非臣颛蒙，所能负荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147340_comment'></div>况今提封万里，守在四夷，帷幄之谋，军国之务，英主裁断，近臣佥同，臣也何人，敢言是选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147340_comment'></div>伏乞陛下特回成命，俯亮愚衷，别择才能，以裨任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147340_comment'></div>则微臣有妨贤之责，敢不罄陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147340_comment'></div>陛下垂则哲之明，必俞所让。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1147340_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年4月</a>　四月，在京为户部郎中，迁吏部郎中，有致谢笏记。作品：谢改吏部郎中依前直馆笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢改吏部郎中依前直馆笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（997年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147357")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147357'>臣锡等言：伏蒙圣慈各赐官告、敕牒，蒙恩除吏部郎中，仍旧充职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147357_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147357_comment'></div>窃念臣等器能无取，文学非优，遭逢既自于先朝，扬历骤升于清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147357_comment'></div>或纶闱效职，或史阁策名，但贻尸素之讥，未展涓埃之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147357_comment'></div>今伏遇陛下嗣登宝位，光启鸿图，普覃雨露之恩，仰荷云天之泽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1147357_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='897c91c05dcf46e8a4f18b35d4a3061e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("897c91c05dcf46e8a4f18b35d4a3061e");'><span id='897c91c05dcf46e8a4f18b35d4a3061e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=998')">997-998年</a>，58-59岁</div><div id='897c91c05dcf46e8a4f18b35d4a3061e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年7月25日</a>　七月二十五日，在京为吏部郎中，上疏论河西力役。作品：论安关辅奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八六。）</span><div id='poem_1147301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论安关辅奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（真宗至道三年七月二十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（997年7月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147301")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147301'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147301'>陛下临御以来，观庶政以仁，接大臣以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147301_comment'></div>闻奏山陵诸事，必泫然流涕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147301_comment'></div>闻奏灵州往事，必恻然动容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147301_comment'></div>圣智渊深，临事能断；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147301_comment'></div>睿机神速，驭下以宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147301_comment'></div>济之以严明，小人屏退而敛迹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147301_comment'></div>博之以询访，大臣畏爱而推诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147301_comment'></div>臣未见时政之是非，亦未见人君之过失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147301_comment'></div>若军旅措置之宜，非臣所能知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147301_comment'></div>若黎民利害之本，微臣辄敢议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147301_comment'></div>民之利莫先于省征徭、宽赋役，民之害莫大于用兵甲、挽刍粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147301_comment'></div>利害有大小，康济有先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147301_comment'></div>今利害之大者无先于舍灵武，康济之先者莫重于安关辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147301_comment'></div>舍灵武则甲兵不兴，甲兵不兴则挽运自息，挽运既息则关辅必宁，关辅既宁则四方无虞，四方无虞则四夷无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147301_comment'></div>臣今所忧者，关西二十五州军，昨经灵武之役，不胜困弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147301_comment'></div>加以时雨稍愆，秋田失种，府库未实，仓廪尚虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147301_comment'></div>若西戎辄敢骚边，北狄忽来犯塞，则朝廷何以备之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147301_comment'></div>关辅何以宁之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147301_comment'></div>臣虞此患必生，臣谓此灾必有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147301_comment'></div>何以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147301_comment'></div>臣窃闻去年九月十九日未时，永兴、环州、庆州、延州、清远军、隰州，同日同时六处地震，塌损城墙，毁坏庐舍，在处州府不敢不奏，所属转运不敢不申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147301_comment'></div>洎灵州送粮草回来，死者十有馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147301_comment'></div>议者即云地震已应于此，臣则未以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147301_comment'></div>夫天垂象动而不息，地生物静以为常，茍当静而动，是失其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147301_comment'></div>若永兴、环、延、庆、隰、清远军六处地震，臣亦窃见报状，延州路祗候、冬官正杨文镒奏称其月是戌月，又是戌日未时，自北上来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147301_comment'></div>臣以为当静而动，动之方位既在关辅，将来虑至戌年，岂无在下者辄动乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147301_comment'></div>关辅若有寇盗弄兵，雈苻聚啸，跨连州郡，僭称王公，则臣虑西川复保剑关之危，南方复恃重江之险，闽中、越中、淮南、湖南岂无见利忘义之人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147301_comment'></div>岂无幸灾乘便之者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147301_comment'></div>愿陛下思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147301_comment'></div>禳此灾者在修德，除此患者在早图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147301_comment'></div>德之修者，以诚信感神明，以言行动天地，以简易理机务，以清静安黎元；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147301_comment'></div>图于早者，减关市之征，放筦榷之利，蠲减租赋，优复流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147301_comment'></div>乡闾与人为害者，募之入军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147301_comment'></div>郡县在官未理者，命之移任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147301_comment'></div>设制科，使怀才抱器者悉为朝廷所用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147301_comment'></div>置屯田，俾弃本竞末者尽为户籍所收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147301_comment'></div>铸农器以结之，储时种以贷之，免五年之租徵，冀十年之生聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147301_comment'></div>如此纾民，民无不安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147301_comment'></div>如此安民，民无不泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147301_comment'></div>《管子》曰：「仓廪实，知礼节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147301_comment'></div>衣食足，知荣辱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147301_comment'></div>既知礼节，又知荣辱，则岂敢为寇盗，岂敢犯禁令！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147301_comment'></div>禁令既不敢犯，寇盗必不敢为，又何忧啸聚之虞，又何虑侵扰之患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147301_comment'></div>此置屯田，其利一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147301_comment'></div>制举科目，不可具陈，今略举可设者：有贤良方正能直言极谏科，才识兼茂明于体用科，道侔伊吕才比管乐科，传道经典达于教化科，详明政术可以理人科，文堪经邦科，武足安边科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147301_comment'></div>臣伏睹太祖朝曾设制科，于时敕限三千字已上成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147301_comment'></div>字数既多，书写不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147301_comment'></div>赐食之后，就试以来，既对天颜，岂无兢惧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147301_comment'></div>又值日晚，固不遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147301_comment'></div>虽有经邦之谋，岂能周悉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147301_comment'></div>虽有安边之策，靡暇敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147301_comment'></div>今若设此科条，但用汉时公孙弘、董仲舒所试之法，则往复问答，既尽见其才谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147301_comment'></div>品藻甄升，信无遗于器业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147301_comment'></div>此设制科，其利二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147301_comment'></div>与人为害者，募之入军，则乡闾静谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147301_comment'></div>在官未理者，命之移任，则臧否详明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147301_comment'></div>税赋蠲减，则民稍苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147301_comment'></div>流亡优复，则民不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147301_comment'></div>放筦榷之利，则米麦可充于边备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147301_comment'></div>减关市之征，则商旅交通于万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147301_comment'></div>暂如此五年，则关辅之民必安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147301_comment'></div>暂如此十年，则灵武之役必息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147301_comment'></div>若以此下主者，若以是问有司，必以臣不达时机，必以臣不谙世务，必以臣只知蠲减赋税以息黎元，而不知供军日费之多少，必以臣只知除放筦榷以安疲俗，而不知岁计备边之盈虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147301_comment'></div>臣岂不知沿边有屯兵，岂不知备边须积粟，岂不知岁时衣裘之赐锡，岂不知将卒酬赏之颁宣，岂不知上供京师之货财，岂不知量留州郡之物色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147301_comment'></div>然以臣所见，则帝王所务，当务广大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147301_comment'></div>官吏所守，各守职司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147301_comment'></div>所职为主计之臣，不得不聚敛供亿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147301_comment'></div>所司在主计之职，不得不经度有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147301_comment'></div>然天生时而地生财，下用力而上节用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147301_comment'></div>时不可失，故授时劝农，使不失时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147301_comment'></div>财生有数，故务穑劝分，使不乏用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147301_comment'></div>财之生也有数，上之用也有节，则民力不困，国用常丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147301_comment'></div>今未喻国家有九年之蓄乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147301_comment'></div>未喻西北隅边郡有六年之蓄乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147301_comment'></div>未喻陕西二十五州军有三年之蓄乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147301_comment'></div>访闻籴麦籴谷，以充折变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147301_comment'></div>将无作有，以应供输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147301_comment'></div>谓供输不得不然，不然则军储无备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147301_comment'></div>谓折变不得不然，不然则军食不充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147301_comment'></div>若如是，可见陕西二十五州军无三年之蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147301_comment'></div>加以民忧再送灵州粮草，臣虑变故从此生，臣忧祸乱从此起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147301_comment'></div>变故未生，陛下得不虑之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147301_comment'></div>祸难未起，陛下得不思之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147301_comment'></div>若以灵州送粮草之人，死者十馀万，已应地震之灾，即国家昨已降敕榜抚谕轸恤也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147301_comment'></div>若未应地震之灾，则臣虑变故起于关辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147301_comment'></div>关辅既有变生，则西川上供钱帛恐未能上供，南北常贡物货亦未得常贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147301_comment'></div>上供既有阻，常贡复未来，乃是国家只知督责关辅之货财，只知供备灵武之粮草，是急小利而忽大利，舍远图而劳近谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147301_comment'></div>愿陛下谋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147301_comment'></div>谋之于未兆则易谋，理之于未乱则易理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147301_comment'></div>臣又闻朝廷昨差使臣往谕迁贼，以礼义观其来意，以恩信导其归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147301_comment'></div>李继迁既忽闻朝廷告哀，亦能举部族大临，缟素受命，贡奉谢恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147301_comment'></div>既未闻乞守塞垣，又未闻乞归朝阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147301_comment'></div>大臣必有拟议，必有臧谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147301_comment'></div>谋之允臧，计必先定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147301_comment'></div>今山陵既在近，边塞虽无虞，黎元尚未苏，仓库尚未实，边防或有骚动，朝廷何以枝梧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147301_comment'></div>关辅或有乱离，朝廷何以制御？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147301_comment'></div>谋之正在今日，理之正当是时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147301_comment'></div>时不再来，又不可失，无使有心者知关辅乱而知剑阁可守，无使适变者见关辅乱而谓天堑可凭，无使关辅所得之货财不侔吴蜀所得之货财，无使关辅所守之疆土不侔吴蜀之疆土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147301_comment'></div>关辅静则蜀货吴财交至，关辅乱则剑外江南各有所守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147301_comment'></div>此所谓舍小利而必得大利，无远虑则必有近忧也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_99_1147301_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年7月26日</a>　七月二十六日，在京为吏部郎中，再上疏论河西力役。作品：论灵州馈运奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八六。）</span><div id='poem_1147302' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147302' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147302?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论灵州馈运奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（真宗至道三年七月二十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（997年7月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147302")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147302_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147302'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147302'>臣未喻陛下降诏以来有人上言否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147302_comment'></div>未审下诏之后有人抗疏否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147302_comment'></div>若未有人上一言，未有人抗一议，即望陛下再降优诏，曲谕圣心，虚伫以待贤良，矜容以求直谅，则怀才抱器者安敢有所隐，蹈忠履信者必尽有所伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147302_comment'></div>臣昨日所上奏章，所陈鄙见，止为关右一时之弊，止为河西一处之言，馀未悉陈，虑烦圣览，须至备述，庶补达聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147302_comment'></div>今灵州闭坚壁以待馈粮，无外援不敢御寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147302_comment'></div>昨闻百姓馈送粮草，死者十馀万人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147302_comment'></div>粮草二十五万，到者七八万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147302_comment'></div>粮草不到者，非戎人劫掠之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147302_comment'></div>百姓不来者，非戎人杀戮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147302_comment'></div>是自相蹈籍，或因被劫夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147302_comment'></div>饥饿既众，死亡遂多，去虽援之以甲兵，回即害之者士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147302_comment'></div>今关西父哭子，弟哭兄，妻哭夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147302_comment'></div>悲哀之声，感动行路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147302_comment'></div>冤枉之苦，轸恻圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147302_comment'></div>臣谓非十年未见生其民，民生十年方可充力役；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147302_comment'></div>臣谓非十年未能聚其财，财聚十年方可备供亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147302_comment'></div>于三十年间，陛下生之、聚之、教之、化之，然后致太平，然后臻至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147302_comment'></div>今臣年五十八，事陛下十二年，年七十，已当外退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147302_comment'></div>十二年间，愿伸微劳以答圣恩，愿罄真诚以报大造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147302_comment'></div>然犬马之年未必保馀龄，葵藿之心幸得承委照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147302_comment'></div>则未退休间，有合言不敢不言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147302_comment'></div>未陨越间，有合奏不敢不奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147302_comment'></div>愿陛下所务者广大，所图者几微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147302_comment'></div>几微者事之先，广大者君之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147302_comment'></div>陛下方欲求至理致太平，无忽事之未萌，勿轻事之未兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147302_comment'></div>臣闻帝者与师处，王者与友处，霸者与臣处，亡国之君与厮役处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147302_comment'></div>与师处则无为，无为是无事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147302_comment'></div>与友处则机务简易，德业光大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147302_comment'></div>驳杂者霸道，不足为陛下言之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147302_comment'></div>暴慢者亡国，安敢对陛下陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147302_comment'></div>道尊德盛者帝之师，才高识远者王之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147302_comment'></div>今陛下睿圣既与天同极，听断乃与日惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147302_comment'></div>若道尊德盛者，陛下劳谦以师之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147302_comment'></div>才高识远者，陛下推诚以友之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147302_comment'></div>友之则四友斯来，师之则三师可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147302_comment'></div>师道见尊，则天下何忧不理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147302_comment'></div>王道得友，则天下何虑不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147302_comment'></div>臣昨日所奏，望陛下且留中不出，为言地震灾祥之必有，为言下动叛离之将作，非外人所可得而知，非大臣不可得而议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147302_comment'></div>留中未出之际，略与大臣言之，其中可行之事，更令近臣议之拟之而后动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147302_comment'></div>天下无异议，中外无异言，择善而从之，从长而行之，不为横议所非，不为非理所破，岂独微臣之幸，其实国家之福。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1147302_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年8月8日</a>　八月八日，在京为吏部郎中，与魏廷式同知审官院、通进银台封驳司，赐金紫，有谢改赐章服笏记。作品：谢改赐章服笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢改赐章服笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（997年8月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147358")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147358'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147358'>臣锡言：臣蒙恩改赐章服，祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147358_comment'></div>伏念臣素无文艺，本乏时才，遭逢既自于先朝，扬历骤升于显秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147358_comment'></div>忝尘斯久，报效未伸，每愧贪叨，但惭尸素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147358_comment'></div>岂谓圣慈曲被，宠命惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147358_comment'></div>象简朱衣，念其久赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147358_comment'></div>金章紫绶，锡以增荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147358_comment'></div>唯励丹诚，上酬玄造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147358_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年11月8日</a>　十一月八日，在京为吏部郎中，又上疏论时事。作品：论防下动奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八七。）</span><div id='poem_1147303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论防下动奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（真宗至道三年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（997年11月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147303")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147303'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147303'>臣昨七月二十五日所进封章，为言地震之灾，是彰下动之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147303_comment'></div>臣经宿思虑，以其事非外人所可得而知，非大臣不可与之议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147303_comment'></div>臣达旦忧惧，以所奏请陛下且留中不出，乞陛下与大臣略言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147303_comment'></div>至二十六日，再上封章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147303_comment'></div>所贵谨密，未审陛下曾以其事与大臣评议否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147303_comment'></div>不知大臣曾闻其事为陛下商较否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147303_comment'></div>今地震之灾渐见，下动之象已萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147303_comment'></div>臣见银台司诸道奏报，自九月初至冬节前，申奏贼盗不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147303_comment'></div>今不一一具奏，虑烦圣聪，且据其可言者一二而言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147303_comment'></div>九月四日施州奏，群贼四百馀人惊劫人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147303_comment'></div>十月七日滑州奏，有贼四十馀人过河北；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147303_comment'></div>十五日卫州奏，有贼七十馀人过河北；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147303_comment'></div>十九日绛州奏，垣曲县贼八十馀人杀县尉成柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147303_comment'></div>西京奏，十月二十三日，有贼一百五十三人入白波兵马都监廨署，并劫一十四家，至午时，夺州船往垣曲，至河阳、巩县界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147303_comment'></div>濮州奏，群贼入鄄城县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147303_comment'></div>单州奏，群贼入归恩指挥营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147303_comment'></div>济州奏，群贼劫金乡、钜野县郭十九家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147303_comment'></div>永兴军奏，虎翼军贼四十馀人劫永兴南庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147303_comment'></div>今月二日西京奏，王屋县贼一百馀人，白高渡溃散军贼六十馀人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147303_comment'></div>七日陕府奏，集津镇群贼六十馀人，并惊劫人户，至午时乘船下去峡石县，群贼自河北渡过河南；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147303_comment'></div>八日西京奏，草贼见把截土壕镇，官私往来不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147303_comment'></div>岂有京师咫尺而群盗如此，边防宁静而叛卒如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147303_comment'></div>臣所谓地震之灾渐见，下动之象已萌，臣为陛下忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147303_comment'></div>臣每见宣命指挥，以诸处奏报，但令巡检使臣掩捕，但令巡检地分袭逐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147303_comment'></div>而安之讨之，未见其嘉谋，备之御之，未见其远虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147303_comment'></div>若其势渐盛，而有谋者与之为谋，其力难制，而思乱者济之为乱，乃是国家失于早图，乃是朝廷失于轻事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147303_comment'></div>今地震之灾渐见，陛下何不早谋而杜其渐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147303_comment'></div>下动之象已萌，陛下何不熟虑而防其萌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147303_comment'></div>臣七月所奏，望再取披详，今所奏望必垂听信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147303_comment'></div>防其萌正在今日，杜其渐不可失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147303_comment'></div>近京盗起既如此，向西民困又如彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147303_comment'></div>昨杨允恭请置粮草车三千辆，要推车兵士一千人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147303_comment'></div>卢之翰两状奏乞自京支拨钱四十五万贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147303_comment'></div>度支奏灵州五月下旬，米每升一贯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147303_comment'></div>要车子运粮，是边上仓廪素无储备矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147303_comment'></div>请自京支钱，是关右帑库素无积蓄矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147303_comment'></div>奏米每斗十贯文，即灵州军民今已饿殍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147303_comment'></div>未审朝廷惜灵州有何所得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147303_comment'></div>弃灵州有何所失？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147303_comment'></div>若因力役未息而中原难起，制御失宜而外方变生，实谓所得不如所失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147303_comment'></div>今陛下宜精于所虑，断在不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147303_comment'></div>若惜灵州必然有益于国家，即乞明降敕书，晓谕天下，使天下知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147303_comment'></div>弃灵州必然有损于国家，亦乞明降敕榜晓谕，使天下知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147303_comment'></div>晓谕之意，以苏息万民为意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147303_comment'></div>取舍之谋，以优恤万民为谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147303_comment'></div>令边敌知取舍之谋，使中外知损益之理，示朝廷之大体，表王道之至公，此所谓陛下修德以禳地震之灾，此乃是陛下早图以防下动之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147303_comment'></div>若贼势渐盛，民患未除，而谋虑之不深，剪灭之未得，被贼辄据州郡，僭称公侯，河北仓廒能先占取，河西部落来与结连，百姓力役之未休，四方观望而相效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147303_comment'></div>此事非细，系社稷之安危，此策非轻，系朝廷之治乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147303_comment'></div>今庙堂之上，必有嘉谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147303_comment'></div>枢轴之间，必有善计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147303_comment'></div>若言小小寇盗，不劳圣虑忧虞，若以屡屡指挥，只令使臣捕逐，如此则群盗终难剪灭，如此则诸处终未平宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147303_comment'></div>若贼徒聚得三、二千人，径度淮南，往保吴、越，则运粮纲船不至京师矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147303_comment'></div>若贼徒取得一、二州郡，善据要冲，则上供钱帛不充国用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147303_comment'></div>因此，则人情必有向背；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147303_comment'></div>人情既有向背，则军情岂无动摇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147303_comment'></div>当此时，北敌辄来骚边，陛下不得不忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147303_comment'></div>四戎辄来犯塞，大臣不得不惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147303_comment'></div>臣今所言激切，不为身谋，所虑安危，实为国计。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1147303_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，与魏廷式不和，有奏状辩其事。作品：奏魏廷式封驳。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏魏廷式封驳状</a><span class='authorDate'>（997年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147400")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147400'>臣今月二十六日受实封敕一道，为魏廷式封驳陈恕等不赴晡临还司敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147400_comment'></div>其奏状云：「臣与田锡同共取旨，其田锡妄奏圣君，遂相矛盾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147400_comment'></div>臣奉圣旨，令独署名衔驳奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147400_comment'></div>奉敕：「宜令田锡详所奏，分析闻奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147400_comment'></div>右，臣昨二十二日于长春殿与魏廷式进呈劄子，臣未读劄子，先奏称魏廷式将断敕，取圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147400_comment'></div>魏廷式遂将三司盐铁使陈恕等不赴晡临断了还司敕对御披读，又将《刑统》第一策于御前读曰：「礼者，恭之本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147400_comment'></div>恭者，礼之舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147400_comment'></div>故《礼运》云『礼者，君之柄，所以别嫌明微，考制度，别仁义』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147400_comment'></div>责其所犯既大，皆无肃恭之心，故曰大不恭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147400_comment'></div>于是臣遂奏云：「御史中丞李惟清所奏，元无『大』字，祗称『有此不恭」』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147400_comment'></div>陛下遂取《刑统》看，并看元敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147400_comment'></div>臣又奏「大不恭」有八条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147400_comment'></div>臣又奏曰：「臣按故事，凡制敕有未允当，即驳正其事，封还诏书，谓之封驳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147400_comment'></div>今此敕已断遣了」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147400_comment'></div>臣又奏：「臣昨日与魏廷式商量，此敕缘是断了敕，然不敢坚执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147400_comment'></div>缘张鉴是臣亲情，虑魏廷式有所疑，今日须至于陛下当面敷奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147400_comment'></div>臣又奏曰：「臣于法律不熟，魏廷式本是法科成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147400_comment'></div>臣乞祗令魏廷式自驳奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147400_comment'></div>寻蒙陛下谓魏廷式曰：「祗卿独自驳奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147400_comment'></div>又再谓魏廷式曰：「卿自驳奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147400_comment'></div>臣又奏曰：「魏廷式欲法寺定断元条，若陛下宽减其罪，所贵恩归陛下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147400_comment'></div>臣之所奏，陛下必一一记得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147400_comment'></div>今魏廷式称臣「妄奏圣君」，所奏安敢辄妄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147400_comment'></div>魏廷式又称臣「遂相矛盾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147400_comment'></div>臣缘所见与魏廷式所见不同，所以不敢与之同驳奏，以此魏廷式奏臣「遂相矛盾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147400_comment'></div>臣与魏廷式同勾当审官院、通进银台封驳司，岂敢与之矛盾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147400_comment'></div>若魏廷式所见与臣所见同，即臣方敢与之同封驳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147400_comment'></div>若魏廷式所见与臣所见不同，即臣岂敢与之同封驳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147400_comment'></div>臣谬因文学，偶忝科名，幸以遭逢，骤尘华显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147400_comment'></div>效官史阁，但阅图书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147400_comment'></div>供职掖垣，曾知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147400_comment'></div>典谟之事，则尝闻之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147400_comment'></div>刑律之书，未尝学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147400_comment'></div>昨八月八日閤门受敕，差臣与魏廷式同职勾当，敢不尽忠于陛下，敢不共力于同官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147400_comment'></div>实非妄有奏陈，辄相矛盾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147400_comment'></div>仰祈圣鉴，俯察愚诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1147400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年1月</a>　正月，在京为吏部郎中，除泰州知州，获准三月初赴任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在京为吏部郎中，将宋太宗朝所作谏疏送实录院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年3月7日</a>　三月七日，在京为吏部郎中，上疏论星变，获宋真宗召对。作品：将赴泰州上奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八七。）</span><div id='poem_1147304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147304' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147304?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将赴泰州上奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平元年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147304")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147304_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147304'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147304'>臣自去年七月至冬节已后三上章，所言者朝廷密谋，所陈者国家大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147304_comment'></div>识见虽浅，不足动于宸聪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147304_comment'></div>果敢所陈，亦足伸于忠节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147304_comment'></div>每至奏覆公事，咫尺天颜，亦望圣聪略赐宣问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147304_comment'></div>岂谓陛下略不询所陈之事，殊不访所贡之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147304_comment'></div>退有忧遑，虑获罪戾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147304_comment'></div>进无听纳，固不遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147304_comment'></div>所以辄拜封章，乞归馆殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147304_comment'></div>旋承敕命，令知泰州，已蒙圣恩，给与假限，许至三月初进发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147304_comment'></div>臣既受敕，不合立班，唯候朝辞，以赴任所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147304_comment'></div>于二月八日方睹御札，许贡刍词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147304_comment'></div>臣子之事君亲，愚直之逢明圣，有所见闻，岂敢缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147304_comment'></div>臣闻君不密则失臣，臣不密则失身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147304_comment'></div>臣去年所上第一章，下在中书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147304_comment'></div>第二、第三章，留中不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147304_comment'></div>臣虑外人窥其曾有贴黄，乞未付中书，且宣召宰臣、枢密使问其可否，然尚有不敢形于奏疏，拟俟面陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147304_comment'></div>所虑者非轻，虑陛下失臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147304_comment'></div>所忧者非细，忧微臣失身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147304_comment'></div>今日陛下若许臣面言，容臣口奏，即乞宣召，必得敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147304_comment'></div>臣于正月十二日得实录院牒，要臣太宗朝所上谏疏，臣已写录，于二月二日送实录院，记其间可行之事、可用之言，先皇帝亦听纳而行之，亦优容而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147304_comment'></div>伏乞陛下令实录院进呈，略赐披览，有先朝未行者，乞择而行之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147304_comment'></div>有今日可用者，乞取而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147304_comment'></div>御札云「良由时事舛误，政化郁堙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147304_comment'></div>臣谓李继迁不合与夏州，又不合呼之为赵保吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147304_comment'></div>虽赐姓与名，已自先朝，然狼子野心，终是异类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147304_comment'></div>昨以陛下登极，虽来进奉，锡之优诏，奖以来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147304_comment'></div>识其奸谋，辨其诡计，则可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147304_comment'></div>锡之土宇，授以节旄，则非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147304_comment'></div>以臣愚蒙，料彼变诈，必不肯久奉朝命，必不能永保塞垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147304_comment'></div>既如此惠之怀之而弗来，讨之除之而未得，翻成姑息，似失机宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147304_comment'></div>臣谓关辅劳扰从此生，国家费耗从此起，是时事舛误之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147304_comment'></div>密院公事，宰相不得与闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147304_comment'></div>中书政事，枢密使不得与议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147304_comment'></div>相承既久，骤改固难，致兵谋不精，国计未善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147304_comment'></div>求之近验，即去年灵州之役，关西之民死者十五馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147304_comment'></div>生民无辜而死者十五馀万，罪在何人而不问，咎将谁执而不知，此政化郁堙之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147304_comment'></div>臣今为陛下言其大者远者，自馀琐屑之事，何足为陛下言之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1147304_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年3月9日</a>　三月九日，在京为吏部郎中，再上疏论星变。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年3月11日</a>　三月十一日，在京为吏部郎中，又获宋真宗召对。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5310db7cf42c4917b0531e2e3dab2d00_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5310db7cf42c4917b0531e2e3dab2d00");'><span id='5310db7cf42c4917b0531e2e3dab2d00_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1003')">1001-1003年</a>，62-64岁</div><div id='5310db7cf42c4917b0531e2e3dab2d00' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年5月8日</a>　五月八日，在京为吏部郎中，获宋真宗召对，请修《御览》和《御屏风》作品：上真宗进经史子集要语。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。孙谱系此文于咸平三年，此据《续资治通鉴长编》卷四九咸平四年六月条改。）</span><div id='poem_1147291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗进经史子集要语</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147291")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147291'>臣闻古者帝王，盘盂皆铭，几杖有诫，起居必视，夙夜不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147291_comment'></div>故汤之《盘铭》曰：「日日新，又日新」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147291_comment'></div>《太公金匮》曰：「武王欲造起居之诫，乃铭于几杖曰：『安无忘危，存无忘亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147291_comment'></div>熟惟二者，后必无凶』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147291_comment'></div>《墨子》曰：「尧、舜、禹、汤书其事于竹帛，篆之盘盂，曰：君子福大而愈惧，爵隆而愈恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147291_comment'></div>远察近视，俯仰有别」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147291_comment'></div>矧黄帝舆几皆铭焉，曰：「吾居民之上，惴惴恐不及」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147291_comment'></div>武王户席必训焉，《席之铭》曰：「无行可悔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147291_comment'></div>《户之铭》曰：「难得而易失」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147291_comment'></div>圣人修德罔怠，然佩服鉴戒，终日不忘，故至德大业，永保天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147291_comment'></div>臣又尝读《唐书》，见高宗命黄门侍郎赵智讲《孝经》于百福殿，因谓之曰：「大旨朕知之矣，即举此经要切处言之，以裨不逮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147291_comment'></div>智曰：「天子有争臣七人，虽无道，不失其天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147291_comment'></div>微臣敢以此言上献」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147291_comment'></div>帝大悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147291_comment'></div>又宪宗听政之暇，探《史》、《汉》、《三国》而来经纶要事，撰书十四篇，号曰《前代君臣事迹》，写于六扇屏风，置于御坐之右，出入观省之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147291_comment'></div>臣每览经史子集，因取其要语，总一十卷，辄用进献，可题于屏，置之御坐，出入观省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147291_comment'></div>所贵日夕观省，冀圣德日新，与尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武比隆也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1147291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1147291'><span class='label'>按：</span>《咸平集》卷一。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷六，《历代名臣奏议》卷一。又见以下诸书，题作《御屏风序》：《隆平集》卷一三，《东都事略》卷三九，《群书考索》前集卷一七，《宋史》卷二九三《田锡传》，嘉靖《洪雅县志》卷四，《古今图书集成》经籍典卷四九七，民国《眉山志》卷一○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1147291_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年5月26日</a>　五月二十六日，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状进宋太宗朝所作封章及《御览》三十卷、《御屏风》五卷。作品：进撰述文字草本。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进撰述文字草本状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年5月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147406")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147406'>右，臣昨五月八日蒙宣诏顾问之次，臣因奏乞以经史中要切之言书于屏风，置于御座之侧，所贵旦夕披览，如座右铭之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147406_comment'></div>臣又奏今陛下以何道理天下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147406_comment'></div>愿以皇王之道为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147406_comment'></div>臣奏旧又有《御览》，但记分门事类，共三百六十卷，取日览一卷，可周岁读遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147406_comment'></div>然不如节略经史子集，作三百六十卷，或万机之暇，日览一卷，所贵理乱兴亡之事，常在目前也，臣欲撰进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147406_comment'></div>至明日，又再承召对，宣喻所言皇王为理之道，可款曲著撰进来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147406_comment'></div>臣遂略言《尚书》尧、舜典是帝道，其注亦甚分明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147406_comment'></div>陛下称「朕亦常看《尚书》，其注颇甚易晓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147406_comment'></div>臣又奉圣旨，令写先帝时所进封章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147406_comment'></div>臣自请假往郑州回，寻写先朝时所进封章，已于五月二十六日诣东上閤门实封进呈讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147406_comment'></div>所有撰进文字两本<span class='inlineComment2'>（隐其名。）</span>，今且各写两卷进呈，取进止，欲依此撰进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147406_comment'></div>如圣旨允所奏，即乞内降札子指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147406_comment'></div>所是馀一卷轴稍多，候撰及三五十卷，旋具奏草进纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147406_comment'></div>今诣通进司进上件草本四卷，随实封状闻奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1147406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年9月26日</a>　九月二十六日，在京为吏部郎中，受命与梅询、孙冕考试开封府举人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年10月</a>　十月，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状谢内降劄子奖谕。作品：谢内降劄子奖谕。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢内降劄子奖谕状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147407")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147407'>右，臣昨日通进司差人送到实封内降札子一道，伏蒙圣慈特加奖谕，并以臣所进文字，令馀上卷帙旋撰集得相次进来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147407_comment'></div>臣本无器业，素乏才能，遭逢先朝，骤历华贯，祗事陛下，未展微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147407_comment'></div>昨因召赴深严，再承顾问，遂有所奏，欲以皇王之道，编撰进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147407_comment'></div>遽承英睿之知，特垂听允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147407_comment'></div>洎撰集之次，馆中将文历令臣署字，随例勘书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147407_comment'></div>所撰集既密受指挥，不敢泄漏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147407_comment'></div>其校雠又难为诉免，不敢奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147407_comment'></div>相次奉敕考试举人，昨已了毕，遂进所撰草本，取候进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147407_comment'></div>岂谓圣恩曲被，睿奖遄临，退思庸浅之才，曷称照临之德？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147407_comment'></div>俯伏愧荷，兢惶失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147407_comment'></div>今因事复有愚诚，合取圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147407_comment'></div>为所撰进文字，卷轴稍多，所有馆中勘书，欲乞蠲免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147407_comment'></div>贵一志得专于检阅，数年方就于功夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147407_comment'></div>兼得逐旋进呈，以备接续披览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147407_comment'></div>仰祈玄造，俯鉴丹怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1147407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年12月</a>　十二月，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状乞荫长子田庆远。作品：奏荫长男庆远一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏荫长男庆远状<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147410")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147410'>右，臣伏以忠于国，莫先于至公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147410_comment'></div>孝于家，莫重于继世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147410_comment'></div>臣去年因逢圣节，辄露私诚，以《六典》素有明文，五品得用资荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147410_comment'></div>遂上言长男庆远，幼能写字，长好读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147410_comment'></div>随臣出入为官，见臣日夕莅事，颇知畏慎，稍识公方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147410_comment'></div>虽文学之间，未能应举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147410_comment'></div>而恭谨之性，足以干家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147410_comment'></div>臣以年齿已衰，生涯未有，除俸禄充给之外，无田园终老可归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147410_comment'></div>虑一旦云亡，卜葬无地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147410_comment'></div>一家私属，失所可忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147410_comment'></div>遂拜封章，与长男希求入仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147410_comment'></div>及经旬月，闻正郎无例该恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147410_comment'></div>然臣男庆远，自来与臣写所奏封章，与臣写所进文字，年已成立，性亦恭勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147410_comment'></div>欲及臣未死之时，聊慰臣有后之意，望不候圣节，不俟郊禋，乞陛下垂特达之恩，遂微臣恳求之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147410_comment'></div>况臣年六十有三，馀七年当已致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147410_comment'></div>以人生百岁，七十者稀，未知七年之间，得事陛下否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147410_comment'></div>若一旦溘如朝露，永谢明时，则遗表进男，亦无及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147410_comment'></div>臣不避罪责，因悉敷陈，伏望圣慈，俯垂悯念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147410_comment'></div>干冒宸扆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1147410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，上疏论制科。作品：上真宗论制科当依汉制取人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。孙谱系此文于咸平三年，此据《续资治通鉴长编》卷四八咸平四年二月丙寅条改。）</span><div id='poem_1147292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗论制科当依汉制取人</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147292")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147292'>臣窃惟唐设制科，有道侔伊吕科，有识洞韬略堪任将帅科，有贤良方正直言极谏科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147292_comment'></div>自太祖朝兵部尚书张昭奏请兴制举，于时据所奏前代制举内选置三科：一、贤良方正能直言极谏科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147292_comment'></div>一、经学优深可为师法科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147292_comment'></div>一、详闲吏理达于教化科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147292_comment'></div>敕文略曰：「应天下诸色人中，不限前资任职官、黄衣草泽等，并可应诏，送吏部，试策论三道，共三千言，以当日内取文理俱优、人物爽秀者，方得解送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147292_comment'></div>其登朝官，亦许上表自举」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147292_comment'></div>虽设制科之名，未尽取人之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147292_comment'></div>何以明之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147292_comment'></div>夫汉诏取人，不限对策字数，随其所对，尽其所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147292_comment'></div>故孝文时晁错对策不过二千字，孝武时董仲舒对策不过二千馀字，然上览之而异焉，乃复策之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147292_comment'></div>凡诏策三问，而所对皆不及二千馀字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147292_comment'></div>洎公孙弘答策，才五百馀字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147292_comment'></div>然汉之得贤良，斯为盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147292_comment'></div>观董仲舒所对策三道，亦非以当日内成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147292_comment'></div>今但依汉之取人，则董、晁、公孙辈，不独汉有也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1147292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，为宋真宗制策。作品：制策。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二二。孙谱系此文于咸平三年，此据《续资治通鉴长编》卷四八咸平四年二月丙寅条改。）</span><div id='poem_1147283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>制策</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147283")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147283'>皇帝若曰：国家承五代乱离之后，稽三王质文之变，太祖以神武定天下，太宗以圣文化域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147283_comment'></div>万里封疆，复禹旧迹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147283_comment'></div>二圣功业，与天比崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147283_comment'></div>德化所被，靡不祗若；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147283_comment'></div>日月所照，罔不率俾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147283_comment'></div>自开创致升平，迨四十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147283_comment'></div>朕以寡昧，嗣纂大位，遵守先训，虑弗克负荷，夙夕未遑宁居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147283_comment'></div>惟万务之几微，鉴烛未明，中心浩然，罔知攸济，兢兢业业，五载于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147283_comment'></div>镇抚夷夏，康济黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147283_comment'></div>虽下承成规，事仍旧贯，庶政用乂，宇县久安，屡降诏书，旁求谠议，五日转对，亦复往制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147283_comment'></div>尚虑君子难进，嘉言攸伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147283_comment'></div>故详延贤良方正之士，咸造于庭，欲闻经国之谋，辅时之策，明予于大道，致予于至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147283_comment'></div>今子大夫其发挥理本，宣扬道要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147283_comment'></div>言又曰从，朕敢忘《洪范》之训？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147283_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147283_comment'></div>大道之行，三代之英，仲尼其犹喟然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147283_comment'></div>又《书》不云乎：「克念作圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147283_comment'></div>孟轲曰：尧舜亦人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147283_comment'></div>朕永惟皇王之理，思复三代之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147283_comment'></div>尧民比屋可封，舜《韶》鸟兽率舞，夏后鱼鳖咸若，文王虞芮让畔，何千古难继？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147283_comment'></div>其或继之者，厥道何从，厥理安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147283_comment'></div>其次适时之务，安可忽诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147283_comment'></div>今三边无虞，重译入贡，制猃狁自古无上策，御奸宄不得已而用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147283_comment'></div>方求闻所未闻，得所未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147283_comment'></div>虑黠虏乘间，屡来骚边；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147283_comment'></div>迁贼负恩，罔畏干纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147283_comment'></div>致劳征戍，每烦供馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147283_comment'></div>供馈出于民力，征戍资于国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147283_comment'></div>专利山海，殖货关市，或讥王道之未融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147283_comment'></div>丰财于农桑，节用于制度，其如边备之未足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147283_comment'></div>斯二途取舍，其术安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147283_comment'></div>又古者十一之税，秦氏太半之赋，其按田收租，始自何代？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147283_comment'></div>计口定算，肇于何时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147283_comment'></div>《春秋》曰：近盬，公室乃贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147283_comment'></div>《管子》曰：谨正盐筴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147283_comment'></div>其义相反，何所适从？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147283_comment'></div>又勤恤人隐，奉若天道，而间岁以来，阴阳不和，水旱作沴，寒暑罹于疾疫，歉俭致其流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147283_comment'></div>夫安上理民，礼乐为急，礼以本天地，乐以和神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147283_comment'></div>岂阴阳之或差，致水旱以作沴，札瘥夭昏，流庸浮冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147283_comment'></div>无乃礼乐之用，其未至乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147283_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147283_comment'></div>上失其道，民散久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147283_comment'></div>讲议礼乐，予将畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147283_comment'></div>观礼以知兴亡，审乐以明理乱，非贤臣弗达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147283_comment'></div>子大夫怀才抱器，学古待问，知己慰荐，副朕所求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147283_comment'></div>各罄尔之所长，交修予之不逮，敷之条对，靡有所隐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1147283_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状乞在京修书。作品：奏乞不差出。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞不差出状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147408")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147408'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147408'>右，臣所撰进文字，旋进五卷讫，未审陛下书于屏风，已置座隅否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147408_comment'></div>所进文字<span class='inlineComment2'>（隐名。）</span>，是臣致君于尧、舜之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147408_comment'></div>尝因宣召，陛下问臣所进文字，几日撰得一卷，臣奏五日撰得一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147408_comment'></div>臣因以日计撰成之数，一年计七十二卷，五年方得成就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147408_comment'></div>虽五日撰得一卷，然须子细披详，虑有差错或误，则检会比覆，以至写净，可七日至八日方了一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147408_comment'></div>今以八日之数，大概总计一月可得三卷，一年得三十六卷，十年方得三百六十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147408_comment'></div>别<span class='inlineComment2'>（隐名）</span>一十卷不在计数外，其馀已进十七卷讫，馀三百四十三卷，计九年馀六个月方始成就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147408_comment'></div>臣虑十年之间，陛下差臣出官，若临时求免差出，是违王命也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147408_comment'></div>又虑十年之间，陛下差臣莅事，若至时欲免差遣，是违圣旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147408_comment'></div>以臣愚见，若差出一郡，不过治一方，孰若留臣在馆殿，常以皇王之道致陛下于尧、舜也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147408_comment'></div>若差莅事，不过供一职，孰若留臣在左右，得以帝霸之道致陛下于尧、舜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147408_comment'></div>臣始乞免勘书，欲专以撰述，蒙圣恩，寻有内降札子下馆中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147408_comment'></div>臣又乞借书，欲广于闻见，亦得睿旨，寻有内降札子下馆中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147408_comment'></div>臣既有书检阅，又无事牵束，以副陛下降纶言奖喻之恩，足以成微臣奉圣旨著撰之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147408_comment'></div>今陛下春秋鼎盛，英睿天资，听政之馀，好古不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147408_comment'></div>若师皇王之道，日新厥德，必十年之内，能致太平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147408_comment'></div>若遵帝霸之道，夕惕若厉，则千载之运，永固鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147408_comment'></div>臣虽衰迈，得见太平之时，臣之私幸足矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147408_comment'></div>臣虽愚蒙，得成所撰之书，臣之夙愿亦足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147408_comment'></div>如圣慈允臣所奏，乞御批札子直付微臣，贵无泄漏，缘所撰书未成，须至慎密，庶免讥谤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147408_comment'></div>干冒宸严。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1147408_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状谢传宣。作品：谢传宣。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，作《御览序》作品：御览序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《宋文鉴》卷八五。）</span><div id='poem_1147451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147451?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御览序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147451")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147451'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147451'>臣闻圣人之道，布在方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147451_comment'></div>六经则言高旨远，非讲求讨论，不可测其渊深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147451_comment'></div>诸史则迹异事殊，非参会异同，岂易记其繁杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147451_comment'></div>子书则异端之说胜，文集则宗经之辞寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147451_comment'></div>非猎精以为鉴戒，举要以观会同，可为日览之书，资于日新之德，则虽白首，未能穷经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147451_comment'></div>矧王者机务馀暇，端拱穆清，所宜不劳躬而得稽古大端，不烦览而达为理大意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147451_comment'></div>臣每读书，思以所得，上补达聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147451_comment'></div>而天启微衷，神佑私志，近因宣召，面得敷陈，可以铭于座隅者书于御屏，可以用于帝道者录为《御览》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147451_comment'></div>今经取帝王易晓之意，史取帝王可行之事，子或总于杂录，集或附之逐篇，悉求切当之言，用达精详之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147451_comment'></div>览之详其义，则事与机会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147451_comment'></div>用之得其时，则名与功偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147451_comment'></div>冀以尘露之微，上裨高深之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147451_comment'></div>即嗣圣功业，与尧舜比崇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147451_comment'></div>生灵富寿，在羲轩之上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1147451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1147451'><span class='label'>按：</span>《皇朝文鉴》卷八五。又见《东都事略》卷三九、《宋史》卷二九三《田锡传》，嘉靖《洪雅县志》卷四，《古今图书集成》经籍典卷四九七，《宋代蜀文辑存》卷一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1147451_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年1月12日</a>　正月十二日，在京为吏部郎中，权干当通进银台司，兼门下封驳事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年1月15日</a>　正月十五日，在京为吏部郎中，上《乞召枢相访问筹谋奏》作品：乞召枢相访问筹谋奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八七。）</span><div id='poem_1147306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞召枢相访问筹谋奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年正月十五日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147306")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147306'>臣昨见差张齐贤充经略使，曾致尧为经略判官，郑文宝为转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147306_comment'></div>臣读孙子《兵书》，云「不尽知用兵之害者，则不能尽知用兵之利」，今未谕张齐贤、曾致尧、郑文宝等尽知用兵之利害否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147306_comment'></div>若尽知利与害，动无遗策，方可委之经略边事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147306_comment'></div>臣读《汉书》，高祖称「运筹帷幄之中，决胜千里之外，吾不如张子房」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147306_comment'></div>今宰相、枢密使是陛下运筹帷幄之臣，不知曾议沿边利害，然后定差张齐贤等否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147306_comment'></div>昨杨琼等不副陛下任使，致失清远军，粮草既委弃不少，人民杀戮驱虏去亦不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147306_comment'></div>今方当春时，兴发兵师，虽救患防虞，自合权变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147306_comment'></div>然圣人动必顺时，则天道助顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147306_comment'></div>今戎狄为患非细，陛下宜召宰相、枢密使，更访以决胜千里之外筹谋，不得轻敌玩寇，致戎狄谓中国无人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147306_comment'></div>若是宰相、枢密使面言不尽，即令直书利害必然之计，画一申奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147306_comment'></div>必然，谓蕃人至若干月必退，若干月必来，其来必胜，其退必败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147306_comment'></div>若宰相、枢密使有所见不同，又不敢果决敷陈必然之策，又忌见同列，则乞陛下于便殿从上一人入，独召与语，使尽其所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147306_comment'></div>臣去年五月六日内殿起居所进转对奏状，言宰相不谙练边事，今乞陛下检寻再披阅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147306_comment'></div>又于去冬所进《御览》第二卷，曾引杜牧注《兵书序》引宰相不知兵之说，望陛下亦重子细披览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147306_comment'></div>况《礼》云：「四郊多垒，卿大夫之辱也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147306_comment'></div>今边境被戎狄侵扰，宰相、枢密使不知以为辱乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147306_comment'></div>不知以为耻乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147306_comment'></div>若不以为辱，又不知耻，是孤负陛下任用，是安于庙堂之上而不知危乱之将至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147306_comment'></div>望陛下速宣召枢相，逐一人人访问，所贵尽其所见，免陛下宵旰之忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147306_comment'></div>臣之此言，言出患入，陛下若不密，即失臣矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1147306_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年1月30日</a>　正月三十日，在京为吏部郎中，上疏乞赈给河北饥民。作品：上真宗赈给河北饥民。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗乞赈给河北饥民</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147293")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147293'>臣今月二十五日所进实封，为霸州、乾宁军死伤人户等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147293_comment'></div>自二十六日至今，又据莫州奏饥死一十六口，沧州奏全家饥死一十七户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147293_comment'></div>虽有指挥下转运司相度，及减斗斛价赈粜，即未见别行指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147293_comment'></div>若有司只如此行遣，实未称陛下忧劳之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147293_comment'></div>陛下为民父母，使百姓饥死，乃是陛下孤负百姓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147293_comment'></div>宰相调燮阴阳，启导圣德，而惠泽不下流，王道未融明，是宰相孤负陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147293_comment'></div>今陛下何不引咎，如禹汤罪己，略降德音，下饥饿杀人处州府，民心知陛下忧恤，然后振廪给贷，以救其死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147293_comment'></div>若仓廪虚而馈运边备尚未足，即日无可给贷，则是执政素不用心所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147293_comment'></div>昔伊尹作相，耻一夫不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147293_comment'></div>今饿杀人如此，所谓焉用彼相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147293_comment'></div>今陛下可将此事以理道略面责宰臣以下，观其何词以对，视其有无怍色，有无忧色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147293_comment'></div>待三日后，或浃旬以来，不上表待罪，不拜章求退，是忍人也，何良相之为乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147293_comment'></div>既非良相，而犹用之，则是陛下不以百姓心为心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147293_comment'></div>若不别进用贤臣，恐危乱之萌，将来滋蔓难图也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147293_comment'></div>《语》曰：「十室之邑，必有忠信」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147293_comment'></div>况今皇家富有万国，岂无人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147293_comment'></div>可于常参官自来五日一转对中，观其所上之言有远大谋略、经纶才业者，可非次擢用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147293_comment'></div>若有其言而无其实，退之以礼，亦合理体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147293_comment'></div>不然，则臣恐国家未能早致太平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147293_comment'></div>岂唯太平之未能致，其忧患不独在边防，而叛乱在内地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147293_comment'></div>此是陛下缵嗣先帝万世基业之急务也，所急之务，莫先于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147293_comment'></div>惟圣聪睿鉴，详微臣之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147293_comment'></div>陆贽云：「贪因循者，终有大患」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147293_comment'></div>今若因循，不早为谋，则虑大患至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147293_comment'></div>今臣所奏，且可先降德音，以禹汤责躬之意以谢天，以尧舜至仁之心以待下，使饥饿地分知陛下忧恤之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147293_comment'></div>臣职在深严，日有闻见，不敢不奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1147293_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年4月8日</a>　四月八日，在京为吏部郎中，以本官兼侍御史知杂事，有致谢笏记。作品：谢兼侍御史知杂事笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢兼侍御史知杂笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年4月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147360")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147360'>臣锡言：伏蒙圣慈赐臣官告、敕牒，授兼侍御史知杂事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147360_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147360_comment'></div>窃念才能无取，齿发已衰，尚列轩墀，每惭尸素，忽沐涵濡之泽，遽尘端副之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147360_comment'></div>矧以申明典章，必资谙练故实。<div class='inline'
