id='poem_sentence_3_1147360_comment'></div>俯循闇懦，宁振起于朝纲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147360_comment'></div>仰玷选抡，但徬徨于官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147360_comment'></div>敢忘勤瘁，上答休明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147360_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年4月23日</a>　四月二十三日，在京为吏部郎中，上疏乞三院御史各归本职。作品：乞三院御史归本职奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八七。）</span><div id='poem_1147307' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147307' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147307?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞三院御史归本职奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年四月二十三日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147307")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147307_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147307'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147307'>臣昨蒙圣恩，授以宪职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147307_comment'></div>按《六典》及《百司举要》、《御史台故事》：自大夫、中丞以下及三院御史，沿革各有人数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147307_comment'></div>今阙班簿，既无定员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147307_comment'></div>有侍御史三人，有殿中侍御史一十二人，有监察御史七人，除邵晔在省司及施谓在患假，馀皆差使在外，却以他官在台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147307_comment'></div>臣谓今之推直官僚乃是古之知推御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147307_comment'></div>按《唐会要》：「兴元元年敕：知东推、西推侍御史各一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147307_comment'></div>台司请令第一殿中同知东推，第三殿中同知西推，仍分日受事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147307_comment'></div>先所置推官二员请停」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147307_comment'></div>又「建中三年台司奏：其知推御史差使改移，旧例有推直官，今请置两员，与本推御史同推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147307_comment'></div>敕旨：依奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147307_comment'></div>此盖随时沿革，因事废兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147307_comment'></div>今三院共有二十一人，或命亲民，或委釐务，宪司之职，似是而非，朝廷用人，如此未审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147307_comment'></div>又准近敕，台寺勘断官令大两省已上保举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147307_comment'></div>臣谓虽令保举，终是他官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147307_comment'></div>臣昨在银台司，见诸道转运司或巡抚使察访外任京朝官功过，具姓名闻奏，有中书劄子下审官院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147307_comment'></div>今欲乞指挥审官院检前后中书劄子，应三院御史二十一人中，曾有贪猥过犯者，不得令在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1147307", 1147307, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>宪秩</span>，可改授他官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147307_comment'></div>其有清慎勤干者，不得令在外官，可诏归本职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147307_comment'></div>去推直因仍之号，抽两省保举之敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147307_comment'></div>所贵复台司之故事，存朝廷之旧规，使百执事各正其名，群有司各亲其职也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1147307_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年4月</a>　四月，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状谢传宣。作品：知杂后谢传宣。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知杂后谢传宣状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147412")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147412'>右，臣十六日中使至，传宣旨：「近者览卿章奏，恐有住滞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147412_comment'></div>为赵诚信差出勾当，不欲别差人来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147412_comment'></div>卿自来章疏，所司不敢住滞，并总收得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147412_comment'></div>今日所为除改事，此名位朝廷甚难其人，亦不妨撰述，虑少暇可慢慢撰述，候及卷数进来，但安心勿过虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147412_comment'></div>或有所见，逐旋闻奏，不欲召卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147412_comment'></div>兼今后不更差人，并降札子去与卿便稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147412_comment'></div>及今后奏状，不要可漏字，上更著白帖子，言里面有贴黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147412_comment'></div>卿自来奏状，朕一一亲览，但祗状内著黄贴子」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147412_comment'></div>俯伏闻命，释愚臣危惧之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147412_comment'></div>兢荣失图，感英主照临之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147412_comment'></div>臣盖念于通进司每下奏状，执政间或有探人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147412_comment'></div>古谓禁闱有九重之严，中堂喻千里之远，盖虞左右辄蔽聪明，所以下之情诚少得上达闻听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147412_comment'></div>今陛下宣示，以臣自来章疏，所司不敢滞留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147412_comment'></div>臣之至愚，固无可采；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147412_comment'></div>但以有所闻见，敢不敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147412_comment'></div>既一一尽达宸聪，则区区得罄臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147412_comment'></div>仍喻臣以近所除兼职，朝廷甚难其人，臣实何人，当兹重选，将何称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147412_comment'></div>但奉至公，上酬圣知，以赎官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147412_comment'></div>仍勉臣以不妨撰述，候及卷数进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147412_comment'></div>令臣但安心，命臣勿过虑，或有所见，逐旋奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147412_comment'></div>臣学识非优，器能无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147412_comment'></div>但以遭逢景运，涓埃无报国之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147412_comment'></div>采摭群书，缃素形致君之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147412_comment'></div>撰集未毕，除改忽新，虑构罪尤，合先敷奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147412_comment'></div>岂谓封章朝达，宣旨夕传，优容同覆载之仁，敦喻表慈怜之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147412_comment'></div>柏台莅公之暇，竹简著书之馀，得以皂囊，上陈丹陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147412_comment'></div>虽虚伫谠直，无间于刍荛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147412_comment'></div>而仰鉴融明，愿倾于葵藿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147412_comment'></div>干冒旒扆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1147412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年5月22日</a>　五月二十二日，在京为吏部郎中，上疏论点集强壮。作品：上真宗论点集强壮。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗论点集强壮</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147295")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147295'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147295'>臣伏睹近日多雨，秋稼颇伤，近京诸州，积潦为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147295_comment'></div>加以差遣使命，点集乡兵，人情不安，物听可骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147295_comment'></div>谓一家虽有数口，三丁必抽两丁，定以强壮之名，备于缓急之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147295_comment'></div>虽不刺面，各遣归农，其如终隶军名，向去须在戎伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147295_comment'></div>当北狄未宾之际，值西戎为害之时，岂不知临时抽差，以补正军阙少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147295_comment'></div>如此，壮丁父母，逐家妻男，有哀恸之哭声，实感伤于和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147295_comment'></div>朝廷宜制理于未乱，枢相当经始而图终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147295_comment'></div>臣窃闻国家府库稍虚，仓廪不实，不然，则何以急急于聚敛财货，孜孜于备御边防？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147295_comment'></div>况庙堂无人，军旅无将，居崇官者皆莫知危亡之渐，食厚禄者悉坐观成败之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147295_comment'></div>边上奏报继来，戎狄侵轶渐近，其好佞言而安圣心者，则曰国家何患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147295_comment'></div>无远虑而有近忧者，不过请圣驾亲征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147295_comment'></div>望陛下以宗社为忧，乞陛下以刍荛可听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147295_comment'></div>臣每奉圣旨，凡有见闻，即令敷陈，敢不遵守！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147295_comment'></div>干冒宸扆，臣无任惶恐激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1147295_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年10月10日</a>　十月十日，在京为吏部郎中，为亡父作墓碣。作品：先君赠工部郎中墓碣。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1147521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先君赠工部郎中墓碣</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147521")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147521'>先君讳懿，字伯达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147521_comment'></div>尝诲谕曰：「余世本京兆人，因唐末乱离，僖宗幸蜀，尔祖徙家至于此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147521_comment'></div>锡披谱牒，锡高祖开，曾祖易直，祖诚，皆高尚不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147521_comment'></div>先君好术数，聚书数千卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147521_comment'></div>博施济众，交亲有婚嫁之累而寠贫者，悉为嫁娶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147521_comment'></div>捐馆之年，无疾而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147521_comment'></div>尝先会乡里，别亲族，大署于厅事之南庑壁曰：「亡，六月二十三日」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147521_comment'></div>果于是日终焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147521_comment'></div>蜀后主时，陵州刺史赵庭让闻先君好古博施之名，署摄本郡司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147521_comment'></div>享年四十有八，以丁巳年六月二十三日终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147521_comment'></div>乃周显德五年<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>冬十二月八日，葬于县西北归仁乡崇教里大茔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147521_comment'></div>先君尝作寿坟，既而筮之曰：「斯坟也，吾不得而居之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147521_comment'></div>洎没后，果别卜宅兆而葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147521_comment'></div>先夫人杨氏，世以孝行称，事舅姑以孝闻，妇道母仪，合于诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147521_comment'></div>甲寅年十一月五日终，享年四十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147521_comment'></div>乙卯年春二月，葬在先君坟西南五十步，以龟筮叶从，不宜行合祔之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147521_comment'></div>由是先君之葬，同大茔而别封树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147521_comment'></div>锡兄弟三人，兄继云；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147521_comment'></div>锡名继冲，后改曰锡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147521_comment'></div>弟继英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147521_comment'></div>姊一人，适宋知让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147521_comment'></div>妹二人，仲适鲜延寿，季适杨怀贵，俱以令淑闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147521_comment'></div>云后更曰筠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147521_comment'></div>锡入关拔解，开封府寄应首荐，御前就试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147521_comment'></div>太宗嗣位之三载，岁在戊寅，九月二日，一举登第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147521_comment'></div>释褐将作监丞，历著作郎，左拾遗，右补阙，起居舍人、知制诰，兵部员外郎，户部、吏部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147521_comment'></div>弟英在故乡，守先人之旧庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147521_comment'></div>锡弟兄相次云亡，兄亡于郑，弟终于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147521_comment'></div>锡幼好读书，慕扬雄、相如为文，先君曰：「观尔之性，必光大吾门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147521_comment'></div>当立身扬名，勉副吾望乎尔也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147521_comment'></div>历谏省，拜章言事，太宗以敕书奖谕曰：「敕田锡，省所上书具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147521_comment'></div>汝贤路奋身，谏垣就列，罔效循循之辈，窃禄居官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147521_comment'></div>思齐谔谔之臣，拜章言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147521_comment'></div>适符虚伫，谅慰深衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147521_comment'></div>朕顷以交趾封邮，非时怙乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147521_comment'></div>广南转运，有状奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147521_comment'></div>言其王师之众，枉被贼臣所害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147521_comment'></div>念其曾未效贡，岂可不为救焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147521_comment'></div>爰命偏师，往安彼俗，固不贪其土地，况寻罢其干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147521_comment'></div>且如京西闲田，素来洼下，就开池沼，良有其由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147521_comment'></div>一则以安泊战船，一则以澄渟水潦，既益皇都之壮丽，亦资士庶之遨游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147521_comment'></div>况其执役之流，皆是下军之士，固不曾差驱编户，妨夺农功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147521_comment'></div>又如髡钳之刑，前王所用，若比之于劓刖，谅有其等差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147521_comment'></div>且令断颈之徒，得遂全身之路，诚非酷法，却大好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147521_comment'></div>自览尔封章，固亦轸余怀抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147521_comment'></div>见令检寻制度，别较重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147521_comment'></div>今后凡有见闻，更在无辞献替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147521_comment'></div>或行或寝，断自朕心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147521_comment'></div>尽节尽忠，勿渝尔志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147521_comment'></div>其于嘉叹，无废寐兴，故兹奖谕，想宜知悉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147521_comment'></div>洎太宗晏驾，皇上嗣位，太宗所赐敕书，已编于《实录》矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147521_comment'></div>先君训谕之言，俾立身扬名以光门族，幸两朝遭遇圣主，身既立而名已扬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147521_comment'></div>先君累赠工部郎中，先夫人追封京兆县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147521_comment'></div>虑年祀寖远，乃撰表墓之碣，立于先君、夫人二坟之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147521_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147521_comment'></div>霜露之感，载怀怵惕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147521_comment'></div>风树之悲，无所迨及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147521_comment'></div>思昼锦还乡而未遂，涕泣西望，因嘉州通判、大理评事万简赴任，托召妹夫杨怀贵与侄嗣宗同访求贞石，以刻斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147521_comment'></div>时咸平五年，岁在壬寅，冬十月十日，嗣子朝请大夫、尚书吏部郎中、兼侍御史知杂事、上柱国、京兆县开国男、食邑三百户、赐紫金鱼袋锡撰述<span class='inlineComment2'>（《咸平集》卷三○，四库全书本。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147521_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1147521'>二十年：按周显德五年当后蜀广政二十一年，必有一误。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1147521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1147521'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147521_0'>⑴ 蜀广政二十年也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1147521_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年10月</a>　十月，在京为吏部郎中，上疏论政事。作品：论政事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八七。）</span><div id='poem_1147308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论政事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147308")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147308'>伏睹内殿起居近罢转对，封章迭送，今已踰年，班行之中，颇有窃议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147308_comment'></div>盖为上章应诏，并无旌酬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147308_comment'></div>失仪被弹，即有责罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147308_comment'></div>虽左右巡使，见失仪不敢不弹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147308_comment'></div>在辅相大臣，知此事不合不奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147308_comment'></div>国家比开言路，将导化源，既欲求其谠言，又不舍其小过，虽弭是非之论，宁符虚伫之怀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147308_comment'></div>况刍荛之词，尚有可采，岂簪缨之列，略无所长？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147308_comment'></div>盖未尝奖一嘉谋，亦未曾降一优诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147308_comment'></div>今郊禋俯近，庆赐将行，可令中书检寻转对，分其优劣，奏其姓名，或降奖谕敕书，或与转改官秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147308_comment'></div>所贵知陛下鉴其用意，感陛下赏其尽忠，表明君好谏之心，彰至仁待下之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147308_comment'></div>臣又睹近敕戒励大臣，谓其不守廉隅，多置资产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147308_comment'></div>禄厚而不知耻者尚应慊恨，官崇而能自省者岂不忧惭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147308_comment'></div>斯乃陛下示之以止足之训词，责之以贪饕之显过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147308_comment'></div>然敕文尚有漏略，事意未得精详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147308_comment'></div>盖文武班官僚不该戒励，似王者命令有失均平，更须颁行诏书，遍下分明条贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147308_comment'></div>在京则已行止绝，外郡则未有指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147308_comment'></div>况近畿阛阓之间，悉大臣资产之地，好利忘义，未知云何擅富兼贫，一至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147308_comment'></div>可以检郡县税籍，自然见公卿户名，其务殖货财，不知纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147308_comment'></div>以贪化下，安得风俗淳和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147308_comment'></div>忘国忧家，岂令官吏廉洁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147308_comment'></div>今敕命施行之后，兼文武豪富之家，可于敕书更布新令，食厚禄者不得与民争利，居崇官者不得在处回图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147308_comment'></div>此乃申明旧章，备载前史，可师古制，以戒贪夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147308_comment'></div>臣又闻有劳绩稍殊，未与区别；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147308_comment'></div>有刑禁久滞，未与辩明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147308_comment'></div>今略举一二言之：有如都官郎中李韶差在广济河，令催辇运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147308_comment'></div>访闻自前界分，每年般得八万馀石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147308_comment'></div>今来李韶界分，一年般得四十五万石，未见酬奖，却归东京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147308_comment'></div>又闻屯卫上将军王汉忠颇知儒书，甚知方略，轻财重义，临事有谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147308_comment'></div>未尝交结中官，亦不曲奉同列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147308_comment'></div>昨赴京阙，似失圣恩，遽令归班，又差典郡，闻于舆论，疑其被谗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147308_comment'></div>今已云亡，孰不嗟惜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147308_comment'></div>臣今闻奏，贵陛下细知，虑侯伯之中，有素秉忠良，不事权贵，介然公直，因致谗言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147308_comment'></div>况临事有谋者求之实难，轻财重义者尤不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147308_comment'></div>良将之体，汉忠得之，未谕此时，弃而不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147308_comment'></div>今若有似王汉忠辈，望陛下选择用之，注意求之，推诚待之，必有英杰，可副指呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147308_comment'></div>又闻齐州制勘公事，颇甚淹延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147308_comment'></div>著作佐郎张检、国子博士张瓘，并是制勘使臣，欲望宣令对扬，问其事意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147308_comment'></div>或法寺受人请嘱，固称奏案未圆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147308_comment'></div>或上司有人主张，使令诣阙披诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147308_comment'></div>张检等必一一闻奏，望陛下亦一一审详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147308_comment'></div>又访闻密院、中书，政出吏胥之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147308_comment'></div>吏胥行遣，只检旧例，无旧例则不行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147308_comment'></div>枢相商议，别无远谋，无远谋则多失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147308_comment'></div>失于边计者，去年失清远军，今年失灵州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147308_comment'></div>失于邦计者，不知府库有无，不知仓廪虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147308_comment'></div>戎夷深入，则请大驾亲往：将帅无功，则取圣慈裁断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147308_comment'></div>所以仓廪盈虚，过不在枢密院；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147308_comment'></div>边防动静，事不属中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147308_comment'></div>因此相承，寖以成例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147308_comment'></div>圣恩若且任用，则不失享富贵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147308_comment'></div>圣旨若令罢免，则不过归班行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147308_comment'></div>昔汉之三公，若罢免则放之归农，若诛戮则赐其自尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147308_comment'></div>其任用既重，则黜责非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147308_comment'></div>操国柄者，所以不敢不尽心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147308_comment'></div>持兵权者，所以不敢不尽节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147308_comment'></div>今则不然，臣下得优逸，而君上但焦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147308_comment'></div>劳逸失于尊卑，实为倒置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147308_comment'></div>故阴阳不顺，水旱不调，法令滋章，盗贼多起，尚率京城父老与百辟千官，五度上章，请加尊号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147308_comment'></div>赖圣君英睿，以为天不可欺，御劄丁宁，示志不可夺，必断来表，深惬群情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147308_comment'></div>由是见宰相以甘言佞上求圣知，以国计军机非己任，盖自来任重责轻之所致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147308_comment'></div>今之所急者，国家帑藏无馀财，仓廪无积粟，但急备边之用，不思经国之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147308_comment'></div>地愈荒而黎民愈贫，事弥繁而资货弥少，官吏自救过不暇，国家欲求治实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147308_comment'></div>若加以水旱之灾，乘以戎夷之患，不知在庙堂者用何智略，总军兵者作何筹谋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147308_comment'></div>臣不晓机务，但以稽古闻于达聪，望陛下详臣所言，听臣所奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147308_comment'></div>赏罚二柄，不必一一问中书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147308_comment'></div>通变万机，不必一一由密院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147308_comment'></div>然后所切者辨认谗谤，察访忠良，速究危乱之已萌，早觉衰微之有渐也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1147308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1147308'><span class='label'>《续资治通鉴长编》原注：</span>「锡自注云：咸平五年九月二十一日。按锡称近敕大臣不守廉隅，多置资产，盖指宰相向敏中也。敏中罢相在十月丁亥，不应在九月便有此奏，当是九月字误，今移付十月末。」<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1147308_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，上疏乞立储。作品：上真宗乞早建储闱。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147290?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗乞早建储闱</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147290")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147290'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147290'>臣窃睹唐宪宗即位改元，元和四年冬十月御宣政殿楼，册皇太子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147290_comment'></div>又按李绛《论事集》，元和三年翰林学士李绛等上言曰：「古先哲王以天下为大器，知一人不可以独理，四海不可以无本，故立太子以副己，设百司以分职，然后人心大定，宗社永宁，有国家者不易之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147290_comment'></div>陛下嗣膺大宝，四年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147290_comment'></div>而储闱未建，典册不行，是开窥觎之端，乖重谨之义，非所以承宗庙、重社稷也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147290_comment'></div>宪宗依所请，下制所司，择日备礼册立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147290_comment'></div>今陛下自纂承大位，改元以来，五年于兹矣，储闱未建，典册不行，岂不虑窥觎之端，岂不思重谨之义？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147290_comment'></div>宜速以宗社永宁为图也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147290_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，上疏论用兵。作品：上真宗论轻于用兵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147294?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗论轻于用兵</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147294")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147294'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147294'>臣窃惟国家断徒以上罪，皆须勘鞠子细，案牍圆备，断官录问，然后行刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147294_comment'></div>其大辟罪，将决断，即给与酒食，命他官监决，虑有称冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147294_comment'></div>及断讫，即录案申奏，奏下大理寺，寺司点检，送至审刑院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147294_comment'></div>院吏披详，如案未圆，理未尽，即罪有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147294_comment'></div>所谓王者之心，重用刑而惜人命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147294_comment'></div>及至北狄骚边，西戎犯境，不先计而后出兵，不先谋而后决战，战失利，即士卒陷殁者既多，人民俘虏者不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147294_comment'></div>不知断徒以上罪，至用刑于大辟，一何用心精密之如彼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147294_comment'></div>而不先计而后出兵，不先谋而后决战，致陷殁士卒者众，俘虏人民者多，一何用心粗疏之如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147294_comment'></div>用心精密之如彼者，是帝王重人命也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147294_comment'></div>用心粗疏之如此者，由将帅轻人命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147294_comment'></div>州郡戮一死罪不当，即罪州郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147294_comment'></div>大理寺、审刑院点检披详漏略，各罪官吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147294_comment'></div>洎至士卒陷殁，人民俘虏，则宰相不过罢免归班为尚书，将帅不过黜降其官为庶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147294_comment'></div>此乃朝廷用刑轻重之相远也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1147294_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状谢许谏事。作品：谢圣旨许谏事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢圣旨许谏事状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1002年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147414")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147414'>右，臣前月二十八日长春殿伏蒙圣慈宣喻，臣昨所奏之事，「朕一一披览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147414_comment'></div>又以其人介然，别无朋党，可耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147414_comment'></div>仍旧令臣知之，即不得泄漏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147414_comment'></div>兼再奉圣旨：「有可奏之事，但上实封，以广朕之闻见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147414_comment'></div>臣受命已来，今已浃旬，内省惶惧，何以堪胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147414_comment'></div>所念臣实何人，一无识见，但以直道，早幸逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147414_comment'></div>先帝以臣遇事敢言，特降敕书奖喻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147414_comment'></div>陛下以臣所进文字<span class='inlineComment2'>（隐名。）</span>，内降札子褒称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147414_comment'></div>荷两朝优假之恩，实千载遭逢之幸，敢不益坚夙志，弥励愚诚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147414_comment'></div>天至高，虽管窥讵识于运行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147414_comment'></div>日至明，而圭测亦知其长短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147414_comment'></div>今陛下嗣守大位，临御兆民，博访贤良，躬亲机务，日新厥德，夕惕若厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147414_comment'></div>以大舜好问之意，文王犹勤之心，昭九庙垂休之灵，保万世无疆之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147414_comment'></div>臣谓萧墙之外，有可闻之事，非因奏覆，固不可得而知，况于远者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147414_comment'></div>清禁之中，有欲见之事，不因求访，固不可得而见，况不求访乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147414_comment'></div>然为臣事君，孰敢不尽忠节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147414_comment'></div>明主待下，常欲闻其直言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147414_comment'></div>《春秋》曰：「子好直言，必思自免于难」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147414_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「既明且哲，以保其身」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147414_comment'></div>故《象》、《系》示吉凶之微，冀君臣保始终之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147414_comment'></div>所以君不密则失臣，失臣者为大臣所憎嫌，为近臣所排斥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147414_comment'></div>憎嫌之深者，则谗构其罪戾，而置之于刑戮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147414_comment'></div>排斥之远者，则诬枉其过咎，而逐之于遐荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147414_comment'></div>此由不密在于君，而所失在于臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147414_comment'></div>伏念臣识既凡庸，性惟愚直，供职兼于台宪，莅事在于狱刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147414_comment'></div>固无微劳，但忧获罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147414_comment'></div>若非陛下与臣为主，则大臣必因事见诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147414_comment'></div>故逐度所上实封，皆乞留中不出，盖虑事不密，而身已危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147414_comment'></div>况臣无才略，安足广陛下见闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147414_comment'></div>臣之愚蒙，敢不守陛下宣喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147414_comment'></div>忧畏惶恐，倍万常情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1147414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1002&endYear=1002')">1002年</a>　本年，在京为吏部郎中，上奏状乞荫长子田庆远。作品：奏荫长男庆远二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年3月1日</a>　三月一日，在京为吏部郎中，再上疏论拣选强壮。作品：上真宗论拣选强壮失信。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗论拣选强壮失信</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平六年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147296")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147296'>臣伏睹去秋已来，霖雨作沴，近畿诸处，水潦为灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147296_comment'></div>虽闻检覆蠲免租税，又闻相度低下，开决沟渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147296_comment'></div>虽忧恤之心，似有所济；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147296_comment'></div>而利害相半，莫知适从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147296_comment'></div>古者不夺农时，虑妨营种，或遇歉岁，即念困穷，故有赈贷粮储，除放徭役，免令凋瘵，不至流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147296_comment'></div>今国家为少阙军兵，防备边戍，遂于曹、郓、宋、亳、陈、蔡、汝、颍之间，点集乡村，拣选强壮，得五七万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147296_comment'></div>访闻始降宣命指挥，只令在本城防守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147296_comment'></div>及至奏闻都数，即并抽赴京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147296_comment'></div>昨近臣何以商量，如此失信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147296_comment'></div>令下民皆怀怨望，岂得无词？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147296_comment'></div>况陛下常好读书，有儒臣时得侍讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147296_comment'></div>《春秋》谓「君命无二」，又曰「信不由中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147296_comment'></div>谅在圣聪，尽达微旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147296_comment'></div>岂有命令既宣于群下，而诚信不由于厥中？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147296_comment'></div>若外国差人在京探事，事无巨细，境外既必尽知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147296_comment'></div>知而图谋，边上未得安静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147296_comment'></div>其所谋者，谓古者以民为邦本，食为民天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147296_comment'></div>今国家取丁壮为兵，以失邦本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147296_comment'></div>以灾伤去食，宁有民天？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147296_comment'></div>粮储何止无馀，边备亦恐不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147296_comment'></div>以此得计，以此乘时，此外国所谋之小者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147296_comment'></div>其所谋之大者，以关西去年秋稼不登，京东今岁春种已失，国家营救之不暇，庙堂图虑之未精，欲以新集未惯之兵，授非才无勇之将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147296_comment'></div>侥倖求胜，轻敌寡谋，此外国所谋之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147296_comment'></div>加以自春以来，多阴少晴，每遇朔风，其来数日不定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147296_comment'></div>变阳春和平之令，入边塞动静之占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147296_comment'></div>臣不晓占书，不知兵略，但以经史所言之事，求灾祥可见之證，以愚意裁量，望圣慈采纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147296_comment'></div>虽兵者凶器，不得已而用之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147296_comment'></div>民为邦本，不得已而取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147296_comment'></div>今五七万人并离农亩，日近更差使臣拣点，岂无物议忧虞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147296_comment'></div>以灾沴之馀，寇盗若起，适足为戎狄之利，有劳宵旰之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147296_comment'></div>检灾伤乃是虚名，行赈贷且非实事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147296_comment'></div>斯乃今日之务最急也，非时之患可忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147296_comment'></div>臣谓非十年不足以聚蓄财货，非十年不足以生育黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147296_comment'></div>二十年间，治之得其宜则无虑，治之失其宜则有患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147296_comment'></div>非二十年，尚未能聚蓄财货，生育黎元，况临事欲制置乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147296_comment'></div>望陛下思今日之急务，虑非时之所忧，示信以结之，善谋以成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147296_comment'></div>若信不由中，事出虑外，恐国家多难，自今日始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147296_comment'></div>臣受先帝拔擢，不敢不言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147296_comment'></div>臣受陛下指挥，不敢不奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1147296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年5月6日</a>　五月六日，在京为吏部郎中，迁右谏议大夫，有致谢笏记。作品：谢改谏议大夫笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147361' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147361' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147361?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢改谏议大夫笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年5月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147361")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147361_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147361'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147361'>臣锡言：伏蒙圣慈赐臣官告、敕牒，授臣右谏议大夫，散官、勋、封、赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147361_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147361_comment'></div>伏念臣遭逢景运，扬历官途，惭无丝发之微劳，上答君亲之大造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147361_comment'></div>岂谓天恩曲被，宸眷猥临，置诸侍从之班，授以箴规之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147361_comment'></div>弥忧官谤，上负圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147361_comment'></div>敢忘献替之诚，上答照临之德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147361_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年5月</a>　五月，在京为右谏议大夫，兼史馆修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年8月6日</a>　八月六日，在京为右谏议大夫，上疏乞询求将相。作品：上真宗乞询求将相。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上真宗乞询求将相</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平六年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147297")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147297'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147297'>臣尝读《唐太宗实录》，见李靖文武材略，隋将韩擒虎即其类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147297_comment'></div>靖再与擒虎论兵，未尝不称善，抚之曰：「可与论孙吴之术也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147297_comment'></div>初，事隋为殿内直长，吏部尚书牛弘见而重之，曰：「李靖，王佐才也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147297_comment'></div>今国家自先帝平晋之后，与戎狄结隙，将相旧人，相次薨谢，边鄙间州县，屡为戎狄所陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147297_comment'></div>皇威不振久矣，时议乃以将相无人亦久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147297_comment'></div>即不知今来朝廷公卿大夫间，有如韩擒虎与李靖论兵否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147297_comment'></div>有人如牛弘知李靖有王佐才否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147297_comment'></div>若有人能论兵，有人负王佐才，未审陛下知之否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147297_comment'></div>有人善论兵，有人负王佐才，乃是帝王合先知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147297_comment'></div>自来皇城司差人探事，又别差探皇城司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147297_comment'></div>探事人如此察探，京城民间，事无巨细，皆达圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147297_comment'></div>近又差朝臣为巡抚使，及差朝臣以点检酒务名目，出外采访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147297_comment'></div>所采访之事，不过民间利病，不过官吏能否而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147297_comment'></div>即未闻委公卿大夫察访善论兵之人，询求有王佐之才者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147297_comment'></div>由是见所求者琐屑，而所忽者远大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147297_comment'></div>陛下若以宗庙社稷为忧，以生灵为念，即宜以远大为务，求将相为急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147297_comment'></div>臣每奉圣谟，令陈鄙见，仰祈英睿，特赐披详。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1147297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年12月</a>　十二月，在京为右谏议大夫，上奏状乞荫次子田庆馀。作品：奏荫次男庆馀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏荫次男庆馀状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147418")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147418'>右，臣伏以千年庆诞之辰，万寿延长之日，臣辄披丹素，上告慈仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147418_comment'></div>臣男庆馀，训以诗书，教之忠孝，幸因圣节，愿在宦途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147418_comment'></div>仰祈日照之明，俯鉴葵倾之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147418_comment'></div>干冒宸扆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147418_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年12月11日</a>　十二月十一日，在京为右谏议大夫，作遗表，卒。作品：遗表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>遗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年12月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147351")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147351'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147351'>臣锡言：臣闻修短之期，固有定数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147351_comment'></div>臣子之志，空恋明时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147351_comment'></div>忍死遗言，瞑目长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147351_comment'></div>臣诚悲诚咽，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147351_comment'></div>伏望陛下以慈俭守位，以清净化人，居安思危，居理思乱，与宗庙社稷为福，与天下亿兆为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147351_comment'></div>臣无任感咽悲哀之至，谨上遗表，永辞圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147351_comment'></div>臣诚哀诚咽，顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1147351_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1003&endYear=1003')">1003年</a>　本年，在京为右谏议大夫，患病告假，上奏状谢传宣抚问。作品：告假谢传宣抚问。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>告假谢传宣抚问状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1003年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147417")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147417'>右，臣昨日伏蒙圣慈以臣有状，暂请患假，特差中使传宣抚问，兼依允所奏，不差医官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147417_comment'></div>伏念臣拙于脉理，昧于摄生，致久病未安，服饵少效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147417_comment'></div>岂谓圣恩之轸恻，俯怜疾苦之缠绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147417_comment'></div>虽自来内殿起居，不敢告免；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147417_comment'></div>因昨日随班舞蹈，顿觉衰羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147417_comment'></div>以此须至上言，仰干睿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147417_comment'></div>犬马之疾，既已医治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147417_comment'></div>君亲之恩，曲加勉喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147417_comment'></div>情有所感，不觉涕零。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1147417_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='faf58c777e494eb4a90f1d01f6b60d8a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("faf58c777e494eb4a90f1d01f6b60d8a");'><span id='faf58c777e494eb4a90f1d01f6b60d8a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=976&endYear=976')">976年</a>，37岁</div><div id='faf58c777e494eb4a90f1d01f6b60d8a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>四月，在洛阳，与宋白同游。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>四月，在洛阳，与宋准结识。<br /></div>

灵宝

-----title
宣城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0ce59f7d56174ab2bbe338de1022d161_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0ce59f7d56174ab2bbe338de1022d161");'><span id='0ce59f7d56174ab2bbe338de1022d161_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=980')">979-980年</a>，40-41岁</div><div id='0ce59f7d56174ab2bbe338de1022d161' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年</a>　春，到宣州通判任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年9月</a>　九月，在宣州通判任，登叠嶂楼，作赋。作品：叠嶂楼赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《咸平集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1147147' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147147' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147147?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叠嶂楼赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（979年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147147")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147147_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147147'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147147'>宛陵之丘，玄晖旧游，城连延兮百雉，世绵历兮千秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147147_comment'></div>流水白云，惜依然而在览；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147147_comment'></div>遗风往事，信恍若兮如浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147147_comment'></div>余以丹陛策名，皇华奉使，通莅于此，乘春以至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147147_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1147147", 1147147, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>驿梅</span>江柳，动游宦之芳怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147147_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1147147", 1147147, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>风观</span>露台，起高明之逸意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147147_comment'></div>叠嶂居先，登之悦焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147147_comment'></div>凭落絮之危槛，向飞花之晚天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147147_comment'></div>复岭连冈，峙昭亭兮作镇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147147_comment'></div>平芜远树，引句水兮为川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147147_comment'></div>因而以古兴怀，临高凝睇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147147_comment'></div>自春秋战国之后，洎吴魏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1147147", 1147147, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>鼎分</span>之际，干戈僭王，乘舆拟帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147147_comment'></div>斯为形胜之区，恃以控临之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147147_comment'></div>襟带三江，咽喉五湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147147_comment'></div>归句践兮称越，隶夫差兮曰吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147147_comment'></div>比弈棋之靡定，唯霸略兮能图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147147_comment'></div>方今禹迹重新，尧封复古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147147_comment'></div>衔王命于北阙，咏皇风于南浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147147_comment'></div>登高而赋，怜宋玉以才多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147147_comment'></div>览景自怡，非仲宣之思苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147147_comment'></div>江渺渺兮涵春，草萋萋兮感人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147147_comment'></div>指苏杭之达道，介常歙兮为邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147147_comment'></div>两桨何归，引迥眸于天际；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147147_comment'></div>微云似画，带斜阳于水滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147147_comment'></div>既而阅谢守之诗，苍苔满石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147147_comment'></div>览独孤之文，芳尘在壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147147_comment'></div>杏花含露，念昔我之来时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147147_comment'></div>菊蕊迎霜，乃今余之暇日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147147_comment'></div>岁云丰稔，民之悦逸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147147_comment'></div>思命俦兮啸侣，聊登楼兮自适。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1147147_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年</a>　本年，在宣州通判任，作朱适考词。作品：录事参军朱适。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷三〇。朱适，生平不详。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_81802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81802'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81802'>近遣司宾小吏时，寄书兼寄十篇诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81802'>自惭不是阳春曲，谁敢徼求作者知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1147429_comment'></div>擒捕盗贼，徵督赋舆，询会有司，比较终考，无宣省责罚，无市肆赊苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147429_comment'></div>临莅疲民，庶几奉职。<div class='inline' -----title
大名
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='704ffb21006c4c2d928eb68ae6cd62d4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("704ffb21006c4c2d928eb68ae6cd62d4");'><span id='704ffb21006c4c2d928eb68ae6cd62d4_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年11月</a>　十一月，随宋太宗亲征，在大名府献《圣主平戎歌》作品：圣主平戎歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_81818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81818?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣方平戎歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81818")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81818_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81818'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81818'>玉关秋早霜飞速，代马新羁逞南牧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81818'>胡人背信窥汉边，刻箭为书召戎族。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81818'>渔阳烽火照甘泉，疆吏飞笺至御前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81818'>睿谋英武何神速，銮舆自欲平三边。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81818'>百万羽林随驾出，杀气皇威先破敌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81818'>贼臣丧阵遽奔逃<span class='inlineComment2'>（毛本作隔河御盖争欢呼）</span>，漳水波清因驻跸。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81818'>宫锦战袍花斗新，绣鞯珠络金麒麟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81818'>天颜威武不可犯，垂鞭按辔视群臣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81818'>汉皇曾上单于台，壮心磊落侔风雷。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81818'>比量英武不足数，圣文神武双全才。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81818'>势可驱山塞沧海，紫气逶迤龙凤盖。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81818'>金花簇敛若星罗，宝细乘舆翼云旆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81818'>涂山禹帝戮防风，涿鹿蚩尤死战锋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81818'>锋铓俱染玄黄血，争如不陈而成功。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81818'>示暇皇欢有馀意，御笔题诗饶绮思。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81818'>翰林承旨先受宣，西掖词臣及近侍。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81818'>诏命交酬继和来，君臣道合何如是。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81818'>和气感天天地宁，日融瑞景笼八纮。<div id='poem_sentence_18_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_81818'>风生旗旆翻龙凤，霜严鼓角喧雷霆。<div id='poem_sentence_19_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_81818'>海神来受军门职，太上祷兵尊帝德。<div id='poem_sentence_20_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_81818'>牢笼万国顿天纲，天纲恢恢恩信广。<div id='poem_sentence_21_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_81818'>胡儿溃散何比之，大明升空逃魍魉。<div id='poem_sentence_22_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_81818'>漳川地阔霜草平，合闱会猎布天兵。<div id='poem_sentence_23_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_81818'>六师雄勇一百万，六班侍卫交纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_24_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_81818'>铁衣间耀金锁甲，鼓旗杂错枪刀鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_27_81818'>雕鹗狰狞搦狐兔，花骢跃龙骄在御。<div id='poem_sentence_27_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_81818'>弓圆明月金镞飞，妖狐中镞骇天机。<div id='poem_sentence_28_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_81818'>兵师会合如波注，山呼万岁震边陲。<div id='poem_sentence_29_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_81818'>东海为樽盛美酒，斟酌酒浆掺北斗。<div id='poem_sentence_30_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_81818'>鸾刀割肉若邱陵，军声汹如狮子吼。<div id='poem_sentence_31_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_81818'>三公拜舞百辟随，鸣珂飞鞚星离离。<div id='poem_sentence_32_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_81818'>云舒二十有四纛，传宣罢猎整鱼丽。<div id='poem_sentence_33_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_81818'>胜气威声压千古，堪笑骊山称讲武。<div id='poem_sentence_34_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_81818'>直馆微臣乐扈随，太平盛事今亲睹。<div id='poem_sentence_35_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_81818'>会看金泥封禅仪，拜章别献新歌诗。<div id='poem_sentence_36_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_81818'>歌诗何以容易进，为受文明天子知<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《咸平集》卷一八）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_37_81818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_81818'></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_81818_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ff621897bfe4423693320a7374f49b36_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ff621897bfe4423693320a7374f49b36");'><span id='ff621897bfe4423693320a7374f49b36_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年</a>，42岁</div><div id='ff621897bfe4423693320a7374f49b36' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年9月</a>　九月，在大名府为河北南路转运副使，上表谢敕书奖谕。作品：谢敕书奖谕上章表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147319' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147319' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147319?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢敕书奖喻上章表</a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147319")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147319_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147319'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147319'>臣锡言：臣今月十九日伏奉敕书，以臣所贡封章，特加奖喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147319_comment'></div>仰荷皇明之鉴，宁胜光宠之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147319_comment'></div>荣抃徬徨，启处无地<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147319_comment'></div>臣闻敢谏非易，纳谏尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147319_comment'></div>盖以臣下抗言，多致触鳞之怒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147319_comment'></div>帝王至贵，骇闻逆耳之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147319_comment'></div>茍非天鉴昭彰，臣诚果敢，何以见圣主优容之德，何以伸直臣謇谔之心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147319_comment'></div>所以陶唐盛时，犹设登闻之鼓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147319_comment'></div>有虞至理，许书告善之旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147319_comment'></div>盖思诱敢言之臣，亦欲闻未知之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147319_comment'></div>伏念臣遭逢陛下，尘忝谏官，虽精诚之中，思有所报，而激切之志，未有所伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147319_comment'></div>近者伏蒙圣恩，荣有差遣，当金殿入辞之际，洎天阶宣上之时，遂以实封，直进御座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147319_comment'></div>小臣愚昧，所见寻常，妄言军国要机，朝廷大体，退而恐惧，伏待诛夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147319_comment'></div>然于忠亮之心，少赎贪饕之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147319_comment'></div>岂期圣造特轸皇慈，优降诏书，褒称贱品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147319_comment'></div>仍颁御札，宣示群臣，见皇王鉴烛之明，示天地包容之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147319_comment'></div>朝廷虽理，而陛下未以为理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147319_comment'></div>黎庶虽安，而陛下未以为安，自此言路洞开，朝纲益整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147319_comment'></div>所谓尧惜一夫之不获，舜于一善而悦闻，成汤之德益新，大禹之谟自远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147319_comment'></div>太平已致，比屋可封，岂独微臣之荣，谅实天下之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147319_comment'></div>臣无任感恩荷圣、激切屏营之至。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1147319'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1147319_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年9月</a>　九月，在大名府为河北南路转运副使，上表进祝寿诗。作品：进乾明节祝圣寿诗表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。孙谱系此文于雍熙四年，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进乾明节祝圣寿诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147318")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147318'>臣锡言：伏以节逢降诞，运属升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147318_comment'></div>《禹贡》万邦，贺紫禁延龄之庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147318_comment'></div>《汉官》百辟，有黄金为寿之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147318_comment'></div>若以诗绮靡于缘情，颂形容于盛德，上采赓歌之旨，旁宗《大雅》之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147318_comment'></div>律以新声，文之近体，为理世变风之什，庆良辰绕电之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147318_comment'></div>用表精虔，实符忠愿<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147318_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下睿圣凝图，文明致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147318_comment'></div>三雍礼乐，敦风教于昌期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147318_comment'></div>万国黎元，悦仁和于太古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147318_comment'></div>封人受赐，欢呼祝寿之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147318_comment'></div>丹凤有灵，鼓舞闻《韶》之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147318_comment'></div>伏念臣素无文艺，叨受皇恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147318_comment'></div>备位谏垣，未举箴规之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147318_comment'></div>出官河朔，惭非经略之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147318_comment'></div>子牟双阙之心，欣逢令节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147318_comment'></div>尧帝千龄之福，愿与称觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147318_comment'></div>情动于中，诗声于外，因成《乾明节祝圣寿》七言诗十九首，谨缮写进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147318_comment'></div>干冒宸聪，臣无任瞻天恋圣、庆抃激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1147318_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年9月</a>　九月，在大名府为河北南路转运副使，上祝寿诗十九首。作品：乾明节祝圣寿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于雍熙四年，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_53763' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53763' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53763?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乾明节祝圣寿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53763")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53763_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_53763_0'>① 原注：十九首，内七首遗落。四库本注：此下河朔。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53763'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53763'>百辟欢呼降诞辰，金樽献酒愿千春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53763'>延年不假丹砂效，亨寿全由圣德新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53763'>古物进来兼药鼎，画图呈处有仙人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53763'>君恩若赏歌诗意，应念甘泉侍从臣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53763'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53763_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53769?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53769'>生日称觞自六宫，香焚甲观画堂中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53769'>太平历数归英主，上寿年龄属圣躬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53769'>玉树有花因瑞雪，钧天呈曲在虚空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53769'>三公进贺祯祥事，先奏河清达帝聪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53769'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53769_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53768' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53768' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53768?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53768_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53768'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53768'>吾皇享福自无涯，百辟称觞礼数加。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53768'>韶乐揭天如上界，炉香映日似轻霞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53768'>空中紫气圆成盖，海上蟠桃暖放花。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53768'>感应圣人千万寿，神仙日月属官家。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53768'></div><div target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53767_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53767'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53767'>皇朝令节号乾明，万国嘻嘻若大庭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53767'>多士进诗随禹贡，千官献酒祝尧龄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53767'>天香晓降闻仙乐，南海秋来见寿星。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53767'>黎庶更思瞻盛礼，待封日观禅云亭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53767'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53767_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53786' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53786' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_53786_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53786'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53786'>鸾杯进酒近天颜，拜舞风清响佩环。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53786'>瑞日正高重御宴，摵鞭才定再催班。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53786'>霓旌绛节仙家乐，金阙银台海上山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53786'>绮陌晓<span id='poem_sentence_4_53786_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53765?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53765'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53765'>圣节祥烟蔼御炉，殿庭严肃响山呼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53765'>远方拜表来朝贡，兼贺虹流电绕枢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_53764_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53764'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53764'>汉家台榭与天通，甲观苍苍紫气中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53764'>佳节夜来宣受贺，寿杯朝进祝延洪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53764'>管弦嘈囋惊花发，同日晴<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作清）</span>和向雪融。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53764'>宴次宫鹦忽飞过，随呼万岁语玲珑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53764_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53764'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53764_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53762?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53762'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53762'>君王降诞继陶唐，每至嘉辰睹异祥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
