id='poem_sentence_2_53762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53762'>万国人臣皆悦乐，巍巍圣德自无疆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53762'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53762_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53761?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53761'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53761'>庆诞长生宝殿中，非烟五色覆诸宫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53761'>酒为天禄资君寿，曲奏霓裳乐帝聪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53761'>悲翠帘前云气紫，珊瑚枝上雪花红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53761'>太平天子闻称贺，先喜年年过<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作遇）</span>岁丰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53761'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53761_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53760?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53760'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53760'>圣节思归会帝京，得随班列祝文明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53760'>河清见底为嘉瑞，海水无波表太平。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53760'>月夜忽闻仙乐奏，宫中时有彩云生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53760'>诗成拜表同封进，愿继词臣雅韵声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53760'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53760_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53787?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53787_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53787'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53787'>日上扶桑第一枝，东方楼阁曙光时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53787'>万邦将启乾明宴，两制应宣御制诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53787'>乐感羽毛皆率舞，神和福禄自来宜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53787'>谏垣班列天颜近，暂乞归朝侍玉墀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53787'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53787_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53766?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53766_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53766'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53766'>河朔虽云近帝乡，时逢庆诞祝君王。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53766'>身心常在三清路，晓夕先装一炷香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53766'>圣寿如山随地久，恩光似日与天长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53766'>策臣所贵无他物，唯献新诪<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作诗）</span>十九章。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53766'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年10月</a>　十月，在大名府为河北南路转运副使，上疏论边事，再获嘉奖。作品：论边事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《宋朝诸臣奏议》卷一二九。）</span><div id='poem_1147298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论边事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（太平兴国七年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（981年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147298")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147298'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147298'>臣闻动静之机，不可妄举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147298_comment'></div>安危之理，不可轻言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147298_comment'></div>利害相生，变易不定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147298_comment'></div>用舍无惑，思虑必精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147298_comment'></div>夫动静之机不可妄举者，动谓用兵，静谓持重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147298_comment'></div>应动而静，则养寇以生奸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147298_comment'></div>应静而动，则失时以败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147298_comment'></div>动静中节，乃得其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147298_comment'></div>今北鄙绎骚，盖亦有以居边任者，规羊马细利为捷，矜捕斩小胜为功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147298_comment'></div>贾怨结仇，乘秋致寇，召戎起舋，职此之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147298_comment'></div>伏愿申饬将帅，审固封守，勿尚小功，许通互市，素获蕃口，抚而还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147298_comment'></div>如此不出五载，河朔之民得务三农之业，亭障之地可积十年之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147298_comment'></div>前岁俶扰边陲，亲迂革辂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147298_comment'></div>今兹张皇声势，颇动人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147298_comment'></div>若猃狁来侵，六龙夙驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147298_comment'></div>戎羯既退，万乘方归，是皆失我机先，落其术内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147298_comment'></div>所以五月兵不得分屯，农时人不得务敛，劳顿斁耗，可胜言乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147298_comment'></div>军国大端，固当慎始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147298_comment'></div>戎族未乱，未烦强图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147298_comment'></div>狄势未衰，何劳力取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147298_comment'></div>待其乱而取之则克，乘其衰而兵之则降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147298_comment'></div>既心服而志归，则力省而功倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147298_comment'></div>自古贪利荐食，不独匈奴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147298_comment'></div>邀功起戎，亦自边将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147298_comment'></div>当鉴前轨，以恢永图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147298_comment'></div>昔汉安帝时，东夷犯境，连年不息，汉颇患之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147298_comment'></div>其主云亡，其子继立，汉乃命使吊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147298_comment'></div>东夷感悦，还汉生口，一隅晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147298_comment'></div>至于南蛮，亦尝畔涣，始由边吏增赋，乘怨为寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147298_comment'></div>光武时西戎犯边，班彪请置护羌校尉，通其货之有无，治其人之冤枉，塞垣遂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147298_comment'></div>诚愿考古道，务远图，示绥怀万国之心，用驾驭四夷之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147298_comment'></div>事戒辄发，理在深谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147298_comment'></div>臣又谓安危之理，不可轻言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147298_comment'></div>国家务大体、求至理则安，舍近谋远、劳而无功则危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147298_comment'></div>为君有常道，为臣有常职，是务大体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147298_comment'></div>上不拒谏，下不隐情，是求至理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147298_comment'></div>帝王之道，忌萌欲心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147298_comment'></div>汉武帝躬秉武节，遂登单于之台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147298_comment'></div>唐太宗手结雨衣，往伐辽东之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147298_comment'></div>率义动之众，徇无厌之求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147298_comment'></div>输常赋之财，奉不急之役：是舍近谋远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147298_comment'></div>沙漠穷荒，得之无用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147298_comment'></div>夷狄遗种，杀之更生：是劳而无功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147298_comment'></div>位下秩卑，敢言者少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147298_comment'></div>言而见听，则进而无疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147298_comment'></div>言而不从，则退而惧罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147298_comment'></div>臣又谓利害相生，变易不定者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147298_comment'></div>兵书曰：「不能尽知用兵之害者，则不能尽知用兵之利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147298_comment'></div>盖事有可进而退，则害之成事至焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147298_comment'></div>可退而进，则利用之事去焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147298_comment'></div>可速而缓，则利必从之而失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147298_comment'></div>可缓而速，则害必由之而致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147298_comment'></div>可诛而赦，则奸宄之心或有时而生害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147298_comment'></div>可赦而诛，则忠勇之人或无心而利国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147298_comment'></div>可赏而罚，则有以害勤劳之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147298_comment'></div>可罚而赏，则有以利僭踰之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147298_comment'></div>能审利害，则为聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147298_comment'></div>以天下之耳听之则聪，以天下之目视之则明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147298_comment'></div>故《书》曰：「明四目，达四聪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147298_comment'></div>惟此聪明，在无壅塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147298_comment'></div>尽去相蒙之弊，乃协知几之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147298_comment'></div>臣又谓取舍不可以有惑，故曰「孟贲之狐疑，不如童子之必至」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147298_comment'></div>思虑不可以不精，故曰「差若毫釐，缪以千里」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147298_comment'></div>自国家图燕以来，连兵未解，财用不得不耗，人臣不得不忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147298_comment'></div>恢复吊伐之名，虽建洪业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147298_comment'></div>可否祸福之实，宜留圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147298_comment'></div>愿陛下精其思虑，决其取舍，无使旷日持久，穷兵极武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147298_comment'></div>为国大计，不得不然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1147298_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fe017966c61f4947bfe07c7d300abf35_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fe017966c61f4947bfe07c7d300abf35");'><span id='fe017966c61f4947bfe07c7d300abf35_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年</a>，43岁</div><div id='fe017966c61f4947bfe07c7d300abf35' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年</a>　春，在大名府为河北南路转运副使，上疏劾相州知州张洎部内不治。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年</a>　本年，在大名府为河北南路转运副使，改知相州，除右补阙，有谢表。作品：谢除右补阙表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147320' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147320' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147320?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除右补阙表</a><span class='authorDate'>（982年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147320")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147320_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147320'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147320'>臣锡言：臣今月二十日，于天雄军得河北南路转运副使李琯差军将赍送进奏院递到官告一通、敕牒一道，伏蒙圣慈授臣右补阙，馀如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147320_comment'></div>纶言进秩，谏省增荣，祗荷宠章，徬徨交积<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147320_comment'></div>伏念臣叨居侍从，有玷清华，薄才误受于圣知，非次骤分于忧寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147320_comment'></div>积粟备边之策，岂是所能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147320_comment'></div>丰财利国之谋，又非素习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147320_comment'></div>伏遇礼行清庙，功告圆丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147320_comment'></div>庆泽惟新，虽下周于庶品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147320_comment'></div>优恩特异，俄叙转于华资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147320_comment'></div>臣每读《唐书》，载观名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147320_comment'></div>裴度蕴三公之业，历此清途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147320_comment'></div>吴兢有良史之才，当兹衮职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147320_comment'></div>臣识非淹邃，辞愧菁英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147320_comment'></div>直馆踰年，未举编修之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147320_comment'></div>乘轺将命，俄兼飞挽之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147320_comment'></div>微效弗伸，荣迁骤至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147320_comment'></div>太平无事，忠言宁补于皇猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147320_comment'></div>封禅有期，观礼但思于丹阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147320_comment'></div>臣伏限所守，不获奔诣宸阶，无任瞻天恋圣、感恩激切、欢呼屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1147320_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年12月14日</a>　十二月十四日，在知相州任，上疏言事。作品：上太宗条奏事宜。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太宗条奏事宜<span class='inlineComment2'>（太平兴国七年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（982年12月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147289")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147289'>臣备位谏垣，出官河朔，虽励忠勤之节，未伸謇谔之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147289_comment'></div>尸素自知，彷徨益切，何以分陛下忧勤之寄，何以副朝廷委用之恩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147289_comment'></div>敢不夙夜有思，涓埃欲效？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147289_comment'></div>愿以刍荛之见，上希英圣之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147289_comment'></div>今陛下命以颁条，委之理郡，亲民之心，无先于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147289_comment'></div>茍所理之郡事简狱空，所亲之民风淳俗厚，所谓莅民有术，御下有能，足以副朝廷任用之恩，有以彰陛下忧勤之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147289_comment'></div>然事有无从而得简，狱有无因而久空，民风未致于淳和，物俗未臻于淳厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147289_comment'></div>虽有莅民之术，无得而施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147289_comment'></div>虽有御下之才，无从而设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147289_comment'></div>况臣闇懦，御下非才，以臣愚蒙，莅民无术，但可言其久弊，恤其未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147289_comment'></div>久弊者，昔近并门，邻于敌境，备边之费，御寇之兵，二十馀年，民不遑息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147289_comment'></div>未安者，今以北狄，迩于塞垣，屯兵御戎，飞刍挽粟，三十馀郡，民不甚丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147289_comment'></div>筦榷货财，网利太密；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147289_comment'></div>躬亲机务，纶旨稍频。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147289_comment'></div>臣所谓网利太密者，酒曲之利，但要增盈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147289_comment'></div>商税之利，但求出剩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147289_comment'></div>或偶有出剩，不询出剩之由；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147289_comment'></div>或偶有亏欠，必责亏欠之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147289_comment'></div>递年比算，只管增加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147289_comment'></div>递月较量，不管欠折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147289_comment'></div>然国家军兵数广，支用处多，课利不得不如此征收，筦榷不得不如此比较。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147289_comment'></div>穷尽取财之路，莫甚于兹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147289_comment'></div>疏通殖货之源，未闻适变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147289_comment'></div>似不知止，殊无定期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147289_comment'></div>今乞国家以关市之征，定其常数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147289_comment'></div>酒曲之利，授以常规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147289_comment'></div>或偶有增加，不更求出剩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147289_comment'></div>或偶有亏折，即可令于出剩时补填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147289_comment'></div>且如州县征科，农桑税赋，年丰则未闻加纳，岁歉则许之停征，自然理得其中，民知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147289_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147289_comment'></div>民生于利，亦犹鱼生于水也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147289_comment'></div>民困于利，又如水涸于鱼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147289_comment'></div>愿更生于谠议，别布新条，当生民既庶之时，是求理酌中之际，天下幸甚，海内幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147289_comment'></div>臣所谓纶旨稍频者，臣尝读扬子《法言》曰：「圣人之道犹日中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147289_comment'></div>又尝览太公《六韬》曰：「圣人之道犹龙首」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147289_comment'></div>龙首谓高视而远听，日中谓融明而烛幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147289_comment'></div>是知君有居上之威仪，臣有奉上之职业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147289_comment'></div>君道务简，简则号令审而人易从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147289_comment'></div>臣道务勤，勤则职业修而事无壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147289_comment'></div>臣伏见陛下忧民太过，视事太勤，每日早于崇德殿受百僚之朝，至日午于讲武殿视万机之事，或进呈申状，或拣阅军人，或躬问缧囚，或亲观战马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147289_comment'></div>自匦而进者，或详其词理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147289_comment'></div>挝鼓以闻者，或询彼冤诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147289_comment'></div>皆金口言词，人人省问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147289_comment'></div>天心揆度，一一区分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147289_comment'></div>有以见陛下劳万机之神，自此见臣下亏事君之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147289_comment'></div>况今四方无事，多垒尽平，何以劳陛下如此太勤，何以使三公因此无愧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147289_comment'></div>盖陛下虑四聪或有所未达，万机或有所未知，文王之心，遂乾乾而夕惕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147289_comment'></div>成汤之意，贵孜孜于日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147289_comment'></div>然陛下何不移此勤劳以求贤，何不改此精专于选士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147289_comment'></div>谏官则置之左右，御史即委以纠弹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147289_comment'></div>给事中当材者，许之封驳诏书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147289_comment'></div>起居郎有文者，命之纪录言动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147289_comment'></div>百职如是，各举其业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147289_comment'></div>千官如是，各得其人，则何忧事不允釐，何虑民不受赐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147289_comment'></div>今有司指挥，多以劄子取圣旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147289_comment'></div>官员注拟，必须引见听敕裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147289_comment'></div>事若允当，则既由宸衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147289_comment'></div>事若未当，则亦归睿断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147289_comment'></div>如此皆劳天听，安用有司？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147289_comment'></div>致陛下视事太勤，忧民太过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147289_comment'></div>况宫阙乃尊严之地，轩墀列清切之班，可以延伫贤良，询求理道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147289_comment'></div>岂宜使押来囚系，或病患军人，或虚词越诉之徒，或侥倖希恩之辈，引之便殿，得面天颜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147289_comment'></div>陛下则随事指挥，临时与夺，其间有骤承顾问，上惧天威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147289_comment'></div>或偶有敷陈，稍惬圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147289_comment'></div>性懦謇讷者，口虽奏而未尽其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147289_comment'></div>奸诈辩词者，言虽当而未必有理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147289_comment'></div>陛下或赐之恩泽，或置以刑名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147289_comment'></div>然睿鉴周通，出令固无于枉滥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147289_comment'></div>而帝庭清肃，终朝岂称于喧嚣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147289_comment'></div>加以条理事宜，或伤烦琐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147289_comment'></div>施行诏敕，遂至稠重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147289_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「王言如丝，其出如纶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147289_comment'></div>王言如纶，其出如纶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147289_comment'></div>喻其以近及远，渐光大于万方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147289_comment'></div>以言训人，可常行于百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147289_comment'></div>简而且要，人则易从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147289_comment'></div>繁而又难，人则易犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147289_comment'></div>《书》曰：「临下以简」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147289_comment'></div>又曰：「御众以宽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147289_comment'></div>御众不以宽，则获罪者多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147289_comment'></div>临下不以简，则从令者少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147289_comment'></div>况帝王有常道，禁令有常程，施令贵乎必行，设禁贵乎必止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147289_comment'></div>若令之无节，奉而行之者必难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147289_comment'></div>禁之无时，遵而止之者亦寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147289_comment'></div>臣所谓网利太密既如彼，圣旨稍频又如此，愿陛下宽臣敢言之罪，察而审之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147289_comment'></div>望陛下听臣敢谏之言，择而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147289_comment'></div>臣复有未谕圣意之事三，又有奏请可行之事二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147289_comment'></div>未谕者，今内职诸司各有公廨，禁林近侍各有本厅，中书是宰相职事之堂，相府是陛下优贤之地，今则于中书外庑置磨勘一司，较朝臣功过之有无，审州郡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1147289", 1147289, "Clauses/243/Comments/0")'>劳能</span>之虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147289_comment'></div>眷言是职，本属考功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147289_comment'></div>岂考功之职不修，而磨勘之名互出？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147289_comment'></div>殊非雅称，深损大纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147289_comment'></div>此臣所谓未谕圣意之事者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147289_comment'></div>其次，御史台本不禁人，今为系囚之所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147289_comment'></div>大理寺旧来置狱，今为检格之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147289_comment'></div>授人之职者，本贵当材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147289_comment'></div>鞠狱以情者，自然无滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147289_comment'></div>或诸侯有大过，或百姓有深冤，乃命台臣，委为制使，宪府之风规自别，刑曹之按鞠无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147289_comment'></div>今则或挝鼓闻天，虚词诣阙，多差殿直承旨，使为制勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147289_comment'></div>使臣殊非理狱之才，骤委鞠人之罪，其间有未明推勘，因致淹延；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147289_comment'></div>或未晓刑章，妄加深刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147289_comment'></div>既临以制书之命，置乎缧绁之中，上畏严威，谁敢拒捍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147289_comment'></div>及当录问，皆伏款词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147289_comment'></div>虽罪至徒流，必该申奏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147289_comment'></div>案既圆备，即据施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147289_comment'></div>岂无陷于非辜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147289_comment'></div>岂无失于有罪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1147289_comment'></div>亏陛下慈仁之旨，损朝廷钦恤之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1147289_comment'></div>此臣所谓未谕圣意之事者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1147289_comment'></div>臣每读史书，至于文集，或匹妇有正廉之节，野人有孝悌之风，尚旌彼门闾，或赐之粟帛，将以离浇漓之俗，亦以行风教之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1147289_comment'></div>修身者由此彰名，尚义者因兹立节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1147289_comment'></div>今国家官僚远宦，不得般家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1147289_comment'></div>父母云亡，不得离任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1147289_comment'></div>墨缞视事，宁安孝子之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1147289_comment'></div>明诏未行，深损圣人之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1147289_comment'></div>此臣所谓未谕圣意者三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1147289_comment'></div>昔汉文在位，称为刑措，岁终断狱者三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1147289_comment'></div>此盖民安其业，乃无咎于刑章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1147289_comment'></div>物失其宜，必自罹于夭枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1147289_comment'></div>是以圣人见一物失宜，则必加恻隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1147289_comment'></div>知一夫失所，则必动哀矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1147289_comment'></div>御一衣，思天下女工之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1147289_comment'></div>尝一膳，思天下农夫之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1147289_comment'></div>故《尚书》曰：「不敢侮鳏寡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1147289_comment'></div>《周易》曰：「信及豚鱼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1147289_comment'></div>豚鱼至微，信犹能及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1147289_comment'></div>鳏寡至贱，侮不敢加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1147289_comment'></div>有以见圣人用心，无微不至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1147289_comment'></div>圣人施惠，无所不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1147289_comment'></div>今河朔数州衙前军将，应宣命配来之者，多江南、两浙之人，虽曾有敕文，许令自便；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1147289_comment'></div>然各无去著，犹系职名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1147289_comment'></div>其间有不请衣粮，只望差使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1147289_comment'></div>设有得该请受，多是折支，时寒无衣，日馁无食，老小相聚，冻饿贫穷，羁旅无图，咨嗟愁苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1147289_comment'></div>与其配之而无用，孰若舍之而放归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1147289_comment'></div>此乃可言者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1147289_comment'></div>今国家封疆甚广，州县至多，令录阙员，据资劳而迁授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1147289_comment'></div>簿尉满任，按岁月以除移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1147289_comment'></div>其间廉吏虽多，抑亦贪夫不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1147289_comment'></div>贪者偶无彰露，刑罚宁加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1147289_comment'></div>廉者未有升闻，旌酬弗及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1147289_comment'></div>言乎赏劝，似未精详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1147289_comment'></div>宜委诸州，遍令申奏，州有几县，县有几员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1147289_comment'></div>奏其善者，则不善者自彰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1147289_comment'></div>奏其廉者，则不廉者自显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1147289_comment'></div>或就加奖饰，或聊与转迁，则廉能既有所归，猥滥者宁无自愧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1147289_comment'></div>扬清激浊，实为致理之先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1147289_comment'></div>易俗移风，宜自亲民之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1147289_comment'></div>此臣谓可言者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1147289_comment'></div>臣缕陈鄙见，烦黩圣听，臣不任惶恐战慄之至。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_147_1147289'></div><div id='poem_sentence_147_1147289_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
邹城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9f5d12d61cd8485c9e39538cc2e63fe0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9f5d12d61cd8485c9e39538cc2e63fe0");'><span id='9f5d12d61cd8485c9e39538cc2e63fe0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年</a>，41岁</div><div id='9f5d12d61cd8485c9e39538cc2e63fe0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年</a>　约于本年，在邹鲁与王禹偁结识。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永年
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d7d550021f77458ca123cbf69d72d484_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d7d550021f77458ca123cbf69d72d484");'><span id='d7d550021f77458ca123cbf69d72d484_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=982')">981-982年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='d7d550021f77458ca123cbf69d72d484' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年11月</a>　十一月，在洺州为河北南路转运副使，上表贺南郊礼成。作品：贺南郊表一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年12月30日</a>　除夜，在洺州为河北南路转运副使，有诗。作品：除夜。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于太平兴国七年，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_53757' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53757' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53757?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（981年12月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53757")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作垂）</span>花酒满卮，绕廊风细动帘帷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53757'>已从半夜分春漏，即是平明受岁时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53757'>或省转官因大庆，元正立仗忆丹墀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53757'>吟思何日承宣召，却得金门和御诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53757'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53757_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年1月1日</a>　元日，在洺州为河北南路转运副使，有诗。作品：元日。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_53740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53740?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_53740'>去年元会立班时，簪绂光辉与礼仪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53740'>今日洺川逢岁旦，延留宾客乐昌期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53740'>朝云暖润轻阴散，晚日融明瑞景迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53740_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='494a872a54d648458964b58a7eae6099_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("494a872a54d648458964b58a7eae6099");'><span id='494a872a54d648458964b58a7eae6099_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>，45岁</div><div id='494a872a54d648458964b58a7eae6099' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　春，赴任知睦州途中，泊船茱萸堰，有诗。作品：茱萸堰泊。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于雍熙二年，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_53754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>茱萸堰泊</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53754")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53754'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53754'>茱萸堰下泊行舟，初落帆樯暮雨收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53754'>寒水漾烟轻似縠，微云笼月澹如秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53754'>登封自惜天涯去，盛事空思国史修。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53754'>达曙不眠灯耿耿，寺钟遥听在西楼<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《咸平集》卷一六）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53754'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53754_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a7fce68f0c78483b95f851845491c18d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a7fce68f0c78483b95f851845491c18d");'><span id='a7fce68f0c78483b95f851845491c18d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>，45岁</div><div id='a7fce68f0c78483b95f851845491c18d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年3月</a>　三月，赴任知睦州途中，游杭州天竺寺，有诗。作品：题天竺寺。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于雍熙二年，此据《咸平集》卷一六《茱萸堰泊》改。）</span><div id='poem_53774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题天竺寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53774")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53774'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53774'>三月杨花扑马飞，联镳来款白云扉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53774'>湖边钟磬含清籁，树杪楼台霭翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53774'>野景留人狂欲住，春光啼鸟劝思归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53774'>萋萋芳草重回首，十里松门照落晖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53774'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53774_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
建德
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f0bd7db14efe4c22bcf13023e90f3658_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f0bd7db14efe4c22bcf13023e90f3658");'><span id='f0bd7db14efe4c22bcf13023e90f3658_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>，45岁</div><div id='f0bd7db14efe4c22bcf13023e90f3658' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年4月</a>　四月，在知睦州任，有诗和温仲舒。作品：和温仲舒残春遣怀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_53746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和温仲舒残春遣怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53746")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53746_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53746'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53746'>丹阙年来奏贺频，金舆侍从望东巡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53746'>越王江上重回首，严子台边再送春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53746'>水国山川怡道性，花时琴酒悦吟神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53746'>烟霞肯欲留君往，宰相方谋用故人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53746'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53746_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年4月</a>　四月，在知睦州任，作《太平颂》作品：太平颂。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二一。孙谱系此文于淳化四年，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太平颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147516")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147516'>圣朝垂统，十有八载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147516_comment'></div>皇帝以仁贤之德，由晋邸而即大位，嗣王业而承庙祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147516_comment'></div>天地气和，日月贞明，协千龄之会昌，应万民之推戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147516_comment'></div>昔舜有大功二十，而尧以鸿图付之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147516_comment'></div>汉文以五让天下，而公卿大臣立之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147516_comment'></div>推鲁史之遗文，得汉家之故事，俦功比德，吾皇兼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147516_comment'></div>稽羲文出震之格言，徵《戴礼》向明之大位，黄麾列仗，洪宝传国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147516_comment'></div>百辟山呼而称贺，万方波朝而会同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147516_comment'></div>一之日覃《连山》作解之恩，布率土眚灾之令，与民更始，趣物于新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147516_comment'></div>号令一发，罪系咸释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147516_comment'></div>雷霆振幽滞，江海荡痕瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147516_comment'></div>自华及夷，逢时乐圣，声悦成歌颂，形动为鼓舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147516_comment'></div>《易》不云乎：「天地革而四时成」，「圣人作而万物睹」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147516_comment'></div>《书》不云乎：民非后不乂，后非民不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147516_comment'></div>律历有五胜之策，图谶应一人之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147516_comment'></div>夏后得内禅之礼，周家称太弟之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147516_comment'></div>公刘积仁，然后武王、成王享大位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147516_comment'></div>高皇拨乱，然后文帝、景帝致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147516_comment'></div>晋以金德王，而孝武称贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147516_comment'></div>唐以武德取，而太宗好理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147516_comment'></div>在渊或跃，所以见王者之兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147516_comment'></div>大明方融，于是喻圣人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147516_comment'></div>自天厌唐德，昭宗失国，四海九州，瓜剖豆分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147516_comment'></div>朱氏称梁，石家号晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147516_comment'></div>居于岐者有僭王之车服，据于邺者拥图霸之甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147516_comment'></div>金陵继阖庐之雄，南海有尉佗之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147516_comment'></div>湘潭咫尺，与中国称邻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147516_comment'></div>庸蜀险固，以一方自大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147516_comment'></div>天子之守不过三千里，诸侯之兵何啻八百乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147516_comment'></div>中原鹿走，高材得掎角之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147516_comment'></div>海水鲸飞，黔首困怀襄之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147516_comment'></div>或暴秦之祚，才二世而亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147516_comment'></div>有夏诸子，或再稔而谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147516_comment'></div>夫差剑盾，修武备以方勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147516_comment'></div>叔孙豆笾，饰礼容而未暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147516_comment'></div>不有天命，国何以兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147516_comment'></div>未遇真主，乱无以弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147516_comment'></div>玄穹所以眷命，皇宋于焉勃兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147516_comment'></div>狱讼讴歌，舍丹朱而归舜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147516_comment'></div>礼乐征伐，黜诸侯而尊王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147516_comment'></div>强本弱枝，兼亡取乱，自兹始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147516_comment'></div>初则灭李筠于泽、潞，次则覆重进于维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147516_comment'></div>南平荆门，西举剑阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147516_comment'></div>命伏波之将，以清岭表；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147516_comment'></div>诏楼船之师，以克江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147516_comment'></div>系三伪主，生致阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147516_comment'></div>求诸前代，罕有威武若斯之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147516_comment'></div>故匈奴畏服而请吏，南蛮奉琛而纳款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147516_comment'></div>虽先朝之英武，底宁寰区；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147516_comment'></div>由吾君之密谋，赞成大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147516_comment'></div>昔鲁、卫为兄弟，晋、郑称昭穆，咸能夹辅王室，保捍宗周，而《春秋》纪其勋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147516_comment'></div>昔唐祖革隋，由太宗之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147516_comment'></div>明皇灭燕，赖肃宗之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147516_comment'></div>寰区果大定，宗社乃再安，故《实录》纪其事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147516_comment'></div>仲尼称「其或继周者，虽百代可知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147516_comment'></div>披皇图而稽帝文，扬英声而腾茂实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147516_comment'></div>尧有天下，以文思允恭之圣，得邦国社稷之臣，始以羲和为日官，次以重华录大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147516_comment'></div>曰弃曰契，克谐俞往之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147516_comment'></div>曰夔曰龙，尽协畴咨之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147516_comment'></div>所谓精求理乱，明辨凶贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147516_comment'></div>众贤既登庸，四凶遂流窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147516_comment'></div>然后土阶三尺，茅茨不剪，垂衣而天下理，不亦陶唐善致太平乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147516_comment'></div>洎舜格艺祖，纂尧之绩，辑五瑞以来群后，巡四岳而省舆民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147516_comment'></div>协时日之无差，同律度而必审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147516_comment'></div>聪明咸达，枢机不壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147516_comment'></div>犹谓其臣曰：「予欲左右有民，汝翼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147516_comment'></div>予欲宣力四方，汝为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147516_comment'></div>华虫藻火之文，以汝明之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147516_comment'></div>六律五声之音，以汝听之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147516_comment'></div>犹以上之过失或未闻，下之谋猷有未达，法谤木之求理，建善旌以表诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147516_comment'></div>《语》曰：「舜无为而理」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147516_comment'></div>又曰：「《韶》尽美矣，又尽善也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147516_comment'></div>斯乃有虞之克肖唐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147516_comment'></div>至于禹勤力于沟洫，致美于绂冕，设簴求谠言之善，泣辜见恤物之仁，拜伯益之昌言，诛防风之后至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147516_comment'></div>《传》曰：「微禹，吾其鱼乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147516_comment'></div>《语》曰「吾无间焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147516_comment'></div>大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147516_comment'></div>汤革夏政，应乎天，顺乎人，用王者之干戈，救生灵之涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147516_comment'></div>肇征葛伯，四国悦之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147516_comment'></div>后战鸣条，天下尊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147516_comment'></div>设总街之大庭，吁谟毕至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147516_comment'></div>解野人之密网，历数攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147516_comment'></div>《书》曰：「东征西夷怨，南征北狄怨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147516_comment'></div>斯所以见禹汤之致雍熙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147516_comment'></div>虽典籍所备载，今古所熟闻，然则远取前王，近方圣代，则尧舜为帝道也，禹汤为王道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147516_comment'></div>举是四君子，而比万乘主，且何愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147516_comment'></div>旷数千载之间，逾七十君之盛，中有汉氏，称刑措而不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147516_comment'></div>迨至唐室，有囚释而自还，亦足方驾皇风，并驱大道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147516_comment'></div>臣今谓继唐者，非大宋乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147516_comment'></div>自陛下临御以来，天下之目，颙然观朝庭之所行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147516_comment'></div>天下之耳，专然听国家之所务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147516_comment'></div>陛下果以天为貌，以道为心，以万民为体，以六合为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147516_comment'></div>谓三王之礼不相沿，五帝之乐非相袭，或因仍旧制，或釐革故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147516_comment'></div>发先庚之教令，施涣汗之恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147516_comment'></div>始以宁边为远图，次以纳谏为切务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147516_comment'></div>振幽拔滞，旌贤进能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147516_comment'></div>蠲关市之征，勉农桑之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147516_comment'></div>哀悼鳏寡，恻隐困穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147516_comment'></div>礼高年，尊有德，封树降漏泉之宠，室家覃疏邑之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147516_comment'></div>王言如丝，其出如纶，不终朝而诏下朝堂，未及夕而令敷国内，才浃旬而恩均天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147516_comment'></div>宜乎至和之气感于天地，不测之神发为祯祥，六辩弗迷，四溟无荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147516_comment'></div>五纬灿编珠之彩，三阶若悬衡之平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147516_comment'></div>雨流润以如膏，雪盈尺而呈瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147516_comment'></div>阊阖风来而应候，贯索星稀而省刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147516_comment'></div>太史铜浑，不失阴阳之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147516_comment'></div>容成玉历，遂更正朔之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1147516_comment'></div>验休徵，考《洪范》，善谋则时寒自应，睿圣则甘泽不愆，斯皆德动天以昭彰，物有感而通泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1147516_comment'></div>语封疆则东际桑林之国，西走葱河之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1147516_comment'></div>日南万里，设都护以怀柔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1147516_comment'></div>漠北五原，化单于之犷骜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1147516_comment'></div>有以见王者无外，书轨大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1147516_comment'></div>岂止代马新羁，愿备六闲之御；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1147516_comment'></div>名翚入贡，来称九译之朝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1147516_comment'></div>论都邑则陈留古封，商丘雄地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1147516_comment'></div>仰浑仪则房、心之分，按地图则豫州之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1147516_comment'></div>左控齐、魏，右引淮、湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1147516_comment'></div>辟里闬以绮纷，凑舟车以鳞萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1147516_comment'></div>皇居壮丽，信威戎而惮夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1147516_comment'></div>都人杂遝，实驾肩而击毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1147516_comment'></div>阅文物则司徒以七教理兆民，乐正以四术教胄子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1147516_comment'></div>贤良待公车之诏，俊造升天府之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1147516_comment'></div>焕然若重离之明，炳焉得奎星之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1147516_comment'></div>谅千古之下，与三代同风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1147516_comment'></div>班马文章，列芸阁麟台之次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1147516_comment'></div>严吾侍从，居石渠金马之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1147516_comment'></div>观武备则精兵三百万，功臣二十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1147516_comment'></div>世祖兼昆阳之众，曹公得刘琮之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1147516_comment'></div>是以军容益严，国威大整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1147516_comment'></div>虽四鄙无事，灵台有偃伯之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1147516_comment'></div>而三农之隙，司马有教战之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1147516_comment'></div>比夫骊山讲武，陋唐世之草仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1147516_comment'></div>泽国观兵，鄙楚君之凭轼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1147516_comment'></div>言盛礼则君尊于上，臣肃于下，法厚坤之有别，本太一以为容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1147516_comment'></div>民得之则父子亲而兄弟和，国用之则祭获祥而战必胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1147516_comment'></div>然后以车服而别之，以爵勋而辨之，以珩佩和鸾以声之，以黼黻絺绣以文之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1147516_comment'></div>故百官象物而动，九贡不戒而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1147516_comment'></div>听雅乐则五音正，六律和，用于方泽而地祇升，奏于圆丘而天神降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1147516_comment'></div>振作于庙，知祖考之来思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1147516_comment'></div>锵洋于庭，感凤皇之戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1147516_comment'></div>朱干玉戚，两阶见象武之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1147516_comment'></div>树羽崇牙，六佾辨用文之德，详制度则明堂为布政之宫，太社为礼神之本，金城俨百雉之峻，天门逾两观之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1147516_comment'></div>谒灵台以视常文，辟太学以优儒教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1147516_comment'></div>连营棋布，若羽林之四十二星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1147516_comment'></div>列署鳞差，比太微之三百六位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1147516_comment'></div>验丰富则全齐曰鱼盐之国，右蜀为金碧之府，南越出珠贝，北燕多健马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1147516_comment'></div>国家既网罗六合，庭衢八荒，异物内流而国用饶，万物均输而公帑富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1147516_comment'></div>陋隋文之俭德，称有羡财；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1147516_comment'></div>轻汉武之事边，肇兴徭算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1147516_comment'></div>较版籍则既庶矣，又富矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1147516_comment'></div>所谓积于不涸之仓，务稼穑也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1147516_comment'></div>藏于不竭之府，勉桑麻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1147516_comment'></div>皆陛下跻之仁寿之域，导其生殖之源，故比屋可封，外户不闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1147516_comment'></div>仲尼观蜡，退而称三代之英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1147516_comment'></div>伊尹持衡，慨然虑一夫不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1147516_comment'></div>语臣寮则庙堂之上得贤相也，三军之师皆良将也，可以侔周之十乱，虞之五臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1147516_comment'></div>儒雅雍容，登瀛洲而论道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1147516_comment'></div>英雄慷慨，画云台而纪勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1147516_comment'></div>功成理定既如彼，礼备乐修又如此，陛下犹以本枝百世，封建亲戚，恩之先而礼之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1147516_comment'></div>乃谓侍臣曰：「昔周王莅祚，以辂车旌旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1147516_comment'></div>夏后之璜玉，封父之繁弱，迨阙巩之甲，密须之鼓，姑洗之钟，商民之族，以为分物，用彰国家之庸，而赐诸弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1147516_comment'></div>封伯禽于鲁，封康叔于卫，封唐叔于晋，左史书之，至今称为美事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1147516_comment'></div>朕于是命有司，陈玉策冠剑，卤簿鼓吹，以营丘四履之国，封皇弟为齐王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1147516_comment'></div>又命太常以金辂茜旆，秬鬯圭瓒，疏鹑首千里之封，迁侍中为京兆尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1147516_comment'></div>又命礼官以虎符兽节，赤茀金舄，分南梁十四郡之地，升太保为兴元连帅」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1147516_comment'></div>信尧亲九族，周重宗盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1147516_comment'></div>楚国析圭，称庄王之九德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1147516_comment'></div>汉家刑典，非刘氏而不王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1147516_comment'></div>宜乎皇基若磐石之安，宗室比维城之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1147516_comment'></div>庸知卜代之吉，何止于三十；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1147516_comment'></div>卜年之永，将逾于万龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1147516_comment'></div>君有威仪而可尊，臣有礼法而可仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1147516_comment'></div>天下无事，海内有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1147516_comment'></div>皇风荡荡，尊卢、赫胥之朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1147516_comment'></div>民物熙熙，柏皇、栗陆之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1147516_comment'></div>脱宝剑以赐骑士，却骏马以驾鼓车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1147516_comment'></div>惜中人之产，而罢露台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1147516_comment'></div>愧吴芮之心，而赐几杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1147516_comment'></div>集书囊以帷殿，列谏疏于御屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1147516_comment'></div>观明堂以去笞刑，画衣冠而别有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1147516_comment'></div>野老或不知帝力，公卿亦耻言人非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1147516_comment'></div>行万里不持寸金，消五兵可为农器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1147516_comment'></div>海牛南卧，远夷占以来朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1147516_comment'></div>楛矢东归，旅宰司其所贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1147516_comment'></div>鱼在藻以遂性，鸮食椹而怀音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1147516_comment'></div>瑞露凝甘，降竹柏之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1147516_comment'></div>景星垂象，助晦朔之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1147516_comment'></div>器车知厚载之仁，丹甑表将丰之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1147516_comment'></div>蓂生近砌，因更月而呈芳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1147516_comment'></div>萐在中包，亦无风而自动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1147516_comment'></div>《书》曰鱼鳖咸若，《诗》称行苇不伤，《由庚》、《蓼萧》，悦遒人之见采；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1147516_comment'></div>《芝房》、《宝鼎》，流乐府以登歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1147516_comment'></div>信宗庙之垂灵，当天地之交泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1147516_comment'></div>攸宜垂黈纩，凝冕旒，栖神于穆清，守道乎玄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1147516_comment'></div>游大庭以怡睿览，升姑射以适皇情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1147516_comment'></div>于是三事大夫率百职卿士，秉桓圭以就列，委苍佩以飏言，曰：「陛下德掩前代，功格玄穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1147516_comment'></div>古称因天事天，因地事地，封禅之礼，历数十世而无睹焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1147516_comment'></div>天其命陛下修阙典，秩无文哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1147516_comment'></div>不然，安得民和神悦兮若是，乾符坤珍之毕臻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1147516_comment'></div>臣等遐详旧仪，得之新礼，欲愿陛下觐群后于东国，展严禋于岱宗，命虞官相高卑之仪，诏掌固施表著之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1147516_comment'></div>泰坛三袭，祠昊穹之神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1147516_comment'></div>圜陛四周，列众星之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1147516_comment'></div>《云门》、《大濩》，施于重壝之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1147516_comment'></div>勾陈执金，周于四门之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1147516_comment'></div>玉辂金根翼于道，殊珍众宝旅于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1147516_comment'></div>庶邦冢君，四夷酋长，环天坛而序立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1147516_comment'></div>佽飞之将，羽林之兵，卫禁署以增威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1147516_comment'></div>于是宵漏未尽，中严外办，服冕裘而上征，鸣玉鸾于太清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1147516_comment'></div>祈昭嘏于万灵，布福寿于群萌，探金策以受神休，封玉检以成大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1147516_comment'></div>然后勒丹碑于云际，霈玄泽于天下，以彰盛烈也，不使七十二君独美于古先也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1147516_comment'></div>皇帝嘉忠诚之恳祷，而犹怀谦德而未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1147516_comment'></div>既而声闻于外，下臣得之于道涂，不觉抃蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1147516_comment'></div>以为美盛德之形容，无先于颂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1147516_comment'></div>虽菲才之无取，幸昌运之重熙，愿以诗声，扬于王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1147516_comment'></div>曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_213_1147516'>德厚称帝，仁胜为王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1147516_comment'></div>仁德兼备，谓之三皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1147516_comment'></div>天命靡常，邦国其昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1147516_comment'></div>吾皇嗣位，南面垂裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1147516_comment'></div>左唐右虞，超周掩商。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1147516_comment'></div>大业于铄，鸿名焜煌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1147516_comment'></div>二仪幽赞，群灵协祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1147516_comment'></div>《河图》启瑞，《洛书》含章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1147516_comment'></div>运逢交泰，时来允臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1147516_comment'></div>君明臣贤，礼备乐详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1147516_comment'></div>书轨大同，贡输相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1147516_comment'></div>风雨弗迷，黎元咸康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1147516_comment'></div>至和之气，感天之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1147516_comment'></div>日流嘉彩，星垂瑞芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1147516_comment'></div>三脊之茅，茁然呈芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1147516_comment'></div>九苞之凤，飘然来翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1147516_comment'></div>堪备缛礼，升告穹苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1147516_comment'></div>泥金载密，燎烟高飏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1147516_comment'></div>鸾车佩衣，交鸣锵锵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1147516_comment'></div>天灵地祇，降福穰穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1147516_comment'></div>用显我皇，太平昭彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1147516_comment'></div>亿万斯年，永永无疆！</div><div id='poem_sentence_234_1147516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　夏，在知睦州任，天旱祈雨，有诗。作品：悯旱。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见董棻《严陵集》卷三。孙谱系此诗于端拱二年，此据诗意改。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年7月</a>　七月，在知睦州任，重建睦州孔子庙，上表请赐祭器、经书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年8月</a>　八月，在知睦州任，应诏上疏论事。作品：上太宗应诏论火灾。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1147286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太宗应诏论火灾</a><span class='authorDate'>（雍熙元年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147286")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147286'>臣伏念臣才谋不迨于古人，职次忝居于谏省，敢不常思补报，用答休明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147286_comment'></div>六年九月十三日诣阁上书，昧死言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147286_comment'></div>陛下于是下御札，俾人直谏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147286_comment'></div>降敕书，奖臣敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147286_comment'></div>七年十二月十四日，又再上奏疏入递，而不知达与未达；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147286_comment'></div>直言虽求用，而不知行与未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147286_comment'></div>今日陛下有所因，方渴闻至言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147286_comment'></div>有所为，方切待直谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147286_comment'></div>引咎自戒，修德弥新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147286_comment'></div>臣谓责在近臣，而不在圣躬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147286_comment'></div>罪在臣辈，而不在陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147286_comment'></div>近日陛下有朝令夕改之事，由制敕所行，时有未当，而无人封駮者，给事中之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147286_comment'></div>给事中若任得其人，制敕若许之封駮，则所下之敕无不当，所行之事无不精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147286_comment'></div>事无不精，则垂为典彝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147286_comment'></div>敕无不当，则编为格式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147286_comment'></div>岂有朝令夕改之弊，岂有不精不当之虞也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147286_comment'></div>臣又见陛下有舍近谋远之事，由言动所为，未合至理，而无人敢谏诤者，是左右拾遗、补阙之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147286_comment'></div>今遗、补是侍从之臣，而不得在左右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147286_comment'></div>职分当献替之事，而未有上封章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147286_comment'></div>自此国家举事有不便于时，遗、补不敢谏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147286_comment'></div>朝廷法令有不合于道，遗、补不敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147286_comment'></div>加以时久升平，天下混一，致陛下谓升平自得，资陛下以功业自多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147286_comment'></div>日迁月移，浸成圣性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147286_comment'></div>左取右奉，无非睿谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147286_comment'></div>所以陛下出一言，乃以谓汤武可偕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147286_comment'></div>陛下行一事，乃以谓尧舜可继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147286_comment'></div>自缵大位，于今九年，四方虽宁，万国虽静，然刑罚未甚措，水旱未甚调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147286_comment'></div>陛下谓之太平，谁敢不谓之太平？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147286_comment'></div>陛下谓之至理，谁敢不谓之至理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147286_comment'></div>方欲为民求福，报天之功，有事于太山，展礼于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147286_comment'></div>人谋虽克，天意未从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147286_comment'></div>火于禁中，将觉悟于英主；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147286_comment'></div>诏下海内，遂布告于舆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147286_comment'></div>近臣闻陛下感悟之言，宁不惕厉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147286_comment'></div>谏官阅陛下忧勤之诏，谁不彷徨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147286_comment'></div>臣所以谓过在近臣，不在圣躬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147286_comment'></div>罪在谏官，不在陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147286_comment'></div>臣死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147286_comment'></div>然臣两度上疏，而陛下不用一二；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147286_comment'></div>今臣在外，而陛下委之以分忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147286_comment'></div>碌碌随众，忧旷遗之靡暇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147286_comment'></div>皇皇有志，思谏诤之未能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147286_comment'></div>今幸天启圣心，神赞皇运，感陛下虚伫待犯颜之谏，致陛下专精求逆耳之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147286_comment'></div>臣是以再罄愚衷，复伸鄙见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147286_comment'></div>臣所谓陛下有朝令夕改者，试举其一二以明之：置而寻废者，农师也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147286_comment'></div>禁而不严者，车服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147286_comment'></div>臣所谓陛下有舍近谋远者，试举其一二以明之：宰相不得用人，而委员外郎差遣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147286_comment'></div>近臣专受责，而求令录封章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147286_comment'></div>自此章奏必多，听用必广；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147286_comment'></div>听用既广，则条制必繁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147286_comment'></div>条制既繁，则依从者少；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147286_comment'></div>既依从者少，则是法令不行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147286_comment'></div>法令不行，则由规画未当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147286_comment'></div>有如前年敕下，令邻近州府互差司理、判官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147286_comment'></div>至今年敕下，却令本州仍旧差置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147286_comment'></div>又如前年敕下，应征科官吏，限前得了即与超升，限外未了即当降黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147286_comment'></div>即不以县有大小之分，税有难易之征，土田沃瘠之不同，岁时丰稔之不等，风俗勤惰之各异，官吏能否之各殊，而一概以程限所拘，一例以升降为定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147286_comment'></div>自后未闻限外欠者降一官，限前了者升一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147286_comment'></div>此无乃垂之空言，示之寡信？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147286_comment'></div>乞今后凡有所奏，或有所陈，幸陛下察而审之，令大臣议而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147286_comment'></div>盖臣下言之则谓封章，陛下行之则出为法令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147286_comment'></div>法令可简而不可使繁，制度可永而不可屡变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147286_comment'></div>变易不定，是彰思虑之不精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147286_comment'></div>繁多难依，是令手足之无措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147286_comment'></div>《尚书》曰「临下以简」，又曰「得师者王」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147286_comment'></div>今宰臣若贤，愿陛下信而用之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147286_comment'></div>宰臣非贤，愿陛下择可用而任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147286_comment'></div>何以置之为具臣，而疑之若众人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147286_comment'></div>百官若举其职，愿陛下听而用之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147286_comment'></div>百官未称其职，愿陛下量其才而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147286_comment'></div>何以置之为备员，而待之若冗秩也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147286_comment'></div>臣谓百职若举，则万事从而自理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147286_comment'></div>百官未修，则万务从而亦隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147286_comment'></div>必若任而疑之，则上下非一心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147286_comment'></div>疑而用之，则君臣非一体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147286_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147286_comment'></div>疑能生谤，谤能生疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147286_comment'></div>疑从谤生，则父子之道或偶亏于慈孝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147286_comment'></div>谤因疑起，则君臣之际或变成于怨尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147286_comment'></div>魏文侯焚谤书，陛下固当知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147286_comment'></div>令狐楚有《辨谤论》，陛下时宜览之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147286_comment'></div>若然则保得臣下始终，全得君上恩宠，方谓君为元首，臣作股肱也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_81_1147286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　秋，在知睦州任，有诗。作品：红树。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于太平兴国八年，此据《咸平集》卷一六《茱萸堰泊》改。）</span><div id='poem_53743' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53743' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53743?labeling=true' target='_blank'>红树<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本注：此下睦州。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53743")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53743'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53743'>秋来嘉树色堪攀，红叶没溪复映山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53743'>半露寺楼深崦里，密笼渔舍夕阳间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53743'>吟看摇落堆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>金井，醉赏扶疏对玉颜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53743'>水国却疑春野秀，似花幽鸟正关关。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53743'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　秋，在知睦州任，有诗寄宋白。作品：秋夜有怀寄副翰宋白舍人。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于太平兴国八年，此据《咸平集》卷一六《茱萸堰泊》改。）</span><div id='poem_53751' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53751' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53751?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋声<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作夜）</span>有怀寄副翰宋白舍人</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_53751'>秋声萧瑟北山椒，赖有琴樽遣寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53751'>书幌静怜斜月鉴，窗灯寒带落花挑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53751'>久辞知己来江国，少寄音书过海潮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53751'>因想玉堂今夜直，建章宫漏正迢迢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53751'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53751_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　秋，在知睦州任，有诗。作品：郡斋书事。<span id='poem_53756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郡斋书事</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53756")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53756_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53756'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53756'>江天短景莫相催，三度逢花折早梅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53756'>仙棹远归思李郭，庐山高会忆宗雷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53756'>林端忽见孤云出，池上欣闻好客来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53756'>昨夜月明霜更苦，卷帘黄叶满青苔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53756'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53756_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53770' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53770' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53770?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暇日偶题</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53770")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53770_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53770'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53770'>年来吟鬓已星星，鸟石溪边叶又零。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53770'>帘下孤灯删草奏，窗间叠嶂读茶经。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53770'>瘴乡怕袭山岚毒，野艇嫌冲水雾腥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53770'>天末岂记归去意，白云掩映数峰青。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53770_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53770'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53770_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郡中遣意寄友人</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53755")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53755_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53755'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53755'>溪云澹澹浪悠悠，十二州中最小州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53755'>花落喜过流水寺，月明懒下看潮楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53755'>药栏梅润秋重换，棋局松阴夜不收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53755'>吟寄故人如借问，钓鱼矶在海西头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53755'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53755_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桐江咏</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53759")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53759'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53759'>桐溪湛湛见游鳞，摇落枫林绕水滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53759'>秋色数行沙上雁，残阳一簇渡头人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53759'>蓝鲜斤生过深涧，雪吼寒潮人富春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53759'>俱是谢公吟咏地，伊余何以继芳尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53759'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53759_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年10月7日</a>　十月七日，在知睦州任，有诗。作品：圣节有怀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于太平兴国八年，此据《咸平集》卷一六《茱萸堰泊》改。）</span><div id='poem_53741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53741?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣节有怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年10月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53741")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53741_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53741'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53741'>南山晴霭御炉烟，回望长安白日边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53741'>率众谢恩呼万岁，思归侍宴已三年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53741'>翠微钟磬行香寺，红叶楼台祝寿筵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53741'>吟想皇州晚来景，云间宫阙夕阳天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53741'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53741_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年12月</a>　十二月，在知睦州任，有贺南郊礼毕表。作品：贺南郊表二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年12月</a>　十二月，在知睦州任，有谢赐历日奏状。作品：谢赐历日二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二六。孙谱系此文于雍熙二年，此据文意改。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='97c663fa395c43e29ce2c49859e0bc9d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("97c663fa395c43e29ce2c49859e0bc9d");'><span id='97c663fa395c43e29ce2c49859e0bc9d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=987')">984-987年</a>，45-48岁</div><div id='97c663fa395c43e29ce2c49859e0bc9d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　本年，在知睦州任，有赋。作品：积薪赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《咸平集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1147149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147149?labeling=true' target='_blank'>积薪赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147149")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147149'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147149'>翘翘错薪，委积交陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147149_comment'></div>后来者渐次居上，先用者逐热相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147149_comment'></div>仰之弥高，或连枝而带叶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147149_comment'></div>怨不在大，喻弃故而从新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147149_comment'></div>其大也降鸾辂于东封，祝圆丘于南至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147149_comment'></div>执玉帛者万国，捧豆笾于群吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147149_comment'></div>礼容具举，乐章大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147149_comment'></div>《书》称柴望，达上帝于升禋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147149_comment'></div>《诗》曰薪蒸，本周人之贵气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147149_comment'></div>虞衡往来，折薪成堆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147149_comment'></div>载来北阙之下，采自南山之隈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147149_comment'></div>辇运错杂，积叠崔嵬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147149_comment'></div>但取禋宗之用，不论瑰异之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147149_comment'></div>譬如为山，岂勉力于勤学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147149_comment'></div>宁媚于灶，不旋踵于贻灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147149_comment'></div>薪既不能自言，人或代之析理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147149_comment'></div>繄吾侪小人，与彼其之子，忧负荷以弗胜，为众多之仰止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147149_comment'></div>匪斧不克，因伐木以致身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147149_comment'></div>受人之知，合不才而省己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147149_comment'></div>始采采于山水之涯，丁丁合《风》《雅》之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147149_comment'></div>积之累之，如京如坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147149_comment'></div>远望比层巢之峻，仰瞻侔累卵之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147149_comment'></div>居中者谓不我遐弃，在下者谓人不我知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147149_comment'></div>美古人善喻，下僚其咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147149_comment'></div>本入用之迟速，胡觖望于高卑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1147149_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　本年，在知睦州任，上书谢赐九经。作品：谢赐九经书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐九经书状</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147395")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147395'>右，臣当州为无经书，乞自办纸就国子监印取《九经》归州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147395_comment'></div>今月若干日，伏奉敕牒，蒙恩却给还纸，特宣赐《九经》书并《释文》者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147395_comment'></div>伏以圣人之道，著在典坟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147395_comment'></div>英主之恩，颁于郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147395_comment'></div>是使桐庐陋壤，化为礼义之乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147395_comment'></div>钓濑遗民，永习《诗》《书》之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147395_comment'></div>伏念臣忝分忧寄，权守诏条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147395_comment'></div>文翁劝学之风，惭无祖述；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147395_comment'></div>宣父化民之道，敢怠师资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147395_comment'></div>是以辄贡封章，乞印经籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147395_comment'></div>上干旒冕，方忧典宪之诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147395_comment'></div>俯降丝纶，特允刍荛之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147395_comment'></div>赐书湖外，文明益播于颂声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147395_comment'></div>函丈席间，问学骤新于王泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147395_comment'></div>伫俟缄之缃帙，置彼頖宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147395_comment'></div>乡校请观，咸遂专经之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147395_comment'></div>郡人传写，免劳阅市之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147395_comment'></div>仰荷殊恩，永为盛事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1147395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　约于本年，在知睦州任，作《雁阵赋》作品：雁阵赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《咸平集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1147162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雁阵赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以「叶落南翔，云飞水宿」为韵。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147162")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147162'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147162'>绝塞霜早，阴山叶飞，有翔禽兮北起，常遵渚以南归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147162_comment'></div>一一汇征，若阵行之甚整；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147162_comment'></div>嗷嗷类聚，比部曲以相依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147162_comment'></div>当乎朔野九秋，湘天万里，风萧萧兮吹白草，雁嗈嗈兮向寒水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147162_comment'></div>单于台下，繁笳之哀韵催来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147162_comment'></div>句践城边，两槊之幽音惊起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147162_comment'></div>颉颃交相，翩翻迭翔，似鱼丽之布列，若鹅鹳之舒张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147162_comment'></div>疏密有绪，高低载飏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147162_comment'></div>天空而残月铺影，水阔而微云间行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147162_comment'></div>应遵丹凤诏书，咸增跃跃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147162_comment'></div>虽是苍鹰鸷勇，敢击堂堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147162_comment'></div>观其唳青霄，横碧落，历江渚，达沙漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147162_comment'></div>来若羽林骑士，闻一鼓以争前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147162_comment'></div>去如翼卫材官，听摐金而稍却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147162_comment'></div>岂天阵地阵之能询，何圆阵方阵之足云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147162_comment'></div>但见乘夕霭，拂朝云，羽翼自高，不让于汉家飞将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147162_comment'></div>烟霞远没，疑沈于朔土孤军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147162_comment'></div>宜乎后伍先偏，声交影接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147162_comment'></div>当塞上之飘雪，值江皋之坠叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147162_comment'></div>纵横势定，阵图按牧野之师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147162_comment'></div>绰约体轻，兵法试吴宫之妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147162_comment'></div>唯有淮之北，汉之南，山如画，水如蓝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147162_comment'></div>离离而霞彩旁衬，一一而波光远涵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147162_comment'></div>旋成偃月之形，悠飏可爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147162_comment'></div>忽变常山之势，首尾相参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147162_comment'></div>乃知接武烟鸿，追踪霜鹄，既横空而似阵，自违寒而顺燠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147162_comment'></div>北方远兮南图，遥云飞兮水宿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1147162_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　约于本年，在知睦州任，游桐谿，有诗。作品：桐谿行。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桐溪行</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81846")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81846'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81846'>东郊驿树连理枝，西庙丛篁十丈围。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81846'>堪将轻素命人画，赍为方物归京师。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81846'>公署石楠圆似盖，画楼北面当厅桧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81846'>桐溪怪石胜太湖，贱如泥土无人爱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81846'>天生弥材地且卑，空山老朽人不知。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
