id='poem_sentence_5_81846'>人不知，睦州右史作歌词。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81846'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_81846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　春，在知睦州任，有诗酬刁衎。作品：酬桐庐知县刁衎歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。罗谱系此诗于雍熙三年，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_81859' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81859' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81859?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬桐庐知县刁衎歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81859")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81859_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81859'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81859'>诏守江西新定郡，二年抚俗谁相问。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81859'>白浪青山绕郡城，卧理烟霞称嘉遁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81859'>帝乡迢迢天一涯，子牟恋阙人不知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81859'>慷慨情怀何企慕，宋璟政事杜牧诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81859'>六县万家人辑睦，鱼盐利人茶货足。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81859'>公家事简案牍稀，芳草疏篱映空狱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81859'>杨柳湖边观钓鱼，芙蓉池上静看书。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81859'>优游天爵浩然性，贵如三入承明庐。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81859'>靖节先生来访我，欣然延入皇<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作黄）</span>堂坐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81859'>敛襟欲坐先发言，捧出尺书双袖间。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81859'>七轴好词同跪授，儒雅礼丰情意厚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81859'>主人识鉴非延陵，金石何烦荣固陋。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81859'>且置琼瑶未暇看，高谈如绮有馀欢。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81859'>黄鹂百啭天欲暮，客去斜阳已半轩。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81859'>焚香道院无人到，风花<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作花风）</span>拂几收真诰。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81859'>却取文编一一看，南朝体制多渊奥。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81859'>两轴七字五字诗，珠贯累累乐府词。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81859'>古于禅月画罗汉，丽于范蠡进西施。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81859'>议论精微穷理窟，赋咏升高能体物。<div id='poem_sentence_18_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_81859'>一篇序送周子通，飘飘思若翻冥鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_19_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_81859'>自有沧浪高尚志，因人命笔生词锋。<div id='poem_sentence_20_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_81859'>尝闻水国清辉殿，曾事吴王侍文宴。<div id='poem_sentence_21_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_81859'>田园未遂归去来，严子台边知一县。<div id='poem_sentence_22_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_81859'>古人穷则善一身，达则惠泽如阳春。<div id='poem_sentence_23_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_81859'>一邑生灵如受赐，何须兼济方为贵。<div id='poem_sentence_24_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_81859'>金门吏隐能安身，何必弃官为逸人。<div id='poem_sentence_25_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_81859'>桐庐山水幸堪赏，歌诗酬唱且相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_26_81859_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_81859'></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_81859_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　秋，在知睦州任，游七里滩，有诗。作品：七里滩。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_53738' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53738' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53738?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七里滩</a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53738")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53738_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53738'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53738'>清泚寒流走白沙，钓台苍翠远嵯峨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53738'>隔溪人语穿芳树，旁岸鱼跳落浅莎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53738'>几处上源堪涉渡，有时野艇并来过。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53738'>秋声不尽吟诗意，七里潺湲奈尔何。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53738'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53738_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年4月</a>　四月，在知睦州任，上表贺曹彬奏捷。作品：贺曹彬奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147321?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺曹彬奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147321")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147321'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147321'>臣锡言：今月七日，进奏院状报三月十七日并州、雁门两路前军都部署、侍中曹彬等奏：三月八日并十日，杀下蕃贼二千馀人，馀三千馀人中伤，其馀并皆逃遁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147321_comment'></div>并涿州、寰州等伪命官吏率百姓僧道归降，已安抚讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147321_comment'></div>伏以皇威大振，戎捷遐闻，才兴貔虎之师，遽破犬羊之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147321_comment'></div>照临所被，欢抃皆同<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147321_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下抚宁万国，底定三边，武经方咏于止戈，文德诞敷于振铎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147321_comment'></div>尚以蓟门遗俗，久不隔于虏廷，燕朔旧疆，宜复归于王略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147321_comment'></div>安边上策，或伐叛以怀来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147321_comment'></div>命帅嘉谋，亦乘机而破敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147321_comment'></div>滹水朝宗之浪，方鼓威声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147321_comment'></div>稿街献捷之音，载光睿算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147321_comment'></div>臣伏限所守，不获奔诣阙庭，无任瞻天恋圣、欢呼激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147321_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年4月</a>　四月，在知睦州任，上表贺潘美奏捷。作品：贺潘美奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147322?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺潘美奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147322")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147322'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147322'>臣锡言：今月十三日，进奏院状报三月十九日至二十日，云、应、幽、朔等州行营都部署、太师潘美等奏，伪命节度副使赵希赞等率军民一万五千馀人归降，并飞狐北杀下贼军三万馀人，活捉到伪命冀州防御使大鹏翼、康州刺史马赟已下，及收到衣甲器械羊马牛畜牌印等不少者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147322_comment'></div>伏以睿算无遗，王师继捷，塞外之飞章叠至，寰中之吉语交闻<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147322_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下圣德昭彰，天机果断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147322_comment'></div>垂衣裳而致理，治即用文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147322_comment'></div>利弧矢以宣威，动惟经武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147322_comment'></div>狼星未灭，宜鈇钺以专征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147322_comment'></div>虎旅争先，鼓雷霆之奋怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147322_comment'></div>伫系单于之颈，郊庙献俘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147322_comment'></div>即覃英主之恩，策勋饮至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147322_comment'></div>车书混一，历数登三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147322_comment'></div>表瑶图保大之功，行玉检告成之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147322_comment'></div>臣限拘外任，恭听捷音，无任欢呼庆快、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1147322_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年4月</a>　四月，在知睦州任，上表贺容怀意奏捷。作品：贺容怀意奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147323' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147323' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147323?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺容怀意奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147323")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147323_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147323'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147323'>臣锡言：今月十七日，进奏院状报三月二十五日至二十六日，内品容怀意等走马到阙奏，大军于涿州南杀下蕃贼一千馀人，并应州及飞狐军伪命官吏率所属二万馀人归降，收到衣甲鞍马钱帛粮草不少者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147323_comment'></div>伏以庙朝决胜，将帅成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147323_comment'></div>四夷八蛮，益震威加之令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147323_comment'></div>一月三捷，未如神速之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147323_comment'></div>凡被照临，同深庆快<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147323_comment'></div>臣闻周称猃狁，汉曰匈奴，负恩则违背欢盟，肆暴则侵挠边鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147323_comment'></div>茍非皇威景铄，王道融明，授金钺以专征，出玉关而拓境，则何以致腥膻族类，来朝礼义之乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147323_comment'></div>舄卤山川，复正要荒之服？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147323_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下至仁无敌，我武惟扬，以帝尧丹浦之师，破丑虏黑山之众，未踰浃日，连下数城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147323_comment'></div>岂烦筑垒以受降，但庆献俘而执馘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147323_comment'></div>饮马长城之窟，金石登歌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147323_comment'></div>鸣鸾日观之峰，人神共悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147323_comment'></div>臣任当求瘼，职忝记言，屡闻奏捷之音，限远对扬之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147323_comment'></div>臣无任惶恋欢呼、激切屏营之至<span class='inlineComment2'>（《咸平集》卷二三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147323_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1147323'>「院状」二字原脱，据文渊阁库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1147323_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年4月</a>　四月，在知睦州任，上表贺潘吉奏捷。作品：贺潘吉奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺潘吉奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147324")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147324'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147324'>臣锡言：今月二十六日，进奏院状报外殿直潘吉今月三日走马到阙奏，三月二十八日大军到灵丘城下，伪命官属七千馀人归降，收到衣甲器械钱帛粮草不少者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147324_comment'></div>伏以王者之师，有征无战；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147324_comment'></div>庙谋之胜，一举万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147324_comment'></div>捷音屡下于边城，喜气弥高于率土<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147324_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下日新圣德，天赞皇勋，舜干方舞于两阶，禹会悉朝于万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147324_comment'></div>蠢兹戎丑，敢逭灵诛，劳将帅以专征，出车徒而薄伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147324_comment'></div>天山牧马，瀚海洗兵，我师无遗镞之勤，彼寇有绝弦之败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147324_comment'></div>燕然铭勒，信千载之一时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147324_comment'></div>梁甫直笾，俟八鸾之肆觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147324_comment'></div>臣亟闻飞奏，但切欢呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147324_comment'></div>白日倾葵藿之心，沧溟系匏瓜之迹，不获随例，蹈舞阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147324_comment'></div>臣无任庆快惶恋、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1147324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年5月</a>　五月，在知睦州任，上表贺李规奏捷。作品：贺李规奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺李规奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147325")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147325'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147325'>臣锡言：今月三日，进奏院状报四月九日外殿直李规走马到阙奏，大军收下云川，杀戮贼军并尽，所有百姓并依圣旨存留安抚讫，并收到衣甲器械鞍马钱帛粮草极多者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147325_comment'></div>伏以王师乘胜，戎垒克平，尽白日之照临，庆皇家之胜捷<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147325_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下恩流万国，威驭四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147325_comment'></div>执玉涂山，猃狁旷宾王之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147325_comment'></div>洗兵瀚海，嫖姚成破虏之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147325_comment'></div>婴城固守者必诛，徯后昭苏者即赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147325_comment'></div>果霈涵濡之泽，俾新污染之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147325_comment'></div>七德彰明，三边静谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147325_comment'></div>伫魁渠之系颈，生致阙庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147325_comment'></div>用亿兆以为心，跻于寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147325_comment'></div>忝分朝寄，远在海涯，恨无羽翼以奋飞，徒仰天颜以咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147325_comment'></div>臣无任惶恋欢呼、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1147325_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年5月</a>　五月，在知睦州任，上表贺张明奏捷。作品：贺张明奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张明奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147326")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147326'>臣锡言：今月七日，进奏院状报四月九日至十一日外殿直张明等相次走马到阙奏，大军于新城东北并蔚州南飞狐口，杀下蕃贼二千馀人，活捉到四百馀人，收到鞍马衣甲器械不少，内外文武臣寮，取十三日称贺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147326_comment'></div>伏以细柳出兵，仗皇威而必胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147326_comment'></div>甘泉举燧，与飞走以俱来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147326_comment'></div>凡闻克捷之音，共庆荡平之策<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147326_comment'></div>伏以王者用刑之理，叛则先诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147326_comment'></div>戎人伏莽之心，困犹思斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147326_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下兆民子育，六合家为，孚大信于豚鱼，薰至和于草木，所以嘉禾生而灵芝出，白雉贡而丹凤来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147326_comment'></div>蠢兹种落之人，不及飞鸣之类，敢背恩信，尚肆陆梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147326_comment'></div>劳沙塞以驱除，污霜锋之杀戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147326_comment'></div>云驱雷扫，蚁散狼嗥，委戈甲以谷量，收马牛于风逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147326_comment'></div>猛将与谋臣之捷，青史书勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147326_comment'></div>三公率百辟以朝，黄金上寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147326_comment'></div>臣忝分忧寄，屡听边功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147326_comment'></div>美盛德之形容，空思作颂：庆吉音而鼓舞，莫睹献俘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147326_comment'></div>臣无任欢呼惶恋、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1147326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年5月</a>　五月，在知睦州任，上表贺简昌寿奏捷。作品：贺简昌寿奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺简昌寿奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147327")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147327'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147327'>臣锡言：今月十一日，进奏院状报四月十八日内品简昌寿走马到阙奏，大军于飞狐北口下寨，有蕃贼救援蔚州，寻赶趁二十馀里，杀下首领二人，并杀契丹三千馀人，捉到马三百馀匹，收到衣甲器械不少者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147327_comment'></div>伏以驱除戎狄，恢复边陲，四方闻胜捷之音，千载庆升平之运<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147327_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下功超邃古，道掩前王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147327_comment'></div>念污俗之来苏，轸渔阳之未下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147327_comment'></div>风雷威令，体天道之恶盈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147327_comment'></div>鼙鼓戒严，谋帅臣之薄伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147327_comment'></div>追奔逐北，斩馘献俘，以败不相救之戎，立举必成功之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147327_comment'></div>伫清氛祲，即咏凯旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147327_comment'></div>汉家无烽火之虞，烽画正要荒之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147327_comment'></div>臣限违朝阙，叨守诏条，陪寿觞称庆以无由，望魏阙欢呼而但切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147327_comment'></div>臣无任抃蹈惶恋、激切屏营之家。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147327_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年5月</a>　五月，在知睦州任，上表贺张冲奏捷。作品：贺张冲奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1147328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147328?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺张冲奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147328")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147328'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147328'>臣锡言：今月十六日，进奏院状报四月二十五日张冲走马赴阙奏，大军在蔚州城下，有城内壮丁许彦钦等结连本城兵士五千馀人，杀逐出契丹首领萧毁理，及捉到伪命同州节度使充蔚州盐城使耿绍并男孙共四人，把定城池归明，寻入城安抚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147328_comment'></div>伏以庙社乘灵，边疆克复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147328_comment'></div>三军勇胜之势，迅如疾雷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147328_comment'></div>万方庆快之心，融为和气<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147328_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下体法玄穹，建用皇极，胜妖以圣明之德，御侮行仁义之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147328_comment'></div>禹别九州，夷狄远居于荒外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147328_comment'></div>唐分十道，云、岚近在于河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147328_comment'></div>戎性不常，狼心既野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147328_comment'></div>中原多事，叛违则辄肆侵渔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147328_comment'></div>圣主临朝，攻取则自然败衄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147328_comment'></div>城中士庶，或逐出于元凶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147328_comment'></div>塞外貔貅，或生擒于渠帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147328_comment'></div>斯乃天赞平戎之策，神资无敌之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147328_comment'></div>致彼人心，自相矛盾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147328_comment'></div>成我国讨，不动干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147328_comment'></div>金微玉关，复置羁縻之郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147328_comment'></div>杨柳杕杜，伫旋逻逤之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147328_comment'></div>昭彰圣功，歌咏睿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147328_comment'></div>臣伏限所守，恭听捷音，阻观露布以献俘，但仰云天而拜庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147328_comment'></div>臣无任欢呼惶恋、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1147328_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年8月</a>　八月，在知睦州任，作睦州孔子庙记。作品：睦州夫子庙记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷九六。）</span><div id='poem_1147487' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147487?labeling=true' target='_blank'>睦州夫子庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（雍熙三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147487")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147487_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147487'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147487'>夫子之道，布在六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147487_comment'></div>深于六经者，得其时、遇其主而用之，则王道明而万邦受其赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147487_comment'></div>夫子之庙，列在郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147487_comment'></div>典于郡县者，习其礼、洁其诚而祀之，则庙貌严而诸儒知所宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147487_comment'></div>不然，则帝王之道未融，卿大夫弃德背义，而朝廷礼乐似是而非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147487_comment'></div>祭祀之礼不修，士庶民淫祀徼福，而春秋享奠如存若亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147487_comment'></div>宜其宫垣阒寂，草木罗生，祠宇荒芜，风雨不庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147487_comment'></div>矧浙江之右，桐溪之滨，建邦于山邑之间，居民多水潦之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147487_comment'></div>岿然旧庙，密迩通沟，当子城东南之隅，在故垒闉阇之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147487_comment'></div>藩篱疏壤，固无数仞之高；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147487_comment'></div>堂庑湫隘，且非两楹之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147487_comment'></div>水至则几筵斯没，水落则塑像其颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147487_comment'></div>不堪庳陋之忧，安仰高明之祀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147487_comment'></div>加以俗巫交惑，徼求木偶之灵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147487_comment'></div>风教未还，奔走金人之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147487_comment'></div>迨乎祀先圣，享先师，食禄者忽略而不知，为儒者流荡而忘返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147487_comment'></div>锡以东岳待封之岁，移殿是邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147487_comment'></div>北戎薄伐之年，议迁此庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147487_comment'></div>人来献地，县亦庀徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147487_comment'></div>宫赞温仲舒佥谋之，护戎张元吉辅成之，督邮丘直方经营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147487_comment'></div>七月某日兴役也，八月上丁释奠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147487_comment'></div>庙无祭器，拜章以请之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147487_comment'></div>郡无经书，上言以求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147487_comment'></div>志素王之新祠，成斯文也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147487_comment'></div>列门人之遗像，题旧赞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147487_comment'></div>翼翼诸庑，不浃日而成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147487_comment'></div>慺慺众心，不俟募而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147487_comment'></div>惜乎乡饮酒之礼久废，人不知尊卑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147487_comment'></div>党有序之学久废，人不识廉耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147487_comment'></div>列郡无轩悬之乐，祭不足观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147487_comment'></div>在笥非衮冕之衣，礼不足取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147487_comment'></div>《白华》、《南陔》之诗寝，则无以警不孝不悌之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147487_comment'></div>頖宫、齿胄之仪亡，则无以训为臣为子之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147487_comment'></div>然庙不立则释奠无所就，礼不备则释菜无所观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147487_comment'></div>是以筑为儒宫，修其祀事，请笾豆之古器，复牲币之旧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147487_comment'></div>祭之者可以交神明，观之者可以知劝教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147487_comment'></div>神明交则福至，劝教明则化行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147487_comment'></div>夫世之浇淳在乎时，礼之用舍由乎上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147487_comment'></div>故颜回谓舜亦人也，孟轲曰回亦人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147487_comment'></div>若然，则克念谓之圣，罔念谓之狂，必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147487_comment'></div>祖述夫子之至仁，宪章颜氏之亚圣，则文中子亦人也，韩文公亦人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147487_comment'></div>乃知取法于延陵季子，问礼于柱史老聃，生而知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147487_comment'></div>学而知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147487_comment'></div>勉人之学，读是碑也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147487_comment'></div>迁庙之志，见是记也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147487_comment'></div>罪言者得于斯，知言者得于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147487_comment'></div>时雍熙三年八月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1147487_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　秋，在知睦州任，有诗和温仲舒。作品：和温仲舒寄赠。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于雍熙二年，此据诗意改。）</span>和温仲舒感怀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于雍熙二年，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_53747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53747' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53747?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和温仲舒寄赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53747")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53747'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53747'>桐江秋水锦鳞肥，闲钓烟波是见机。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53747'>野步共游芳草径，吟情对启白云扉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53747'>醉来拾笔题红叶，睡觉凭栏望翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53747'>官满替人如未到，蒹葭玉树且相依。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53747'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53747_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和温仲舒感怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53748")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53748'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53748'>郡斋松盖翠斜攲，客至鸣琴汎酒卮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53748'>江上正当摇落景，天涯空惜太平时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53748'>寻残幽谷春难到，兰茂深林众岂知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53748'>上国三千王百里，杨梅熟日是归期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53748'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　秋，在知睦州任，有诗。作品：倚楼。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于雍熙二年，此据诗意改。）</span>秋怀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于雍熙二年，此据诗意改。）</span>桐江即事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于太平兴国八年，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_53784' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53784' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53784?labeling=true' target='_blank'>倚楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53784")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53784_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53784'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53784'>西楼吟倚若为情，情似浮云处处生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53784'>翠叠乱山千里阔，红翻晴叶一川明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53784'>散分野色渔村小，斜衬秋光雁阵横。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53784'>回望帝乡归未得，芦花如雪绕江城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53784'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53784_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53752' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53752' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53752?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53752")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53752_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53752'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53752'>蒹葭深处古严州，吟向潺湲为送秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53752'>云映疏钟红叶寺，浪摇孤角翠微楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53752'>土茅路远催先贡，霜稻天晴趁早收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53752'>零落黄花正西<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作哂）</span>笑，应怜印绶尚淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53752'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53752_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_53758' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53758' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53758?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桐江即事</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53758")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53758_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53758'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53758'>沧州深隐未言归，三载桐江解印迟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53758'>官职清华非不达，性灵疏拙欲何为。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53758'>闲移夫子青山庙，拟立严陵钓渚碑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53758'>兼喜溪云每相狎，时来窗户伴吟诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53758'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53758_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　秋，在知睦州任，登七里濑危楼，有赋。作品：望京楼赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《咸平集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1147148' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147148' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147148?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望京楼赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147148")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147148_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147148'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147148'>馀杭上游，古曰严州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147148_comment'></div>入松院兮何处，七里濑兮清秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147148_comment'></div>归去来兮，陋风土之卑湿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147148_comment'></div>日云暮兮，为印绶之縻留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147148_comment'></div>危楼乃登，京师是望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147148_comment'></div>天遥而阊阖来风，海阔而蓬莱架浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147148_comment'></div>云成宫阙，似瞻丹禁之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147148_comment'></div>吾岂匏瓜，久恋沧江之上？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147148_comment'></div>虽汎兰桡，游泳乎子陵之滩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147148_comment'></div>沙虱有毒，又巇险乎鸣渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147148_comment'></div>虽攀云梯，登眺乎乌龙之山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147148_comment'></div>山岚瘴人，恶跻升乎绝顶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147148_comment'></div>《诗》不云乎「式微」，《书》亦畏乎「怀归」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147148_comment'></div>濯缨兮南涧之水，盈襜兮北山之薇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147148_comment'></div>葵藿载倾，虽见小人之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147148_comment'></div>枢机一发，岂知君子之机！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147148_comment'></div>然何所不适，孤怀自惜，欲将体物之辞，留向他山之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147148_comment'></div>登高必赋，羡海水之朝宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147148_comment'></div>徒歌曰谣，望长安兮见日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147148_comment'></div>始余来兮，蒹葭苍苍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147148_comment'></div>今余言归，白露为霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147148_comment'></div>安得乘彼白云，归乎帝乡？</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1147148_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年12月</a>　十二月，在知睦州任，上表贺田重进奏捷。作品：贺田重进奏捷表一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　本年，在知睦州任，有诗寄人。作品：偶题因怀张王二谏议。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。张、王二谏议，名不详。孙谱系此诗于雍熙二年，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_53788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶题因怀张王二谏议</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53788")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53788'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53788'>理郡三年政未闻，孤城僻在浙江濆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53788'>金门路远书难寄，水国吟馀日又曛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53788'>半夜啼猿千里客，数峰残雪一溪云。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53788'>诗中赢得为官况，不让樊川杜使君。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53788'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　约于本年春，在知睦州任，有诗。作品：登郡楼望严陵钓台。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一五。孙谱系此诗于通判宣州时，此据诗意改。）</span><div id='poem_81806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登郡楼望严陵钓台</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81806")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_81806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81806'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81806'>溪上严陵古钓台，倚楼凝望自徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81806'>先生能保孤高节，英主尝师王霸才。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81806'>日暮白云迷草莽，岸平春水浸莓苔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81806'>登临不尽微吟兴，花落东风首重回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81806'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_81806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年1月</a>　正月，在知睦州任，有谢赐历日奏状。作品：谢赐历日一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二六。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年1月</a>　正月，在知睦州任，上表贺田重进奏捷。作品：贺田重进奏捷表二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span>贺田重进奏捷表三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年1月</a>　正月，在知睦州任，迁起居舍人，依前直史馆，有谢表。作品：谢转起居舍人表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。孙谱系此事于雍熙二年，此据《咸平集》卷二三《贺卢汉赟奏胜捷表》改。）</span><div id='poem_1147335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转起居舍人表</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147335")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147335'>臣锡言：今月七日，递中伏蒙圣恩赐臣官诰敕牒，特授臣起居舍人，依前直史馆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147335_comment'></div>祗膺宠命，迁陟华资，不离近侍之班，俄忝记言之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147335_comment'></div>徬徨拜受，荣惧交并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147335_comment'></div>伏念臣遭遇明时，践扬清贯，才识固惭于兼茂，勤劳常愧于未伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147335_comment'></div>遗补美官，继尘闺籍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147335_comment'></div>封章鄙见，尝受圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147335_comment'></div>加以兼馆殿之清华，历藩宣之委寄，荣踰始望，忝已居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147335_comment'></div>岂谓才毕严禋，遽沾庆泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147335_comment'></div>珥笔丹墀之下，恋阙罙深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147335_comment'></div>颁条沧海之滨，分忧岂称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147335_comment'></div>敢忘恭恪，以赎贪叨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年1月</a>　正月，在知睦州任，上表贺卢汉赟奏捷。作品：贺卢汉赟奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。孙谱系此文于端拱元年，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺卢汉赟奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147329")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147329'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147329'>臣锡言：今月二十三日，进奏院报十二月二十五日代州驻泊副部署卢汉赟等差高班内品李延遇入奏，契丹贼军入界打劫，寻于土镫寨杀下蕃贼，斫到首级二千馀个，活捉到契丹五百馀人，马一千馀匹，及杀下北大王男一人、监军舍利一人首级，夺到牛羊车帐衣甲器械不少者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147329_comment'></div>伏以方隅胜捷之音，天聪远达；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147329_comment'></div>华夏欢呼之列，日域遐周<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147329_comment'></div>臣闻边鄙之虞，有备无患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147329_comment'></div>蕃戎之性，驱去复来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147329_comment'></div>是资逻逤之兵，时闻克捷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147329_comment'></div>可赏嫖姚之将，屡献功勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147329_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下道德为藩，慈俭曰宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147329_comment'></div>王度贞明于金玉，皇风混一于车书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147329_comment'></div>戎狄来朝，必饰稿街之馆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147329_comment'></div>犬羊入寇，即兴榆塞之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147329_comment'></div>周宪章五帝之谋，得驾御四夷之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147329_comment'></div>俘囚操袂，郊庙登歌，彰军礼之允修，见睿谋之不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147329_comment'></div>臣方膺诏旨，将赴阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147329_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣、欢抃激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1147329_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='75f1598ab5674376b1260263427e38ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("75f1598ab5674376b1260263427e38ce");'><span id='75f1598ab5674376b1260263427e38ce_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>，45岁</div><div id='75f1598ab5674376b1260263427e38ce' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　本年，在知睦州任，游钓台，有诗。作品：钓台怀古。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷一六。孙谱系此诗于太平兴国八年，此据《咸平集》卷一六《茱萸堰泊》改。）</span><div id='poem_53749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_53749' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/53749?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钓台怀古</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_53749")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_53749_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_53749'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_53749'>闲读铭词扫绿苔，溪边永日自徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_53749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_53749'>白云遗迹今亲到，青史高名不可陪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_53749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_53749'>千古烟霞为己有，一竿风月避谁来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_53749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_53749'>松巅老鹤应相识，时唳和风下钓台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_53749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_53749'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_53749_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
淮阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ddf03cb1ac4f46b0a6bad2e9fbba73fe_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ddf03cb1ac4f46b0a6bad2e9fbba73fe");'><span id='ddf03cb1ac4f46b0a6bad2e9fbba73fe_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=992')">990-992年</a>，51-53岁</div><div id='ddf03cb1ac4f46b0a6bad2e9fbba73fe' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年1月8日</a>　正月八日，到知陈州任，有谢表。作品：陈州谢恩表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1147336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈州谢恩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年1月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147336")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147336'>臣锡言：臣去年十二月二十七日，蒙恩改授官资，兼受敕权知郡事，已于今月八日上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147336_comment'></div>祗膺朝命，颁守诏条，内省非临莅之才，外任当重繁之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147336_comment'></div>感载恩宠，虽实知荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147336_comment'></div>夙夕忧惶，何以致理<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147336_comment'></div>臣每念文学之性，固无所长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147336_comment'></div>谅直之心，庶几有补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147336_comment'></div>始自秘省，擢升谏官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147336_comment'></div>初上封章，遽蒙听纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147336_comment'></div>寻下御札，遍求直言，仍赐臣敕书，以示嘉奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147336_comment'></div>以臣所言者罢交趾之役，以臣所谏者去髡钳之刑，其馀所陈，不敢备述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147336_comment'></div>敕书喻臣曰：「今后凡有见闻，更在无辞献替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147336_comment'></div>或行或寝，断自于朕心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147336_comment'></div>尽节尽忠，勿渝于尔志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147336_comment'></div>臣所以尝思启沃，上答圣明，每有见闻，必陈章疏，非敢沽直臣之誉，但欲酬英主之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147336_comment'></div>臣盖远人，幸逢昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147336_comment'></div>冒涉遐阻，入关知蜀道之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147336_comment'></div>孤苦零丁，挈家比秋蓬之转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147336_comment'></div>遇陛下初登宝位，亲主文衡，于七十四中，忝第二人及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147336_comment'></div>不数年，列在遗补，带馆殿之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147336_comment'></div>先前年，擢知制诰，为侍从之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147336_comment'></div>忝幸若斯，报答无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147336_comment'></div>去岁稍因愆亢，方轸念劳，臣奉敕于太一宫祷告灵仙，祈求雨雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147336_comment'></div>臣所以输忠罄节，因事上言，言多狂愚，事颇切直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147336_comment'></div>天聪采听，亦有施行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147336_comment'></div>圣慈优容，幸无罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147336_comment'></div>洎陛下受宝策以新徽号，御正殿以朝千官，臣以岁节假中，先受恩命，为差出则无例告谢，未朝谢则无因立班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147336_comment'></div>行事捧策之仪，空思佩委；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147336_comment'></div>祝寿称觞之礼，不与山呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147336_comment'></div>恋阙之心，但倾葵藿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147336_comment'></div>颁条之寄，若履冰渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147336_comment'></div>朝廷重委之荣，惧不克荷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147336_comment'></div>交亲相勉之意，亦有所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147336_comment'></div>以臣屡因上书，致兹落职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147336_comment'></div>虽文翰之职，岂臣所能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147336_comment'></div>而物论之间，以臣为诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147336_comment'></div>臣心匪石，虽获罪以宁辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147336_comment'></div>众口若钳，岂达聪之有补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147336_comment'></div>况臣迹疏性拙，言直道孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147336_comment'></div>虑公事之阙遗，去天颜之咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147336_comment'></div>敢不躬亲郡政，上副忧勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147336_comment'></div>佩服官箴，免孤任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147336_comment'></div>然锡尽心无愧，期百生酬君父之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147336_comment'></div>揣分自知，重两制比神仙之职。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1147336_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年1月</a>　正月，在知陈州任，上奏状谢加朝散大夫阶。作品：谢加朝散大夫阶。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1147389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加朝散大夫阶状</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147389")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147389'>右，臣今月八日进奏院递到敕牒一道，蒙恩加朝散大夫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147389_comment'></div>国家以因时覃庆，与物惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147389_comment'></div>勋阶叙进之恩，本酬殊效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147389_comment'></div>雨露无私之泽，亦及微臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147389_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，岂任感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147389_comment'></div>臣窃念素无文学，骤忝掖垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147389_comment'></div>遭逢致身，实知玷幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147389_comment'></div>出入受命，徒罄忠勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147389_comment'></div>方解职于纶闱，俾颁条于藩省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147389_comment'></div>阶衔转改，名品迁升，益为按部之荣，弥励履冰之节。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1147389_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年3月</a>　三月，在知陈州任，有诗寄苏易简等人，求和作。作品：代书呈苏易简学士希宠和见寄以便题之于郡斋也。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81817?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代书呈苏易简学士希宠和见寄以便题之于郡斋也</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81817")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81817'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81817'>金殿尝闻金口言，词臣官职是神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81817'>三年偶忝西垣职，致身似得文章力。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81817'>感激思酬圣主恩，危言所以难缄默。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81817'>出入金门与玉堂，屡因狂直拜封章。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81817'>御戎救旱无上策，言词不足动君王。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81817'>改官出职归郎署，粉围正秩惭叨据。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81817'>仍命淮阳颁诏条，元正不得与趋朝。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81817'>中书舍人捧宝策，加美徽称尊帝尧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81817'>大明殿里上寿酒，翰林学士先群寮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81817'>独有淮阳知郡吏，为典郡符蒙借紫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81817'>閤门引谢正衙辞，撰日忽忽办行李。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81817'>都门柳色早春天，繁台寺中排祖筵。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81817'>离杯满劝不惜醉，醉别上马魂黯然。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81817'>客心易感须如是，回思故国三千里。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81817'>子云相如俱蜀人，我今五十君青春。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81817'>春秋鼎盛正清贵，我年渐似下坡轮。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81817'>下车犹未踰期月，官舍初经禁烟节。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81817'>残阳乍听吹角声，台榭梨花簇香雪。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81817'>独酌不欢何所为，孤怀无绪怀己知。<div id='poem_sentence_18_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_81817'>十八学士相念否，应笑骨凡格且卑。<div id='poem_sentence_19_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_81817'>地仙敢言谪仙宦，海槎却有上天时。<div id='poem_sentence_20_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_81817'>陈州去京地不远，莫惜音书来慰勉。<div id='poem_sentence_21_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_81817'>若得工夫可作歌，歌中言语不厌多。<div id='poem_sentence_22_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_81817'>毕三情旨颇似我，向二宋四及李大。<div id='poem_sentence_23_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_81817'>请与副阁王舍人，呈似此歌希唱和<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_24_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_81817'></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_81817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_81817'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_24_81817_0'>⑴ 四库本注：毕相士安、向相敏中、宋给事湜、李相沆、副阁王禹偁。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_81817_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年7月</a>　七月，在知陈州任，有诗酬句中正。作品：留别句中正学士。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留别句中正学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81847")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81847_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81847'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81847'>玉人欲归留不住，南山出云作朝雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81847'>雨中却柅使车轮，主人重得延嘉宾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81847'>嘉宾有诗留别我，句句高奇字字新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81847'>新若新花凝宿露，高似秋天晓星布。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81847'>奇于云起成峰峦，鲛人泪珠盈玉盘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81847'>浪大月照如金线，金线交加珠可贯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81847'>玦离环合间珠圆，风生玉步声珊珊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81847'>珍奇若此为重赐，斋沐焚香然后看。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81847'>三复吟看既忘倦，命笔和来才思缓。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81847'>桃李难酬琼玖珍，野老美芹聊贽献。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81847'>与君俱是锦江人，今幸星轺来过陈。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81847'>乡情交分忍轻别，少留可待早秋辰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81847'>秋光月华伴行色，步步随君归紫宸。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81847'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_81847_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年9月8日</a>　九月八日，在知陈州任，有诗赠友。作品：赠别琅邪评事兼寄两制旧友。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠别琅邪评事兼寄两制旧交<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作友）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（990年9月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81862")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81862'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81862'>醴泉少府王评事，秀气神清好奇异。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81862'>读书击剑善弹琴，仲容信是青云器。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81862'>我从蜀国来咸秦，长安久客多风尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81862'>因此移居清渭北，与君在彼初相识。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81862'>相识经今二十年，支离契阔长相忆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81862'>去年罢直西掖垣，君亦醴泉方解官。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81862'>关中路遥宛丘道，不远千里来相看。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81862'>我忝淮阳知郡事，郡斋喜闻嘉客至。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81862'>槐花横时初到来，菊花开时言欲回。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81862'>主人苦留留不住，为君采菊登高台。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81862'>高台临古道，北走<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>还京秋已老。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81862'>白日远长安，西归出关天已寒。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81862'>神仙作尉道虽在，骨肉为累心且宽。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81862'>与君俱年五十一，老去时光转堪惜。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81862'>况今秋暮冬欲残，七十唯馀十八年。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81862'>未知十八年之间，悲欢得丧与险艰。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81862'>到得七十即为幸，此外浮生何足言。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81862'>明日正逢重九日，未忍与君张祖席。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81862'>樽前新菊含露滋，茱萸丹实星离离。<div id='poem_sentence_18_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_81862'>茱萸撷芳菊延寿，寿酒满满莫固辞。<div id='poem_sentence_19_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_81862'>淮阳郡吏若早替，帝乡即有相见期。<div id='poem_sentence_20_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_81862'>两制交朋若相问，为我勤勤多谢之。<div id='poem_sentence_21_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_81862'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_81862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_81862'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_81862_0'>⑴ 自注：音奏。《汉书》曰：北走邯郸道。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_81862_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年9月</a>　九月，在知陈州任，有诗酬宋湜、贾黄中。作品：酬宋湜贾黄中二学士菊花之什兼呈诸厅学士。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬宋湜贾黄中二学士菊花之什兼呈诸厅学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81857")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81857'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81857'>靖节先生曾赏菊，东篱有霜花正开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81857'>翰林主人共赏菊，北门吟咏有馀才。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81857'>一唱再和才力健，兼金酬以瑛琼瑰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81857'>善歌使人继其志，远寄淮阳知郡吏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81857'>淮阳郡中方燕居，跪读重缄尺素书。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81857'>中有五章章八句，复有三<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作二）</span>章同一处。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81857'>五章千叶菊花词，一章副翰学士诗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81857'>一章酬和季<span class='inlineComment2'>（毛本、汪本作李）</span>左司。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81857'>人前再读与三复，人从日边初到时。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81857'>敛手先问诸学士，骇目乍窥文字奇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81857'>两制别来今已久，朝寄苑丘权太守。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81857'>眼底唯嫌簿领繁，耳冷不闻骚雅言。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81857'>重阳锡宴不得与，湛露空思奉至尊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81857'>忽捧新诗若为意，闻诗胜得千金赐。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81857'>受知益感恩顾深，吟赏请言清丽致。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81857'>清如玉树生天风，丽若露花开锦宫。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81857'>水精盘中置明月，绛火珊瑚枝叶红。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81857'>珍则难酬青玉案，文律词锋并化工。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81857'>因事喻怀堪自惜，神化丹青与刀尺。<div id='poem_sentence_18_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_81857'>丹青晕淡刀尺裁，先春雪中生早梅。<div id='poem_sentence_19_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_81857'>春饶桃李及时发，牡丹占断芳菲来。<div id='poem_sentence_20_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_81857'>芍药羞人娇且妒，玫瑰倚栏笑欲语。<div id='poem_sentence_21_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_81857'>帝里春从何处归，巫山雨散朝云飞。<div id='poem_sentence_22_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_81857'>遗红堕翠归天下，不失年年三月期。<div id='poem_sentence_23_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_81857'>天生百卉各有时，彼何太盛此何迟。<div id='poem_sentence_24_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_81857'>兼葭苍苍凝白露，西风萧萧向秋暮。<div id='poem_sentence_25_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_81857'>月华篱落有霜华，映篱丛薄生黄花。<div id='poem_sentence_26_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_81857'>花寒叶冷无蜂蝶，固无宝马与香车。<div id='poem_sentence_27_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_81857'>每因九月当重九，暂时采撷浮樽酒。<div id='poem_sentence_28_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_81857'>金钿浮动万岁杯，为君庆祝南山寿。<div id='poem_sentence_29_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_81857'>菊不能言为作歌，金壶酒倾生绿波。<div id='poem_sentence_30_81857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_81857'>重台千叶若堪赏，栽培好近金銮坡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_81857_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年12月</a>　十二月，在知陈州任，上奏状谢赐历日。作品：谢赐历日三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二六。孙谱系此文于淳化二年，此据文意改。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年</a>　冬，在知陈州任，有诗进呈宋太宗。作品：进瑞雪歌。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进瑞雪歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81839")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81839'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81839'>圣德昭彰动天地，岁岁丰穰为上瑞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81839'>明年有闰节气迟，冬深有雪方及时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81839'>三农但喜及时雪，天心帝力岂得知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81839'>臣忝颂条居<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>近辅，劝课农桑理舆赋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81839'>宛丘之下为封部，宣布皇恩愧襦裤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81839'>王泽流而有颂声，因而拜手献歌行。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81839'>歌云岁云暮兮日云暮，白云初向斜阳度。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81839'>斜阳韬掩云舒布，惨惨阴风生北户。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81839'>风来带得霏霏花，花轻片片如琼葩。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81839'>冻黏寒缀纷交加，陌上逡巡铺玉沙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81839'>琪树瑶台相间出，落梅堕絮初堆积。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81839'>映箔横沾翡翠纹，拂窗斜度琉璃隙。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81839'>飘飘千里度龙山，袤丈萧关与玉关。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81839'>海上银台对金阙，水精帘栊鉴明月。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81839'>万年枝上夜辉光，上林先似梨花发。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81839'>黎元有望既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作复）</span>满望，手足舞之而蹈之。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81839'>因思去岁在京师，国家将议改元时。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81839'>时雪未呈盈尺瑞，百神奔走应祷祈。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81839'>海风吹起澄江练，织女金刀碎裁剪。<div id='poem_sentence_18_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_81839'>剪作天花撒翠微，茫茫六合生光辉。<div id='poem_sentence_19_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_81839'>明月宫中玉臼杵，霜兔捣药云母飞。<div id='poem_sentence_20_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_81839'>风筛乍似琅玕宝，翔鸾飞下啄瑶墀。<div id='poem_sentence_21_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_81839'>金门廊庑龙尾道，贺雪千官趁朝早。<div id='poem_sentence_22_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_81839'>吾皇为喜表丰年，六出飞花不令扫。<div id='poem_sentence_23_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_81839'>枢相侍臣初奉宣，宣赴中书赐御筵。<div id='poem_sentence_24_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_81839'>光禄移厨供玉馔，上樽赐酒中官劝。<div id='poem_sentence_25_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_81839'>宣令不醉不得归，席上仍令各赋诗。<div id='poem_sentence_26_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_81839'>诗成封进同奏谢，御制歌行竞传写。<div id='poem_sentence_27_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_81839'>拜舞欢呼感圣明，千年遭遇作门生。<div id='poem_sentence_28_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_81839'>微臣忝幸在两制，得以歌诗乐太平。<div id='poem_sentence_29_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_81839'>而今出典淮阳郡，组绶辉华佩金印。<div id='poem_sentence_30_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_81839'>才微任重副忧勤，履薄临深守廉慎。<div id='poem_sentence_31_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_81839'>圣人德泽如阳春，阳春及物无不均。<div id='poem_sentence_32_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_81839'>微臣怀抱如葵藿，葵藿向阳堪喻身。<div id='poem_sentence_33_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_81839'>今因瑞雪献歌咏，西垣再愿演丝纶。<div id='poem_sentence_34_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_81839'></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_81839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_81839'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_81839_0'>⑴ 原作君，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_81839_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年</a>　本年，在知陈州任，有诗抒归隐之思。作品：归去来。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>归去来</a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81865")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81865'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81865'>归去来，诗不云乎，王事一埤遗我兮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81865'>终日孜孜，心力疲劳齿发衰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81865'>尔今已年五十二，前去七十几多时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81865'>尔性虽拙颇好学，尔才虽短颇好诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81865'>文学歌诗之外非乐为。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81865'>金门玉堂若无分，随分官职胡不归。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81865'>苟能遣得婚嫁累，又何苦忧伏腊资。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81865'>尔不闻仲尼曰，饭疏食饮水，曲肱而枕之。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81865'>乐亦在其中，浮云富贵非尔宜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81865'>表圣表圣，尔当念兹而在兹，勿使无其实而有其词。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81865'>尔若舍灵龟而观朵颐，无乃见尔痴尔痴<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《咸平集》卷二○）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_81865_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年5月14日</a>　五月十四日，在知陈州任，坐稽留杀人狱责授检校右散骑常侍、海州团练副使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
连云港
-----detail
