href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年6月11日</a>　六月十一日，到海州团练副使任，随谢表进《感圣恩诗》二十三韵。作品：海州谢恩表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1147337' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147337' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147337?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海州谢恩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（992年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147337")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147337_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147337'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147337'>臣锡言：伏蒙圣慈以臣莅事疏遗，录问淹滞，尚宽恩宥，责授检校右散骑常侍、海州团练副使，已于今月十一日到州讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147337_comment'></div>祗膺朝命，感惧难任<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147337_comment'></div>臣闻惩劝欲行，赏刑必正，示无私于天下，表至理于区中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147337_comment'></div>实圣明所守之先，纲纪有常之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147337_comment'></div>臣素无才识，本乏声尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147337_comment'></div>每念生于剑南，鄙在草野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147337_comment'></div>父母训励，早令读书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147337_comment'></div>乡里荐称，遂谋干禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147337_comment'></div>相继数举，未成一名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147337_comment'></div>洎朝廷书轨混同，文物光被，臣始携持老幼，涉历险艰，往来咸秦，羁旅京阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147337_comment'></div>值陛下嗣登宝位，振起儒风，微才不遗，群英咸至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147337_comment'></div>臣年三十九及第，便授官资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147337_comment'></div>达不因人，骤升华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147337_comment'></div>阁下三载，每愧忝尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147337_comment'></div>淮阳二年，遂致遗旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147337_comment'></div>据其罪戾，合窜遐荒，尚蒙宥过之恩，俾列副戎之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147337_comment'></div>东海之郡，去京不遥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147337_comment'></div>南风之薰，顺流而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147337_comment'></div>程途自便，骨肉随行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147337_comment'></div>罪重责轻，恩深感极，泄涕知幸，惊魂省躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147337_comment'></div>循过咎之所因，荷生成之罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147337_comment'></div>披陈愚恳，虽在表章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147337_comment'></div>叙罄感怀，合贡歌咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147337_comment'></div>谨奉表称谢，并进五言《感圣恩》诗二十三韵，干冒宸严以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1147337_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年</a>　春，在海州团练副使任，量移单州团练副使，有谢表。作品：谢量移单州表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1147338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢量移单州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147338")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147338'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147338'>臣锡言：今月四日，进奏院递到官告一通，敕牒一道，责授单州团练副使，散官、勋如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147338_comment'></div>五色丝纶，颁于海上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147338_comment'></div>贰车官秩，移近京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147338_comment'></div>既拜命以欣荣，弥省躬而感惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147338_comment'></div>伏以禋宗云毕，庆赐遂行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147338_comment'></div>舍爵策勋，方霈惟新之泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147338_comment'></div>赦过宥罪，遐均作解之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147338_comment'></div>臣每念遭逢，骤尘清切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147338_comment'></div>入居纶阁，莫伸润色之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147338_comment'></div>出典郡符，有误忧勤之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147338_comment'></div>俾从左宦，尚未周星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147338_comment'></div>爰遇严禋，例该殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147338_comment'></div>沧溟之上，随槎泛以将归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147338_comment'></div>白日之辉，觉葵倾而愈近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147338_comment'></div>敢忘补报，仰答休明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1147338_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
涟水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c2c87ba045e543459110b77ae811f6d6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c2c87ba045e543459110b77ae811f6d6");'><span id='c2c87ba045e543459110b77ae811f6d6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年</a>，54岁</div><div id='c2c87ba045e543459110b77ae811f6d6' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，赴单州途中过涟水军，上奏状乞于涟水军暂住。作品：乞住涟水军寄居。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞住涟水军寄居状</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147396")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147396'>右，臣近蒙恩泽，量移单州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147396_comment'></div>荣庆之怀，寻具表章称谢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147396_comment'></div>行迈之次，辄有衷恳披陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147396_comment'></div>臣昨离海州，今至涟水，访闻纲运稍并，河道未通，孤舟深惮于溯流，尽室复当于畏景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147396_comment'></div>乞从私便，须至上言，进退忧虞，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147396_comment'></div>夙夕循省，岂合徼求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147396_comment'></div>但以君亲之恩，所祈或遂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147396_comment'></div>日月之照，洞鉴无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147396_comment'></div>臣素以寠贫，又无兼力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147396_comment'></div>所到之处，既阙人船；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147396_comment'></div>出陆之时，仍乏鞍乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147396_comment'></div>欲乞且寄涟水，以俟后时郊禋，庶令亲属之间，稍遂便安之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147396_comment'></div>干冒旒扆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1147396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，寄居涟水军，上奏状谢许暂居涟水军。作品：谢许涟水寄居。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢许涟水寄居状</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147397")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147397'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147397'>右，臣今月十四日伏睹敕下涟水军，伏蒙圣慈依臣所奏，为乞于涟水军暂住，以俟后时郊禋，兼蒙恩便于涟水军请给料钱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147397_comment'></div>臣伏念请求之恳，虽上达于天聪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147397_comment'></div>忧惕之心，虑有烦于圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147397_comment'></div>方虞罪戾，难逃鈇钺之诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147397_comment'></div>岂谓允俞，俯降丝纶之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147397_comment'></div>加以天慈曲被，月俸仍沾，恤其羁旅之人，遂以便安之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147397_comment'></div>省躬怀感，聚族知恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147397_comment'></div>白日近于帝乡，举头虽见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147397_comment'></div>沧波远于魏阙，回首犹赊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147397_comment'></div>恭俟凤历三周，鸡竿肆赦，已遂量移之志，例该牵复之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147397_comment'></div>当补过以输忠，冀酬恩而展效。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，寄居涟水军，上奏状谢侄田昌裔加阶。作品：谢侄男昌裔加阶。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢侄男昌裔加阶状</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147398")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147398'>右，臣今月十六日递中敕牒到，臣侄男、前涟水主簿昌裔蒙恩加文林郎阶者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147398_comment'></div>伏以礼毕圜丘，庆覃方国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147398_comment'></div>自天之泽，既霶霈于寰区；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147398_comment'></div>犹子之荣，遽转加于阶级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147398_comment'></div>光生里巷，宠浃私庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147398_comment'></div>载惟枝叶之亲，得与簪缨之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147398_comment'></div>举家知感，聚族为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147398_comment'></div>难酬覆焘之恩，徒训廉勤之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147398_comment'></div>臣昨因谪宦，已遂量移，寻蒙圣慈，许寄涟水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147398_comment'></div>忽睹丝纶之命，荣庆既同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147398_comment'></div>但倾葵藿之心，欢呼所共。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1147398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，寄居涟水军，有诗送韩援赴京。作品：送韩援赴阙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《咸平集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_81845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_81845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/81845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送韩援赴阙</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_81845")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_81845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_81845'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_81845'>逢君南浦落花时，送君南浦草离离。<div id='poem_sentence_0_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_81845'>离魂自与白云断，两桨去时乘夕晖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_81845'>昔时汉家称八使，登车便有澄清意。<div id='poem_sentence_2_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_81845'>吾皇宵旰念黎民，歌咏皇华遣使臣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_81845'>昭文馆殿选学士，巡抚使名名号新。<div id='poem_sentence_4_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_81845'>二人分得淮南道，人自日边来既早。<div id='poem_sentence_5_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_81845'>敷宣朝旨达君恩，淮阳父老私有言。<div id='poem_sentence_6_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_81845'>言逢太平歌且舞，利病达聪皆悉闻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_81845'>我昔南宫与西掖，后来谪宦为迁客。<div id='poem_sentence_8_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_81845'>庆泽量移往单州，长淮涂次泊孤舟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_81845'>昌黎工部未相识，一见怡然如旧游。<div id='poem_sentence_10_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_81845'>诗酒论交各相许，何如李白杜工部。<div id='poem_sentence_11_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_81845'>海上往来将月馀，烟波寄诗兼寄书。<div id='poem_sentence_12_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_81845'>书里情深若江汉，诗中意重若琼琚。<div id='poem_sentence_13_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_81845'>今说归京忍轻别，别夜波光荡明月。<div id='poem_sentence_14_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_81845'>若到朝廷话鄙夫，为说子牟心恋阙。<div id='poem_sentence_15_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_81845'>阙下交游忆者谁，翰林苏毕韩损之<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：韩丕字损之。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_81845'>凭君与达相思意，梦向金銮款北扉。<div id='poem_sentence_17_81845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_81845'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_81845_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
天水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='71ed8554da2c4b22a5bc2a0d1b3351bd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("71ed8554da2c4b22a5bc2a0d1b3351bd");'><span id='71ed8554da2c4b22a5bc2a0d1b3351bd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年</a>，58岁</div><div id='71ed8554da2c4b22a5bc2a0d1b3351bd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=997&endYear=997')">997年4月</a>　四月，出使秦州，赐崇信军节度使王显加恩官告。<br /></div>

-----title
泰州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cfe7010a008e4d478a8d9bf879dd6168_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cfe7010a008e4d478a8d9bf879dd6168");'><span id='cfe7010a008e4d478a8d9bf879dd6168_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=1001')">998-1001年</a>，59-62岁</div><div id='cfe7010a008e4d478a8d9bf879dd6168' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=998&endYear=998')">998年4月5日</a>　四月五日，到知泰州任，上奏状致谢。作品：泰州谢上。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1147401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泰州谢上状</a><span class='authorDate'>（998年4月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147401")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147401'>右，臣昨奉诏旨，差知泰州，已于今月五日到任上事讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147401_comment'></div>伏念臣素无才术，骤历官常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147401_comment'></div>先帝误知，置之外制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147401_comment'></div>陛下擢用，列于内庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147401_comment'></div>臣每忧致疏遗，惭无裨益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147401_comment'></div>难进易退，辄效古人，量材授官，因告明主，遂有状奏，乞归馆中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147401_comment'></div>兼以太祖史书，久未了毕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147401_comment'></div>集贤职分，愿效勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147401_comment'></div>岂谓圣意丁宁，优寄差使，出令典郡，委以亲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147401_comment'></div>告谢之时，既叨敦喻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147401_comment'></div>入辞之后，仍有所陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147401_comment'></div>遽荷殊恩，累降中使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147401_comment'></div>再蒙召对，复得颁宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147401_comment'></div>仰戴恩光，实踰始望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147401_comment'></div>恪守官次，敢不尽忠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147401_comment'></div>自至临行，合有所奏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147401_comment'></div>爰当发日，曾上实封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147401_comment'></div>窃计愚诚，寻达睿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147401_comment'></div>臣识见素浅，年齿已衰，惟陛下以特达知臣，唯臣以愚直奉陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147401_comment'></div>兼因宣召，面奉指挥，候到本州，若有公事，或入递申发，或赴阙奏来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147401_comment'></div>臣实何人，骤承宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147401_comment'></div>况外郡以常行之事，自素有定规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147401_comment'></div>若旧敕有未便之条，必奏取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147401_comment'></div>臣乍违严扆，每念冕旒，敢竭愚诚，敬尘圣鉴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1147401_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年10月</a>　十月，在知泰州任，上表贺傅潜等奏捷。作品：贺傅潜等奏胜捷表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1147341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺傅潜等奏胜捷表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147341")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147341'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147341'>臣锡言：今月八日，进奏院状报镇定高阳关马步军都部署傅潜等奏，九月十七日，先锋、都监石普等杀下蕃贼二千馀人，斫到贼头五百个，夺到马五百匹，衣甲器械不少，奉圣旨取二十五日称贺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147341_comment'></div>伏以明君御宇，圣谟方协于天机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147341_comment'></div>猛士守方，武略咸遵于庙算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147341_comment'></div>果致平戎之绩，以成御寇之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147341_comment'></div>凡在照临，孰不欢庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147341_comment'></div>臣尝读《汉书》，每筹边事，当文帝承祧之始，有匈奴犯塞之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147341_comment'></div>骑入云中，兵屯细柳，但设备胡之策，未闻克狄之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147341_comment'></div>伏惟崇文广武圣明至孝皇帝陛下道冠成康，德高文景，承太祖太宗之大业，应无为无事之昌期，三边平宁，万邦谧静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147341_comment'></div>禋祀宿斋清庙，方表孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147341_comment'></div>效庆灵者百神，执玉帛者万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147341_comment'></div>岂犬羊之众，敢肆猖狂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147341_comment'></div>劳貔虎之师，遂行剪灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147341_comment'></div>以前茅之斥候，成破竹之功勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147341_comment'></div>捷奏星驰，朝闻旒冕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147341_comment'></div>欢声雷动，夕遍寰区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147341_comment'></div>千官庆武定之基，四海仰威加之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147341_comment'></div>臣伏限所守，不获称庆阙廷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1147341_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年11月</a>　十一月，在知泰州任，上表贺宋真宗受册尊号。作品：贺册尊号表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1147342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺册尊号表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147342")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147342'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147342'>臣锡言：臣伏睹报状，宰臣百官上册尊号者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147342_comment'></div>伏以圣主承祧，方新凤历；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147342_comment'></div>群臣推美，爰上鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147342_comment'></div>巍巍既与天比崇，赫赫同大明之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147342_comment'></div>凡在覆载，无不欢呼<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147342_comment'></div>臣早逢昌运，常事先朝，见盛德大业之光辉，成积善馀庆之昭报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147342_comment'></div>仁莫先于守位，孝莫大于扬名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147342_comment'></div>伏惟崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下宝祚传昌，璿图毓粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147342_comment'></div>三载谅阴之礼，候纪爰周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147342_comment'></div>千官拱极之仪，推崇敢后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147342_comment'></div>以为至道广大，上玄崇高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147342_comment'></div>经天纬地谓之文，禁暴戢兵谓之武；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147342_comment'></div>惟睿曰圣，烛理为明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147342_comment'></div>孝惟百行之先，仁冠五常之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147342_comment'></div>封章屡达，听览方回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147342_comment'></div>冲让合于道枢，虚受符于《易》象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147342_comment'></div>尚以荐享清庙，禋祀郊丘，方从徽美之称，以示后先之式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147342_comment'></div>恭以春秋鼎盛，皇王节高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147342_comment'></div>虽成康仁贤，岂迨盛烈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147342_comment'></div>文景俭静，孰侔嘉猷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147342_comment'></div>庆赐浃于华夷，大礼光于典策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147342_comment'></div>南山在咏，永隆万寿之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147342_comment'></div>北极居尊，益表千龄之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147342_comment'></div>臣限拘符竹，方远阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147342_comment'></div>不获从玉辂之清尘，侍祠俎豆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147342_comment'></div>捧宝函之编简，就列轩墀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1147342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年11月</a>　十一月，在知泰州任，上表贺大赦。作品：贺大赦表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺大赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147343")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147343'>臣锡言：臣今月十四日，伏睹制书大赦天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147343_comment'></div>伏以圣德广大，鸿名昭彰，报功于天，推恩逮下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147343_comment'></div>发涣汗之大号，示乾健之垂文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147343_comment'></div>庆赏兼行，罪戾并释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147343_comment'></div>覆载之内，欢呼毕同<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147343_comment'></div>臣闻郊祀天地，配享祖宗，孝莫大于斯，礼莫盛于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147343_comment'></div>伏惟崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下绍登宝位，继守丕图，英睿禀于自然，仁和发于至性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147343_comment'></div>三载恭默，万方平宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147343_comment'></div>示慈惠则删约条科，念忠贤则委用耆旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147343_comment'></div>文德在省，礼乐居先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147343_comment'></div>武功其神，暴乱自弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147343_comment'></div>以一阳来复，有事于南郊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147343_comment'></div>肆赦遂行，宣令于北阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147343_comment'></div>夕遍天下，先阳春而布和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147343_comment'></div>风行域中，与品物而更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147343_comment'></div>释放刑禁，矜宽过尤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147343_comment'></div>蠲复租征，招怀违叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147343_comment'></div>勋劳先赏，遗滞旁求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147343_comment'></div>惠孚茕嫠，恩加存没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147343_comment'></div>合天波之荡涤，同寿域之跻升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147343_comment'></div>凤仪九成，方乐升平之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147343_comment'></div>山呼万寿，伫观封禅之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147343_comment'></div>臣恭守诏条，远在淮表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147343_comment'></div>执笾豆而侍祠祭，就列无由；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147343_comment'></div>倾葵藿而仰照临，驰诚但切。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1147343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年12月</a>　十二月，在知泰州任，上表谢加上柱国勋阶。作品：谢加勋表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147344?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加勋表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147344")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147344'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147344'>臣锡言：臣今月九日，伏蒙圣慈赐臣官告一通，敕牒一道，加上柱国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147344_comment'></div>祗荷宠光，不任感惧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147344_comment'></div>进受勋级，弥觉忝尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147344_comment'></div>伏念臣幸逢昌运，早践周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147344_comment'></div>东观西垣，扬历斯久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147344_comment'></div>内庭外郡，委任非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147344_comment'></div>惭无茂异之才，上答照临之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147344_comment'></div>今以郊祀云毕，庆赏方行，是先春布令之辰，与物惟新之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147344_comment'></div>懋功业者酬其爵土，旌绩效者转以勋阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147344_comment'></div>臣素无微劳，亦受殊赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147344_comment'></div>柱国加于上字，既荷峻迁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147344_comment'></div>励节发于中诚，敢忘尽瘁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1147344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年12月</a>　十二月，在知泰州任，以宋真宗亲征，上表致意。作品：行在起居表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>行在起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（999年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147345")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147345_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147345'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147345'>臣锡言：今月十五日递中伏睹御札，以逆胡犯顺，大驾亲征，法天道之运行，举王师以薄伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147345_comment'></div>百神受职，二仪储祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147345_comment'></div>风霜助肃于皇威，金玉必真于圣裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147345_comment'></div>臣锡伏限所守，不获扈随。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1147345_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年12月</a>　十二月，在知泰州任，上奏状谢赐历日。作品：谢赐历日四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二六。孙谱系此文于咸平三年，此据文意改。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=999&endYear=999')">999年</a>　本年，在知泰州任，与许逖结亲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年1月</a>　正月，在知泰州任，上表贺德音。作品：贺德音表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年2月</a>　二月，在知泰州任，上表贺宋真宗还京。作品：贺圣驾还京表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。孙谱系此文于咸平二年，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147346' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147346' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147346?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺圣驾还京表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147346")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147346_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147346'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147346'>臣锡言：今月七日，伏睹制置茶盐司报状，圣驾正月二十二日还京者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147346_comment'></div>伏以万方系望，鸾舆景从以天旋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147346_comment'></div>六师凯还，凤阙策勋而饮至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147346_comment'></div>照临之下，欢庆毕同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147346_comment'></div>臣闻圣明御宇，既任贤抚理以安民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147346_comment'></div>夷狄犯边，则命将驱除而出境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147346_comment'></div>布在方策，形于诗声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147346_comment'></div>伏惟崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下嗣启丕图，恭临大宝，圣文神武，禀自天资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147346_comment'></div>睿算英谋，谅符幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147346_comment'></div>八表混同于书轨，百蛮奔走于梯航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147346_comment'></div>诏边吏以戢兵，来远人以修德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147346_comment'></div>而契丹久隔朝化，未悛祸心，侵轶边陲，劫略生聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147346_comment'></div>疆埸飞奏，将帅请行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147346_comment'></div>圣慈轸恤于黎元，大驾躬亲于征讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147346_comment'></div>天道助顺，王师立功，不期月而塞垣谧宁，未踰时而车辂旋复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147346_comment'></div>星辰环拱，既瞻北极之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147346_comment'></div>士庶山呼，伫庆东封之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147346_comment'></div>臣忝分朝寄，远限淮滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147346_comment'></div>当鸣鸾顺动之时，无由扈从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147346_comment'></div>及翠凤回还之日，莫遂班迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147346_comment'></div>仰首尧天，向日但倾于葵藿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147346_comment'></div>驰心魏阙，朝宗空羡于波澜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1147346_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年3月1日</a>　三月一日，在知泰州任，上疏论举武勇才器堪任武职事。作品：论举武勇才器奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全宋文》卷八七。）</span><div id='poem_1147305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论举武勇才器奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸平三年三月一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147305")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147305'>臣伏见去年十一月十四日赦文，欲兴行武举，令所司条奏以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147305_comment'></div>今年二月一日，又见转运司行下御史台牒，限五日内举员外郎以下见任京朝官有武勇才器堪任武职，安排充沿边亲民差遣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147305_comment'></div>以臣所见，若为边上要人，访求有武勇才器者，急速如此，窃虑未得尽理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147305_comment'></div>盖见往年朝臣中求武勇者，得刘墀、郑宣等数人，刘墀以易州陷没契丹，郑宣卒无劳效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147305_comment'></div>今又朝臣中求人，臣虑朝臣中武勇者少，设使有武勇，多不愿在武职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147305_comment'></div>况限之以五日奏举，若非相谙识，岂易得人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147305_comment'></div>臣恐举非其人，有误陛下任使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147305_comment'></div>今日是陛下注意于良将之时，是选求文武材干为沿边刺史之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147305_comment'></div>夫理乱必有渐，而安危必先见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147305_comment'></div>臣曾上章，为关西地震是下动之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147305_comment'></div>奏状进入后，降在中书，寻却奉圣旨取索入内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147305_comment'></div>相次，近京诸处，多报军贼逃背，沿黄河劫掠军县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147305_comment'></div>后来驱除，虽稍宁息，昨契丹犯境，闻龙猛兵士三二千人诈作契丹，掳劫河北，今闻散在兖州山林间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147305_comment'></div>又近日西川驻泊神卫军都虞候王均作乱，奔冲剑门，寻已杀戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147305_comment'></div>近又访闻河东州郡泽、潞间亦有盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147305_comment'></div>此实下动之萌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147305_comment'></div>昨李继迁虽授夏州节度使，在彼自称西平王，岂不为将来边患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147305_comment'></div>国家积储粮草，缮完甲兵，尚要素有其备，岂得良将谋臣，料敌制胜，国家却素无备？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147305_comment'></div>若求骑射之艺，勇猛之人，兵法中自有选求之法，便求得人，但要有智谋者指使之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147305_comment'></div>所谓获兔者犬，指踪者人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147305_comment'></div>况善用兵者，人无勇怯，以智略使之，则怯者有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147305_comment'></div>今若限以五日举有武勇才器者，臣实虑怀才抱器者未尽得，奇谋远见未易知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147305_comment'></div>愿陛下于宰相近密商量，别画选求之策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147305_comment'></div>若且于见今节度、防、团、刺史、诸司使副中，有智见勋劳者，选择使用，在陛下以赏罚二柄使之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147305_comment'></div>往年杨业击契丹，侯延广守灵州，人多称许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147305_comment'></div>若见今节度、防、团、刺史、诸司使副中，因赏罚激励，岂无杨业、侯延广辈为国家立功勋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147305_comment'></div>臣又以江南、两浙，自去年至今，民饿者十八九，未见国家精求救疗之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147305_comment'></div>初闻遣使煮粥俵给，后来更不闻别行轸恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147305_comment'></div>今月十二日，有杭州差人赍牒泰州会问公事，臣问彼处米价，每升六十五文足，彼中难得钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147305_comment'></div>又问疾疫死者多少人，称饿死者不少，无人收拾，沟渠中皆是死人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147305_comment'></div>却有一僧收拾埋葬，有一千人作一坑处，有五百人作一窖处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147305_comment'></div>臣又问有无得雨，称春来亦少雨泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147305_comment'></div>臣问既少雨泽，麦苗应损，称彼处种麦稀少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147305_comment'></div>又问饥馑疾疫去处，称越州最甚，萧山县三千馀家逃亡，死损并尽，今并无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147305_comment'></div>其馀明、杭、苏、秀等州积尸在外沙及运河两岸不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147305_comment'></div>虽未审虚实，然屡有听闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147305_comment'></div>兼闻常、润等州死损之人，村保各随地分埋瘗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147305_comment'></div>况掩骼埋胔，是国家所行之事，文王葬枯骨而天下归心，今积尸暴骨如是，而使僧人收藏，村保埋瘗，甚无谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147305_comment'></div>伏乞陛下命使吊奠，以慰幽魂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147305_comment'></div>遣人掩藏，免伤和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147305_comment'></div>所贵王者德泽，及于存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147305_comment'></div>然后访有兼并之家，能出财助国者优奖之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147305_comment'></div>有储蓄之家，能发廪救民者旌酬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147305_comment'></div>又宜放一二年税赋，免三二年徭役，非富商大贾之税不用税，非摘山煮海之货不用徵，用此以安民心，以防盗起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147305_comment'></div>去年淮南地震，臣已画时奏讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147305_comment'></div>又闻江南地震尤甚，望陛下宣御札、降德音以禳灾异，访问枢相以放税赋、减课利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147305_comment'></div>若不可减，臣请以近事比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147305_comment'></div>臣读《五代史》，梁朝、后唐、晋、汉及周，封疆不及千里，江南、两川、两浙、荆湖、广南，各有主帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147305_comment'></div>当时中国多事，尚欲制御蕃戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147305_comment'></div>自太祖平吴、取蜀、下广南，太宗平河东，吴越王举国归朝廷，此国家封疆万里，税赋课利百倍于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147305_comment'></div>除边上所费外，但减省不急之用，则仓廪府库自然盈馀，何必于江、浙饥馑疾疫之后，籍其所出税赋课利，以赡军国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147305_comment'></div>今江南二十七州军，两浙一十六州军，宜知若干州是饥馑疾疫之处，若干不是饥馑疾疫之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147305_comment'></div>其他无灾沴、人无疾疫处，依每年上供钱帛粮草外，馀系灾沴处，朝廷早行指挥，以有均无，以多济寡，以安民生，以防盗起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147305_comment'></div>臣又访闻江、淮每年漕运五百六十万硕米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147305_comment'></div>今年春运不如常年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147305_comment'></div>其江、浙共四十四州军，上供钱帛之数，臣即不知，亦不知朝廷今春规画之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147305_comment'></div>臣但以四十四州军有饿死疾疫处，州军放税赋、减课利、免徭役，是国家安民生、防盗起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147305_comment'></div>《易》不云乎：「君子以思患而预防之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147305_comment'></div>又兵法曰：「攻其东南，备其西北」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147305_comment'></div>谓敌若攻城之东南，当先防备其西北，虑敌人出其不意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147305_comment'></div>今若西北沿边未息侵扰，东南沿海复有骚动，则临时制御必费力，临时筹度难成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147305_comment'></div>今虽差杨允恭等江、淮、两浙巡检，屏除盗贼，朝廷已有此指挥，然于防盗起之萌，致民安之渐，未见朝廷经度也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147305_comment'></div>况所求武勇才器者，要沿边任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147305_comment'></div>又以所举三班使臣，如犯入己赃，即连坐举主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147305_comment'></div>若三班中求廉谨、有行止者，岂得无人，其实亦难得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147305_comment'></div>若连坐举主，则举者必少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147305_comment'></div>又所举员外郎见任京朝官，不如举状，责在举主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147305_comment'></div>如此求人，虑难得人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147305_comment'></div>如此求沿边任使，虑未副圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147305_comment'></div>夫事有本末，理有远近，今不急求谋臣而先求武勇，不思将来之患而务目前之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147305_comment'></div>《易》曰：「王公设险，以守其国」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147305_comment'></div>《汉书》有盗卒起杀长吏、取库兵、放禁囚、驱人民作乱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147305_comment'></div>今诸处城池多不修筑，坏垣填堑，往来如平地，万一卒有盗起，逐处官吏何以固守？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147305_comment'></div>加以在营兵士多非精锐，在库甲仗少有坚完，道路出入之要冲，山川险阻之形胜，有不相统摄之处，有不相叶同之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147305_comment'></div>况太平既久，士卒不惯行阵，将帅不知战守，加以士卒骄而将帅鄙，致昨来傅潜辈临事而茍且，遇敌而进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147305_comment'></div>伏望陛下以选求将帅为急务，以博访谋猷为上策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147305_comment'></div>若止三班中求任使，文班中求武勇，臣窃惧失朝廷大计，失国家大事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147305_comment'></div>臣读《汉书》，见日蚀、地震，必降诏书，求直言极谏之士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147305_comment'></div>必降德音，复赦宥复除之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147305_comment'></div>自去年九月八日淮南地震，九月十六日夜月食，未见降御札、下德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147305_comment'></div>夫至大者天地之变，知几者圣哲之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147305_comment'></div>乞陛下以圣哲知几之心，答天地示变之异，经心于远者大者，图事于未萌未兆，覃恩于饥馑疾疫之处，布德于月食、地震之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147305_comment'></div>况臣忧国之心非今日，言事之疏非一章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147305_comment'></div>自前年将赴任泰州蒙宣召时，后殿面奉圣旨，令臣今后有事入递奏来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147305_comment'></div>今具实封进呈，伏乞圣慈特赐留在禁中披览，可行可止，断在宸衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_84_1147305_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年4月</a>　四月，在知泰州任，子田庆远与许逖之女成婚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年9月</a>　九月，在知泰州任，上表贺老人星见。作品：贺老人星见表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺老人星表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147348")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147348'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147348'>臣锡言：今月十六日，进奏院录到宰臣与百寮诣东上閤门拜表贺老人星见，并批答者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147348_comment'></div>伏以圣君御历，自膺万寿之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147348_comment'></div>上帝垂祥，方协千龄之运<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147348_comment'></div>臣闻动天以德，由诚信发于中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147348_comment'></div>与日齐明，谓照临迨于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147348_comment'></div>伏惟崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下纂承二圣，勤劳万几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147348_comment'></div>以大舜仁孝之心，嗣守洪业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147348_comment'></div>以轩皇清静之理，抚安生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147348_comment'></div>时当太平，物遇至化，和气所感，殊祥遂臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147348_comment'></div>南极见乎寿星，东璧灿其垂象，应秋分之日，当夜朗之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147348_comment'></div>兆民式瞻，仰黄明润大之色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147348_comment'></div>太史伏奏，还祉祐昭彰之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147348_comment'></div>《洪范》休徵，一曰富，二曰寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147348_comment'></div>陛下富有万国，寿比南山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147348_comment'></div>宰臣百寮，既献华封之祝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147348_comment'></div>微臣外任，但怀子牟之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147348_comment'></div>魏阙来归，将觐于三载；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147348_comment'></div>尧樽上寿，阻与于千官。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1147348_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年11月</a>　十一月，在知泰州任，上表贺克复益州。作品：贺克复益州表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺尅复益州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147349")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147349'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147349'>臣锡言：十月三十日，进奏院报十月八日閤门准枢密院劄子，雷有终等奏，九月二十日已取下益州城池，入城杀下贼军三千馀人，所有在城百姓并无杀害，已招安讫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147349_comment'></div>九日，文武臣寮称贺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147349_comment'></div>伏以圣君御极，当书轨之混同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147349_comment'></div>叛卒逆谋，怙山川之险阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147349_comment'></div>枭巢既破，龟城已宁，凡在照临，孰不庆抃<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147349_comment'></div>伏惟崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下谟猷天纵，道德日新，至信及于豚鱼，深恩被于草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147349_comment'></div>昨以坤维分野，民或罹灾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147349_comment'></div>井络妖氛，兵因致讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147349_comment'></div>成算授之于中禁，捷音自至于外区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147349_comment'></div>剑阁先平，刀州后破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147349_comment'></div>王师出如时雨，儒臣应于将星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147349_comment'></div>果成克捷之功，共乐升平之庆，臣忝分朝寄，远在海陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147349_comment'></div>窥邸吏之飞申，已除小寇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147349_comment'></div>闻鼎司之入贺，尽率具寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147349_comment'></div>限守土于淮滨，阻缀班于阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147349_comment'></div>诚如葵藿，但倾向日之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147349_comment'></div>迹在江湖，空羡朝宗之浪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1147349_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年11月</a>　十一月，在知泰州任，上表贺杀王均。作品：贺杀下王均表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1147350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺杀下王均表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147350")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147350'>臣锡言：今月五日，进奏院报雷有终差寄班供奉官安守忠到阙奏，石普、杨怀忠、马贵同共部领军马往荣州路赶趁溃散军贼王均等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147350_comment'></div>十月三日到富顺监，杨怀忠、马贵前阵先与贼人相见，一合杀下军贼，斫到王均首级，掩杀招降到贼人并草补人员等共六千馀人，夺到衣甲器械物色不少，其贼并已剪除净尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147350_comment'></div>奏闻，奉圣旨，劄与中书、閤门、御史台，取今月二十二日称贺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147350_comment'></div>伏以王师所至，无不成功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147350_comment'></div>睿略遐宣，屡闻献捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147350_comment'></div>凡在区宇，孰不欢呼<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147350_comment'></div>臣每读邸报，方乐时平，巴蜀久安，边隅无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147350_comment'></div>防秋戍卒，忽自叛违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147350_comment'></div>御侮出师，已闻剪灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147350_comment'></div>由天道之助顺，见圣策之无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147350_comment'></div>伏惟崇文广武圣明仁孝皇帝陛下嗣守丕图，恭临大宝，跻民于仁寿之域，待下以诚信之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147350_comment'></div>猛士守方，以恩威而抚驭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147350_comment'></div>远人受赐，同覆载之生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147350_comment'></div>岂谓将校负心，辄怀逆节，据城池而僭窃，劳师旅以荡除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147350_comment'></div>尚望生全，更敢逃遁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147350_comment'></div>天施疏网，岂漏凶徒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147350_comment'></div>阵有前锋，先诛元恶，断其首领，夺到甲兵，掩杀至多，招降不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147350_comment'></div>捷奏星驰于阙下，欢声雷动于域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147350_comment'></div>益部山川，永息寇虞之患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147350_comment'></div>蜀城父老，式歌吊伐之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147350_comment'></div>仰庆昌期，弥隆景运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147350_comment'></div>臣忝分朝寄，介在淮滨，趋玉阶以无由，望金门而伸悃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1147350_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年12月</a>　十二月，在知泰州任，上奏状谢赐历日。作品：谢赐历日五。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二六。孙谱系此事于咸平四年，此据文意改。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年12月</a>　十二月，在知泰州任，上奏状乞替还朝。作品：泰州乞替。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。孙谱系此事于十月，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泰州乞替状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1000年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147402")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147402'>右，臣辄披丹恳，上黩皇明，仰祈临照之恩，俯鉴忧虞之抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147402_comment'></div>臣至道三年，蒙恩差与魏廷式同勾当审官院、通进银台封驳司事，因魏廷式奏三司使陈恕已下犯大不恭罪，为所奏与御史中丞李惟清所奏不同，臣所以不敢同其所奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147402_comment'></div>自是魏廷式与臣不和，以此上章乞归馆殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147402_comment'></div>适值三馆中差安德裕、席希叟、韩援、宋镐、王纶、李建中、张复、曾会、乐史、路振等出典州郡，时闻圣意谓臣亦求差遣，遂有敕差臣知泰州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147402_comment'></div>臣以本无意求出，祗为魏廷式性识粗疏，难与之久处，臣所以先自求退，乞归馆殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147402_comment'></div>因诣崇政殿告乞免此差遣，圣旨未允，臣更不敢辞免，遂等候春水进发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147402_comment'></div>未进发间，伏睹二月五日御札以彗星见，令臣下各陈所见，臣遂于三月七日上章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147402_comment'></div>是日至未时，宣召顾问，蒙恩以临行特有颁赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147402_comment'></div>八日，朝辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147402_comment'></div>九日，复进封札子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147402_comment'></div>十一日，中使至，再宣召于崇政殿西阁顾问，仍蒙金口问喻甚日进发，祗半年与替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147402_comment'></div>兼奉圣旨：或有事要面奏，但乘递马赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147402_comment'></div>臣到任上事后，寻发奏谢，状中亦略言讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147402_comment'></div>盖州郡常事，可行即行，不足更烦圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147402_comment'></div>但忧离违陛下左右之后，或有谗谤，所以臣不遂半年与替之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147402_comment'></div>臣今在任已二年八个月，三逢圣节，以官秩未满，朝觐无由，不获随班上寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147402_comment'></div>所谓身在江湖之上，心归魏阙之下，挥涕感恋，情不能忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147402_comment'></div>虽夙夜在公，敢不惕励；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147402_comment'></div>而旦夕望替，盖忧疏遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147402_comment'></div>兼去年曾具奏闻，为臣男长城与即今知兴元府、国子博士许逖家结亲，于今年四月成迎讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147402_comment'></div>缘许逖始因官在泰州居住，臣久在任，虑非稳便，愿归京师，且在馆殿供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147402_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，允臣所奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1147402_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年1月</a>　正月，在知泰州任，获准归阙，上奏状致谢。作品：谢得替。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二七。孙谱系此事于咸平三年十月，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147403?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢得替状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147403")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147403'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147403'>右，臣今月一日，伏蒙圣慈赐臣敕一道，差膳部郎中崔维翰知泰州军州事替臣，令臣候替人到，交割讫，发来赴阙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147403_comment'></div>臣伏念近发奏章，求解所任，追思僭易，方抱忧虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147403_comment'></div>盖以臣素无才能，叨膺任使，考秩将满，劳效蔑闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147403_comment'></div>虽常佩官箴，敢忘惕励；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147403_comment'></div>而愿归仙殿，庶免旷遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147403_comment'></div>岂谓皇明俯鉴于忠诚，睿德特容于上请，今已祗受制旨，恭俟替人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147403_comment'></div>当献岁之令辰，捧出纶之优诏，俯偻拜命，欢呼戴恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147403_comment'></div>路虽远于清淮，心已归于丹阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147403_comment'></div>朝觐在即，荣庆交深。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1147403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年1月</a>　正月，在知泰州任，上表贺德音。作品：贺德音表二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《咸平集》卷二三。孙谱系此事于咸平二年，此据文意改。）</span><div id='poem_1147313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺德音表<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1001年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29680, "北宋", "田锡", "poem_title_1147313")'>田锡</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147313'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147313'>臣锡言：今月二十一日，刑部连到德音，已画时施行讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147313_comment'></div>伏以丝纶作解之恩，非时霶霈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147313_comment'></div>华夷至和之感，向日欢呼<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147313_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下神道知几，文明以理，金玉必贞于王度，机衡以奉于天时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147313_comment'></div>宜乎二仪万灵，祥瑞交荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147313_comment'></div>五风十雨，稼穑屡丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147313_comment'></div>所以答上帝之高明，思下民之劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147313_comment'></div>念其阙乏，或贷以馀粮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147313_comment'></div>恤其罪辜，或省乎庶狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147313_comment'></div>尚疏法网，用涤恩波，取《连山》宥罪之文，行出綍眚灾之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147313_comment'></div>重刑减降，残赋蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147313_comment'></div>仍宽聚啸之徒，俾启自新之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147313_comment'></div>人心感悦，春云护肃杀之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147313_comment'></div>帝德昭宣，秋日丽清光之彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147313_comment'></div>臣忝分忧寄，方远丹墀，臣无任抃蹈激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1147313_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1001&endYear=1001')">1001年2月</a>　二月，在知泰州任，以宋白荐举贤良方正，召还。<br /></div>
-----end
